Surah An’am

            ♦ _*NOOR O ZULMAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (789)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ وَجَعَلَ الظُّلُمَاتِ وَالنُّورَ ۖ ثُمَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بِرَبِّهِمْ يَعْدِلُونَ*

_"Tamam Ta'reefen Allah ke liye makhsoos hain Jisne Aasmanon aur Zameen ko banaya aur Usne tareekyon (Andheron) aur Roshni ko paida kiya. Phir bhi Kafir log doosron ko apne Rab ka Hamsar thaira rahe hain."_
(Surah An'am: 1)

📚📖 🍁
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Aaj se ham Surah Ki Tafseer ka aghaz kar rahe hain. Shurua'at Allah ki Hamd o Sana se ho rahi hai.
🍁
Imam Hasan Askari (as):
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ka 5 Mazahib ke logon se Mubahesa hua. Un mein se ek Majoosi the.
Majoosi ka Aqeeda ye tha ke Duniya ko 2 sifaton mein taqseem karte hain: Khair aur Shar (Good & Evil). Dono ek doosre ke mutazad hai (opposite). Ek Fael (Doer) do opposite kaam nahi karta, isliye dono ka Fael (Doer) alag alag hain. Mein Kainat ke Mudabbir (Manager) do hain. Khair ka Manager Noor aur Shar ka Manager Zulmat (Taareeki) hai.
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne jawab diya agar ye reason hai to phir do kiyon balke zyada hone chahiye. Rang bhi bahut zyada hain to har Rang ka ek Fael.
Phir Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Noor o Zulmat dono ek doosre ki zid (opposite) hain. Ek ki tabiyat mein saud (Ascending) hai aur doosre ki tabiyat mein Nuzool (Descending) hai. Ab batao ke do admi ek hi time par do opposite direction mein nikle ek East to doosra West ki taraf. Ab agar dono apne apne direction mein chalte rahen to kiya dono ek doosre se mil sakte hain?"_
Unhone ne kaha nahi.
Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Phir ye batao ke jab Noor o Zulmat ek doosre ke opposite hain to phir Tulu' (Sunrise) aur Ghuroob (Sunset) ke waqt ikhatte kaise ho jate hain. Jabke unke ijtema mahal hona chahiye tha, iske bawajood unka imtezaj (merger) kaise hota hai?"_
Ye sunkar Majoosi ke paas koi jawab nahi tha.
(Kitab Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Tu apni Noor ki Roshni mein rakhna aur Tareekyon se door rakhna.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚
_*Surah An'am:*_
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Poori Surah An'am ek hi martaba nazil hui thi. Nuzool ke waqt 70,000 Farishton ne iski Mashaiyat ki thi aur woh use Nabi e Akram (saww) ke paas lekar aye the. Lehaza tum is Surah ki Ta'zeem aur Ehteram karo. Is mein Total lafz *"Allah الله*"  sattar 70 bar mazkoor hua hai. Agar logon ko is Surah ke Fawaid ka Ilm ho jaye to woh ise kabhi na chhoden."_
(Kitab Sawabul Aamaal)
📚
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Jo Surah An'am ki pahli 3 Ayaat padhe to Allah 40,000 Farishton ko muwakkal karega jo apni Qayamat tak ki Ibaadat ka Sawab uske liye tehreer karte rahenge aur saton Aasmaan se ek Farishte ko nazil karta hai jiske haath mein lohe ka guzar hota hai. Jab Shaitan uske dil mein waswasa ya koi khayal dalna chahe to woh use us Aheni Gurz (Iron Rod) se maarta hai."_
(Sawabul Aamaal, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                ♦ _*TEENAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (790)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هُوَ الَّذِي خَلَقَكُمْ مِنْ طِينٍ ثُمَّ قَضَىٰ أَجَلًا ۖ وَأَجَلٌ مُسَمًّى عِنْدَهُ ۖ ثُمَّ أَنْتُمْ تَمْتَرُونَ.*

_"Wohi to hai jisne tumhe Mitti se paida kiya, phir tumhare liye zindagi ki ek muddat muqarrar kar di, phir ek tay shuda muddat uske paas hai phir bhi tum shak mein mubtila ho. Wohi ek Khuda Aasmanon mein bhi hai aur Zameen mein bhi."_
(Surah An'am: 2)

📚📖 ⏳
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Har Insaan Mitti se bana hai lekin is Mitti ki bhi alag alag quality hoti hai. Mitti ki quality ki mutabiq is Duniya mein Insaan harkatein karta hai.
🍁
Imam Zainul Abidin (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Anbiya e Karam ke Quloob aur abdaan (Heart & Body) dono ko "Teenat e Illiyeen *طينت عليين*" se paida kiya aur Momenin ke Dilon ko us Teenat se paida kiya aur Momenin ke Abdaan ko usse kam darje ki Teenat se paida kiya. Kuffar ke Quloob o Abdaan dono ko "Teenat e Sijjeen *طينت سجين*" se paida kiya. Phir dono Teenon ko ek doosre se milaya. Isi ikhlaat (mixture) ki wajah se Momin ke ghar Kafir paida hota hai aur Kafir ke ghar Momin paida hota hai aur isi Teenat ke merger ki wajah se Momin ghalat kari kar leta hai aur Kafir Nek kaam kar baithta hai. Momin ke Dil apne Madda e Takhleeq (Matter of Creation) ki taraf mushtaq rahte hain aur Kafiron ke Dil apne Madda e Takhleeq ki taraf mael rahte hain."_
(Usoole Kaafi)
🍁
Imam Sadiq (as):
"Teenat 3 tarah ki hain:
(1) Anbiya aur Momin ki Teenat lekin Anbiya ki Teenat Aala Tareen aur fazilat ki hamil hai. Ahle Imaan "Teen e Lazib *طين لازب*" ki shakh hai. Allah Ta'ala Anbiya Karam aur unke Shiyon mein judai nahi dalega jabke Nasibi ka Madda e Takhleeq "Hamain Masnoon" *حماء مسنون* " wali Teenat hai aur Mustaza'feen مستضعفين ka talluq aam khak خاك (Mitti) se hai. Momin apne Imaan se munharif nahi hoga aur Nasibi adawat e Ahle Bait (as) se baaz nahi ayega aur Allah ki Mashiyat ke apne Faisle hain."
(Usoole Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hamari Teenat ko Illiyeen mein barqarar rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⏳
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)! Main aur aap dono ek teenat (mitti) se khalq kiye gaye hain. Aur jo mitti oos mitti se bach gayi oos se hamare Shiyo'n ko khalq kiya gaya hai aur jab Qayamat ka din hoga to logo'n ko unki Maa ke naam se pukara jaayega siwaaye aap ke Shiyo'n ke. Pus unko unke baap ke naam se pukara jaayega, kyun ki unki wilaadat paak hai."_
Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p208
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ _*AJAL-E-MUSAMMA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (791)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هُوَ الَّذِي خَلَقَكُمْ مِنْ طِينٍ ثُمَّ قَضَىٰ أَجَلًا ۖ وَأَجَلٌ مُسَمًّى عِنْدَهُ ۖ ثُمَّ أَنْتُمْ تَمْتَرُونَ * وَهُوَ اللَّهُ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَفِي الْأَرْضِ ۖ يَعْلَمُ سِرَّكُمْ وَجَهْرَكُمْ وَيَعْلَمُ مَا تَكْسِبُونَ*

_"Wohi to hai jisne tumhe Mitti se paida kiya, phir tumhare liye zindagi ki ek muddat muqarrar kar di, phir ek tay shuda muddat uske paas hai phir bhi tum shak mein mubtila ho. Wohi ek Khuda Aasmanon mein bhi hai aur Zameen mein bhi. Woh tumhare poshida (hidden) aur khule Raaz (Open Secrets) ko bhi jaanta hai aur jo kuchh tum kar rahe ho Woh use bhi jaanta hai."_
(Surah An'am: 2 - 3)

📚📖 ⌛🕰
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ayat no. 2 ke zel "Teenat" ke bare mein kuchh Rivayaat pesh ki thi. Usi Ayat mein jo doosra mauzoo hai woh 'Ajal e Musamma *أجل مسمى*" hai.  Means Fixed Time.
⏰
Imam Sadiq (as):
"Allah ne jo muddat muqarrar ki hai use "Ajal" kahte hain aur "Ajal" ki do qismen hain:
(1) "Ajal e Ghair e Musamma" wo Khuda ki Marzi par mauqoof (depend) hai aur use aage peeche karta rahta hai.
(2) "Ajal e Musamma" (Fixed Time) ye wo Ajal hai jiska faisla Shabe Qadr mein kar diya jata hai aur woh ek saal mein nafizul amal (execution) hoti hai aur isi "Ajal" ke mutalliq Allah farmata hai:
_"Pas jab unki mi'aad (term) poori ho jaati hai to  na wo ek ghante peechhe ho sakte hain aur na hi aage ho sakte hain."_ (Aa'raaf: 34)
Ek sawal par Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya:
"Ajal e Musamma" se wo waqt murad hai jise Malakul Maut ke liye Shabe Qadr mein muqarrar kar diya hai."
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)
⏱
Sawal Kiya gaya: kiya Allah zaati taur par har jagah maujood hai?
Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya:
"Makanaat to Aqdaar (fixed place) hain aur jab tum ye kahte ho ke Woh Makaan mein bazaate khud maujood hai to isse laazim aata hai ke tum kah rahe ho ke Woh Aqdaar aur ghair Aqdaar mein maujood hai. Lekin Woh apni Makhlooq se juda hai. Usne jo kuchh paida kiya hai Woh uska Ilm o Qudrat o Saltanat o Hukoomat ke aitbar se ahata kiye hue hai (All Encompassing).
(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hamara Ajal e Musamma (Maut) ba khair ho.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo Sile Rahem karega 4 inaam Allah se paayega: Allah ki mohabbat, wus'at e Rizq, *Umr mein izafa,* Jannat mein daakhil hoga."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p117)
⌛
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Zina ke 6 bure natije hote hain, 3 duniya mein aur 3 Akherat mein: Duniya mein ye ke chehre ki khubsoorati khatm ho jaati hai, Faqr (gareebi) aur tangdasti gher leti hain aur *Umr kam ho jaati hai,* Akherat mein ye ke Khuda ke gazab ka nishana banta hai, Hisaab mein sakhti hoti hai aur hamesha ke azaab ka mustahaq hota hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p379)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ _*HAQ KA MAZAAQ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (792)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا تَأْتِيهِمْ مِنْ آيَةٍ مِنْ آيَاتِ رَبِّهِمْ إِلَّا كَانُوا عَنْهَا مُعْرِضِينَ * فَقَدْ كَذَّبُوا بِالْحَقِّ لَمَّا جَاءَهُمْ ۖ فَسَوْفَ يَأْتِيهِمْ أَنْبَاءُ مَا كَانُوا بِهِ يَسْتَهْزِئُونَ*

_"Unke paas unke Rab ki jo bhi Nishani aati hai woh usse munh mod lete hain. Unhone Haq ko jhutla diya jo unke paas aaya hai jiska woh Mazaaq uda rahe hain, anqareeb uski khabrein unhe pahuchengi."_
(Surah An'am: 4 - 5)
📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Yahan is baat ka zikr hai ke jabke Haq unke saamne tha  aur woh Haq ka mazaaq uda rahe the. Isliye Musalman itne firqon mein bat gaya anqareeb jab Akhari Haq ka zahoor hoga tab unhe pata chalega ke woh kaisa mazaaq udate the. Us Din ke intezaar mein ham sab hain.

Bare Ilaha Imam Mahdi (atfs) ke Zahoor jald jald farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍁
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Mujhe 3 logo'n par bada rahem aata hai aur waqe'an wo is qaabil hai ke unpar rahem kiya jaaye. Ek izzat wala shakhs jise izzat ke baad zillat naseeb ho aur ek daulat-mand shakhs jo daulat-mandi ke baad mohtaaj ho jaaye aur ek Aalim jiske ghar waale usko jaahil kehte ho...aur uski mazaaq uraate ho'n."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v4, p305)
☘
Imam Reza (as)
_"Jo shakhs zabaan se Tauba kar lekin Dil mein pashemaani aur sharmindagi na ho to goya usne Allah ka mazaaq udaya hai."_
(Tauba Aagosh e Rehmat)
🍀
Imam Ali (as)
_"Momin ka chiraag hamare Haq ki maarefat hai aur badtareen Andhaapan hamare fazl se Aa'nkhein band kar lena hai."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          ♦ _*AZAAB-E-ILAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (793)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَلَمْ يَرَوْا كَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ مِنْ قَرْنٍ مَكَّنَّاهُمْ فِي الْأَرْضِ مَا لَمْ نُمَكِّنْ لَكُمْ وَأَرْسَلْنَا السَّمَاءَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِدْرَارًا وَجَعَلْنَا الْأَنْهَارَ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهِمْ فَأَهْلَكْنَاهُمْ بِذُنُوبِهِمْ وَأَنْشَأْنَا مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ قَرْنًا آخَرِينَ*

_"Kiya unhone nahi dekha ke Hamne unse qabl kitni aisi qaumon ko halak kiya hai jinhen Hamne Zameen mein aisa Aqdaar diya tha ke is jaisa Aqdaar tumhe nahi diya. Hamne un par Aasmaan se khoob Baarish barsayen aur Hamne unke neeche Nehren baha di thi. Akhirkar Hamne unhein Gunahon ki padaash mein halaak kar diya aur unki jagah doosri qaumon ko le aye."_
(Surah An'am: 6)

📚📖 🌵
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Zajaj ka kahna hai ke Qarn *قرن* ka itlaq us muddat ke logon par hota hai jin mein koi Nabi ho ya Ahle Ilm ka koi tabqa ho aur is mein kam saal ya zyada saal ho isse koi farq nahi padta kiyonki Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:
*خيركم قرني ثم الذين يلونهم.*
_"Mera daur sab se behtar hai. Phir un logon ka daur behtar hai jo iske baad ayenge."_
(Tafseer Majmaul Bayan)
🐲
Allah ne Guroor o Takabbur karne wale, Sarkash, Zalim logon par etaab ki barish barsa kar halaak kar diya. Ye sabaq ainda qaumon ke liye hai ke sarkashi ka natija kiya hota hai.
Aaj kal bhi aap log dekhte honge ke kahin Selaab, to kahin Zalzala to kahin bijli ka girna wa bhari barsat hona jiske natije mein sekdon ya hazaron log halaak ho jaate hain. Allah Zalim nahi, Woh zulm nahi karta lekin Zalim ko kadi se kadi saza bhi deta hai. Ye sab hadsaat o waqeat doosron logon ke liye sabaq hote hain taake woh hoshiyar ho jayen.

Bare Ilaha hame un gunahon se Ma'af farma jo Tera Ghazab se qareeb karte hain aur hamari halakat ka sabab bante hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌵🐲
Ameerul Mo'meneen Imam Ali (as)
_"Tajjub hai aur mujhe kaise tajjub na ho un giroho'n ki khataao'n par jinhone apne Deen ki Hujjato'n mein ikhtelaaf paida kar rakhe hain. Jo na Nabi ke naqsh e qadam par chalte hain, na Wasi ke amal ki pairavi karte hain, na Gaib par Imaan laate hain, na aib se daaman bachaate hain. Maskook (doubtful) cheezo'n par amal karte hain aur apni khwaisho'n (ki duniya) mein chalte phirte hain. Unke nazdeek bus wohi cheez achchi hai jisko wo achcha samajhte hain aur wohi cheez buri hai jisko wo bura jaante hain. Mushkil gutthiyo'n ko suljhaane ke liye unhone apne Nafso'n par etemaad kar liya hai aur mushtaba (Doubtful) cheezo'n mein apni raai par bharosa kar liya hai, goya unme se har shakhs apna Imam hai aur usne apni jagah jo faisla apni raai se kar liya hai uske baare mein ye khayaal karta hai ke ise qaabil e itminaan zariyo'n se haasil kiya hai."_
(Gorar ul Hakam, Vol 2, p494, Nahjul Balagah, Khutba 88 (Jisme Logo'n Ki Halaakat Ke Asbaab Bayaan Kiye Gaye Hain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

 DUSHMANANE ISLAM KI HATDHARMI

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (794)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَوْ نَزَّلْنَا عَلَيْكَ كِتَابًا فِي قِرْطَاسٍ فَلَمَسُوهُ بِأَيْدِيهِمْ لَقَالَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا إِنْ هَٰذَا إِلَّا سِحْرٌ مُبِينٌ*

_"Aur agar Ham Aap (saww) par Kaagaz par likhi hui Kitab nazil karte aur log unhe haathon se chhoo lete to bhi Kufr karne wale yehi kahte ke ye khullam khulla Jadoo hai."_
(Surah An'am: 7)

📚📖 😏
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Har cheez jis par kuchh likha jaye use Qirtas *قرطاس* kahte hain. Aaj ke zamane paper par likha jata hai isliye aaj zamane ke mutabiq 'Paper' ko Qirtas kah sakte hain.

Guzishta Ayaton mein zikr hua tha ke jin logon ne Allah ki Nishaniyon ka, Uske Deen ka inkaar kiya, Haq ka inkaar kiya, ya Munafeqat ki Allah ne un par sakht Azaab de kar halaak kar deta hai aur unki jagah doosri ummaten le leti hain. Unhone bahut si sharte rakhin jaise ke agar Farishte unke saamne Kitab lekar nazil hon. Ye log sirf Mazaaq uda rahe the, inko Deen samajhna nahi tha, isliye halaak kar diya. Allah Ta'ala is Ayat mein farma raha hai ke agar likhi hui Kitab bhi unke saamne pesh kar di jaati tab bhi woh is Jaadu bata dete aur kisi madari ka khel ke taur par hansi udate. Jaise ke Yazeed ne Karbala ke waqae ke baad saaf taur par kah diya tha ke Mohammed (saww) ka Deen kuchh nahi tha balke Bani Hashim ka ek khel tha.

Bare Ilaha hame aise Jadoogaron ke shar se mehfooz rakh jo logon ko pareshan karte hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😎
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"3 log Jannat mein nahi jayenge: Sharaab peene waala, Rishtedaaro'n se tallukaat khatm kar dene waala aur jaadu ko maanne waala."_
(Tanzeemul Makatib)
🤓
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jo koi najumi / jyotishi (astrologer) ki peyshangoi (bhavishyavaani / prediction) par yaqeen karta hai to usne Quran ka inkaar kiya."_
(Greater Sins II, Sorcery - 31st Greater Sin)
🙃
Imam Ali (as):
_"…Agar koi shakhs bad-shaguni ka shikaar ho to uski parwaah kiye baghair Allah ka naam lekar apne kaam se kaam rakhna chahiye…"_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p609)

♦ _*FARISHTA NABI KIYON NAHI?*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (795)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالُوا لَوْلَا أُنْزِلَ عَلَيْهِ مَلَكٌ ۖ وَلَوْ أَنْزَلْنَا مَلَكًا لَقُضِيَ الْأَمْرُ ثُمَّ لَا يُنْظَرُونَ * وَلَوْ جَعَلْنَاهُ مَلَكًا لَجَعَلْنَاهُ رَجُلًا وَلَلَبَسْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ مَا يَلْبِسُونَ*

_"Aur Kafiron ne kaha ke un par (Nabi e Akram saww) Farishta kiyon nahi utara gaya? Aur agar Hamne Farishta utara hota to ab tak faisla bhi ho chuka hota. Phir unhe koi mohlat hi na di jaati. Agar Ham Farishte ko bhi utarte to use insaani roop de kar hi ravana karte aur unko usi shak mein hi mubtila karte jis mein woh ab mubtila hain."_
(Surah An'am: 8 - 9)

📚📖 🤔
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein us Sawal ka jawab diya gaya hai jo Kuffar aur Sardar e Quraish ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) se kiya tha. Sawal ye hai ke Allah ne ek Farishte ko Nabi bana kar kiyon nahi bheja?
🍃
Imam Hasan Askari (as) iske jawab mein farmate hain jo ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya hai:
"Farishte tumhare hawaas (sense) mehsoos nahi kar sakte, kiyonki woh to hawa jaisi Lateef Makhlooq hai aur agar bil farz tumhari quwwat e deed (Vision Power) mein izaafa kar diya jata aur tum Farishte ko dekhne lag jaate to tum use Farishta hi tasleem na karte kiyonki aane wala Farishta Insaani shakl mein hota aur tum uski zahiri shakl dekh kar yahi kahte ke ye to insaan hai. Isi liye Allah ki Hikmat ka taqaza ye hua ke Woh kisi Farishte ko bhejne ke bajai kisi insaan ko hi Nabi o Rasool bana kar ravana kare aur uske haath par aise Mo'jezaat zahir kare jo aam insaanon ki dastars se bahar hon, kiyonki agar Parinda parvaz (fly) kare to us mein hairat ja koi pahlu nahi hota. Aur agar insaan kisi Parinde ki tarah parvaz kare to ye Mo'jeza shumar kiya jayega. Allah ne to mamle ko tumhare liye asaan banaya hai lekin khwah makhah ki sakhtiyon ko apne liye tajweez kar rahe ho."
(Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hamare Imaan ko shako shubhhaat se door rakh.
*يَا اَللهُ يَا رَحْمٰنُ يَا رَحِيْمُ يَا مُقَلِّبَ الْقُلُوْبِ ثَبِّتْ قَلْبِىْ عَلٰى دِيْنِكَ۔*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as)
se sawaal huwa ke kya Farishto'n ki tadaad zyada hai ya Bani Adam ki? Aap ne farmaya:
_"…Aasmaan mein rehne wale Farishto'n ki tadaad rooy e zameen ke zarraat (sand particles) se bhi zyada hai. Aasmaan ke har goshe mein koi na koi Farishta maujood hai jo Khuda ki tasbeeh o taqdees kar raha hai. Zameen ke har darakht par koi na koi Farishta hai…Jitne bhi Farishte hain wo sab ke sab Ahle Bait (as) ki Wilayat ke zariye se Allah ki nazdeeki haasil karte hain aur hamare mohibbo'n ke liye maghferat talab karte hain aur hamare dushmano'n par la'nat karte hain aur Khuda se darkhwaast karte hain ke Aal e Muhammad (as) ke dushmano'n par azaab naazil kare."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p394)
🌾
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Insaan ke 2 kaandho'n par 2 Farishte muqarrar hain. Daayein jaanib (right side) wala Farishta baayein jaanib (left side) waale par haakim aur ameer hai. Jab insaan koi bura amal anjaam deta hai to daayein jaanib wala baayein jaanib wale se kehta hai, "Likhne mein jaldi mat kar, usko 7 ghanto'n (7 hours) ki mohlat de'. Jab 7 ghanto'n ki mohlat khatm ho jaaye aur wo shakhs Tauba na kare to phir wo daayein jaanib wala kehta hai, "Likho, ye shakhs kitna be-hayaa aur be-sharm hai"."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v2, p154)
🎋
Rasule Khuda (saww):
(HUM-SHAKL E ALI (as)) _"Shab e Me'raj main ne Arsh ke darmiyaan ek Farishte ko dekha jiske haath mein ek Noor ki talwaar thi aur wo us talwaar se yun khel raha tha jaise ke Ali ibne Abi Taalib (as) Zulfiqar ke saath khelte hain. Aur jab Farishton ko Ali ibne Abi Taalib (as) ki ziyarat ka shauq hota hai to wo us Farishte ke chehre ko dekhte hain. Main ne arz ki, "Parwardigaar, kya ye mera bhai Ali ibi Taalib hai?" Allah Ta'ala ne kaha, "Muhammad (saww)! Ye ek Farishta hai jise Maine Ali ibne Abi Taalib (as) ki surat par paida kiya hai. Ye Mere Arsh ke darmiyaan Meri Ibadat karta hai aur iski nekiyaan aur tasbeeh aur taqdees Qayamat ke din talak Ali ibne Abi Taalib (as) ke naama e Aamaal mein likkhi jaati rahengi."_
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p277)

     ♦ _*TAREEKH (HISTORY)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (796)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَقَدِ اسْتُهْزِئَ بِرُسُلٍ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ فَحَاقَ بِالَّذِينَ سَخِرُوا مِنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا بِهِ يَسْتَهْزِئُونَ * قُلْ سِيرُوا فِي الْأَرْضِ ثُمَّ انْظُرُوا كَيْفَ كَانَ عَاقِبَةُ الْمُكَذِّبِينَ*

_"Aye Rasool (saww)! Aap ke pahle bhi Rasoolon ka mazaaq udaya ja chuka hai magar un mazaaq udane walon par akhirkar wohi haqeeqat musallat ho kar rahi jiska woh Mazaaq udate the. Aap kah den Zameen mein chal phir kar dekho aur takzeeb karne walon ka kiya anjaam hua hai."_
(Surah An'am: 10 - 11)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Taarikh/History ki Kitaben hame pichhli qaumon ki harkaat, unko tariqqiyan ya zawal, ghaltiyon ke manazir pesh karti hai. Jab ek insaan Taarikh ke auraaq (pages) ko palatta hai to goya woh un guzishta qaumon ke darmiyan se guzar raha hota hai. Woh apni Virtual Aankhon se un sab ko dekhta aur unse sabaq hasil karta hai jiske sabab woh taraqqi mein ek qadam aage badhata hai. Qur'an ne bhi mukhtalif waqeat pesh kiye taake Musalman kuchh ibrat hasil karen. Is Ayat mein isi baat ki taraf ishaara kiya gaya hai. Deen ka mazaaq udana ye sirf aaj ki baat nahi guzishta qaumon ne bhi mazaaq udaya hai. H. Nooh (as) ko Kishti banate dekh log unka mazaaq udate the lekin hamne dekha ke Qaum e Nooh (as) ka kiya hashr hua. Ye Ayat Qur'an mein kai jagah repeat hui hai aur Allah ne yehi takeed ki hai ke Duniya chalo phiro aur dekho kiya kiya ho raha hai. Yahan sirf sun lene ki baat nahi balki khud apni Aankh se dekhne ki baat hai yani yaqeen ke saath dekho taake iska ham par asar ho. Jo haqeeqi Tarikhdan the unhone poori Duniya mein ghoome aur wahan ki manazir pesh kiye. Taarikh sirf information ya GK Jaankari ke liye nahi hoti. Na ye Entertainment ka zariya hoti hai jab ise filmaya jaata hai. Taarikh ka asl maqsad ibrat hasil hota hai. Qur'an mein Hazrat Yusuf (as) ka poori poori Life history pesh ki hai aur Allah ne isko Ahsanul Qasas qarar diya hai. (Best Story). Taarikh ham par ek khas chhap chhodti hai jis achhe ya bure asaraat ho sakte hain. Achchhe asaraat Neki ki raah mein madadgar sabit hote hain. Ye Taarikh ka hi natija hai ham Rasool o Aimma ki unke Wiladat o Shahadat ke mauqe par unki sawane Umri padh kar unka zikr kiya jaata hai. Agar log Taarikh nahi padhte to woh in Waqe'at ko bhool jaate. Isliye Taarikhon ka zikr qaum ko zinda rakhta hai warna jo ye kahte hain Taarikh mat padho sirf amal karo, woh murda qaum hai. Agar ek haqeeqi Hadi ko bhool gayi hai to kal unko bhi bhula degi jinke nashe qadam par aaj chal rahi hai. Isliye zaroori hai ke Taarikh par nigah rakhen aur research ke dayre ko wasee karen, is tarah har waqt apni Aankhen khuli rakhen.

Bare Ilaha hame Taufeeq ata farma ke ham Duniya se apni Taarikh mein achhi chhap chhod kar jaye aur mustaqbil mein log ibrat hasil karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😂
Imam Hasan (as)
_"Mazaaq haibat (awe / roab) ko khatm kar deta hai aur khamosh insaan ki haibat zyada hoti hai."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p85)
🤣
Imam Ali (as)
_"Har cheez ka Beej hota hai aur Dushmani ka beej mazaaq hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, Vol 6)

♦ _*SAB KA MAALIK ALLAH HAI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (797)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ لِمَنْ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ ۖ قُلْ لِلَّهِ ۚ كَتَبَ عَلَىٰ نَفْسِهِ الرَّحْمَةَ ۚ لَيَجْمَعَنَّكُمْ إِلَىٰ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ لَا رَيْبَ فِيهِ ۚ الَّذِينَ خَسِرُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ فَهُمْ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ*
_"Aap kah den ke bhala batao Aasmaano aur Zameen mein jo kuchh hai wo kis ka hai? Kah den ke *sab kuchh Allah hi ka hai.* Usne apne Zaat par Rehmat ko lazim kar liya hai. Woh Qayamat ke Din tum sab ko zaroor jama karega. Is mein koi shak nahi hai. Woh log jinhone apne khasare ka saz o samaan kiya hai woh Us par Imaan nahi rakhte."_
(Surah An'am: 12)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Insaan kitna hi haath paon mare, jatan kare, gunah kare ya Nek Amaal kare sab ko Allah ki taraf palatna hai. Isliye jab koi marta hai to kahte hain:
*إِنَّا لِلَّهِ وَإِنَّا إِلَيْهِ رَاجِعُونَ*
_"Ham Allah hi ke hain aur Allah hi ki taraf hame palat kar jana hai."_ (2:156)
🍃
Qayamat ke Din Allah sab ko Maidan e Mahshar mein jama karega. Us Din kisi ki nahi chalegi siwai Allah ke ya jisko Allah ijazat de. Yahan is baat ki khas tawajjo dilaye hai ke Allah ne apne upar Rehmat karna wajib kar diya hai lekin jo Azaab Woh bandon ko deta hai wo Insaan ki khud Aamaal ki wajah se hai.
🌾
Hazrat Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Allah ne apni Zaat par Rehmat ko lazim kiya hai', Uski Rehmat Uske Ghazab par sabqat (preferred) rakhti hai. Woh Sidq o Adl ki takmeel ka baes hai. Allah apne bandon par apni taraf se Ghazab ki ibteda (start) nahi karta. Bande Ghazab e Ilahi ke asbaab (Causes) khud faraham karte hain aur yahi Yaqeeni Ilm hai aur Taqwa ka Ilm hai."_
(Rauza e Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hama par Qayamat ke Din Apni Rehmat se pesh aana na ke Apni Adalat se.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🔥
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Momin ke saaye ke alaawa Qayamat ki zameen Aag hai. Beshak uska Sadqa  hi uska saayebaa'n (shade) hoga."_
(Sawaabul Aamaal o Iqaabul Aaamal)
🌍
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Allah ke 12000 Aalam hai jinme se har ek saato'n Aasman aur Zameen se bada hai aur inme se har ek ke rehnewale dusre aalam ke rehnewaalo'n se anjaan hai."_
(Sharh Dua e Kumail)

🎹🎼🎻🎸🎺🎷🥁
Imam Reza (as):
_*"Jis shakhs ke ghar mein dhhol, baa'nsuri ya geet-sangeet ki koi bhi cheez ya shatranj 40 deen tak rahe to wo shakhs Allah ke Gazab (gusse) ko daawat deta hai."*_
(Greater Sins, II)

 ♦ _*SAB KA MAALIK ALLAH HAI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (798)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَهُ مَا سَكَنَ فِي اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ ۚ وَهُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ*

_"Aur Raat ke andhere aur Din ke ujale mein jo bhi sukoonat pazeer (rahte) hai wo Allah ka hi hai aur Woh Sunnewala, Jannewala hai."_
(Surah An'am: 13)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke guzishta Ayat mein bayan kiya gaya ke sab kuchh Allah ka hai. Yahan is Ayat mein bhi yahi zikr hai. Aisa nahi hai ke Ujale Khuda ke bas mein ho jabke Andhera Shaitan ke bas mein. Raat Din ja Malik bhi Allah hai. Jahan Suraj hai wahan sirf Din rahta hai lekin is Aalam (Universe) mein jahan Suraj ki roshni nahi pahunchti wahan sirf Andhera hi Andhera hai. Dono jagahon ka Malik Allah hai. Un jagahon par jo bhi rahte hain unka bhi Malik Allah hai.

Bare Ilaha hamare upar Tera Saya qayam rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🏡
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jab tak bande ki rihaaish-gaah (ghar) gair-maaruf (unknown / agyaat) rehti hai, banda achcha rehta hai. Jab rihaaish-gaah mash'hoor ho jaaye to fitno'n mein ghir jaata hai aur phir wohi shakhs saabit qadam reh sakta hai jise Allah saabit qadam rakhe."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p322)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                   ♦ _*ALLAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (799)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ أَغَيْرَ اللَّهِ أَتَّخِذُ وَلِيًّا فَاطِرِ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَهُوَ يُطْعِمُ وَلَا يُطْعَمُ ۗ قُلْ إِنِّي أُمِرْتُ أَنْ أَكُونَ أَوَّلَ مَنْ أَسْلَمَ ۖ وَلَا تَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ*

_"Aap kah den ke kiya Khuda ko chhod kar mein kisi aur ko apna sarparast bana lo jo ke Zameen o Aasman ka Khaaliq hai. Woh Ta'am (Food) khilata hai jabke Use Ta'am nahi khilaya jata? Aap kah den ke mujhe to yahi hukm diya gaya hai ke mein sab se pahle Uske saamne gardan jhukaon aur mujhe ye hukm mila hai ke tum Mushrekin mein hargiz shamil na hona."_
(Surah An'am: 14)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaaton aur is Ayaat mein Wahdaniyat e Khuda ka zikr ho raha hai.
Is Ayat ka Shaane Nuzool ye hai ke Quraish ki jab har taraf se shikast (defeat) ho rahe thi to unhone Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ko apni taraf khechna chaha aur unke zariye paigham pahunchaya ke woh jo chahe woh dene ko tayyar hain Maal o Daulat, Zan o Badshahat lekin woh unke Buton ko bura kahna chhod den. Janabe Abu Talib (as) jinhone har waqt Nabi e Khuda (saww) ki muhafizat ki Rasool e Khuda (saww) ka jawab unko sunaya ke agar woh ek haath mein Suraj aur ek haat mein chand bhi laa kar rakh den to woh Tauheed e Khuda ka Paigham nahi chhodenge.
(Majmaul Bayan, Tarikh e Tabari)
Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ne na ke apne bhatije ki hifazat ki balke Tauheed ki hifazat ki. Balke yun kaha jaye ke unhone Tauheed ko pala hai.
Allah ne is Ayat mein unko jawab diya ke woh kiya Allah ko khilayenge jabke Allah sab ko khilata hai. Buton ko chhod kar Ek Allah ke saamne tasleem ho jao.
Musalmano mein ye Imaan e Tauheed ki kamzori hai ke Allah aur uske Sachche Rahbaron ko chhod kar idhar udhar ghairon ke darwazon par apna sar jhukate hain. Ye bhool jaate hain ke Rozi ka dene wala Allah hai. Phir bhi ek Roti ki khatir Musalman bik jaata hai. Bhale woh zaban se Kalma e Tauheed padhe lekin uske andar bahut sare Buton ki Muhabbat hoti hai jaise Daulat, Jaa o Hasham, Nafsani Khwaheshat, Fuhosh, Jhoot o Makkari se lagao waghaira jiske aage woh apna sar jhuka deta hai. Woh Allah aur uske Rasool ki baton ko follow nahi karta balke apni Dil ki baat ko follow karta hai. Allah ke Imaan ke saath in sab cheezon ka mix ho jaana usko Shirk ki taraf le jaata hai.

Imam Sajjad (as)
_"Pus, Hamd Tere liye hai ke Tu ne mere dil ko shirk se paak kiya."_
_"Aye Parwardigaar! Teri Hamd ke muqaabil meri zabaan ki kya haisiyat hai aur ne'mato'n aur ehsaano'n ke saamne mere amal ka kya wazn hai? Mere Maabud! Teri sakhawat ne meri aarzu ko badhaaya aur Teri qadr-daani ne mere amal ko qubool farmaya hai."_
(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumaali)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Main apni Ummat ke liye na to Momin se darta hun aur na Mushrik se darta hun, kyun ki Momin ka Imaan usko gumraahi se bachaa lega aur Mushrik ko uska shirk tabaah kar dega. Albatta main apni ummat ke silsile mein us Munafiq se darta hun jiski zabaan Ilm ka mazhar nazar aaye, jo baat to Neki ki karta hai aur amal burai ke karta hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p87)

  ♦ _*REHMAT-E-KHUDA WANDI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (800)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ إِنِّي أَخَافُ إِنْ عَصَيْتُ رَبِّي عَذَابَ يَوْمٍ عَظِيمٍ * مَنْ يُصْرَفْ عَنْهُ يَوْمَئِذٍ فَقَدْ رَحِمَهُ ۚ وَذَٰلِكَ الْفَوْزُ الْمُبِينُ*

_"Aap (saww) kah den ke agar meine apne Rab ki nafarmani ki to mujhe Bade Din (Roze Qayamat) ke Azaab ka dar hai. Us Din jo Azaab se bach gaya to us par Khuda ne bada hi Rahem kiya aur yehi wazeh kamyabi hai."_
(Surah An'am: 15 - 16)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Majmaul Bayan mein hai ke Rehmat e Ilahi jab tak kisi ke shamil e haal na ho us waqt tak Azaab se bachna na-mumkin hai.
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Us Zaat ki Qasam jiske qabza e ikhtiyar mein meri jaan hai koi bhi shakhs apne Aamaal ki wajah se Jannat mein nahi hoga."_
Logon ne kaha: _'Ya Rasoolallah! Kiya Aap bhi?'_
Aap (saww):
_"Mein bhi Aamaal ki wajah se Jannat mein dakhil nahi hunga, siwai iske ke Allah mujh par apni Rehmat o Fazl ka saya kare."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

_"Aye mere Ma'abud aur mere Sardar aur mere Maula aur mere Parwardigar! Maan le ke main Tere Azaab par Sabr karunga, magar Teri Rehmat se judaai par kyun kar Sabr karunga? Aur maan le ke main Teri Aag ki hararat sah lunga, magar Teri nazar e karamat ke badal jaane ko kyun kar bardasht karunga? Ya Aatish e Jahannum mein kyun kar qaraar paaunga, jabke Teri Ma'afi ki ummeed lagi hui hai?"_
(Imam Ali (as): Dua e Kumail)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Jab banda koi gunah karta hai to chaahe wo Aalim ho, magar jis waqt apne Nafs ko apne Parwardigar ki nafarmani mein daalta hai, to us waqt wo jaahil ho jata hai."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p85)

        ♦ _*ALLAH: QAAHIR HAI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (801)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنْ يَمْسَسْكَ اللَّهُ بِضُرٍّ فَلَا كَاشِفَ لَهُ إِلَّا هُوَ ۖ وَإِنْ يَمْسَسْكَ بِخَيْرٍ فَهُوَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ * وَهُوَ الْقَاهِرُ فَوْقَ عِبَادِهِ ۚ وَهُوَ الْحَكِيمُ الْخَبِيرُ*

_"Agar Allah tumhe kisi qasam ka nuqsan pahunchaye to Uske siwa koi nahi jo tumhe is nuqsan se bacha sake aur agar Woh tumhe kisi bhalai se bahramand kare to, Woh har cheez par Qadir hai."_
_"Woh apne bandon par Kaamil Ikhtiyarat rakhta hai aur Woh Hikmat o Khabar wala hai."_
(Surah An'am: 17 - 18)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Reza (as):
 "Khuda Qaahir hai yani Khuda bandon par mukammal Ikhtiyarat rakhta hai aur baaz bande baaz bandon par bhi Ikhtiyarat rakhte hain, lekin Khuda aur bandon ke Ikhtiyarat ke Zaraye aur unke anjam mein farq hai. Bande jab bandon par Ikhtiyar hasil karte hain to woh badi mehnat o mashaqqat ya makr o madarat se ikhtiyar hasil karte hain aur unke ikhtiyar hamesha ke liye bhi nahi hote, chand roza ikhtiyar hasil karte hain aur phir zerdast zabardast aur zabardast zerdast ban jate hain. Jabke Khuda ko apne Ikhtiyar ke liye un zaraye ki koi zaroorat nahi. Khuda ki har Makhlooq Fitri taur par Khuda ke saamne aakiz o laachar hai aur Khuda ke iraade ke saamne kisi Ko chashme zadan ke liye bhi dam marne ki majaal nahi hai aur Woh "Kun Fayakoon *كن فيكون*" ka Maalik hai. Bando par bhi ism (noun) "Qaahir *قاهر*" ka itlaaq hota hai aur Khuda par bhi ism "Qaahir *قاهر*" ka itlaaq hota hai lekin dono ke mafhoom mein wazeh farq hai."
(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Tere Qaher se mehfooz rakhna.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Riwayat:
Imam Ali Naqi (as) ke mojizaat mein manqool hai ke ek zargar (goldsmith / sonaar) Imam (as) ka padosi tha. Khalifa e Abbasi ke Wazir ne use bula ke ek qeemati Nagina (gemstone) uske supurd kiya ke uspe ek naqsh kunda kar ke use Angoothi mein jad de. Zargar use le gaya lekin chot padne par wo qeemati Nagina beech se 2 tukde ho gaya. Is tarah toot jaane se uske gair-maamuli (extraordinary) qeemat ghat gayi. Zargar bahut hi pareshaan huwa aur Imam (as) ki khidmat mein haazir ho kar waqiya arz kiya. Imam (as) ne farmaya, _"Khuda Qaadir hai. Tum mutmaeen raho aur maayus na ho (koi mushkil aisi nahi ke jo Qudrat e Khuda ke saamne aasaan na ho)."_
Aap ne jo usay nasihat farmayi uske baad hi uske paas Wazir ne ek khaas aadmi ke zariye paigham bheja ke, _"Zargar sahab! Meri 2 biwiyaa'n hai. Main ye Nagina ek ke liye banwana chahta tha lekin dusri biwi ne mujhe zehmat mein daal diya hai kyun ki wo bhi isi tarah ka Nagina chahti hai aur doosra mere paas maujood nahi hai. Kya ye ho sakta hai ke iske 2 hisse kar ke dono ke liye ek ek Angoothi banwa do? Main uske liye tumhe kaafi inaam bhi dunga"._ Zargar ne kaha, _"Usko barabar ke 2 hisso'n mein taqseem karna mushkil hai. Ho sakta hai Vazeer ke iqbaal se aisa kaam ho jaaye"._
Is tarah usne ek badi raqam bhi wasool ki aur Imam (as) ki khidmat mein haazir ho kar Shukriya bhi pesh kiya. Insaan ko chahiye ke apni ummeed sirf Khuda ki zaat se waabasta rakhe.
(Sachche Waqeaat - Ayatullah Dastgaib Shirazi, p207)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦☝🏻 _*TAWHEED☝🏻*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (802)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ أَيُّ شَيْءٍ أَكْبَرُ شَهَادَةً ۖ قُلِ اللَّهُ ۖ شَهِيدٌ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَكُمْ ۚ وَأُوحِيَ إِلَيَّ هَٰذَا الْقُرْآنُ لِأُنْذِرَكُمْ بِهِ وَمَنْ بَلَغَ ۚ أَئِنَّكُمْ لَتَشْهَدُونَ أَنَّ مَعَ اللَّهِ آلِهَةً أُخْرَىٰ ۚ قُلْ لَا أَشْهَدُ ۚ قُلْ إِنَّمَا هُوَ إِلَٰهٌ وَاحِدٌ وَإِنَّنِي بَرِيءٌ مِمَّا تُشْرِكُونَ*

_"Aap (saww) kah den ke sab se badh kar kis kis Gawahi hai? Aap (saww) kah den ke mere aur tumhare darmiyan Allah Gawah hai. Aur meri taraf us Qur'an ki Waḥy ki gayi hai taake tumhe aur jis jis tak Uska Paigham pahunche sab ko mutanabbe (warning) kar dun. Kiya tum ye gawahi dete ho ke Allah ke saath aur Ma'bood bhi hain? Aap (saww) kah den ke mein uski Gawahi nahi deta. Aap (saww) kah den ke bas Woh Ma'bood Wahid hai aur jo kuchh tum Shirk kar rahe ho, mein usse bezaar hun."_
(Surah An'am: 19)

📚📖 ☝🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Tawheed ki silsilewar Ayaat jaari hain:

Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
Is Ayat ke zel mein:
_"Ailaane Nubuwwat ke ibtedai dino mein Mushrekin e Makkah ne Aanhazrat (saww) se kaha: "Muhammad! Kiya Khuda ko Risalat ke liye tumhare alawa aur koi banda nahi mila tha? Duniya ka koi bhi shakhs tumhari Risaalat ki tasdeeq nahi karta. Had ye hai ke hamne Yahood o Nasaara se tumhare mutalliq poochha to unhone bhi yehi kaha ke Nubuwwat o Risaalat ja hamari Kitabon mein kahin zikr nahin hai, lehaza agar Aap Nabi hain to apni Risaalat ka koi gawah pesh karen."
Uske jawab mein Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya: _"Mere aur tumhare darmiyan bas Allah gawah hai."_ (Ye Ayat phir nazil hui.)
☝🏻
Mohd bin Esa bin Ubaid ka bayan hai ke Imam Musa Kazim (as) ne mujhse poochha:
_"Agar tumse poochha jaye ke Allah "Shay *شئ*" hai ya "La Shay *لا شئ*" hai to tum kiya jawab doge?"_(Thing or Nothing)
Raavi:
"Allah ne Qur'an Majeed mein (6:19) lafz "Shay =Thing, Cheez" ka ka itlaaq kiya hai: _"Sabse badh kar kis Shay ki Gawahi hai?"_ mein ye kahunga ke Allah "Shay" hai lekin Woh aur Ashya *اشياء* ke jaisa nahi hai kiyonki "Mashiyat *مشىيت*" ke inkaar se Khuda ka ibtaal ابطال aur nafi (negation) lazim aati hai."
Meri ye guftagu sunkar Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Tumne sach aur durust kaha."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
☝🏻
Ameerul Mo'meneen Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Pyare Farzand! Agar tere Rab ka koi Sharik hota to Uske Rasool bhi tere paas aate aur Uski Mamlakat o Sultanat ke aasaar bhi tumhe dikhaye dete aur Uske Afa'al (Action) o Sifaat (Attributes) ko bhi pahchante, lekin haqeeqat ye hai ke Woh Tanha Ma'bood (Alone Deity) hai aur Woh Zaat o Sifaat (Essence & Attributes) mein waisa hi hai jaisa ke Usne Khud apna Ausaf (Attributes) kiya hai. Uski Hukoomat mein Uske madde muqabil (similar) nahi hai aur Woh Hamesha Baqi rahega."_
(Nahjul Balagha)

Bare Ilaha hame Muwahhid bane rahne par sabit qadam rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ☝🏻
Ayat mein " *و من بلغ*" (jis jis tak ye Paigham pahunche....) se murad kiya hai? Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) ne farmaya:
_*"Is se murad Ale Muhammad (as) hain.* Imam bhi Qur'an ke zariye se logon ko isi tarah mutanabbe (warning) karega jaise Rasoole Akram (saww) ne mutanabbe kiya tha."_
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

♦ _*GUZISHTA KITABON MEIN NABI (saww) AAMAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (803)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الَّذِينَ آتَيْنَاهُمُ الْكِتَابَ يَعْرِفُونَهُ كَمَا يَعْرِفُونَ أَبْنَاءَهُمُ ۘ الَّذِينَ خَسِرُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ فَهُمْ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ*

_"Jin logon ko Hamne Kitab di hai woh use itni achhi tarah se jaante hain jaisa ke woh apne beton ko jaante hain. Woh log jinhone apne khasare ka saaz o samaan kiya hai woh Imaan nahi layenge."_
(Surah An'am: 20)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat ke zel mein Rivayat pesh ki thi jis mein Quraish ne ilzaam lagaya tha ke inka to kahin bhi zikr nahi hai. Uske jawab mein ye Ayat nazil hui.
📚
Imam Sadiq (as):
"Ye Ayat Yahood o Nasaara ke mutalliq nazil hui aur *"يعرفونه*" mein zameer (pronoun) ka ishaara Hazrat Khatmi Martabat (saww) ki taraf hai. Yani Ahle Kitab Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko itni achhi tarah se jaante pahchante the jaisa ke woh apne beton ko jaante pahchante the. Aur iski wajah ye thi ke Allah Ta'ala ne Taurat, Zuboor aur Injeel mein apne Habib aur unke Sahaba ke ausaf bayan kiye the aur Allah ne Kutub e sabeqa (Earlier Books) mein Aanhazrat (saww) ki jaye Wiladat (Birthplace) aur unki jaye Hijrat aur unki Be'sat ka tazkara kar diya tha. Jaisa ke is Ayat (Al Fath: 29) mein. Chunanche Rasoole Khuda (saww) aur unke Ashaab ba safa ki Sifaat Taurat o Injeel mein bhi maujood thi jise Ahle Kitab achhi tarah jaante pahchante the, jab Allah ne Aapko mab'oos kiya to unhone Aap (saww) ke Ausaaf ki wajah se Aapko pahchan liya the lekin jaanne ke bawajood Aapka inkaar kiya."
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame apne Nabi (saww) ke naqshe qadam par chalne ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚 _*Taqleed:*_
Imam Sadiq (as)
se sawaal kiya gaya, _"Awaam e Yahood o Nasaara (Jewish people and Christian people) jo khud Kitaab ka Ilm na rakhte the aur unka Deen apne Ulama se suni sunayi cheezon ke taabe' (dependent / nirbhar) tha. Aur Khuda ne un awaam (janta) ki is liye mazammat (condemn / ninda) ki hai ke wo apne Ulama ki taqleed mein the. Pus, jab unke Ulama ki taqleed haraam thi to hamari awaam ke liye Ulama ki taqleed kaise jaez hai?"_
Imam (as) ne farmaya: _"Hamare awaam aur Ulama aur Yahood ke awaam aur Ulama mein farq bhi hai aur ek lihaz se masawaat (samaanta) bhi hai. Awaam e Yahood ko maaloom tha ke unke Ulama jhoot bolte hain, haraam khaate hain, rishwat lete hain aur sifarisho'n aur rishtedariyon aur rawa-daariyo'n ki bena par Ahkam e Khuda ko tabdeel kar dete hain; jin logon par naraaz ho, unko huqooq se mehroom kar dete hain aur jin par raazi hon unko na-haq amwaal (maal) dilwate hain, wagairah. Lihaza, Khuda Wande Kareem ne unki is andha-dhund taqleed ki mazammat farmayi hai. Isi tarah hamare awaam bhi agar apne Ulama ko faasiq, kunba-parwar (nepotism / pariwaar-waad), maal e duniya ke talabgaar aur haraam-khor paayein ke jis par raazi ho usko na-haq maal dilwaye aur jis par naraaz ho usko apne jaez huqooq se bhi mehroom kar de, garz ye ke bad-diyaanat (dishonest / be-imaan) hon, to aise Ulama ki taqleed karne mein hamare awaan aur Yahood ke awaam mein koi farq nahi hai. Lekin, Fuqaha mein jo shakhs apne nafs ko Haraam se bachaane wala, Deen ka Nigehban, khwaish ka Mukhalif aur apne Maula ke farman ki ita'at karne wala ho, pus, awaam ke liye uski taqleed karna jaez hai..."
(Tafseer e Anwaar e Najaf, v2, p128)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                   ♦ _*SHIRK*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (804)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَنْ أَظْلَمُ مِمَّنِ افْتَرَىٰ عَلَى اللَّهِ كَذِبًا أَوْ كَذَّبَ بِآيَاتِهِ ۗ إِنَّهُ لَا يُفْلِحُ الظَّالِمُونَ*

_"Aur isse badh kar bhala koi Zalim kaun hoga jo Allah par jhoota Bohtan lagaye ya Allah ki nishaniyon ki takzeeb kare. Yaqeenan Zalim Nijaat nahi payenge."_
(Surah An'am 21)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Allah Mushrekin ke bare mein kinayatan sawal kar raha ke issa bada Zalim kaun ho sakta hai? *"ومن اظلم*" Qur'an mein 15 jaghon par mukhtalif maana mein aya hai. Shirk Zulm e Azeem hai jaisa ke H. Luqman ne Quran mein apne bete ko nasihat karte waqt farmaya. Zulm sangeen is liye hai kiyonki Zulm 3 par ho raha hai.
(1) Allah par Jhoota Bohtan sab se bada zulm.
(2) Apne aap par Zulm, kiyonki Parwardigar Buzurg o Bartar ke muqabile mein Patthar ya mitti ke buton ke samne apne aap ko gira kar pasti ki jaanib le jaata hai.
(3) Ma'ashere (Society) par zulm karta hai kiyonki uski bure asaraat Society par padte hain to society puraganda ho jaati hai.
Allah ko jhutla kar woh ek Azeem Gunah Karta hai. Gunah ka murtakib hona apne aap par zulm karna hai. Iske liye zaroori hai ke Jihad e Nafs kare.
Insaan ki Fitrat gawara nahi karti ke woh apne Khaaliq ko na pahchaane. Apne Paalnewale ko woh kaise bhula sakta hai ya tohmat laga sakta hai.
🍁
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Zulm 3 tarah ke hain: Ek zulm aisa hai jise Allah Ta'ala baksh dega, aur ek zulm aisa hai jise Allah hargiz na bakhshega, aur ek zulm aisa hai jis se chashm-poshi (nazar-andaaz) nahi karega. *Pus, wo zulm jise Allah hargiz na bakhshega wo Shirk hai.* Wo zulm jise Allah baksh dega wo aisa hai jise bande ne khud apne hi upar kiya hoga. Aur wo zulm jis se Wo chashm-poshi na farmayega wo Haqqul Ibaad (bando'n ke haq) ke mutalliq hai."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p109)

Bare Ilaha hame aisi raah se door rakhna jo Shirk ki tarah le jaati ho.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as):
_"Zulm karte waqt apne baare mein Khuda ke Adl ko yaad rakho aur taaqat o qudrat ke waqt ye yaad rakho ke tum Khuda ki Qudrat se baahar nahi ho."_
(Gorar ul Hakam, v2, p33)
🍁
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Mujhe 3 afraad ke alaawa Ummat ke tamaam afraad ki najaat ki ummeed hai jo hamare haq ki maarefat rakhte hun._
_(1) Zaalim Badshah,_
_(2) Khwaishaat ka ghulam,_
_(3) Jo khule aam bad-kaariyaa'n karta hai."_
(Khisaal, p76)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (805)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَيَوْمَ نَحْشُرُهُمْ جَمِيعًا ثُمَّ نَقُولُ لِلَّذِينَ أَشْرَكُوا أَيْنَ شُرَكَاؤُكُمُ الَّذِينَ كُنْتُمْ تَزْعُمُونَ * ثُمَّ لَمْ تَكُنْ فِتْنَتُهُمْ إِلَّا أَنْ قَالُوا وَاللَّهِ رَبِّنَا مَا كُنَّا مُشْرِكِينَ * انْظُرْ كَيْفَ كَذَبُوا عَلَىٰ أَنْفُسِهِمْ ۚ وَضَلَّ عَنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يَفْتَرُونَ.*

_"Jis Din Ham un sab ko jama karenge. Phir Ham Shirk karne walon se kahenge tumhare woh Sharik kahan hain jinki shirakat ka tum guman kiya karte the?_
_Woh iske alawa aur koi Fitna na utha sakenge (yani yahi kahenge) Aye Parwardigar! Teri Qasam hargiz Mushrik na the. Dekho woh is waqt apne aap par kaisa jhoot tarashenge aur wahan unki sab banaoten gum ho jayengi."_
(Surah An'am: 22 - 24)

📚📖 😏
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Phir Ahle Mahshar ko doosre maqamat par jama kiya jayega. Wahan unhe bolne ki ijazat di jayegi to woh apni safai mein ye kahenge. Ayat (6:23) iske baad Allah unke munh par mohr laga dega, us waqt unke haath paon aur unki khalen guftgu karengi aur woh apni har nafarmani ki gawahi denge. Phir unki zabanon se Mohr utha li jayegi to woh apni khalon se kahenge ke tumne hamare khilaf kiyon gawahi di? Unki khalen kahengi hamse Us Khuda ne baten karayi hai Jisne har shay ko goyayi di hai."_
(Kitabut Tauheed)
😓
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Jin logon ne hamari Ayaat ki takzeeb ki woh Hidayat ki awaaz sunne se bahte hain aur Kalma e Haq kahne se goonge hain. Woh Kufr ki tareekyon mein rihaish pazeer hain aur (6:39) ki Ayat mein is Ummat ki qadarya afraad ki tardeed ki gayi hai. Allah Ta'ala Qayamat ke Roz unhe Sayebeen, Nasaara aur Majoosiyon ke saath mahshoor karega. Woh us waqt kahenge: (6:23,24)"_
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi)
😏
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Ye woh log honge jinhone Duniya mein rah kar Tauheed ka iqraar kiya hoga lekin unka Imaan unhen isliye fayda na dega ke unhone Rasoolon ki Mukhalefat ki hogi aur Anbiya ki sadaqat  mein shak kiya hoga aur unhone Anbiya ke Ausiya se Ahd Shikni ki hogi aur Aala (Highest Rank) ke badle Adna (Lowly) ko pasand kiya hoga. Isi liye Allah Ta'ala unke Imaani da'we ko qubool nahi karega aur Allah ne unke mutalliq farmaya: (6:24)."_
(Kitab Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Imaan par qayam rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim Qummi)

_*Hadis e Lauh mein Imam Askari (as) ka zikr:*_
*"ابو محمد الحسن بن على(ع) الرفيق، أمه جاريه، إسمها سمانة، تكني بٱم الحسن، الْخَازِنَ لِعِلْمِی  وَ أُکمِلُ ذَلِک بِابْنِهِ محمد رَحْمَةً لِلْعَالَمِینَ عَلَیهِ کمَالُ مُوسَی وَ بَهَاءُ عِیسَی وَ صَبْرُ أَیوبَ فَیذَلُّ أَوْلِیائِی فِی زَمَانِهِ وَ تُتَهَادَی رُءُوسُهُمْ."*

_"Abu Mohd Al Hasan bin Ali (as), Al Rafeeq, unki madaregrami Kaneez Samana, unki Kunniyat Ummul Hasan, Ilm ka Khazana, unke bete Muhammad par (Imamat) ki takmeel hui."_
(Kamaluddin, Vol 1, P-308)

            ♦ _*MUSHREKEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (806)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يَسْتَمِعُ إِلَيْكَ ۖ وَجَعَلْنَا عَلَىٰ قُلُوبِهِمْ أَكِنَّةً أَنْ يَفْقَهُوهُ وَفِي آذَانِهِمْ وَقْرًا ۚ وَإِنْ يَرَوْا كُلَّ آيَةٍ لَا يُؤْمِنُوا بِهَا ۚ حَتَّىٰ إِذَا جَاءُوكَ يُجَادِلُونَكَ يَقُولُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا إِنْ هَٰذَا إِلَّا أَسَاطِيرُ الْأَوَّلِينَ * وَهُمْ يَنْهَوْنَ عَنْهُ وَيَنْأَوْنَ عَنْهُ ۖ وَإِنْ يُهْلِكُونَ إِلَّا أَنْفُسَهُمْ وَمَا يَشْعُرُونَ*

_"Un mein se baaz log aise hain jo kaan laga kar tumhari baton ko tawajjo se sunte hain magar Hamne unke Dilon par parde dal diye hain jiski wajah se woh kuchh nahi samajhte aur unke Kaanon mein garani (dat, butchh, cover) dal di hai aur agar woh Hamari tamam Nishaniyan bhi dekh len phir bhi woh un par Imaan nahi layenge yahan tak ke woh tumhare paas aa kar tumse jhagda karte hain to Inkaar karne wale ye kahte hain ke yeh to purani logon ki dastane hain."_
_"Woh logon ko Haq qubool karne se rokte hain aur khud bhi isse door rahte hain aur woh apne aap ko hi halakat mein dal rahe hain magar unhe shu'oor nahi hai."_
(Surah An'am: 25 - 26)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat Kuffar e Quraish ke liye nazil hui hai. Lekin kuchh Mufasserin ne is Ayat mein Bani Hashim ke kuchh afraad (Tafseer e Ali ibne Ibrahim mein bhi) aur Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ke liye ulte maani mein liya hai aur bataya jata hain ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki Tableegh mein rukawat dalte the. Jabke guzishta Ayaton se mila kar dekhen to ye un logon ke liye hai jinka zikr pichhli Ayaton mein bhi hua hai.
Jabke baaz Al Sunnat Ulama ne H. Abu Talib (as) ko Momin qarar diya hai, jaise Ibne Abil Hadeed, Qastalani, Seera Halabi waghaira ne. Jabke Abu Talib (as) ne na ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki hifazat ki balke Islam ko bachaya hai.
Janabe Abu Talib (as) ke Rasoole Akram (saww) ke liye kuchh Asha'ar is tarah bayan hue hain:
(Tarjuma)
_"Aye mere bhateeje Khuda ki Qasam jab tak Abu Talib mitti mein na so jaye aur Lahed ko apna bistar na bana le Dushman hargiz tujh tak nahi pahunch sakenge._
_Lehaza kisi cheez se na dar aur apni zimmedari aur mamooriyat ka iblagh kar, basharat de aur Aankhon ko thanda kar._
_Tu ne mujhe apne Maktab ki dawat di aur mujhe achhi tarah maloom hai ke tera hadaf o maqsad, pando nasihat karna aur bedar karna hai, tu apni dawat mein Ameen aur Sahih hai._
_Mein bhi jaanta hun ke Muhammad (saww) ka Deen o Maktab tamam Deeno o Maktabon mein sab se behtar Deen hai._
_Aye Quraish kiya tumhe maloom nahi hai ke Muhammad (saww) Musa (as) ki misl hain aur Musa (as) ke manind Khuda ke Paighambar aur Rasool hain jinke ki peshengoyi pahli Aasmani Kitabon mein likhi hui hai aur hamne use paa liya hai."_
_"Khuda ke bande usse khas lagao rakhte hai aur jise Khuda wand Ta'ala ne apni Muhabbat ke liye makhsoos kar liya ho us shakhs se ye lagao ne mauqa nahi hai."_
(Ref: Khazana tul Adab, Tareekh ibne Kaseer, Sharh e Ibne Abil Hadees, Fathul Baari, Bulooghul Adab, Tareekh Abul Fida, Seerah Nabawi, Shaikhul Abateh .....)
(Ikhtesar ke liye sirf tarjuma pesh kiya jabke Arabic mein in Kutub mein maujood hai.)

Jab khud H. Abu Talib (as) ne in alfaaz mein iqraar kiya hai, phir bhi adawat e Hazrat Ali (as) dilon mein itna bhara hai ke unke walid ko Kafir aur is Ayat ka misdaq qarar dete hain.

Bare Ilaha hame Abu Talib ke wafadaron mein mehshoor karna.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Ek martaba Jibreel (as) Rasule Khuda (saww) par naazil huwe aur kaha, "Khallaq e Aalam aap ko Salaam kehta hai aur farmata hai ke Maine uspar Aatish e Dozakh ko haraam qaraar diya hai jiski sulb (loins) se tum paida huwe aur jiske shikam (peyt) mein tum rahe (Yaani J. Abdullah aur J. Aamina par) aur Aatish e Dozakh ko haraam kiya hai uspar jisne tumhari kifaalat aur muhafizat ki hai (Yaani Abu Talib (as) par)."_
Hayaat ul Quloob, v2, p67

  ♦ _*AYATULLAH KO JHUTLANA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (807)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَوْ تَرَىٰ إِذْ وُقِفُوا عَلَى النَّارِ فَقَالُوا يَا لَيْتَنَا نُرَدُّ وَلَا نُكَذِّبَ بِآيَاتِ رَبِّنَا وَنَكُونَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ * بَلْ بَدَا لَهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يُخْفُونَ مِنْ قَبْلُ ۖ وَلَوْ رُدُّوا لَعَادُوا لِمَا نُهُوا عَنْهُ وَإِنَّهُمْ لَكَاذِبُونَ*

_"Kaash Aap us waqt unki haalat dekhte jab woh Dozakh ke kinare khade kar diye jayenge to woh us waqt bhi kahenge: Aye kaash! Hame Duniya mein wapas bhej diya jaye to ham apne Rab ki Nishaniyon ko nahi jhutlayenge aur ham Imaan laane walon mein shamil honge."_
_"Baat ye hai jis haqeeqat ko woh chhupate the woh unke saamne ayan ho kar aa jayegi. Aur agar bilfarz unhe Duniya mein lauta bhi diya jaye to bhi woh wohi kuchh karenge jisse unhe roka gaya aur Yaqeenan woh jhoote hai."_
(Surah An'am: 27 - 28)

📚📖 🍪🥣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Isi tarah ki Qur'an mein ek aur Ayat guzar chuki hai (2:167).
Ayatullah yani Allah ki Nishaniyan. Allah ki Nishaniyan sirf Allah ki tarah se hoti hain. Rivayaaton mein Aimma e Masoomeen (as) ko Ayatullah ka khitab diya gaya hai. Jo Allah ki Nishaniyon ki itteba' karega usko Momin kahte hain.
🕌
Rivayat:
Jabir bin Abdullah Ansari  Imam Ali (as) ke saath Masjid e Kufa mein dakhil hue to Imam Ali (as) kisi se farma rahe hain jabke koi dikhai nahi de raha tha: _"Khuda ki Qasam mein nahi kar sakta."_ unhone Maula se daryaft kiya to farmaya:
_"Ay Jabir! Mujhe Wadiye Barhoot ka nazara dikhaya gaya, meine dekha mere Dushman ko uske Taboot mein Azaab diya jaa raha hai, aur mujhe pukar raha hai: Ya Abul Hasan, Ya Ameerul Mo'meneen! Mujhe Duniya mein wapas bula lo ham aapki Fazilat o Wilayat ki gawahi denge. Tab meine kaha: _"Khuda ki Qasam mein nahi kar sakta, aisa nahi hoga."_ Phir Imam Ali (as) ne ye Ayat (6:27-28) padhi. Phir farmaya:
_"Ay Jabir! Jo bhi Nabi (saww) ke Wasi ko jhutlayega woh Qayamat ke Din Andha uthaya jayega aur Qayamat ke Maidan mein munh ke bal ghaseeta jayega."_
Isiliye jo Ayatullah Aimma e Masoomeen ko jhutlayega aur khud sakhta Ayatullah ko follow karega uska yehi haal hoga.
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Al Burhan, Vol 3, P-23)

Bare Ilaha hame Tere Nishaniyon ki Ma'arefat ata kar taake unki itteba' kar saken.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Aye Ali (as)! Roz e Qayamat main, tum aur Jibreel (as) Siraat par baithhenge aur koi uspar se nahi guzrega magar wo jiske paas tumhari Wilayat ke sabab se aatish e Dozakh se Nijaat ka parwana hoga."_
(Isbaat e Imamat - Allamah Majlisi, p75, Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p52)
🍁
Imam Ali (as)
_"Afsos hai uspar jiska dushman usay nasihat kare."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p52)

                ♦ _*DUNIYA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (808)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالُوا إِنْ هِيَ إِلَّا حَيَاتُنَا الدُّنْيَا وَمَا نَحْنُ بِمَبْعُوثِينَ*

_"Woh kahte hain ke Zindagi sirf hamari is Duniya tak mehdood (limited) hai, aur ham marne ke baad uthay nahi jayenge."_
(Surah An'am 29)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jis Duniya mein ham rah rahe hain ye ek Temporary Zindagi hai. Balke ye Life Examination Hall hai. Marne ke baad ki zindagi permanent zindagi hai. Ye ham log nahi samajh paate hain. Maut ko har koi dekhta hai. Isliye ye koi nahi kah sakta ke life eternal (La mehdood) hai. Ye communist idea ghalat hai ye chhoti si Duniya hai jitna maze udana hai uda lo. Ya ye ke kal kisne dekha hai aaj jitni masti karni hai kar lo. 31st December ki Raat ko isi nazarye ke tahet Entertainment karenge jis mein Gunah ke alawa aur kuchh nahi hoga. Kuchh bhi kar len lekin Aakhir (Akherat) mein pakde jayenge. Kiyonki inke paas Qayamat ya Akherat jaisa koi Aqeeda nahi hai. Agar ham Nai Saal ki shurua'at Gunahon se karenge to uska pura Saal gunahon mein guzrega aisi hi ummid ki ja sakti hai. Lekin Nek o Saleh afraad is Duniya ki lazzaton mein koi interest nahi rakhte.
🌍
Rivayaat mulaheza hon:
Imam Ali (as)
_"Duniya Momin ka Qaid-Khana, Maut uska tohfa aur Jannat uski manzil hai. Duniya kaafiro'n ki Jannat hoti hai aur maut usay is (jannat) se judaa karnewali  aur Aag uski manzil hoti hai."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Duniya)
🌍
Allah (swt)
_"Duniya mein zyada aarzuein na banao, kyun ki is se tera dil sakht ho jayega aur jiska bhi dil sakht ho jaata hai wo Mujh se duur ho jaata hai."_
(Al Kaafi, Ahaadis e Qudsi, Aastaan e Quds Razawi)
🌏
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Duniya mein Zohad ye nahi ke insaan oon (wool) ke kapde pehne aur bagair saalan ke sukhi roti khaaye balke Zohad ye hai ke Aarzu aur Khwahish lambi na ho."_
(Mishkaat ul Anwaar (Urdu)

*رَبَّنَا آتِنَا فِي الدُّنْيَا حَسَنَةً وَفِي الْآخِرَةِ حَسَنَةً وَقِنَا عَذَابَ النَّارِ*
_"Aye hamare Rab! Hame Duniya mein bhi bhalai de aur Akherat mein bhi bhalai de aur Aag ke Azaab se hame bacha."_ (2:201)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌎
Imam Musa Kazim (as):
_"Aye Hisham! Khuda ne aqalmand logon ko nasihat ki hai aur Akherat ke liye talluq rakhne wala banaya hai, aur kaha hai ke Duniyavi Zindagi siwai khel kood ke aur kuchh nahi hai aur Akherat Muttaqi aur Parhezgar logon ke liye behtar hai, kiya tum apni aql aur fikr ko kaam mein nahi laate ho."_
(Noorus Saqlain, Vol 1, P-711)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (809)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا إِلَّا لَعِبٌ وَلَهْوٌ ۖ وَلَلدَّارُ الْآخِرَةُ خَيْرٌ لِلَّذِينَ يَتَّقُونَ ۗ أَفَلَا تَعْقِلُونَ*

_"Dunyavi Zindagi to ek khel tamasha ke alawa kuchh nahi jabke Akherat ka Ghar un logon ke liye behtar hai jo Taqwa rakhte hain. Kiya tumhari Aql mein ye baat aati hai?"_
(Surah An'am 32)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke pichhi Ayat ke zel mein bhi farmaya ke ye Duniya mukhtasar aur Mehdood hai. Is Ayat mein Allah farma raha hai ke Duniya kuchh nahi bas Khel kood hai.
(Yazid ne kaha tha ke Muhammad ka Deen kuchh nahi bas Bani Hashim ka khel tamasha tha.)
Khel ek waqtiya aur temporary cheez hoti hai. One Match hoti hai ek team haarti to ek team jeeti hai. Phir khel khatm, jeetne wala ina'am lekar khushi khushi chala jata hai. Ham bhi is Duniya mein Test Match ke liye hain, hamesha is stadium mein nahi rahna hai. Khel khatm hone par wapas apne ghar jana hai. Isliye ham jahan se aye hain wahin wapas jaana hai. Hamara permanent Ghar Akherat hai. Ham sab is Duniya mein players hain, kaun kab out ho jaye kisi ko nahi pata. Isliye koi player nahi chahega ke ball fail jay, ya no ball ho.
Entertainment waste of time hai. Entertainment mein Music, Dance, Song, Drinks, enjoyment yehi hota hai. New year ki Shabbedari mein Duniya parast logon ne yehi kiya. Ye sab kuchh nahi sirf time pass hai. Koi Aql mand insaan ye nahi bata sakta ke iska koi fayda hai, siwai iske ke uske kuchh period ghat gaye. Ek saal khatm hua, aapki ek inning ho gayi, ab doosri inning ke liye tayyar hona hai. Player agar Match mein kuchh faltu waqt zyada le le to penalty lag jaati hai.

Imam Musa Kazim (as):
_"Hisham! Allah ne (is ayat mein) Ahle Aql ko nasihat ki hai aur Akherat ki targheeb di hai."_
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain, Vol 1, P-711)

Bare Ilaha hamare liye Naya Saal khushiyon bhara ho jis mein hamari Nekiyon mein aur izaafa ho.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

🙇 🌍
Imam Ali (as)

(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Duniya)
🌏
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Duniya Akherat ke liye behtareen madadgaar hai."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v12, p50)
🌎
Imam Ali (as)
_"Duniya Daulat se haasil ki jaati hai aur Akherat Amal se."_
Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Duniya
🍃🍂
Imam Ali (as)
_"Jo apni Akherat sa'nwaar lega, Allah uski Duniya sa'nwaar dega."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Akherat)

               ♦ _*AKHERAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (810)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَوْ تَرَىٰ إِذْ وُقِفُوا عَلَىٰ رَبِّهِمْ ۚ قَالَ أَلَيْسَ هَٰذَا بِالْحَقِّ ۚ قَالُوا بَلَىٰ وَرَبِّنَا ۚ قَالَ فَذُوقُوا الْعَذَابَ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَكْفُرُونَ*
*قَدْ خَسِرَ الَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا بِلِقَاءِ اللَّهِ ۖ حَتَّىٰ إِذَا جَاءَتْهُمُ السَّاعَةُ بَغْتَةً قَالُوا يَا حَسْرَتَنَا عَلَىٰ مَا فَرَّطْنَا فِيهَا وَهُمْ يَحْمِلُونَ أَوْزَارَهُمْ عَلَىٰ ظُهُورِهِمْ ۚ أَلَا سَاءَ مَا يَزِرُونَ*

_"Un logon ne khasara uthaya jinhone Khuda ke saamne hazir ho kar takzeeb ki. Yahan jab achanak wo ghadi aa jayegi to kahenge afsos ham se ye kaisi kotahi hui. Us waqt woh apni pushton (back) par hi apne Gunahon ka bojh laade honge. Kaisa bura bojh hai jise woh uthai honge."_
_"Un logon ne khasara uthaya jinhone Khuda ke saamne hazir ho kar takzeeb ki. Yahan jab achanak wo ghadi aa jayegi to kahenge afsos ham se ye kaisi kotahi hui. Us waqt woh apni pushton (back) par hi apne Gunahon ka bojh laade honge. Kaisa bura bojh hai jise woh uthai honge."_
(Surah An'am 30 - 31)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Akherat mein Kafiron ki kiya haalat hogi ye manzar is Ayat mein pesh kiya hai. Allah unse poochhega Haqq dekha? Haan dekha, is Haq ka ham inkaar karte the.  Aur Rivayat mein hai:
*العلى مع الحق و الحق مع العلى.*
_"Ali (as) Haq ke saath aur Haq Ali (as) ke saath."_
Chunke woh Haq ka inkaar karenge to Azaab ka maza bhi chakhenge. Allah ne kiya manzar kashi ki hai ke Kitne ghaate mein woh log hain, Gunahon ka kitna bura bojh woh uthaye phir rahe honge. Tab bhagne ke koi raasta nahi rahega.

Bare Ilaha Akherat mein hame in giroh mein na rakhna aur ham us Din tere Karam ke mushtaq hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo shakhs hamare dushmano'n aur hum par zulm karne waalo'n ke Kufr mein shak kare, wo khud Kaafir hai."_
(Aeteqadaat - Shaikh Sadooq, p107)
☘
Imam Ali (as)
_"Har shakhs waqt e niza mujhe dekhta hai aur dekhega, chaahe wo Momin ho ya Kaafir. (Ayatullah Dastghaib Shirazi wazaahat karte hain ke Momeneen ke liye H. Ali (as) ki ziyarat ne'mat hai kyun ki Hazrat ke jamaal e dilkash ka mushahida Momin ke liye har lazzat se laziz-tar hai aur kaafir o munafiq ke liye hazrat (as) ka deedar qeher e Parwardigaar ka mazhar hoga)"_
Ma'ad, p38
🌿
﻿Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Jo banda Ali (as) par doosre as'haab ko fazilat o fauqiyat (preference / praadhanya) de, wo yaqeenan Kaafir hai."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p623)

♦ _*LOGON KE COMMENTS PAR SABR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (811)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَدْ نَعْلَمُ إِنَّهُ لَيَحْزُنُكَ الَّذِي يَقُولُونَ ۖ فَإِنَّهُمْ لَا يُكَذِّبُونَكَ وَلَٰكِنَّ الظَّالِمِينَ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ يَجْحَدُونَ * وَلَقَدْ كُذِّبَتْ رُسُلٌ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ فَصَبَرُوا عَلَىٰ مَا كُذِّبُوا وَأُوذُوا حَتَّىٰ أَتَاهُمْ نَصْرُنَا ۚ وَلَا مُبَدِّلَ لِكَلِمَاتِ اللَّهِ ۚ وَلَقَدْ جَاءَكَ مِنْ نَبَإِ الْمُرْسَلِينَ*

_"Ham jaante hain ke unki baaten sun kar Aapko dukh pahunchta hai. Ye log Aapko hi nahi jhutla rahe balke Zalim log Allah ki Ayat (Ayatullah) ki takzeeb kar rahe hain."_
_"Aapse pahle bhi bahut se Rasoolon ko jhutlaya ja chuka hai magar in Rasoolon is Takzeeb aur izaaon par jo unhone pahunchayi gayi thi sabr kiya tha yahan tak ke Hamari madad unke shamile haal hui. Allah ki baaton ko badalne ki kisi mein taqat nahi hai aur Rasoolon ke waqeat Aap tak to pahunch hi chuke hain."_
(Surah An'am: 33 - 34)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah ki Nishani means Ayatullah ye title Rivayaat ke mutabiq Allah ke muntakhab Rasool o Aimma ko diya gaya hai.
🍁
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Alqama! Logon ki raza haasil karna dushwar hai aur unki zabano se mehfooz rahna intehai mushkil hai. Logon ki zabano se to Khuda ke Anbiya o Rusul aur Hujaj e Ilahi mehfooz nahi rahe the. Logon ne Habib e Khuda (saww) ke Dawa e Risaalat ki takzeeb ki to Allah ne apne Habib ko tasalli dete hue ye Ayat farmayi (6:34)"_
(Amaali e Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)
☘
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Rasool e Khuda (saww) ne apne Wasi ke fazael bayan kiye to logon ke Dilon mein Nifaq paida hone laga aur woh Aap (saww) ke mutalliq tarah tarah ki baten banane lag gaye. Allah Ta'ala ne Aap (saww) ko tasalli dete hue farmaya (6:33)."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🌿
Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
(Jab Aapke saamne ye Ayat 6:33 padhi gayi)
_"Zalimon ne be tahasha Aanhazrat (saww) ki takzeeb ki thi lekin unhe ye jura'at  na hui thi ke woh apni taraf se Batil (Wasi) pesh karke Aap (saww) ke Haq ko jhutlate."_
(Roza e Kaafi)

Bare Ilaha Dushman ki Ta'anon par hame Sabr ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📃
Imam Sadiq (as) ne khat ke zariye apne Shiyon ko ye Paigham diya:
_"Tumhare Imaan ki us waqt tak takmeel na hogi jab tak tum par woh halaat se na guzren jo tum se pahle Saleheen par guzre the. Tumse tumhari jaan o maal ka imtehan liya jayega aur tumhe Dushmanane Khuda se bahut si aziyyat naak baten sunna hongi aur tumhe har baat par Sabr karna hoga. Log tumhe ruswa karenge aur tum se Bughz rakhenge aur tumhe Khuda ki Raza aur Akherat ke Ghar ke husool ke liye tamam tar mazalim bardasht karna padenge. Tumhe ghussa ke ghoont peene honge. Log tumhari sachchi baton ko jhutlayenge aur tumse Bughz o Inaad rakhenge, magar tumhe Sabr ka Daman mazbooti se thaamna hoga. Allah Ta'ala ne Jibrael Ameen (as) ki zabani apne Habib ko ye Paigham bheja. Sabr (Al Ahqaaq:35) aur ye Ayat 6:33)"_
(Roza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

             ♦ _*AYATULLAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (812)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنْ كَانَ كَبُرَ عَلَيْكَ إِعْرَاضُهُمْ فَإِنِ اسْتَطَعْتَ أَنْ تَبْتَغِيَ نَفَقًا فِي الْأَرْضِ أَوْ سُلَّمًا فِي السَّمَاءِ فَتَأْتِيَهُمْ بِآيَةٍ ۚ وَلَوْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ لَجَمَعَهُمْ عَلَى الْهُدَىٰ ۚ فَلَا تَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْجَاهِلِينَ*

_"Aur agar unki berukhi Aap (saww) par giraan (hard) hai to agar tum mein itna zor hai to Zameen mein koi Surang (Tunnel) dhoondho ya Aasmaan mein Seedhi laga kar unke paas koi nishani laane ki koshish karo. Aur Allah agar chahta to to sab Hidayat par jama kar sakta tha lehaza nadaan na bano."_
(Surah An'am: 35)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
'Ayatullah' means Sign of Allah, Allah ki Nishani. Allah ne Duniya mein apni Nishaniyan rakhi hain taake unhe dekh kar Allah ko pahchana ja sake. Jaise Ka'aba Allah ki Nishani hai, Ye Kainat Allah ki Khalq ki hui Nishani hai waghaira. Jis cheez ki nisbat Allah se hai woh Allah ki Nishani hai. Isi tarah Anbiya wa Rusul bhi Allah ki Nishaniyan hai kiyonki woh Allah ki taraf se hai. Isi tarah Hamare Rasool (saww) ke Janashin o Rahnuma wa Aimma jo Khuda ki taraf se muntakhab shuda hain, woh bhi Allah ki Nishaniyan hain. Khud se koi ban jaye ya log chunne se Ayatullah nahi hoga.
Is Ayat mein Allah ne Dushmanane Ayatullah ko challenge kiya hai ke agar himmat hai Hamari Ayaat ke muqabile tum apne chune hue Rahbar pesh karo. Chahe Zameen ki tha ya Aasmaano ki unchaiyon dhoondh dalo, koi Nishani nikal lo.
Zaroori baat jo samajhne ki hai jo ye sawal paida hota ke Allah jo itna Qadir o Mutalq hai sab ko Hidayat yaafta kiyon nahi bana deta.  Allah chahe to sab ko Musalman wa Momin o Muttaqi bana de?
Agar Examination Hall mein koi Student Teacher se Question Paper ke baare mein Teacher se sawal kare ke aapko to sab aata hai, aap ye paper solve kar do, mujhe kiyon diya hai solve karne ke liye. Aap kahenge ye bewakoofi wala sawal hai.
Bas yehi haal is Duniya ka hai, jo karna hai hame karna hai, jiska Ajr Allah dega. Haq ki talash hame karna hai, Allah ne to bas clues, Alternatives pesh kar diye hain, selection hamare haath mein hai. Bas Malakul Maut ayega aur aapke amaal ka paper ghaseet kar bolega 'Time up' chaliye Duniya chhodye. Isliye jo time aapke paas hai us mein apne amaal ka paper poora kar len.

Bare Ilaha hame Nek Aamaal karne ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Hazrat Khatami Martabat Muhammad (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)! Allah ne Ummat ke ikhtelafat o ifteraq (differences) ka faisla kar diya hai aur agar Khuda chahta to sab ko Hidayat par jama kar sakta tha aur un mein kisi ko kisi se ikhtelaf na hota aur Amr e Ilahi mein koi tanaza (dispute) paida na hota aur koi Mafzool (Afzal ka follower) kisi Sahebe Fazl (Afzal) ki Fazilat ka inkaar na karta."_
(Manaqib e Ibne Shahre Ashoob, Raavi Salman Farsi)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

            ♦ _*ZINDA QAUM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (813)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّمَا يَسْتَجِيبُ الَّذِينَ يَسْمَعُونَ ۘ وَالْمَوْتَىٰ يَبْعَثُهُمُ اللَّهُ ثُمَّ إِلَيْهِ يُرْجَعُونَ*

_"Haq ki awaz par sirf wohi log Labbaik kahte hain jo Haq ki awaz sunte hain aur murdon ko Allah Qabron se uthayega, phir woh Uski taraf palat jayenge."_
(Surah An'am: 36)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jo Qaum Haq ki Awaaz par Labbaik kahe wohi Zinda Qaum hai kiyonki is Ayat mein Allah ne Ishaara diya ke woh baqi sab murde hain jinhe Allah ki taraf palatna hai aur jawabdeh hona hai. Allah ne har tarah se Haq ka tarruf karaya. Haq ne Haq ki baat sunayi. Aur Haq Allah ki muntakhab Ayaat, yaani Allah ke numainde aur Masoom Rehbar hain jiski ek kadi aaj bhi Parda e Ghaibat mein Zinda hai. Jab Zahoor hoga to Haq ki awaaz par puri Duniya Labbaik Ya Mahdi (atfs) pukaregi.

Bare Ilaha hame Ansaare Imam e Zaman (atfs) mein shumar farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ☘
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Log 4 qism ke hain:_
_(1) Jaahil: Halaak-shuda khwaish e nafsaani ka gulaam,_
_(2) Taaqat-war Ibadat-guzaar: Jis qadar zyada Ibadat karta hai us qadar zyada mutakabbir (abhimaani / ghamanddi) hota hai,_
_(3) *Aisa Aalim jo apni aaqebat (anjaam) ki parwah kiye baghair logon ki taarif pasand karta hai,*_
_(4) *Aisa insaan jo Ma'arefat ke saath raah e Haq par chal raha hai aur Haq par qayem rehne ko pasand karta hai lekin kamzor aur magloob (powerless) hai. Ye shakhs tere zamane ka behtareen shakhs hai aur iski Aql sab se behtar hai.*"_
(Khisaal, p138)
🍁
Imam Ali (as)
_*"Momin ka chiraag hamare Haq ki maarefat hai aur badtareen andhaapan hamare fazl se aa'nkhein band kar lena hai.*"_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)

Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Saheb e Amr (atfs) ka zahoor us waqt tak na hoga jab tak har qaum ko hukumat ka mauqa na de diya jaaye taaki koi ye na keh sakey ke agar hamari hukumat hoti to hum Adl qayem karte. Un sab ke baad Imam Qaim (atfs) Haq aur Adl ke saath zahoor karenge."_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v12, p166)

                  ♦ _*MOJIZA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (814)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالُوا لَوْلَا نُزِّلَ عَلَيْهِ آيَةٌ مِنْ رَبِّهِ ۚ قُلْ إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَادِرٌ عَلَىٰ أَنْ يُنَزِّلَ آيَةً وَلَٰكِنَّ أَكْثَرَهُمْ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ*

_"Aur unhone kaha ke us par Rab ki taraf se koi Nishani kiyon nahi utari gayi? Aap (saww) kah den ke Allah Ta'ala utarne par Qudrat rakhta hai lekin unki aksariyat nadaani mein mubtila hai."_
(Surah An'am: 37)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Sawal do tarah ke hote hain ek kuchh jaankari hasil karne ke liye aur doosri tarah ka sawal kinayatan hota hai yani sawal karne wale ko jawab ki koi khwahish nahi hoti. Yani woh Taane ke taur par istemal hota hai. Yahan is Ayat mein Kuffar jo apni hat dharmi mein atal the jaisa ke guzishta Ayaat se zahir hai, unhone sirf Rasool (saww) ka mazaaq udaya hai. Kiya Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Mojize karke nahi dikhaye! Qur'an khud ek mojiza hai. Yahan unke sare Mojize ginane gunjaish nahi, qaereen Kitaben refer kar sakte hain.
Allah har Shay par Qudrat rakhta hai. Nabi jo bhi Mojiza dikhata hai woh Khuda ki Qudrat se dikhata hai. Mojiza dikhana Tableeghi maqsad ke tahet hota hai. Har jagah Nabi Mojiza nahi dikhata.
Karbala mein agar Imam Husain (as) chahte to poori Yazidi fauj fana ho jaati, lekin asal maqsad pamaal ho jaata. Kiya Rasool Khuda (saww) aisa nahi kar sakte the ke koi Mojiza dikhate aur saare Kuffar ek waqt mein Musalman ho jaate jaisa ke guzishta Ayaat mein Allah ne yehi baat batayi hai. Lekin asl cheez har kaam ke pichhe ek Hadaf ya maqsad hota hai.

Bare Ilaha hame hamare Nek maqsad mein kamyabi ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Hamara Rab us waqt bhi Aalim *عالم* tha jab 'Maalum' *معلوم* cheez hi wajood mein nahi aayi thi aur Wo us waqt bhi 'Samee' *سميع* (sun'ne waala) tha jab suni jaane waali koi awaaz paida nahi huwi thi. Aur Wo us waqt bhi 'Baseer' *بصير*  (dekhne waala)  tha jab dikhayi dene waali koi cheez abhi khalq hi nahi hui thi aur Wo oos waqt bhi 'Qadeer' *قدير* (saheb e Qudrat) tha jab koi zeyr a qudrat cheez ma'as e shahood par nahi aayi thi…"_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p78)

    ♦ _*JANWAR AUR PARINDE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (815)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا مِنْ دَابَّةٍ فِي الْأَرْضِ وَلَا طَائِرٍ يَطِيرُ بِجَنَاحَيْهِ إِلَّا أُمَمٌ أَمْثَالُكُمْ ۚ مَا فَرَّطْنَا فِي الْكِتَابِ مِنْ شَيْءٍ ۚ ثُمَّ إِلَىٰ رَبِّهِمْ يُحْشَرُونَ*

_"Zameen par chalne wale tamam Jaandar aur apne paron se parwaaz karne wale tamam parinde sab tumhari tarah ki hi Ummaten hain. Hamne unke Navishta e Taqdeer mein koi kasar nahi chhodi. Phir ye sab apne Rab ki taraf mehshoor kiye jayenge."_
(Surah An'am: 38)

📚📖 🐴🐪🐫🦌🐐🦅🦇
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as): 🐪
_"Jis Oont par teen chaar bar Hajj ka safar kiya jaye to Allah use Bahishti (Jannati) Janwaron mein se qarar deta hai."_ (Doosri rivayat mein 7 bar hai.)
(Man Ka Yahzarul Faqih)
🧦🦌🐐
Imam Sadiq (as):
(Moze par Masah ke mutalliq farmaya.:
_"Jab Qayamat ka Din hoga to Allah Ta'ala har cheez ke ajza ko uske asl ki taraf lauta dega. Us waqt khaal Bakri ko lauta do jayegi. Ab khud hi batao jinhone Bakri ki khaal se bane hue Moze (Socks) par Masah kiya hoga to unka Wuzu kahan jayega?"_
(Usoole Kaafi)
🐪 🏇
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Qayamat ke Roz sirf chaar afraad sawar honge. Ek mein hunga, doosre Ali (as) honge, teesre meri dukhtar Fatema Zehra (sa) hongi, aur chauthe Hazrat Saleh honge. Mein us Din Buraq par sawar hunga, meri beti Fatema (sa) meri Naqa Usbah par sawar hongi, Hazrat Saleh Naqatullah par sawar honge, jiski kunche kati gayi thi. Ali (as) Noor ke ek Naqa (she-Camel) par sawar honge jiski mahar Yaqoot ki hogi aur Ali (as) ne us waqt green colour ke do hulle pahen rakhen honge."_
(Kitabul Khisaal)

(Haiwanat par Ahadis bahut hain lekin yahan gunjaish nahi hai.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Reza (as):
_"Abdul Aziz! Log jihalat ka shikar hain aur Deen ke mutalliq dhoke me mubtila hain. Allah ne us waqt tak apne Nabi ko Duniya se hi nahi uthaya jab tak Deen ki takmeel na kar di aur un par Qur'an utaara jis mein har cheez ki tafseel maujood hai aur Allah ne Qur'an mein Halaal o Haraam, Hudood o Ahkam aur unke tamam cheezon ki wazahat kar di hai jiski logon ko ehtiyaj (zaroorat) ho sakti hai. Chunanche Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: "Hamne Kitab mein koi kami nahi chhodi."(6:38)_
(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

        ♦ _*TAKZEEB-E-AUSIYA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (816)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَالَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا صُمٌّ وَبُكْمٌ فِي الظُّلُمَاتِ ۗ مَنْ يَشَإِ اللَّهُ يُضْلِلْهُ وَمَنْ يَشَأْ يَجْعَلْهُ عَلَىٰ صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ*

_"Woh log jinhone Hamari Ayaat ki takzeeb ki hai woh behre (deaf) aur goonge (dumb) hain. Woh tareekyon mein pade hue hain. Khuda jiski gumrahi chahta hai Hukm kar deta hai aur jise chahe Siraat e Mustaqeem par khada deta."_
(Surah An'am: 39)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Mufasserin ka kahna hai ke Bahron se murad wo Muqallidin (followers) hain jo baghair chun o chera ke apne Gumrah Rahbaron ki pairavi karte hain aur jo Haqaeq ko achhi tarah samajhte hain lekin apni hasiyat aur apne maddi munafe ki hifazat ke liye unhone apne Munh par mohre sukoot (silence) lagai hui hai, ye dono giroh Jihalat o Khud parasti ki Tareeki mein giraftar hain."
(Tafseer e Al Mizan, Vol 7, 84, Tafseere Namoona)
☘
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Ye Ayat un logon ke mutalliq nazil hui jinhone Ausiya ki takzeeb ki. Woh log bahre aur goonge hain aur woh tareekyon mein rihaish pazeer hain. Aulade Iblees ka koi bhi fard Ausiya par Imaan layega."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🌾
Khulasa ye ke jaisa ke pahle bata chuke hain Sirate Mustaqeem Ahle Bait (as) ka raasta hai aur jinhone inko jhutlaya woh tareekiyon mein pade hain aur unse Allah Ghazabnak hota hai.

Bare Ilaha hame Siraate Mustaqeem par baqi rakh  
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sajjad (as)
_"Mere Allah! Rahem farma mujh par jab mere paas jaan na rahe, Tere huzoor bolne mein jab meri zabaan goongi ho jaaye aur Tere sawaal par meri aql gum ho jaaye. Pus, meri sabse badi Ummeed-gaah! Mujhe oos waqt na-ummeed na kar, jab meri haajat sakht ho, mujhe naadani par duur na farma, meri kam-sabri par mehroom na rakh, meri haajat ke mutaabiq ataa kar aur meri kamzori par rahem farma."_
(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumaali)

    ♦ _*ALLAH KO PUKARNA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (817)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ أَرَأَيْتَكُمْ إِنْ أَتَاكُمْ عَذَابُ اللَّهِ أَوْ أَتَتْكُمُ السَّاعَةُ أَغَيْرَ اللَّهِ تَدْعُونَ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ * بَلْ إِيَّاهُ تَدْعُونَ فَيَكْشِفُ مَا تَدْعُونَ إِلَيْهِ إِنْ شَاءَ وَتَنْسَوْنَ مَا تُشْرِكُونَ*

_"Zara soch kar batao ke agar tum par Allah ka Azaab aa jaye ya Qayamat aa pade to us waqt kiya tum kisi ghairullah ko pukaroge agar tum sachche ho? Aise waqt mein to tum sirf Allah ko hi pukaarte ho. Phir agar Woh chahta hai to is musibat ko tumse taal deta hai aur us waqt tum apne sharikon ko bhool jaate ho."_
(Surah An'am: 40 - 41)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
"Ayat ka maqsad ye hai ke Allah ne Mushrekin se farmaya hai ke jab tum par koi Mushkil ghadi aayi hai to us waqt tum khalis Allah ko ho pukarte ho aur Mushkil door ho jaati hai to tum Khuda ko bhool jaate ho jabke musibat mein tum apne Buton bhool jaate ho."
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim)

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
(Lafz "Allah" ki tashreeh)
_"Hajaat ke waqt jis ki taraf rujoo' kiya jaye jab tamam zahiri umeeden toot jayen aur asbaab munqata ho jayen to us waqt jiski taraf rujoo' kiya jaata hai Woh " *Allah الله*" hai."_
"Is Duniya mein agar bade se bada Badshah bhi kiyon na ho aur logon ki Hajaat poori karta ho, us par bhi aisa waqt zaroor aata hai jab woh khud sakht Haajat Mand hota hai aur is sakht Haajat ke waqt Woh bhi Khuda ki taraf rujoo' karta hai. Albatta ye alaihda baat hai ke Haajat poori hone ke baad woh khuda ko bhula de. Kiya tu ne Allah ke ye farman nahi suna. (6:40).
(Kitabut Tauheed)

Bare Ilaha Mushkil Khushal ke sadqe mein hamari mushkilon ko door farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
Imam Husain (as):
_"Aye Wo, jise maine apni bimari mein pukara to shifa di, uryaani mein pukara to libaas diya, bhook mein pukara to mujhe ser kiya, pyaas mein pukara to sairab kiya, pasti mein izzat di, nadaani mein Ma'arefat bakshi, Tanhai mein kasrat di, safar mein wapas pahunchaya, tang-dasti mein mujhe maal diya, madad maangi to meri madad farmayi, tawangar tha to mera maal nahi chhina."_
(Dua e Arafa)
🙏🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Allah ke 99 naam hai, jo koi Usay in naamo'n se pukarega uski Dua mustajab hogi aur jo koi inhe yaad karega wo Jannat mein daakhil hoga.'_
(Uddatud Dai)
