   ♦ _*TAZARRO' (HUMBLENES)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (818)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَقَدْ أَرْسَلْنَا إِلَىٰ أُمَمٍ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ فَأَخَذْنَاهُمْ بِالْبَأْسَاءِ وَالضَّرَّاءِ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَتَضَرَّعُونَ * فَلَوْلَا إِذْ جَاءَهُمْ بَأْسُنَا تَضَرَّعُوا وَلَٰكِنْ قَسَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ وَزَيَّنَ لَهُمُ الشَّيْطَانُ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ*

_"Aur tumse pahle Hamne bahut si Qaumo ke paas apne Rasool bheje hain. Hamne in Aqwam (tribes) ko Masaeb o Aalaam mein mubtila kiya taake woh aajezi (humble) karte hue jhuk jayen. Jab Hamare taraf se un par sakhti aayi to unhone aajezi ki ravish kiyon na apnai? Iska sirf yahi sabab tha ke unke dil sakht ho chuke the aur Shaitan ne unke Samal unke liye aarasta kar diye the."_
(Surah An'am: 42 - 43)

----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
"Tazarro' *تضرع* literally means: Doodh ke pistan mein aa jane aur Doone wale ke saamne iske mutee' (obedient) hone ke ma'ane mein hai. Isliye terminologically (istelahan) ita'at (obedience) ke maani mein istemaal hota hai. Yaani bala o musibat Allah insaan par isliye ata karta hai taake woh Uske saamne inkisari se pesh aaye aur Takabbur se parhez kare.
🌾
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Tazarro' (Humbly)" ke liye haath Dua ke liye buland kiye jayen aur dayen bayen ki Ungliyon ko harkat deni chahiye."_
_"Dua e Tazarro' mein apne Angust  Sababa (Index Figure) ko chehre ke saamne harkat Deeni chahiye?"_
(Usoole Kaafi)
🎋
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Tazarro' ke liye dono haathon ko buland karna chahiye aur unhe harkat de kar apni aajezi ka izhaar karna chahiye."_
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🌾
Imam Kazim (as)
_"Aye Hishaam! Zara'at (plant / paudha) narm zameen mein ugati hai, pattharo'n par zara'at nahi ugati. Isi tarah tawaazoh (humility / humbleness / namrata) se qalb mein hikmat (wisdom) aabad hoti hai, mutakabbir (takabbur karne wale) aur jabbar (zaalim) ke dil mein hikmat aabad nahi huwa karti."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p173)
🎋
Imam Ali (as)
_"Jis Qalb (dil) mein khushoo (humbleness / vinamrata) na ho aur jis Aa'nkh se aa'nsu na nikle hon aur jis Ilm ka koi faayda na ho, usme koi khair o bhalaai nahi hai."_
(Adaab e Islami, v2, p60)
🌾
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Ilm haasil karo aur Ilm ke saath khud ko Hilm o burd-baari (sahan-sheelta) se muzayyan karo aur jisko ta'aleem do ya jis se ta'aleem haasil karo, un sab ke saath inkesari (namrata) se pesh aao aur jaabir aur mutakabbir (ghamandi) Ulema ki tarah na ho jaao ke tumhari haq baatein tumhare galat aamaal ke saath rukhsat ho jayen."_
(Adaab e Islami, v2, p72)

Bare Ilaha hame ijz o inkesari se pesh aane ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       *12th January 2018, Friday,*

        ♦ _*MUNKIR E VILAYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (819)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَلَمَّا نَسُوا مَا ذُكِّرُوا بِهِ فَتَحْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ أَبْوَابَ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ حَتَّىٰ إِذَا فَرِحُوا بِمَا أُوتُوا أَخَذْنَاهُمْ بَغْتَةً فَإِذَا هُمْ مُبْلِسُونَ * فَقُطِعَ دَابِرُ الْقَوْمِ الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا ۚ وَالْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ*

_"Phir jab unhone is Nasihat ko faramosh (bhool) kar diya jo unhe ki gayi thi to Hamne un par Khush hali ke tamam darwaze khol diye yahan tak ke jo Ne'maat unhe di gayi thi wo unhe khush ho gaye to Hamne unhe achanak pakad liya. Phir woh mayoos ho gaye. Zulm karne walon ki jad kaat di gayi aur tamam Ta'reefen Allah ke liye makhsoos hain jo tamam Jahanon ka Paalne wala hai."_
(Surah An'am: 44 - 45)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
(Is Ayat ki Tafseer mein farmaya:)
_"(Iska ek morid ye bhi hai) ke logon ko Hazrat Ali (as) ki Vilayat ka Hukm diya gaya tha. Jab unhone is Hukm ko faramosh kar diya to unhe Khush Haali de di gayi aur jab woh apni Khush Haali par naaz kar rahe honge to achanak Qaem e Ale Muhammad (atfs) (Imam Mahdi) ki Hukoomat qaem kar di jayegi to yun mehsoos hoga ke Munkareen e Ali (as) ki Hukoomat Duniya mein kabhi qaem hi nahi hui thi."_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim Qummi)
🍁
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
(Iski zinda misal is tarah di)
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Bani Umayya ko achanak giraftar karega aur iske baad Hukoomat Bani Abbas mein chali jayegi. Allah Ta'ala unko khul kar giraftar karega."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🍂
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Vilayat e Ali (as) ke Munkaron ko Khuda ki taraf se dheel di jaati hai aur un par Duniyavi Ne'maat ki barish ki jaati hai. Iske baad Khuda ki taraf se unki giraft hoti hai. Bani Abbas ki Hukoomat bhi isi istedraj (referrals) ka karishma hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🌿
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ke ghulam Qambar ko Hajjaj ke samne pesh kiya gaya to to usne poochha ke Ali (as) ke liye kiya kaam karta tha. Qambar ne kaha ke mein Aap (as) ke liye Wuzu ke asbab faraham karta tha. Hajjaj ne poochha ke Ali (as) Wuzu se farigh hote the to kiya kahte the. Qambar ne kaha ye Ayat padhte the: (6:44)
🍃
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Jab tum ye dekho ke Khuda Gunahon ke Muqabile mein Ne'mat bakhshta hai to tum samjh lo ke ye saza ka Muqadma (Introduction) aur Tamheed hai. Ayat (6:44)"_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🍀
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Aye Adam ke bete! Jab tu ye dekhe ke Khuda tujhe pay dar pay Ne'maten bakhsh raha hai jabke tu gunah karta jaa raha hai to tu Uski Saza aur Azaab se darr kiyonki ye Azaab ka Muqadma hai."_
(Nahjul Balagha, Kalma 25)

Bare Ilaha hame aisi Ne'mat ata mat karna jo hame gumrah kar de.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ☘
Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Khuda ki Qasam! Jin logon ke paas zindagi ki tar o taaza o shadab Ne'maten thin aur phir unke haathon se nikal gayen ye unke Gunahon ke murtakib hone ki padaash hai kiyonki Allah to kisi par Zulm nahi karta. Agar log us waqt jabke un par musibaten toot rahi hon aur Ne'maten unse zael ho rahi hon, sidq niyyat aur rujoo' e qalb se apne Allah ki taraf mutawajjeh hon to Woh bargashtah (returned) hone wali Ne'maton ko phir unki taraf palta dega aur har kharabi ki islah kar dega."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

         ♦ _*AYAAT-E-ILAAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (820)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ أَرَأَيْتُمْ إِنْ أَخَذَ اللَّهُ سَمْعَكُمْ وَأَبْصَارَكُمْ وَخَتَمَ عَلَىٰ قُلُوبِكُمْ مَنْ إِلَٰهٌ غَيْرُ اللَّهِ يَأْتِيكُمْ بِهِ ۗ انْظُرْ كَيْفَ نُصَرِّفُ الْآيَاتِ ثُمَّ هُمْ يَصْدِفُونَ * قُلْ أَرَأَيْتَكُمْ إِنْ أَتَاكُمْ عَذَابُ اللَّهِ بَغْتَةً أَوْ جَهْرَةً هَلْ يُهْلَكُ إِلَّا الْقَوْمُ الظَّالِمُونَ*

_"Aap kah den kabhi tum socha ke agar Allah tumse tumhari Sama'at (hearing) aur Beenai (Sights) chheen le aur tumhare Dilon (Hearts) par mohr (Seal) laga de to Allah ke alawa koi aisa hai jo tumhe ye Quwwaten wapas kar sakta ho?"_
_"Dekho Ham kis tarah apni  Nishaniyan bar bar unke saamne pesh kar rahen hain aur woh kis tarah se nazrein chura rahe hain?"_
_"Aap kah den ke kabhi tumne ye bhi ghaur kiya ke agar Allah ki taraf se tum par achanak ya khul kar Azaab aa jaye to kiya Zaalim logon ke alawa koi aur halaak kiye jayenge?"_
(Surah An'am: 46 - 47)

📚📖 🌿
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Jis tarah se Allah Sama'at o Beenai chheen le to Uske alawa koi ye Ne'maten wapas nahi lauta sakta. Usi tarah se agar Khuda kisi se Hidayat ki taufeeq salb (takes away) kar le to use bhi koi hidayat nahi de sakta."_
(Mazeed is Ayat (6:47) ke bare mein farmaya:)
_"Jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) Hijrat karke Medina tashreef laye to Aap (saww) ke Ashaab ko bimari aur takaleef mein ne apni lapet mein le liya. Logon ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke paas apni tangi ki shikayat ki to Allah ne ye Ayat nazil farmayi aur is Ayat ke zariye Allah ne logon ko ye baat samjhayi ke tumhe Duniya ki chand roza takaleef o zahmaat to zaroor pahunchegi lekin tum par woh Azaab e Aleem nazil nahi kiya jayega jisse ummaten halaak ki jaati hain. Halaakat karne wala Azaab e Aleem Zalim aqwaam par hi nazil kiya jaata hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Wazeh rahe ke Aimma (as) bhi Rivayaat ke mutabiq hamare liye Ne'mat hain.

Bare Ilaha hame aise asbaab se door rakh jo hamari Ne'maten salb kar lete hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sajjad (as)
_"Wo gunah jo Ne'maton ko badal dete hain wo ye hain:_ _(1) Logo'n par zyadati karna,_
_(2) Khairaat karne aur neki karne ki aadat chhor dena,_
_(3) Kufraane Ne'mat karna,_
_(4) Shukr e Khuda na bajaa laana."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p86)
🍁
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Main apne baad apni Ummat ke liye 3 cheezo'n se darta hun.:_
_(1) Pehli ye ke Qur'an ki galat taaweel (interpretation) karenge,_
_(2) Aalim ki lagzish (galati) ko talaash karenge,_
_(3) ya daulat ki wajah se sarkash (rebellious) ho jayenge._
_Main tumhe unse bachne ka tariqa bhi batata hun:_
_(1) Qur'an se taalluq rakho, uski Aayaat e Mohkamaat (ke jinke maani waazeh (clear / spashtt) hain) par Amal karo; aur uski Aayaat e Mutashabihaat (ke jinke maani waazeh nahi) par Imaan rakho._
_(2) Aalim ke sahi iqdaam (actions) ki itteba' (follow) karo aur uski lagzish (ghalati) ko mat dhoondo._
_(3) Maal ke liye Ne'mat ka Shukr adaa karo aur usme se garibo'n ke huqooq adaa karo."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p175)
☘
Imam Ali (as)
_"Akherat ki Ne'mat se wohi shakhs nawaza jayega, jisne duniya ki balaa par Sabr kiya hai."_
(Gorar ul Hakam, v1, p29)

        ♦ _*MO'MIN & FAASIQ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (821)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا نُرْسِلُ الْمُرْسَلِينَ إِلَّا مُبَشِّرِينَ وَمُنْذِرِينَ ۖ فَمَنْ آمَنَ وَأَصْلَحَ فَلَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا هُمْ يَحْزَنُونَ * وَالَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا يَمَسُّهُمُ الْعَذَابُ بِمَا كَانُوا يَفْسُقُونَ*

_"Ham to Rasoolon ko Basheer (Khushkhabari denewala) wa Nazeer (Daranewala) bana kar bhejte hain. Phir jo Imaan layen aur apni Islah kar len to unke liye na to koi khauf hoga aur na woh ghabrayenge."_
_"Aur jo Hamari Ayaat ko jhutlayenge to woh apni nafarmanyon ki wajah se Saza bhugtenge."_
(Surah An'am: 48 - 49)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayaat mein Momin aur Faasiq ka criteria (me'yar) bataya gaya hai.
Jaisa ke pahle bhi bataya jaa chuka hai Anbiya wa Aimma e Huda Ayatullah hain, Allah ki Nishaniyon mein se hain. Jo in par Imaan layega woh Momin aur jo inko jhutlaega woh Faasiq.

Bare Ilaha hame Mo'meneen ki fehrist mein qaem rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🔰
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Khuda Wande Aalam irshaad farmata hai ke Badshahon ko bura na kaho kyun ki Main hi unko muqarrar farmata hun. Jaisi riaya (parja) hoti hai uspar waisa hi Haakim musallat karta hoo'n. Agar riaya bad-kirdaar, Khuda ki na-farmaan hoti hai to waisa hi bad-kirdaar o na-insaaf Haakim unpar muqarrar hota hai. Lihaza, logo'n ko chahiye ke bajaaye Badshah e bad-kirdaar ko bura kehne ke, apni islaah karein taaki Khuda unpar neku-kaar Haakim muqarrar farmaye."_
(Roohul Hayaat - Allama Majlisi, p597)
🔰
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Faasiqo'n ki sohbat se bacho, is liye ke buraai buraai se mil hi jaati hai."_
(Adaab e Islami, v1, p262)
🔰
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Faasiq (immoral / paapi) se (dosti se) hamesha parhez karna chahiye kyun ki wo ek luqma balke oos se bhi kamtar (less) ki khaatir tujhe farokht karne (bechne) se na chukega. Logo'n ne puchha, "Maula! 'Luqme se bhi kamtar' ka kya matlab hai?" Imam (as) ne farmaya ke, "Sirf uski laalach ke liye (yaani luqma haazir na ho, sirf ummeed ho ke shaayad mil jaaye)"._
(Dosti, p20)
🔰
Imam Sadiq (as)
se sawaal kiya gaya ke _*"Ek shakhs aap ki Ahadees logo'n mein bayaan karta hai aur usko logo'n mein mashhoor karta hai aur logo'n ke aur aap ke Shiyo'n ke dilo'n ki islaah (sudhaar / reform) karta hai aur doosra shakhs Aabid (Ibadat-guzaar) hai magar wo aap ki Ahadees ko logo'n mein bayaan nahi karta. In dono mein kaun afzal hai?" Aap ne farmaya, "Hamari Ahadees bayaan karne wala aur hamare Shiyo'n ke dilo'n ki islaah karne wala 1000 Aabido'n se behtar hai."*_
(Al Kaafi, v1, p73)

                    ♦ _*WAḤY*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (822)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ لَا أَقُولُ لَكُمْ عِنْدِي خَزَائِنُ اللَّهِ وَلَا أَعْلَمُ الْغَيْبَ وَلَا أَقُولُ لَكُمْ إِنِّي مَلَكٌ ۖ إِنْ أَتَّبِعُ إِلَّا مَا يُوحَىٰ إِلَيَّ ۚ قُلْ هَلْ يَسْتَوِي الْأَعْمَىٰ وَالْبَصِيرُ ۚ أَفَلَا تَتَفَكَّرُونَ*

_"Aap (saww) kah den ke mein tumse ye nahi kahta ke mere paas Allah ke khazane hain aur na mein Ghaib ka Ilm rakhta hun aur mein tumse ye bhi nahi kahta ke mein Farishta hun, mein to bus sirf us Waḥy ki pairavi karta hun jo mere taraf bheji jaati hai. Kiya Andha aur dekhnewala dono barabar ho sakte hain. Kiya tum ghaur nahi karte?"_
(Surah An'am: 50)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Ali Reza (as) ke paas aapke kuchh Pairokar jama the aur unhone Anhazrat (saww) ki un Ahadees ka tazkara kiya jin mein ek hi cheez ke mutalliq ikhtelaf paya jata hai to Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Allah Ta'ala ne kuchh cheezen Haraam ki hain aur kuchh cheezen Halaal ki hain aur kuchh faraez ki adaygi ko Wajib qarar diya hai. Ab agar tumhare paas koi aisi Hadees pahunche jis mein Halaal e Khuda ko Haraam ya Haraam e Khuda ko Halaal kaha gaya ho ya kisi Farz ki ahmiyat ko khatm kiya gaya ho to us Hadees par Amal karne ki gunjaish nahi hai. Kiyonki Rasoole Khuda (saww) Halaal e Khuda ko Haraam nahi karte the aur Haraam e Khuda ko Halaal nahi karte the aur yehi baat Qur'an Majeed mein in Alfaaz mein bayan ki gayi hai. ("Mein to us Waḥy ki pairavi karta hun jo meri taraf bheji jaati hai"). Anhazrat (saww) Tableegh e Risalat mein hamesha Waḥy e Ilahi ki pairavi karte the aur Khudai Ahkam pahuchane par ma'moor the."_
(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

Rasool e Khuda (saww) jo bhi bayan karte the sab Waḥy e Parwardigar hota tha. Jaisa ke doosri Ayat mein bhi hai:
*وَمَا يَنْطِقُ عَنِ الْهَوَىٰ * إِنْ هُوَ إِلَّا وَحْيٌ يُوحَىٰ*
_"Aur woh apni khwahish e Nafs se nahi bolta, ye ek Waḥy hai jo us par utari jati hai."_
(Surah Najm: 3 - 4)

Isliye Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke jaane ke baad jis Ummat ke Rehbar ne Haaram ko Halaal aur Halaal ko Haraam kiya usne sirf Rasool (saww) ki nafarmani nahi ki balke Parwardigar ki nafarmani ki, aur Ummat ko gumrah kiya. Woh aur uski pairokar sab seedhe Jahannam mein jayenge.

Bare Ilaha hame Tere Nabi e Kareem (saww) ki sunnat par amal karne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👥
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Hazrat Fatima Zahra (sa) ki azmat ke sabab Allah Ta'ala ne unki zurriyat par aatish e Dozakh ko haraam kar diya hai."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p113)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       *16th January 2018, Tuesday,*

                 ♦ _*TAQWA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (823)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَأَنْذِرْ بِهِ الَّذِينَ يَخَافُونَ أَنْ يُحْشَرُوا إِلَىٰ رَبِّهِمْ ۙ لَيْسَ لَهُمْ مِنْ دُونِهِ وَلِيٌّ وَلَا شَفِيعٌ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَتَّقُونَ*

_"Aap (saww) us Waḥy ke zariye unko Nasihat karen jo Uska Khauf rakhte hain ke apne Rab ke saamne is haal mein pesh kiye jayenge ke Uske alawa unke liye koi Madadgar aur Shafa'at karne wala na hoga taake (woh Nasihat se mutassir ho kar) Taqwa ki ravish ikhtiyar karen."_
(Surah An'am: 51)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Khauf e Khuda ki takeed ki gayi hai. Nasihat bhi sirf wohi qubool karenge jiske dil mein Khauf e Khuda hoga. Jo Khauf e Khuda nahi rakhta uske sab waaz o nasihat be asar hoti hai.
📚
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo log Khuda ka Khauf rakhne wale hon to unhe Qur'an Majeed ke zariye se nasihat karo, kyonki Qur'an Shafa'at karne wala hai aur uski Shafa'at qubool bhi ki jayegi."_
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha ham par Qur'an ki Taa'leemat ka asar ho aisi Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😢
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Khauf e Khuda se rone waali aa'nkh par Aag Haraam ki gayi hai._"
Kirdaar Saazi, v2, p7
😢
Imam Sajjad (as)
_"Khauf e Khuda ka matlab rona aur aa'nsu bahana nahi hai, kyun ki jab Taqwa na ho jo usay gunaho'n se roke, ye khauf jhoota hai._" (Fear of God does not mean weeping or shedding tears, for as long as there is no piety which keeps him from sins, the fear is false)
(Uddatud Daee, ch4)
😱
Imam Ali (as)
_"Duniya mein reh kar Akherat ke liye zaad e raah jamaa karo aur behtareen zaad e raah Taqwa hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p620)
🧔🏻
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Aalim jab apne Ilm ke mutabiq amal nahi karta to uske waaz / nasihat ka asar logon ke dil se zaail ho jaata hai jaise baarish ka saaf paani chattan se."_
(Al Kaafi, v1, p95)

♦ _*AHLE IMAAN GHURABA KO DOOR NA KARO*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (824)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تَطْرُدِ الَّذِينَ يَدْعُونَ رَبَّهُمْ بِالْغَدَاةِ وَالْعَشِيِّ يُرِيدُونَ وَجْهَهُ ۖ مَا عَلَيْكَ مِنْ حِسَابِهِمْ مِنْ شَيْءٍ وَمَا مِنْ حِسَابِكَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ شَيْءٍ فَتَطْرُدَهُمْ فَتَكُونَ مِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ*

_"Aap (saww) un logon ko door na karen jo apne Rab ko Subah Shaam pukarte hain aur woh Uski Khushnoodi ka iraada rakhte hain. Unke hisaab ka Aapse koi talluq nahi hai aur tumhare hisaab ka unse koi talluq nahi hai. Agar Aapne aise afraad ko apne door kiya to Aap Zalimon mein se ho jayenge."_
(Surah An'am: 52)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ek martaba Quraish ke sardar Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke paas se guzre to us waqt aap ke paas Suhaib, Khabab, Bilal, Ammar aur doosre Ghareeb aur kamzor Musalman baithe the. Unhone Anhazrat (saww) se kaha:
_"Muhammad (saww)! Aap ne apni qaum ko chhod kar inhe apna saathi bana liya hai kya ham inke pairokar ban jayen? Allah ko agar Ehsaan karna hi tha to Use yehi afraad dikhai diye? Aap inhe apne paas se dhutkar den. Agar Aap ne aisa kiya to shayad ham Aapki itteba' kar len."_
Tab Allah Ta'ala ye Ayat nazil ki. Chunanche Salman aur Khabab bade fakhr se kahte the ke ye Ayat hamare mutalliq hai.
(Majmaul Bayan, Tafseer Tha'labi, Noorus Saqlain)

Medina mein Ghareeb Ahle Imaan rahte the jinhe "Ashaab e Suffah *أصحاب صفه*" kaha jata tha. Rasoole Khuda (saww) unki dekh bhal karte the aur unke liye Khaana bhi bhejwate the. Woh log Aap (saww) ke paas aate jaate the. Aap (saww) unhe apne qareeb karte the aur unke saath baith kar pyar Muhabbat ki baten karte the. Daulat mand afraad ko Aapka ye tarz e amal pasand nahi tha. Unhone Aap (saww) se kaha ke Aap unhe apne se door kar den.
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim)

Bare Ilaha hame Taufeeq de ke ham Ghareeb Mo'meneen ki zyada zyada imdad kar saken.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👥
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Mera Mutakabbir Daulat mand logon se bhala kya wasta hai? Kya mein un logon ko apne door kar dun jo Subah o Shaam Khuda ka zikr karte hain aur Rizq e Halaal talaash karte hain. Agar meine unhen apne aap se dhutkar diya to mein Zalemeen mein qarar paonga."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹
*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*

             *30th Rabius Sani 1439*
       *18th January 2018, Thursday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
         ♦ _*AZMAISH (TEST)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (825)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَكَذَٰلِكَ فَتَنَّا بَعْضَهُمْ بِبَعْضٍ لِيَقُولُوا أَهَٰؤُلَاءِ مَنَّ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ بَيْنِنَا ۗ أَلَيْسَ اللَّهُ بِأَعْلَمَ بِالشَّاكِرِينَ)

_"Is tarah Hamne ba'az (kuchh) ki ba'az ke zariye se Azmaish (Test) ki hai taake woh unhe dekh kar kahen ke kya yehi woh log hain ke hamare darmiyan jin par Khuda ne Ehsaan kiya hai. Kya Allah Shukr guzaron ko zyada behtar nahi Jaanta?"_
(Surah An'am: 53)

📚📖 ⚔
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
*"Fitna فتنة"* ke lughvi (literal) meaning ye hai ke Sone aur Chandi ko Aag ke dabao ke niche rakhna taake khaalis aur na khaalis hissa juda ho jaye. Isliye jahan kahin dabao aur sakhti ho ye lafz istemal hota hai. Maslan Imtihaan, Mushkilat ki shiddat. Azaab ki shiddat. Ya kisi ko dhoka dekar dabao dalna, fasaad waghaira sab isi lafz se mushtaq hain. Urdu mein Fitna giri isi fasaad ke mafhoom mein ata hai.
(Tafseer Namoona)
🏅🥈
Hazrat Luqman:
_"Sone aur Chaandi ki aazmaish Aag mein daal kar ki jaati hai aur Momin ki aazmaish takleef ke zariye hoti hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p109)
📝
Is Ayat ma'ani pichhli Ayat se jude hain jahan kaha gaya tha ke Gharib Momin shakhs ko dhutkaro mat. Allah kisi ko Daulat de kar azmata hai to kisi ko ghurbat de kar. Daulatmand jab khairat nahi karta to ghuruba par zulm karta hai, Ghareeb agar apni ghurbat par Sabr ke bajai chori, ya qatl o gharat kare to woh bhi ek Fitna hai aur woh is exam mein fail ho jata hai. Isliye ghareeb ye shikwa nahi kar sakta ke usko daulat di, mujhe nahi di. Allah sabko maslahet ke mutabiq deta hai. Bas bande ko chahiye aur Uski Raza hasil karne ki koshish kare, kisi kiya dena woh Uske ikhtiyar mein hai.
📝
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Allah Ta'ala aazmaish mein padne waale aur Tauba karne wale Bande se mohabbat karta hai aur jo gunahon se parhez kare wo us se afzal hota hai."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p424)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Taufeeq de ham tere har Imtihan ki manzilon se kamyabi se guzar jayen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤲🏻
Imam Ali (as)
_"Aye Sahib e Karam! Aye Mere Parwardigaar!_
_Tu meri kamzori ko jaanta hai ke Duniya ki zara zara azmaish aur uski maamuli takleefein aur jo na-pasand cheezein Ahl e Duniya par guzarti rehti hain (unhe main bardaasht nahi kar sakta),_
_bawajood iske ke wo azmaish aur wo takleefein qaaimi nahi hoti, uski muddat thodi aur uski baqaa chand-roza hoti hai._
_To bhala phir mujhse Akherat ki Balaa aur usme musibaton ke wurood ki bardaasht kyun-kar ho sakegi?_
_Halaanki wahan ki muddat lambi hogi aur baaqi rehna uska daaemi (permanent) hoga aur jo usme phans jayenge unke azaab ko halka na kiya ja sakega, is liye ke wo azaab Tere Ghazab, Tere Inteqam aur Tere Ghusse ke sabab se hoga aur Tere Ghusse ko na Aasmaan bardaasht kar sakte hain, na Zameen._
_Aye mere Sardaar! To bhala meri kya haalat hogi? Halaanki main Tera ek kamzor, zaleel, haqeer, miskeen aur aajiz banda hun._
(Dua e Kumail)

               ♦ _*SALAAM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (826)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا جَاءَكَ الَّذِينَ يُؤْمِنُونَ بِآيَاتِنَا فَقُلْ سَلَامٌ عَلَيْكُمْ ۖ كَتَبَ رَبُّكُمْ عَلَىٰ نَفْسِهِ الرَّحْمَةَ ۖ أَنَّهُ مَنْ عَمِلَ مِنْكُمْ سُوءًا بِجَهَالَةٍ ثُمَّ تَابَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ وَأَصْلَحَ فَأَنَّهُ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ * وَكَذَٰلِكَ نُفَصِّلُ الْآيَاتِ وَلِتَسْتَبِينَ سَبِيلُ الْمُجْرِمِينَ*

_"Jab tumhare paas woh log ayen jo Hamari Ayaat par Imaan rakhte hain to unse kaho ke tum par Salamti ho (Salamun Alaikum). Tumhare Rab ne Apni Zaat par Rehmat ko Laazim kar diya hai. Agar tum mein se kisi ne nadani se burai ka irtekab kiya ho aur phir uske baad usne Tauba kar li ho aur apni Islaah kar li ho to Allah Bakhshne Wala, Meherban hai."_
_"Is tarah Hamne apni Nishaniyan khul kar bayan karte hain taake Mujrimon ki raah bilkul khul kar saamne aa jaye."_
(Surah An'am: 54 - 55)

📚📖 🙏🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat un Ghareeb Ahle Imaan ke mutalliq nazil hui hai jinke bare mein Mutakabberin ne kaha tha ke Aap (saww) unhe apne se door rakhen. Is Ayat ke nuzool ke baad jab bhi Ghareeb o Muflis Musalman Aap (saww) ke paas aate to Aap (saww) unhe Salam karte the aur kahte the ke Khuda ka Shukr hai Jisne meri Ummat mein se aise afraad paida kiye hain jin par Salam karne ka mujhe Hukm diya hai.
(Rivayat Imam Sadiq (as)
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus)

Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Khuda us shakhs par rahem kare jo Maut se pahle Tauba kar le. Tauba Gunahon ki Aalaish ko dho deti hai aur halakat ke kuwen mein girne bacha leti hai. Allah ne apne Nek bando ki Tauba karne ka Ailaan kiya hai aur is Ayat mein farmaya hai (6:54) aur (4:110)("Aur jo koi burai kare ya apne aap par zulm kare phir Khuda se isteghfar kare to Woh Khuda Bakhshne Wala, Meherban payega.")_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame jab bhi Duniya se uthana to Maghfoor uthana.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_*"Salaam karna Sunnat hai aur uska jawaab dena waajib hai."*_
(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p325)
🍃
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Salaam hamari millat ka tohfa aur hamari taraf se amaan (safety) ki zamaanat hai."_
(Adaab e Islami, v2, p222)
🍂
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Salaam Khuda Wande Aalam ka ek naam hai, lihaza usko apne darmiyaan buland awaaz se adaa kiya karo."_
Adaab e Islami, v2, p226
🍁
Imam Ali (as)
_"Mujrim par ehsaan kar ke uske jaraaim (apraadh) ko khatm kar do."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p44)

Note: Rivayaton mein ne Salam karne ki in lafzon mein takeed. Kisi aur alfaz se nahi.

                 ♦ _*TAUHEED*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (827)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ إِنِّي نُهِيتُ أَنْ أَعْبُدَ الَّذِينَ تَدْعُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ ۚ قُلْ لَا أَتَّبِعُ أَهْوَاءَكُمْ ۙ قَدْ ضَلَلْتُ إِذًا وَمَا أَنَا مِنَ الْمُهْتَدِينَ*

_"Aap (saww) kah den ke Khuda ke alawa jinki tum Ibaadat karte ho, mujhe unki Ibaadat se mana kiya gaya hai._
_Aap (saww) kah den ke mein tumhari khwaheshat ki pairavi nahi karunga. Agar meine aisa kiya to phir mein bhatak jaonga aur Hidayat paane walon mein nahi rahunga."_
(Surah An'am: 56)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke pahle bata chuka hain ke hamara Rasool Waḥy e Khuda par amal karta hai.
Kuffar ke muqabile ham bhi is Ayat dohrane chahiye, kiyonki yehi ek Muslim ka Aqeeda hona chahiye.
👆🏻
Hamare Rasool ka nasab hi muwahhid tha.

Imam Ali (as)
_"Wallah! Na mere Baap ne buton ki parastish (idol-worship) ki, na mere Dada Abdul Muttalib ne, na mere Jadd e buzurg Janab Hashim ne, na Abde Munaaf ne. Balke wo log Ka'abe ki jaanib rukh kar ke Namaz padhte the aur Deen e Ibrahim (as) par qayam the aur Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke Deen se mutamassik rahe."_
(Hayaat ul Quloob, v2, p67)

Bare Ilaha hame Tauheed e Khuda dayem o qayem rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤲🏻
Imam Sajjad (as)
_"Aye Ma'bood! Mujhe Rozi mein izafa, Watan mein aman aur mere Maal aur meri Aulaad ke bare mein Aankhon ki thandak ataa' farma aur Apni Ne'maton mein mujhe khusoosi hissa, Badan mein sehat o tandurusti, Badan mein tawanayi aur Deen mein salamati inaayat farma aur mujhe aise amal ki taufeeq de ke main Teri bandagi aur Tere Rasul Hazrat Muhammad (saww) ki farma-bardari mein rahun. Jab tak Tu mujhe zinda rakhe, mujhe Apne oon bandon mein qaraar de jinka hissa Tere yahan un bhalaiyun mein bahut zyada hai jo Tu ne naazil ki aur naazil karta hai, Maah e Ramzan mein, Shab e Qadr mein aur jo Tu har saal naazil karta hai; yaani wo Rehmat jise Tu phailata hai, wo aaraam jo Tu deta hai, wo sakhti jise Tu door karta hai; aur Gunah jo Tu maaf farmata hai."_
(Dua e Abu Hamza Shimali)

          ♦ _*TALAB-E-AZAAB*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (828)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ إِنِّي عَلَىٰ بَيِّنَةٍ مِنْ رَبِّي وَكَذَّبْتُمْ بِهِ ۚ مَا عِنْدِي مَا تَسْتَعْجِلُونَ بِهِ ۚ إِنِ الْحُكْمُ إِلَّا لِلَّهِ ۖ يَقُصُّ الْحَقَّ ۖ وَهُوَ خَيْرُ الْفَاصِلِينَ * قُلْ لَوْ أَنَّ عِنْدِي مَا تَسْتَعْجِلُونَ بِهِ لَقُضِيَ الْأَمْرُ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَكُمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِالظَّالِمِينَ*

_"Aap (saww) kah den ke mein apne Parwardigar ki taraf se wazeh Daleel par qaem hun aur tumne use jhutla diya hai. Mere paas woh cheez nahi hai jiske ke liye tum jaldbazi ka muzahera kar rahe ho. Faisle ka ikhtiyar saare ka saara Allah ko hasil hai. Woh Haq bayan karta hai aur Wohi behtareen Faisla Karne wala hai."_
_"Aap (saww) kah den ke agar wo cheez mere paas hoti jiski tumhe jaldi hai to mere aur tumhare darmiyan ab tak faisla ho chuka hota. Allah Zalimon ko achhi tarah se Jaanta hai."_
(Surah An'am: 57 - 58)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
"Bayyanah *بينة*"  ke lughvi (literal) meaning yeh hai ke jo do cheezon ke darmiyan is tarah judai dal de ke un mein kisi tarah se dubara ittesal aur bahami talluq na ho sake. Istelahan Roshan aur Wazeh Daleel ko kaha jata hai. Do Adil ki Gawahi ko bhi kaha jata hai. Iske maani "Mo'jezat" se liye jaate hai kiyonki isse Haq ko Batil se juda karte hain.
Paighambar e Islam bahut se Mo'jezat dikha chuke the. Baqi sab Anbiya ne bhi Mo'jezat dikhaye.
Lekin ye mutaleba ke agar Aap (saww) Haq par hain to ham par Azaab nazil karen, zaroori nahi ke usi waqt poora ho jaye, Allah mohlat deta hai.
Jaisa ke ye mutaleba in Ayaton mein aya hai: (Hud:32), (Araaf:70, 77), (Bani Israel: 96). Ye sab na-maqool taqaze the. Ek sir phire Noman bin Haris ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) se mutaleba kiya: Agar Ghadeer mein Hazrat Ali (as) ki Khilafat ka jo aap ne ailan kiya, agar ye Ailan Allah ke taraf se tha to mere upar Aasman se ek patthar aa pade. Aur aisa hi hua.
(Ma'arij: 1)
Logon ne jab Allah ki Tauheed ko nahi maana to, Rasool ki Nabuwwat se inkar kiya to bhi Allah Azaab ko taalta raha lekin Vilayat e Ali (as) karne wale par turant Azaab aa gaya ye Azaab tal nahi sakta tha.
Faisla Allah ke haath mein hai kab kis par Allah Azaab nazil kare.
⛓
Is Ayat ka ek mafhoom ye bhi hai ke Kuffar se kaha gaya ke tum jis Azaab ka mujh se mutaleba kar rahe ho aur jis liye tum jaldbazi kar rahe ho us Azaab ka nazil karna mere bas mein nahi hai. Agar mere bas mein hota to kab ka faisla ho chuka hota.
(Noorus Saqlain)
⛓
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Munafeqeen e Ummat se farmaya:
_"Tum meri jald maut ke khwahish mand ho lekin ye cheez hamare ikhtiyar mein nahi hai. Tum chahte ho ke mein Duniya se jald chala jaon taake tum mere baad mere Ahle Bait (as) par zulm kar sako."_
(Rauza e Kaafi)

Bare Ilaha hame Tere Azaab se door rakh aur ham Rehm o Karam farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⛓
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"3 Gunah aise hain jinka Azaab bahut jaldi is duniya mein mil jaata hai aur usko Akherat ke liye muakkhar (delay / vilamb) nahi kiya jaata aur wo ye hain:_
_(1) Waledain ki narazgi,_
_(2) Logon par zulm karna aur_
_(3) Ehsaan aur Ne'mat ka kufr karna."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Mufeed, p389)

            ♦ _*ILM-E-KHUDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (829)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَعِنْدَهُ مَفَاتِحُ الْغَيْبِ لَا يَعْلَمُهَا إِلَّا هُوَ ۚ وَيَعْلَمُ مَا فِي الْبَرِّ وَالْبَحْرِ ۚ وَمَا تَسْقُطُ مِنْ وَرَقَةٍ إِلَّا يَعْلَمُهَا وَلَا حَبَّةٍ فِي ظُلُمَاتِ الْأَرْضِ وَلَا رَطْبٍ وَلَا يَابِسٍ إِلَّا فِي كِتَابٍ مُبِينٍ*

_"Aur Uske paas Ghaib ki Chabiyan hain jinhe Uske alawa koi nahi Jaanta aur Darakht se jo bhi patta girta hai Khuda use Jaanta hai. Zameen ke tareek pardon mein koi dana aisa nahi jisse Woh ba Khabar na ho. Khushk o Tar (Dry & Wet) sab kuchh ek khuli Kitaab mein likha hua hai."_
(Surah An'am: 59)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Allah ke Ilm ka tazrah hai. Tamam Asraar o Ghaib ki Chabiyan Allah ke paas hain. Lekin Allah jisko chahe in mein koi bhi chaabi de sakta hai taake woh isse faiz hasil kar sake. Is tarah jab kahte hain ke Anbiya wa Ausiya Ilm e Ghaib rakhte hain, iska matlab ye nahi ke unka Ilm Allah ke barabar ho gaya, balke unke paas utna hi Ilm hai jitna Allah ne ikhtiyar diya hai aur apne Ilmi Khazane ki chaabi di hai. Misaal ke taur par Hidayat sirf Allah ke haath main hai lekin Anbiya wa Ausiya ko bhi Hidayat ka zimmah diya gaya hai.
📖
Jaisa ke Rivayaat mein hai Qur'an mein har Ayat 50 Batn yani meaning hai aur 1 Batn ke 50 Batn hain, isliye Qur'an ek lafz ke kai meaning ho sakte hain, isko wohi bata sakta hai jiske paas Ilm-e-Kitab hai. Jaise yahan Dana se murad Bachcha bataya gaya hai.
🧓🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Girne wale patte se Isqaat hone wala bachcha (Abortion) murad hai aur Dane se bachcha murad hai aur Zameen ke tareek pardon se Arhaam e Ummahat (Womb of Mothers) murad hain aur Tar se zinda rahne wala bachcha murad hai aur Khushk se jaldi mar jaane wala bachcha murad hai. In tamam baton ka ilm Kitab e Mubeen mein maujood hai."_
(Ma'anil Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain, Usoole Kaafi, Tafseer e Ayyashi, Man La Yahzarul Faqih)

Ye maloomat sirf Raasekhoona fil Ilm wale se mil sakti hai:
📚
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ka farman: "Har Khushk o Tar cheez ka Ilm Kitab e Mubeen mein maujood hai" aur Allah ye bhi farmata hai: "Aap kah den ke mere aur tumhare darmiyan bataur gawah Allah Kaafi hai aur mera gawah hai jiske paas tamam Kitab ka Ilm maujood hai. ( *و من عنده علم الكتاب*) aur isse Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) murad hain. Natija ye hai ke har khushk o tar ka Ilm Kitab mein hai aur Kitab ka Ilm Hazrat Ali (as) ke paas hai. Lehaza har khushk o tar ka Ilm bhi unke paas maujood hai."_
(Ehtejaaj e Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Taufeeq ata farma ke ham Uloome Ale Mohammad (as) se faiz hasil kar saken.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚
Imam Baqir (as)
_"Allah Ta'ala ka Ism e Aazam 73 harfo'n mein hai. Hamare Ahlebait (as) ke paas uske 72 huroof hain aur ek harf Allah Ta'ala ke paas hai jiski bina par Ilm e Gaib ko Usne Apni zaat ke liye pasand farmaya aur Apne hi paas rakha hai. Pus, har qism ki quwwat o taaqat bus Oosi ke paas hai."_
Meezan ul Hikmah, v4, p916
📚
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Jab Allah Ta'ala kisi bande ke saath Neki aur Ehsaan ka iraada karta hai to usko Deen mein Fiqh (soojh boojh) ataa karta hai (yaani Ilm e Deen aur Fiqh ataa karta hai)"_
(Amaali - Shaikh Mufeed, p263)
📚
Imam Ali (as)
_"Jiski tum Ibadat karte ho, pehle Uski Ma'arefat ko apne Dil mein bilkul raasikh (firm / dridh) kar lo taaki jiske irfaan ke baad tum Ibadat ke liye a'aza aur jawaareh (body parts) ko harkat dete ho, uska tumhen fayda haasil ho sake."_
(Adaab e Islami, v2, p217)

           ♦ _*HAMARI JAAN*_ ♦
  ♦ _*QABZA-E-QUDRAT MEIN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (830)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَهُوَ الَّذِي يَتَوَفَّاكُمْ بِاللَّيْلِ وَيَعْلَمُ مَا جَرَحْتُمْ بِالنَّهَارِ ثُمَّ يَبْعَثُكُمْ فِيهِ لِيُقْضَىٰ أَجَلٌ مُسَمًّى ۖ ثُمَّ إِلَيْهِ مَرْجِعُكُمْ ثُمَّ يُنَبِّئُكُمْ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ*

_"Woh wohi hai jo Raat ko tumhari Roohein qabz karta hai aur Din mein jo kuchh karte ho Woh use jaanta hai. Phir Woh tumhe karobar ki Duniya mein bhej deta hai taake muqarrar muddat poori ki jaye. Akhirkar Uski taraf tumko lautna hai aur phir Woh (Qayamat ke Din) tumhare Aamaal ki tumko khabar dega."_
(Surah An'am: 60)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala ye khabar de raha hai ke Woh apne bandon ko Raat ke waqt sote mein wafat deta hai aur ye "Chhoti Wafat" hoti hai. Pas Jab sote hai aur jab Maut aati hai dono mein Rooh Badan se alag hoti hai lekin roz Jaagne par phir laut aati hai, lekin Maut ke baad mein Rooh palat kar nahi aati.
Rivayaat mein manqool hai ke har Insaan ke saath ek Farishta muakkal hai, jab Insaan sota hai to woh Farishta uski Rooh ko apne haath mein le leta hai, agar Allah qabz e Rooh ka hukm deta hai to woh qabz kar leta hai warna uske jism mein lauta deta hai *أجل مسمى* se murad har shakhs ki Maut hai. Phir Qayamat ke Din use pesh kiya jayega aur hisab kitab jaza o saza jogi.
Kuchh Farishte woh hain jo Insaan ke Amal ko mehfooz rakhte hai (save) Jaisa ke is Ayat mein hai (Infitar: 10-12)
Aur jab Maut ka waqt aata hai to Farishte uski Jaan nikal lete hain. Aimma Huda (as) se manqool hai ke Malakul Maut ke bahut se madadgar Farishte (supporters) hote hain jo Jaan qabz karte hain aur jahan Khuda ka hukm hota hai woh arwah (souls) ko wahan pahunchate hain.

Bare Ilaha hame Maut dena to sukoon ki dena.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚰
Amirul Momenin Imam Ali (as)
_"Mujhe Ta'jjub hai us shakhs par jo apni Maut par ikhtiyaar nahi rakhta phir apni Aarzuon (Ambitions) ko kaise badhata hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, Vol 6)
⚰
Imam Baqir (as)
_"Momin ki nishaani ye hai ke jab uski Maut ka waqt aata hai to uske chehre ka rang jitna safed tha us se zyada safed aur raushan ho jaata hai, pehsani par paseena aane lagta hai, uski Aankhon se aansuon ki tarah rutubat bahne lagti hai; to yehi uski Rooh nikalne ki nishaani hai…"_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v1, p100)
🛌
Imam Ali (as)
_"(Zyada) sona / sleeping ek bahut bada dushman hai, jis se Umr bhi kam ho jaati hai aur zyada Sawab bhi khatm kar deta hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v8)

       *6th Jamadi ul Awwal 1439*

         ♦ _*SAREEUL HISAAB*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (831)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَهُوَ الْقَاهِرُ فَوْقَ عِبَادِهِ ۖ وَيُرْسِلُ عَلَيْكُمْ حَفَظَةً حَتَّىٰ إِذَا جَاءَ أَحَدَكُمُ الْمَوْتُ تَوَفَّتْهُ رُسُلُنَا وَهُمْ لَا يُفَرِّطُونَ * ثُمَّ رُدُّوا إِلَى اللَّهِ مَوْلَاهُمُ الْحَقِّ ۚ أَلَا لَهُ الْحُكْمُ وَهُوَ أَسْرَعُ الْحَاسِبِينَ*

_"Woh apne bandon par Mukammal Ikhtiyar rakhta  hai aur Woh tum par Nigrani Karnewale (Farishte) bhejta hai yahan tak ke jab tum mein se kisi ko Maut ka waqt aa jaata hai to Hamare bheje hue Farishte uski Jaan nikal lete hain aur Woh zarrah barabar bhi kotahi nahi karte."_
_"Phir sab ke sab apne Haqeeqi Aaqa ki taraf lautai jaate hain. Faisle ka tamam Ikhtiyar Use hi hasil hai aur Woh Hisaab lene mein Tez hai."_
(Surah An'am: 61 - 62)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat ke zel kuchh Rivayaat guzishta Ayaat ke zel mein bayan ho chuki hain. Is Ayat mein bhi same tazkara hai.
Allah har cheez par Ghalib hai aur Kaynat ki har cheez Uske Jalaal o Azmat aur Kibriyai ke saamne gardan jhukaye hue hai. Allah Nigehbaan Farishte bhejta hai. Kuchh Farishte woh hain jo Insaan ke Jism ki hifazat karte hain jaisa ke Farmane Qudrat hai: _"Har shakhs ke aage aur peechhe uske muqarrar kiye hue Nigran lage hue hain jo Allah ke Hukm se uski dekh bhal karte hain."_(Ra'ad:11)
(Noorus Saqlain)
📝
Imam Husain (as) ke ek ghulam ne Aap (as) se kaha ke jab Marwan charpai par letta to ye Ayat padhta: (6:62)
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Ji haan! Mein aur mere saathi Khuda ke Huzoor mein pesh honge to Woh hamen Jannat rawana karega aur Marwan aur uske Saathiyon ko Dozakh rawana karega."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)
📝
Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) se poochha gaya ke Allah Makhlooq ka Hisaab kaise lega jabke Woh Makhlooq ki nigahon se ojhal hoga?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Jis tarah se Woh nigahon se ojhal rah kar unhen Rizq deta hai usi tarah se ojhal rah kar bhi Hisaab karega."_
(Majmaul Bayan)
📝
Rivayaat mein hai ke _"Allah tamam Makhlooq ja Hisaab itni hi der mein le lega jitni der mein ek Bakri doohi jaati hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Riwayat mein hai 'Wallahu Sari'ul Hisaab' (Aur Allah jald (bahut teyz / swiftly) hisaab lene waala hai) (Surah Baqarah, Ayat 202) ki tafseer mein likha hai "Allah Ta'ala aa'nkh jhapakne ki deyr mein tamaam makhluqaat ka Hisaab le lega".
(Majmaul Bayaan, Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p391)

Bare Ilaha hamare Hisaab Kitab mein Teri Rahmat o Karam ke Ummidvar hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📝
Imam Ali (as)
_"Yaqeenan Aaj amal hai, Hisaab nahi; aur Kal (Qayamat ke din) Hisaab hoga, Amal nahi."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Amal)
📝
Imam Sadiq (as)
se sawal huwa ke kya Farishton ki ta'daad zyada hai ya Bani Adam ki?
Aap ne farmaya:
_"…Aasmaan mein rehne waale Farishton ki ta'daad rooy e zameen ke zarraat (sand particles) se bhi zyada hai. Aasmaan ke har goshe mein koi na koi Farishta maujood hai jo Khuda ki Tasbeeh o Taqdees kar raha hai. Zameen ke har darakht par koi na koi Farishta hai... Jitne bhi Farishte hain wo sab ke sab Ahle Bait (as) ki Wilayat ke zariye se Allah ki nazdeeki haasil karte hain aur hamare Muhibbon ke liye maghfirat talab karte hain aur hamare Dushmanon par La'anat karte hain aur Khuda se darkhwast karte hain ke Aal e Muhammad (as) ke Dushmanon par Azaab naazil kare."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p394)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                     ♦ _*DUA'*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (832)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ مَنْ يُنَجِّيكُمْ مِنْ ظُلُمَاتِ الْبَرِّ وَالْبَحْرِ تَدْعُونَهُ تَضَرُّعًا وَخُفْيَةً لَئِنْ أَنْجَانَا مِنْ هَٰذِهِ لَنَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الشَّاكِرِينَ * قُلِ اللَّهُ يُنَجِّيكُمْ مِنْهَا وَمِنْ كُلِّ كَرْبٍ ثُمَّ أَنْتُمْ تُشْرِكُونَ*

_"Aap (saww) kah den ke tumhe Khushki aur Tari (Wet & Dry) ki tareekyon (darkness) se kaun Nijaat deta hai? Aur Woh Kaun hai jisse tum gidgida kar aur chupke chupke Dua'yen mangte ho? Aur Kisse kahte ho ke agar Usne hame isse Nijaat de di to ham zaroor shukr ada karne walon mein se jayenge?"_
(Surah An'am: 63 - 64)

📚📖 🤲🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jab Insaan kisi mushkil mein phansta hai to yeh uski fitrat ka taqaza hai ke apne Palne wale ko pukarta hai bhale maane ya na maane. Ye baat har Insaan apne aap mein Wijdaan karta hai ke Nijaat ki Ummid sirf aur sirf Usi se hi lagayi ja sakti hai. Yahan tak ke Firaun bhi akele mein chhup kar Allah se Dua karte tha jabke zaheran khud Khudai ka dawa karta tha.
Is Ayat mein Allah insaan ki wo Kaifiyat bayan kar raha hai ke jab uski aas sab jagah se toot jaati hai to palat kar wapas Khuda ko hi pukarta hai. Pahle chup chap dua karta hai, phir jaise jaise uski maang ki shiddat badhti jaati hai woh cheekh cheekh kar naala wa sheva karta hai, gidgidata hai, us waqt woh poora Tazarro' (humbleness) ki haalat mein aa jaata hai. Wada karta hai ke agar meri Dua qabool ho gayi to mein Tera Shukr guzar rahunga.
Jabke Allah Insaan ki Haajat baghair maange poori kar sakta hai, lekin Allah chahta hai ke insaan Uske saamne apni majboori Zahir kare, uske andar kar Takabbur khatm ho, Aqeeda e Tauheed mein pukhtagi ho, Imaan Kaamil ho, Usi par Tawakkal kare, Woh yeh maan le ke saari mushkilon ka hal sirf Allah hi ke haath mein hai.
Saath mein ye bhi yaad rahe ke ham itne qabil nahi hain ke sirf ham apne bal boote par Allah ko manva len, yahan bhi shifarish ki zaroorat hai. Agar unka wasta de kar Dua maangi jayegi jinko Allah pasand karta hai, jo Allah ke Mehboob hain to ho sakta hai hamari Dua jald qubool ho jaye. Anbiya, Auliya aur Ahle Bait (as) se zyada Allah kisi aur ko Mehboob nahi rakhta. Tafseel ki yahan gunjaish nahi hai. Dua se mutalliq Kitabon ka study karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤲🏻
Ek martaba Rasoole Akram (saww) ka guzar aise logon se hua jo buland awaaz se Dua mangne mein masroof the.
Aap (saww) ne unse farmaya:
_"Tum kisi Bahre aur Ghaib ko to nahi pukar rahe. Tum Sunnewala aur Qareeb ko pukar rahe ho."_
🤲🏻
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Behtareen Dua wo hai jo chupke se ki jaye aur behtareen Rizq woh hai jo kifayat kare."_
(Tafseer Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Rasoole Khuda (saww)
_"Dua e Tazarro' mein apne Chehre ke saamne Sababah Ungli (Index finger) ko harkat do aur yehi Dua e khafeefa hai."_
(Usoole Kaafi)

Aaj Shabe Juma hai Dua-e-Kumail padhen aur uske tarjume par ghaur karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹
         🤲 *DUA-E-KUMAIL* 🤲
*********************************
_".....Ya Allah mein Tujhse gidgida kar, Aajezi (Tazarro'), Khuzoo' o Khusoo', girya wa zari ke saath sawal karta hun ke:_

_Tu meri khataon se chashm poshi farma (neglect),_

_Mujh par rahem farma,_

_Aur jo kuchh Tu ne meri Qismat mein likha hai us par mein raazi rahun aur Qana'at karun,_

_Aur har haalat mein tere (bando se) Tawazo' (humble) se pesh aaon,_

_Ya Allah! Mein Tere Huzoor mein us shakhs ka sa sawal karta hun jis par faqon ke kadake guzarte hon magar Teri hi bargah mein usne sakhtiyon ki haalat mein apni Haajat pesh ki ho, aur jo kuchh Tere khazane mein ho uske bare mein uski khwahish badhi hui ho."_

_*"Teri Hukoomat se bhag kar nikal jaana Na-mumkin hai."*_

         ♦ _*AZAAB KI QISMEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (833)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ هُوَ الْقَادِرُ عَلَىٰ أَنْ يَبْعَثَ عَلَيْكُمْ عَذَابًا مِنْ فَوْقِكُمْ أَوْ مِنْ تَحْتِ أَرْجُلِكُمْ أَوْ يَلْبِسَكُمْ شِيَعًا وَيُذِيقَ بَعْضَكُمْ بَأْسَ بَعْضٍ ۗ انْظُرْ كَيْفَ نُصَرِّفُ الْآيَاتِ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَفْقَهُونَ*

_"Aap (saww) kah den ke Woh is baat par Qudrat rakhta hai ke tum par upar se Azaab nazil kare ya tumhare qadmon ke neeche se Azaab bheje ya tumhe girohon mein taqseem kar de aur ek giroh ko doosre giroh ki taqat ka maza chakha de. Dekho Ham kis tarah ulat palat kar ke apni Nishaniyan bayan kar rahe hain taake woh Haqeeqat ko samajh len. "_
(Surah An'am: 65)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Upar ke Azaab se Dhuen (Smoke) aur chinghar (Roar) ka Azaab murad hai aur qadmon ke neeche ke Azaab se Zameen ka dhans jana murad hai aur girohon mein taqseem (Firqe-Sects) karne se murad hai ke logon  ke darmiyan ikhtelafat itni shiddat paida kar len ke musleh giroh (Groups with weapons) tashkeel paa jayen aur woh ek doosre ko qatl karne lag jayen aur ye teeno qism ke Azaab Ahle Qiblah par nazil ho chuke hain."_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim Qummi)
🐉
Imam Sadiq (as) wa Ibne Abbas se rivayat hai:
_"Upar ke Azaab se murad Zalim Salateen (Unjust Kings) ka Azaab murad hai aur qadmon ke neeche ka Azaab se Ghulam murad hain jin mein koi bhalai na hi."_
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)
🐲
Jab bhi kisi Insaan par Bala ya musibat aan padti hai uski do hi wajah hai ya to Azaab hai ya phir Aazmayish.
Tafseer e Kalbi mein mazkoor hai ke Nabi e Akram (saww) ne Namaz padhi aur Khuda se darkhwast ki Woh ke meri Ummat par upar aur neeche se Azaab nazil na kare aur unhe girohon mein taqseem na kare. Allah ne pahli Dua qubool ki lekin akheri nahi. Aap (saww) ne phir se darkhwast ki. Lekin jawab mein ye Ayat nazil hui:
_"Kiya logon ne ye samajh rakha hai ke unhe sirf *آمنا* (ham Imaan laye) kahne par chhod diya jaye aur unki aazmayish na hogi?"_ (Ankaboot:2)
Is Ummat mein Nabi ke baad Fitna ka barpa hona zaroori hai, taake Sadiq (sachche) aur Kaazib (Jhoote) ko juda juda kiya ja sake, kyonki Waḥy munqata ho chuki hai aur Talwar baqi hai aur Roz e Qayamat tak Nazaryat ka ikhtilaf qaem rahega.
Jaisa ke Rasoole Akram (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Jab meri Ummat mein Talwar shuru hogi to wo Qayamat tak chalti rahegi."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame har tarah ke Azaab se door rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👥
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Buri hamsaygi (paros- Neighbourhood) Insaan ko Insaan ke haathon Azaab dene ki ek shakl hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

         *9th Jamadi ul Awwal 1439*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
           ♦ _*MUNKIR-E-HAQ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (834)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَكَذَّبَ بِهِ قَوْمُكَ وَهُوَ الْحَقُّ ۚ قُلْ لَسْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ بِوَكِيلٍ * لِكُلِّ نَبَإٍ مُسْتَقَرٌّ ۚ وَسَوْفَ تَعْلَمُونَ*

_"Aur Aap (saww) ki Qaum ne is Haqeeqat ka inkaar kar diya hai haalanki Woh Haq hai. Aap (saww) kah den ke mein tumhara Nigehban nahi hun. Har khabar ke zahoor pazeer hone ka ek waqt muqarrar hai, anqareeb tumko maloom ho jayega."_
(Surah An'am: 66 - 67)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ab tak jo tazkara hua in Ayaat mein Allah ne khulasa kar diya. Pichhli Ayat mein zikr hua tha ke Allah upar neeche se jo balayen nazil karta hai chahe Azaab ho ya Test sirf isliye ke Haq ko pahchan len. Itni nishaniyan dekhane ke bawajood bhi aksariyat Haq ka inkaar karti hai. Lekin unke maanne ya na manne se Allah aur uske Rasool ko koi farq nahi padta. Rasool par ye hatman zimmedari nahi ke sab ko ba Imaan bana de. Rasool ka kaam hai khabar dena jo ke unhone pahuncha di. Jo hona hai apne waqt par hoke rahega. Inkaar karne walon ko khud bhugatna padega.

Bare Ilaha hame Haq ke Ma'arefat ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📖
Mashoor o Ma'roof hadis
Rasoole Khuda (saww)
_*"Ali (as) Haq ke saath aur Haq Ali (as) ke saath hai."*_
🍂
Imam Ali (as):
_"Momin ka chiraag hamare Haq ki maarefat hai aur badtareen andhaapan hamare fazl se aa'nkhein band kar lena hai."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)
🍁
Imam Askari (as):
_"Jis izzat-daar ne Haq ko chhora wo zaleel huwa aur jis zaleel ne Haq par amal kiya wo saheb e izzat huwa."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p233)
👉🏻
Ziyarat e Arbaeen:
_"…Pus hujjat tamaam kar di unhone (Imam Husain (as) ne) Daawat e Haq mein aur apni nasihat ko pesh kiya aur apne khoon o dil ko Teri raah mein baha diya taaki tere bandon ko jihalat aur zalalat se nikalein…"_
(Ziyarat e Arbaeen)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      *10th Jamadi ul Awwal 1439*
       *28th January 2018, Sunday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
         ♦ _*GHALAT BAITHAK*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (835)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا رَأَيْتَ الَّذِينَ يَخُوضُونَ فِي آيَاتِنَا فَأَعْرِضْ عَنْهُمْ حَتَّىٰ يَخُوضُوا فِي حَدِيثٍ غَيْرِهِ ۚ وَإِمَّا يُنْسِيَنَّكَ الشَّيْطَانُ فَلَا تَقْعُدْ بَعْدَ الذِّكْرَىٰ مَعَ الْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ * وَمَا عَلَى الَّذِينَ يَتَّقُونَ مِنْ حِسَابِهِمْ مِنْ شَيْءٍ وَلَٰكِنْ ذِكْرَىٰ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَتَّقُونَ*

_"Aur jab un logon ko dekho jo hamari Ayaat par nukta chiniya (criticise) kar rahe hain to unse doori ikhtiyar kar lo yahan tak ke woh is guftgu ko chhod kar doosri baaton mein lag jayen aur agar Shaitan tumhe ye baat faramosh kara de to phir yaad aane ke baad Zalim logon ke saath mat baithen.  Nuqta chini karne walon ka hisaab Ahle Taqwa ke zimme bilkul nahi hai lekin unhe nasihat karte rahna chahiye taake woh ghalat ravish se baaz aa jayen."_
(Surah An'am: 68 - 69)


----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
📚📖 🙇 👥
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
"Teen tarah ki Mahafil Allah ko na-pasand hain aur Khuda un par Azaab bhejta hai. Tum in Majalis mein shirkat na karo aur unke saath nashist o barkhast (meeting) na rakho."
"(1) Wo Majlis jis mein Jhoote Fatwe jaari hote hain.
(2) Wo Majlis jis mein hamara boseeda aur hamare Dushmanon ka zikr tar o taaza ho.
(3) Wo Majlis jahan hamari itteba' se roka jaata ho aur tumhe maloom ho."
Phir Aap (as) ne Ayaten padhen:
"(1) Ayat (6:108) (2) Ayat (6:68) (3) Ayat (Nahl: 116)"
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
👤👥
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jahan 3 Munkire Haq jama hote hain to wahan 3 Shayateen unki Mahfil mein sharik ho jaate hain. Jab woh guftgu karte karte hain to Shayateen bhi un jaisi guftgu karte hain aur jab woh hanste hain to Shayateen bhi unke saath hanste hain aur jab woh Khuda ke doston se shikwa karte hain to Shayateen bhi unke saath milkar dostan e Khuda ka shikwa karte hain.  Jo koi Momin is Mahfil mein baitha ho to use us waqt wo Mahfil chhod deni chahiye aur use Shayateen ka ham nashin nahi banna chahiye, kyonki jab Allah ka Ghazab ya Uski Laa'nat nazil hui to unhe koi bhi nahi bacha sakega."_
_"Jo aisa na kar sakta ho to apne Dil mein unse Nafrat kare aur us Mahfil se khada ho jaye, agarche Bakri doone ke waqt ke barabar ya Oontni ke doone ke barabar hi kyon na khada hona pade."_
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Kaano par Wajib kiya hai ke jin baton ko sunna Haraam hai wo unse parhez karen aur aisi baton ko tawajjo se na sunen jin ke sunne par Allah naraaz hota hai jaisa ke Irshaade Khuda wandi hai (6:68)"_
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
👥
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Khuda ki Zaat aur Qur'an Majeed ke andar jhagadna aur bahes ho to aisi Majlison se kinara kashi ikhtiyar kar lo."_
_"Jis Mahfil mein Qasas par nukta chini ho rahi ho to us Mahfil se uth kar chale jao."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)
👥
Imam Zainul Abidin (as):
_"Insaan ko ye ikhtiyar nahi ke woh jis ke saath chahe baith jaye. (6:68)"_

Bare Ilaha hamari Aulaad ko ghalat sohbat o sangat se mehfooz rakh.

(To be cont'd........ )
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      *11th Jamadi ul Awwal 1439*
       *29th January 2018, Monday,*

          ♦ _*GHALAT SOHBAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (835) (Continued..)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا رَأَيْتَ الَّذِينَ يَخُوضُونَ فِي آيَاتِنَا فَأَعْرِضْ عَنْهُمْ حَتَّىٰ يَخُوضُوا فِي حَدِيثٍ غَيْرِهِ ۚ وَإِمَّا يُنْسِيَنَّكَ الشَّيْطَانُ فَلَا تَقْعُدْ بَعْدَ الذِّكْرَىٰ مَعَ الْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ * وَمَا عَلَى الَّذِينَ يَتَّقُونَ مِنْ حِسَابِهِمْ مِنْ شَيْءٍ وَلَٰكِنْ ذِكْرَىٰ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَتَّقُونَ*

_"Aur jab un logon ko dekho jo hamari Ayaat par nukta chiniya (criticise) kar rahe hain to unse doori ikhtiyar kar lo yahan tak ke woh is guftgu ko chhod kar doosri baaton mein lag jayen aur agar Shaitan tumhe ye baat faramosh kara de to phir yaad aane ke baad Zalim logon ke saath mat baithen.  Nuqta chini karne walon ka hisaab Ahle Taqwa ke zimme bilkul nahi hai lekin unhe nasihat karte rahna chahiye taake woh ghalat ravish se baaz aa jayen."_
(Surah An'am: 68 - 69)

----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
📚📖 🙇 👥
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Moosa Kazim (as) ne Jafari (Raavi) se poochha ke tum ko Abdul Rahman bin Yaqoob ke paas baitha hua dekha tha?
Jafari ne kaha wo to mera Mamu hai.
Imam (as):
"Woh Khuda ke mutalliq ghalat baten karta hai, aur Use un sifat se muttasif karta hai jinse woh Munazzah hai lehaza tum uske saath uthna baithna chhod do."
Jafari: "Agar woh ghalat nazaryat ka parchar karta hai to usse mera kiya bighadta hai. Mein to uske Aqaed ko tasleem nahi karta."
Imam (as):
_"Kya tujhe ye khauf nahi hai ke us par Khuda ka Azaab nazil ho to tum bhi uski lapet mein aa jaoge?"_
(Noorus Saqlain)
👥
Imam Baqir (as) ne Muslim (Raavi) ko Qazi ke paas baithne par aitraaz kiya to usne kaha:
"Ye Qazi mera ehtram karta hai, isliye kabhi kabhi mein uske paas jakar baith jaata hun."
Imam (as):
_"Tumhare paas is baat ki kya zamanat hai ke us par Laanat nazil ho aur tum bhi uski lapet mein na aa jao."_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)
👥
Hazrat Esa (as) se logon ne puchha, "Ya Ruhullah (as)! Humein kin logon ki sohbat mein baithna chahiye?" To Aap (as) ne farmaya, _"Unki sohbat mein jinko dekh kar tumhen Khuda ki yaad aaye aur jinka kirdaar tumhen Akherat ki taraf raghib kar sake"._
(Dosti, p33)
👥
Imam Mohd Taqi (as) & Imam Ali (as):
_"Bure logon ki sohbat Nek logon ke mutalliq badgumaniya paida karti hain."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza (as), Noorus Saqlain)
👥
Imam Kazim (as):
_"Aalim ki sohbat mein koode (garbage) par baithna, jaahil ki sohbat mein aala darje ke farsh (top quality carpet) par baithne se behtar hai."_
(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p337)
👥
Imam Husain (as)
_"Ahl e fisq o fujoor (khullam khulla gunah karne walo’n) ki sohbat badnaami ki baat hai."_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v78, Aqwaal 14 Masumeen (as), p93)
👥
Imam Ali (as):
_"Ghatiya logon ki sohbat se bacho. Ghatiya log wo hain jinhe Allah ka khauf nahi hai aur un mein Ambiya (as) ke qaatil bhi hain aur un mein hamare dushman bhi hain."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p631)

Bare Ilaha hamari Aulaad ko ghalat sohbat o sangat se mehfooz rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

           ♦ _*DEEN KA MAZAAQ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (836)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَذَرِ الَّذِينَ اتَّخَذُوا دِينَهُمْ لَعِبًا وَلَهْوًا وَغَرَّتْهُمُ الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا ۚ وَذَكِّرْ بِهِ أَنْ تُبْسَلَ نَفْسٌ بِمَا كَسَبَتْ لَيْسَ لَهَا مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ وَلِيٌّ وَلَا شَفِيعٌ وَإِنْ تَعْدِلْ كُلَّ عَدْلٍ لَا يُؤْخَذْ مِنْهَا ۗ أُولَٰئِكَ الَّذِينَ أُبْسِلُوا بِمَا كَسَبُوا ۖ لَهُمْ شَرَابٌ مِنْ حَمِيمٍ وَعَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ بِمَا كَانُوا يَكْفُرُونَ*

_"Aur logon ne apne Deen ko khel bana liya hai Aap (saww) unhe chhod den. Un logon ko Dunyavi Zindagi ne dhoke mein dal diya hai. Haan ye Qur'an padhkar nasihat o tanbeeh karte raho ke kahin koi shakhs apne Aamaal ki shamat mein mubtila na ho jaye jabke Allah ke alawa koi Madadgar aur Shafa'at karne wala na hoga aur agar wahan koi mukammal Fidya de kar bhi chhootna chahega to bhi wo Fidya qubool na kiya jayega. Ye woh log hain jo apni kamai ki wajah se musibat mein giraftar honge aur unke Kufr ki wajah se unhe peene ke liye khaulta hua Paani milega aur unke liye Dardnaak Azaab hoga."_
(Surah An'am: 70)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat un logon ke liye hai jo Deen ko koi ahmiyat nahi dete. Yazeed ne apne darbar mein khullam khulla Ailan kiya ke Deen e Islam to Bani Hashim ka ek khel tha, na koi Waḥy nazil hui na koi Kitab. Lekin Ahle Bait (as) ne Sabr kiya aur uska zulm sahte rahe lekin Tableegh e Deen phir bhi karte rahe.
Hazrat Ali (as) wa Fatema Zehra (sa) dekhte rahe aur Sabr karte rahe, unke saamne Deen ko badla jaa raha tha, Deen ke saath khel khela jaa raha tha. Koi Halaal ko Haraam kar raha tha ya Halaal ko Haraam kar raha tha. Koi sharaab ke nashe mein Imam e Jamat ke faraez anjaam de raha tha. Ka'abe par aag barsai gayi, Rasool ki beti ka ghar jalaya gaya. Zulm jo Saqeefa se shuru hua tha uski inteha Karbala mein hui. Pas Yazeed ka ye qaul in sab ka nichod tha, yani Islam us waqt mit gaya hota agar Ahle Haram (as) ne isko bachaya na hota.

Ayat ka ye mafhoom nahi ke Kuffar se Jihad na karo, chhod do. Islam mein Defence (Difa) hai attack nahi. Isliye agar koi nahi maan raha hai na maane woh khud bhugtenga. Allah ne is ayat mein bata diya uska kiya hashr hoga.
Khuda ke yahan koi Rishwat nahi chalegi ke chalo khuchh de kar Azaab ko talwa diya jaye. Islam ne Tauba ka darwaza khula rakha hai, Rishwat nahi. Lekin Mohd wa Ale Mohammad (as) kisi ki Shifaarish kar den to qubool ho sakti hai lekin woh aise ki Shifaarish karenge nahi. Kyonki Ale Rasool (as) ko khush karna Allah ko kush karna hai. Ale Rasool (as) kabhi Zaalim se khush nahi rah sakte.
(Maidah: 57), (Araaf:51) mein bhi isi tarah ka zikr hai.

Bare Ilaha hame zalimon ke shar mehfooz rakh aur Dushmenan e Islam par Allah ki La'anat ho.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😏
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jo shakhs Khuda ke Deen ko khel tamasha banayega, Khuda Wande Aalam usay hamesha ke liye Jahannum mein daal dega."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p731)
🙂
Imam Ali (as):
_"Apni umr ko khel-tamasho'n mein na ga'nwa do warna duniya se khaali haath jaaoge."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v8, p854)

                ♦ _*TAUHEED*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (837)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ أَنَدْعُو مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ مَا لَا يَنْفَعُنَا وَلَا يَضُرُّنَا وَنُرَدُّ عَلَىٰ أَعْقَابِنَا بَعْدَ إِذْ هَدَانَا اللَّهُ كَالَّذِي اسْتَهْوَتْهُ الشَّيَاطِينُ فِي الْأَرْضِ حَيْرَانَ لَهُ أَصْحَابٌ يَدْعُونَهُ إِلَى الْهُدَى ائْتِنَا ۗ قُلْ إِنَّ هُدَى اللَّهِ هُوَ الْهُدَىٰ ۖ وَأُمِرْنَا لِنُسْلِمَ لِرَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ*

_"Aap kah den kya ham Allah ko chhod kar unko pukaren jo hamen na to nafa' de sakte hain na hamen nuqsan de sakte hain? Aur jab Allah ne hamen Hidayat kar di hai to kiya iske baad ham ham ulte paon phir jayen aur kya ham us shakhs ki tarah se ban jayen jise Shayateen ne sehraon mein bhatka diya ho aur woh hairan o sargardan phir raha ho. Jabke uske saathi use pukaar rahe hon ke "Idhar aa" ye seedhi raah maujood hai? Aap kah den ke Allah ki Hidayat hi Haqeeqi Hidayat hai aur hamen ye Hukm mila hai ke ham tamam Jahanon ke Parwardigar ke saamne sar tasleem kham kar den."_
(Surah An'am: 71)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Kuffaron se sawal kiya gaya hai aur hamara Deen mustahkam hai. Ham jis Daata ko maante hain Wohi hame sab kuchh de sakta hai, Usko chhod kar kyon aise ke paas jayen jisse hame kuchh nahi mil sakta. Isliye ham apne Khuda ke saamne sar tasleem karte hain, ham Musalman hain.

Bare Ilaha hame jab bhi is Duniya se uthana Musalman uthana.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Imam Ali (as):
_"Nek Amal jaisi koi Tijaarat (business) nahi aur Sawaab jaisa koi Munafa (Profit) nahi."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p771)
🕌
Hazrat Luqman:
_" Apni duniya ko Akherat ke liye bech de taaki duniya o Akherat dono mein tu faayda paaye aur Akherat ko duniya ke liye mat bech warna dono jagah nuqsaan hoga."_
(Hayatul Quloob, v1)

                 ♦ _*NAMAZ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (838)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَأَنْ أَقِيمُوا الصَّلَاةَ وَاتَّقُوهُ ۚ وَهُوَ الَّذِي إِلَيْهِ تُحْشَرُونَ*

_"Aur ye ke Namaz qaem karo aur Uska Taqwa ikhtiyar karo aur Wohi to hai Jiski taraf tum mehshoor kiye jaoge."_
(Surah An'am: 72)
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
📚📖 🕌 🙇
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah Ta'ala hukm de raha Namaz qaem karo. Namaz har Musalman par Wajib hai aur iska tark karnewale ke liye sakh Azaab hai aur Jahannam ke sab sa badtareen nichli jagah *سقر* Saqar hai.
🕌
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
*«الصلاة عمود الدين إن قبلت قبل ما سواها وإن ردّت ردّ ما سواها».*
_"Namaz Deen ka Sutoon (Pillar) hai, agar ye qubool ho gayi to sab qubool aur ye radd to sab radd."_
🕌
Sirf Namaz wajib hi nahi balke Allah unko kos raha hai jo Namaz ko halka samajhte hain.

*فَوَيْلٌ لِلْمُصَلِّينَ * الَّذِينَ هُمْ عَنْ صَلَاتِهِمْ سَاهُونَ * الَّذِينَ هُمْ يُرَاءُونَ*

_"Wail ho un Namaziyon par  jo apni Namaz se ghaflat baratte hain, Riyakari karte hai..."_
(Surah Ma'un: 4 - 7)
🕌
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
*«ليس منّي من استخفّ بصلاته».* (بحار الانوار 79/136)
_"Jo Namaz ko halka samjhe woh ham mein se nahi hai."_
🕌
Aisa sochna bhi ghalat ke ham to Ahle Bait (as) ke chahne wale hain woh hamari Shafa'at kar denge.
🕌
Imam Sadiq (as) farmate hain:
 *«إنّ شفاعتنا لا تنال مستخفاَ بالصّلاة».* (بحار الأنوار 47/2)

_"Hamari Shafa'at us tak nahi pahunch sakti jo Namaz ko halka samjhe."_
🕌
_*Rivayaat:*_
Janabe Fatema Zahra(s.a): _"Khuda wand-e-aalam ne Namaz ko tumhare liye takabbur se doori karar diya hai."_
(Ayan-us-Shia, V-1, pg-316)
🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Namaz ko mere liye Aankhon ki thandak qaraar diya hai aur Namaz ki mohabbat mere dil mein is tarah rakhi hai jis tarah bhooke ko khaane se aur pyaase ko paani se mohabbat hoti hai, lekin bhooka khaana khaane ke baad aur pyaasa paani peene ke baad seyr o sairaab (contented) ho jaata hai lekin main Namaz se hargiz seyr nahi hota."_
(Adaab e Islami, v2, p225)
🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Har Namaz ke waqt ek Farishta logo'n ko awaaz deta hai ke "Uthho aur wo Aag jo tumhare liye raushan ki gayi hai usay apni Namazo'n se bujhaao"._
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq , p461)
🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Ek shakhs ki Jamaat mein padhi huwi ek rakaat Namaz, uski uske ghar mein padhi huwi 40 saal ki Namaz se afzal hai."_
(Wasaail, v5, p374)

Bare Ilaha hame hamesha Namaziyon mein shamil rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

         ♦ _*SOOR (TRUMPETS)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (839)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَهُوَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ بِالْحَقِّ ۖ وَيَوْمَ يَقُولُ كُنْ فَيَكُونُ ۚ قَوْلُهُ الْحَقُّ ۚ وَلَهُ الْمُلْكُ يَوْمَ يُنْفَخُ فِي الصُّورِ ۚ عَالِمُ الْغَيْبِ وَالشَّهَادَةِ ۚ وَهُوَ الْحَكِيمُ الْخَبِيرُ*

_"Aur Usi ne hi Aasman aur Zameen ko Haq ke saath paida kiya aur jis Din Woh kahega ke Qayamat bapa ho ja to bapa ho jayegi. Uska farman Haq hai aur jis Din Soor phoonka jayega usi Din Usi ki Badshahi hogi. Woh Ghaib o Hazir ka Jannewala hai. Woh Sahibe Hikmat aur Bakhabar hai."_
(Surah An'am: 73)

📚📖 🗣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Majmaul Bayan mein marqoom hai ke lafz "Soor *صور*" ke mutalliq ek qaul ye hai ke woh ek nafeel qism ki cheez hogi jise Israfeel pahli bar phoonkenge to tamam Duniya ka khatma ho jayega aur jab woh doosri bar phoonkenge to poori Duniya dubara zinda ho jayegi. Kyonki " *صور*" Jama (Plural) ka Seegha hai (Singular: *صورة*)
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Sahibe Soor ne is waqt Soor ko apne munh mein le liya hai aur is ka waqt qareeb aa chuka hai aur Usne Hukme Khuda Wandi ko sunne ke liye apne kaan jhuka liye hain ke Hukm ho to Soor phoonke."_
Sahaba ne poochha to ham kya kahna chahiye?
Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Tum kaho:_
" *حَسْبُنَا اللَّهُ وَنِعْمَ الْوَكِيل*"
(Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame uthana to ba Imaan uthana.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🗣
Imam Reza (as):
_"H. Khizr (as) ne Aab e Hayaat piya hai, wo Soor phoonke jaane ke waqt tak zinda rahenge. Wo hamare paas aate hain aur Salaam karte hain. Hum unki awaaz sunte hain magar unko dekhte nahi. Jis jagah unka zikr kiya jaata hai wo wahaa'n maujood hote hain. Pus, jo bhi unka zikr kare to unpar Salaam bheje. Wo Hajj ke mauqe par Makkah mein aate hain, Hajj karte hain aur Arafat mein khade hote hain aur Momino'n ki Dua par Aameen kehte hain. Jald hi Allah Ta'ala H. Khizr (as) ko Qaim e Aal e Muhammad (atfs) ka moonis qaraar dega. Jab wo logon ki nazron se poshida honge to oos tanhaai mein H. Khizr (as) unke rafeeq honge."_
(Falsafa e Ghaibat e Mahdi (atfs) , p148)
🗣
Riwayat:
_"Namaz e Wehshat e Qabr ke padhne ke fauran baad Khuda usi lamhe 1000 Farishton ko ek poshaak aur ek hulla libaas ke 2 kapde jo poore badan ko dhhanp dete hain, ke saath Mayyat ki Qabr ki taraf rawana farma deta hai, aur uski Qabr ki tangi ko Soor phoonkne ke din tack kushaada (spacious) karta rahega. Khud Namaz padhne waale ko is qadar Nekiyaan ataa karta hai jitni cheezon par Suraj ki raushani padti hai, aur uske 40 darje buland kiye jaate hain."_
(Kirdaar Saazi, v2, p17)

♦ _*WAALID HAZRAT IBRAHIM (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (840)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذْ قَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ لِأَبِيهِ آزَرَ أَتَتَّخِذُ أَصْنَامًا آلِهَةً ۖ إِنِّي أَرَاكَ وَقَوْمَكَ فِي ضَلَالٍ مُبِينٍ*

_"Aur jab Ibrahim (as) ne apne Baap (Chacha) Aazar se kaha kya tu Buton ko Khuda banata hai? Mein tujhe aur teri Qaum ko khuli gumrahi mein dekh raha hun."_
(Surah An'am: 74)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Aazar ko Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ka Ab *اب* se mukhatib kiya hai. Aam Musalman Aazar ko Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ka Baap samajhte hain, jabke aisa nahi hai. Ale Muhammad (as) ki Rivayaat ke mutabiq Aazar unke Murabbi *مربى* (palnewale) the aur rishte mein unke chacha the.
Lafz *اب* (Ab) kaseer maana mein istemal hota hai. Arab mein ye lafz Baap, Chacha aur Dada ke maani mein istemal hota hai.
Jaisa ke ye Ayat (2:133) mein hai "....ham aapke Ma'bood aur Aapke Aaba' Ibrahim, Ismael aur Ishaq ke Ma'bood e Wahid ki Ibaadat karenge...." Is Ayat mein Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke beton ne Hazrat Ibrahim (as) aur digar ko apne walid Yaqoob ka "Ab" kaha. Jabke Ibrahim (as) Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke Dada the, Hazrat Ismail (as) unke chacha the aur Hazrat Ishaq ke sage Walid the.
Arabic mein asli Walid ko " *والد*" kahte hain. Ham dekhte hain ke Hazrat Ibrahim (as) is Ayat (Ibrahim:114) mein Aazar ke liye Dua-e-Maghferat ke liye bezaari ikhtiyar kar rahe hain aur Ayat (Ibrahim:41) mein apne Waledain ke liye Dua kar rahe hain, yahan lafz *لوالدي* istemal hua hai. Jabke Ibrahim (as) ke asli Baap ka naam "Tarakh *تارخ* tha jo Tauheed ke manne wale the.
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

Ye baat Rivayaat se musallam hai ke hamare tamam Anbiya ke nasl (yani maa baap) sab Muwahhid  *مواحد* the (Tauheed par Eteqaad rakhnewale) jaisa ke Nabi e Kareem (saww) ne farmaya:

*لم يزل ينقلنى الله من اصلاب الطاهرين إلى أرحام المطهرات حتى أخرجنى  فى عالمكم هذا.*

_"Allah Ta'ala ne mujhe Pakeezah Aslaab *اصلاب* se, Pakeezah Arhaam *أرحام* mein muntaqil karta raha yahan tak ke mujhe tumhare is Jahan mein muntaqil kiya."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hamare Waledain ki Maghfirat farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👥
Imam Sadiq (as) se ek shakhs ne puchha ke,
_"Janabe Musa (as) jaadugaro'n ke muqable mein ghabra gaye the, jab ke Janabe Ibrahim (as) to Aag se bhi na ghabraaye?"_ Imam (as) ne jawaab diya:
_"Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke sulb mein Muhammad (saww) aur Aal e Muhammad (as) ke anwaar the"._
(Tafseer e Anwaar e Najaf, v15, p14)
👥
Imam Ali (as):
_"Wallah! Na mere Baap ne Buton ki parastish (idol-worship) ki, na mere Dada Abdul Muttalib ne, na mere jadd e buzurg Janabe Hashim ne, na Abde Munaaf ne. Balke wo log Ka'abe ki jaanib rukh kar ke Namaz padhte the aur Deen e Ibrahim (as) par qayam the aur Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke Deen se mutamassik rahe."_
(Hayaat ul Quloob, v2, p67)

♦ _*DALEEL E WUJOOD E KHUDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (841)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَكَذَٰلِكَ نُرِي إِبْرَاهِيمَ مَلَكُوتَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَلِيَكُونَ مِنَ الْمُوقِنِينَ*

_"Aur is tarah se Hamne Ibrahim (as) ko Aasmanon aur Zameen ka Nizam e Saltanat dikhate the taake woh Yaqeen karnewalon mein se ho jayen."_
(Surah An'am: 75)

----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
"Jab Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke liye Zameen ke hijaab uthaye gaye to Aap (as) ne dekha Zan on Mard Zinah mein masroof the. Aap (as) ne bad Dua ki to woh dono mar gaye. Phir Aap (as) ne ek jode ko na mashroo' fe'l mein maloos paya to Aap (as) ne bad Dua ki to woh joda bhi mar gaya. Phir Aap (as) ne teesre jode ko dekha aur badkari dekh kar bad Dua ki......"
"Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ko Waḥy ki: "Aye Ibrahim! Teri Bad Dua qubool hai lekin mere bandon par Bad Dua na karna. Agar Mein chahta to sire se unhe paida hi na karta. Meine Makhlooq ki teen qismen paida ki hai:"
"(1) Jo Meri Ibaadat karti hai aur jo Mere saath kisi ko sharik qarar nahi deti.
(2) Jo Mere alawa doosron ki pooja karti hai woh Mere haath se nikalne wale nahi hain.
(3) Jo  Mere ghair ki Ibaadat karti hai. Mein unke sulb se aise log paida karunga jo Meri Ibaadat karne wale honge."
(Roza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
☁🌥
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Allah ne Arsh ko chaar Anwaar se paida kiya. Surkh (Red) Noor ko uske juz banaya aur surkh cheezon ko usi surkh Noor ki wajah se surkhi naseeb hui. Sabz (Green) Noor ko uska juz banaya. Sabz cheezon ko sabzi (greenery) is sabz noor ki wajah se mili. ...(Isi tarah zard (Yellow), safed (White). Safed cheezon ko isi Safed Noor se Safedi mili hai. Aur woh Ilm hai jo Allah ne Hameleen Arsh ko taleem farmayi aur iska talluq Uske Noor se tha. Chunanche Uski Azmat o Noor ki wajah se Ahle Imaan ke dilon ko baseerat ata hui aur Uski Azmat o Noor ki wajah se Jahilon ne Us se Dushmani ki aur Uski Azmat o Noor ki wajah se Zameen o Aasman ki tamam Makhlooq ne mukhtalif Aamaal ko wasila  bana kar Uski Raza ko dhoondne ki koshish ki. Kaynat ki tamam Ashiya ko Allah ne apne Noor o Azmat se utha rakha hai aur Woh apne liye kisi Nafa o Nuqsan , Maut o Hayaat aur dubara uthne ki taqat nahi rakhte. Har cheez Qudrat e Khuda se uthi hai aur Khuda har cheez ko uske markazi Nuqte se hatne nahi deta aur har cheez se unka ahata kiye hue hai. Woh har cheez ki Hayaat hai aur har cheez ka Noor hai. Allah un ausaaf se kahi Buland o Bartar hai jo log uske mutalliq bayan karte hain. Arsh ke Haamil woh Ulama hain jinhe Khuda ne apna Ilm ata kiya hai aur Allah ne apni Saltanat mein jo kuchh bhi paida kiya hai woh chaar se bahar nahi aur usi Badshahat ka Mushaheda Allah ne apne Asfiya ko karaya aur apne Khaleel ko bhi Mushaheda karaya aur Ayat (6:75) ka yehi mafhoom hai. Haamelin e Harsh Allah ko bhala kaise utha sakte hain jabke Usi ki ata kardah Hayaat se unke dilon ko zindagi mili hai aur Uske Noor ke Faizan se unhe Uski Ma'arefat ki hidayat naseeb hui hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha Teri Azmat o Jalal ka wasta hame Duniya wa Akhirat mein Kamyabi ata farma.

            ♦ _*MUSHAHEDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (842) (Continued....)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَكَذَٰلِكَ نُرِي إِبْرَاهِيمَ مَلَكُوتَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَلِيَكُونَ مِنَ الْمُوقِنِينَ*

_"Aur is tarah se Hamne Ibrahim (as) ko Aasmanon aur Zameen ka Nizam e Saltanat dikhate the taake woh Yaqeen karnewalon mein se ho jayen."_
(Surah An'am: 75)

📚📖 🌏☁
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke liye Aasmanon ke Hijabaat hata diye gaye the aur unke liye Zameen ke Hijabaat bhi utha diye gaye the. Unhone poori Zameen ka Mushaheda kiya aur jo kuchh Zameen ke neeche aur hawa ke upar hai unhone un sab cheezon ka Mushaheda kiya. Muhammad Mustafa (saww) ko bhi isi tarah ka Mushaheda karaya gaya tha aur tumhare saathi (means mujhe) aur iske baad Aimma (as) ko bhi is tarah ka Mushaheda karaya gaya. "_
(Al Kharaij wal Jaraih, Noorus Saqlain)
🌥🎠
Hazrat Imam Zainul Abedin (as) se poochha gaya: "Kya Allah ke liye Makan muqarrar kiya ja sakta hai?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Allah isse Buland o Bala hai."_
Sael: "To phir Allah ne apne Habib ko Me'raj kyon karai thi?"
Aap (as) farmaya:
_"Allah ne isliye Me'raj karai ke Woh chahta tha ke unka banda Aasmanon ki Badshahat aur Khuda ki San'at ke ajaeb aur uski takhleeq ki raf'aton ko dekh sake."_
Sael: Ayat (Najm: 8-9) ka kya matlab hai?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Rasoole Khuda (saww) Noor ke Hijabaat ke qareeb gaye phir jhuk kar Zameen ki Badshahat ki taraf dekha to Aapko yun laga jaise do Kamano ya isse bhi kuchh kam fasla ho."_
(Kitab Ilalush Sharay)

Bare Ilaha hame Aamaal ko Me'raj ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍲🍪
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Jo shakhs 3 Musalmanon ko khana khilaye to Allah Ta'ala Aasmaano ki Badshahat mein qaem 3 Jannaton ka Ta'am (khana) khilayega. Khuda use Firdaus, Tooba aur Jannat e Adn ke us darakht ke meve khilayega jise hamare Rab ne apne haath (Qudrat) se Jannat e Adn mein kasht kiya hai."_
👉🏻
_"Sabr karne wale Masakeen ke liye khush khabri ho. Yehi log Aasmaano aur Zameen ki Badshahat ka Mushaheda karenge."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

♦ _*DALEEL E WUJOOD E KHUDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (843)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَلَمَّا جَنَّ عَلَيْهِ اللَّيْلُ رَأَىٰ كَوْكَبًا ۖ قَالَ هَٰذَا رَبِّي ۖ فَلَمَّا أَفَلَ قَالَ لَا أُحِبُّ الْآفِلِينَ * فَلَمَّا رَأَى الْقَمَرَ بَازِغًا قَالَ هَٰذَا رَبِّي ۖ فَلَمَّا أَفَلَ قَالَ لَئِنْ لَمْ يَهْدِنِي رَبِّي لَأَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْقَوْمِ الضَّالِّينَ * فَلَمَّا رَأَى الشَّمْسَ بَازِغَةً قَالَ هَٰذَا رَبِّي هَٰذَا أَكْبَرُ ۖ فَلَمَّا أَفَلَتْ قَالَ يَا قَوْمِ إِنِّي بَرِيءٌ مِمَّا تُشْرِكُونَ*

_"Chunanche jab us par Raat chhayi to usne ek Taara dekha. Kaha: 'Ye mera Rab hai?' Jab wo doob gaya to kaha: 'Mein doob jane walon se muhabbat nahi rakhta.' Phir jab usne Chaand ko chamakte hue dekha to kaha: 'Ye mera Rab hai?' Jab Chaand doob gaya  to kaha: 'Agar mera Rab ne mujhe hidayat na ki hoti to mein gumrah logon mein shamil ho jaata.' Phir usne Suraj ko chamakte hue dekha to kaha: 'Ye mera Rab hai? Ye bada hai.' Jab Suraj doob gaya to kaha ke meri Qaum! mein is sab se bezaar hun jinhen tum Khuda ka sharik thairate ho. "_
(Surah An'am: 76 - 78)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Khalifa Mamoon ke Darbar mein debates hote rahte the. Mamoon ne Imam Reza (as) se sawal kiya ke "Aap Anbiya (as) ko Masoom maante hain to is Ayat (6:76) ka kya maqsad hai."
Imam (as) ne jawab mein farmaya:
"Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne jis daur mein Aankh kholi thi to us waqt 3 qism ke log wahan maujood the:
(1) Zohra Sitare ki Ibaadat karne wale.
(2) Chaand ki pooja karne wale.
(3) Suraj ki pooja karne wale.
Jab Aap (as) ghar se bahar aye aur logon ke 3 giroh dekhe aur jab Raat chhayi to Aap (as) ne Sitara Parast (Star Worshiper) se kaha ke 'ye mera Rab hai? ' Aap (as) ka ye farman unki taeed ke bajae inkaar par mabni tha. Jab Taara doob gaya to farmaya 'Mein doob jane walon se muhabbat nahi karta kyonki doob jana Haadis (Created) ki sifat hai, Qadeem (Everlasting) ki sifat nahi hai. Phir Aap (as) ne Chaand dekha to Chaad Paraston (Moon Worshipers, Chandrama poojari) ko khitab kar ke farmaya kya ye mera Rab hai? Jab Chaand doob gaya to farmaya: 'Agar mere Rab ne meri Rehnumayi na ki hoti to mein gumrah logon mein ho jaata. Jab Subah hui aur Suraj nikla to farmaya kya ye mera Rab hai, ye to Zohra aur Chaand se bada hai? Phir Zohra, Chaad Paraston (Moon Worshipers, Chandrama poojari), Suraj Paraston (Sun Worshipers, Surya Poojari) ke teeno giroh ko khitab kar ke farmaya: 'Meri Qaum! Mein inse bezaar hun jinhen tum sharik thairate ho. Meine yaksoo ho kar apna chehra Us Zaat ki taraf kar liya Jisne Aasmano aur Zameen ko paida kiya aur mein Sharik karne walon mein se nahi hun."
Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne teeno jumlon se teenon ka ibtaal (negation) kiya tha..... Ye Daleel o Hujjat unki zaati paida karda nahi thi balke Khuda ki taraf se Ilaam ( *الهام*) kardah thi. Isliye Allah ne farmaya: Ayat (6:83)"
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke saath Mab'oos farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Jo koi ek Din aur Raat Bimaar rahe aur ayadat karne waalon se apni bimari ki takleef ki shikayat na kare to Allah Ta'ala usko Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke saath mab'oos karega taaki wo Pul e Siraat se unke pichhe Bijli ki tarah guzar jaaye."_
(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p444)
