         ♦ _*DALEEL E FITRAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (844)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنِّي وَجَّهْتُ وَجْهِيَ لِلَّذِي فَطَرَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ حَنِيفًا ۖ وَمَا أَنَا مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ * وَحَاجَّهُ قَوْمُهُ ۚ قَالَ أَتُحَاجُّونِّي فِي اللَّهِ وَقَدْ هَدَانِ ۚ وَلَا أَخَافُ مَا تُشْرِكُونَ بِهِ إِلَّا أَنْ يَشَاءَ رَبِّي شَيْئًا ۗ وَسِعَ رَبِّي كُلَّ شَيْءٍ عِلْمًا ۗ أَفَلَا تَتَذَكَّرُونَ*

_"Maine to yaksoo ho kar apna rukh Us Hasti ki taraf kar diya hai jisne Aasmaano aur Zameen ko paida kiya hai aur mein Sharik karne walon mein se nahi hun."_
_"Aur uski Qaum ne usse jhagda kiya to usne kaha: 'Kya tum Allah ke mutalliq mujh se jhagadte ho? Halaanki Usne mujhe Rahe Raast (Right Path) dikha di hai aur mein tumhare thairai hue Sharikon se nahi darta. Haan mera Rab jo chahe wo ho sakta hai. Mera Rab ka Ilm har cheez par chhaya hua hai to kya tum Nasihat hasil na karoge?"_
(Surah An'am: 79 - 80)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Hazrat Ibrahim (as) Wujood e Khuda ko mukhtalif tareeqon se sabit kiya. Jaisa ke guzishta Ayaat mein Aasman ko dekh kar. Aapke chacha Aazar Badshah ke Nujoomi, Mandir ke incharge bhi the. But traashna unka kaam tha. Usne Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ko jo But banaye the de diye ke inhe bech kar aao. Unhone Buton ke gale mein rassi bandhi aur ghaseetna shuru kiya aur farmaya: "Koi hai jo inhe khareede jo sarasar Nuqsaan den aur zarra barabar fayda na den?" Phir Aap (as) unhe Paani aur keechad mein dal kar kahte: "Lo Paani pee lo! Kuchh baten bhi karo!" Jiske natije mein Aazar ne unhe ghar mein qaid kar diya.
(Rivayat Imam Sadiq (as), Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi)

Imam Mohd Baqir (as) se jab is Ayat (6:77) mein *الضالين* ke bare mein poochha to farmaya:
_"Ye woh hain jinhone Misaaq (Covenant of God) ko bhula diya."_

Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal kiya ke kya Nabi (saww) ke pahle log gumrah the ya hidayat yafta?
Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Woh Hidayat par nahi the. Woh Uski *Fitrat* par the jis par Khuda ne unhe paida kiya. Allah ki Takhleeq mein koi tabdeeli nahi ho sakti. Woh us waqt Hidayat nahi paa sakte the jab tak Khuda ki taraf se unhen Hidayat na milti. Kya tumne Ibrahim (as) ka qaul nahi suna (لئن لم....... Ayat: 6:77) yaani mein Misaaq ko faramosh karne wala ban jaonga."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

Fitrat ke bare mein tafseel Ayat Surah Rum: 30 ke zel mein ayegi. Mukhtasar taur par ye ke Allah ne hamen Deen Fitrat mein paida kiya. فطر means kis cheez ki lambai mein cheerna. Istelahan Paida karne ke maani liye jaate hai. Islam Deen e Fitrat hai. Jab pyas lagti hai to Paani peete hain, bhook lagti hai to Khaana khaate hain, koi hansi ki baat suni to hanse, gham hua to roye.... Ye sab Fitrat hai yaani ye sab Allah ne hi hamare andar by default install karke bheja hai. Khuda Shanasi ke liye koi complicated Proofs ki zaroorat nahi. Ye jo Hazrat Ibrahim (as) practical karke dikha rahe the ye Daleel e Fitrat thi, jise har insaan qubool karta hai, inkaar ki koi wajah baqi nahi rahti. Phir bhi agar woh inkaar kar raha hai to iska matlab ye hua ke uski Fitrat so gayi hai, yani uski Fitrat par gunahon ke parde pade hain. Maslan koi aapko koi pasandida joke sunaye lekin aap koi usko tassur na den, means nahi hanse, ya koi aap ko kahe aapki maa ka inteqal ho gaya aur aap chup chap sun len to aap usko kiya kahenge. Yani us mein Fitrat ka koi maddah nahi raha. Deen e Hanif ka matlab yehi hai jisko fitrat pahchan jaye.

Bare Ilaha hamari soyi hui fitrat ko jagah de.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌓
Imam Sadiq (as) se Maghrib ka waqt poochha.
Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Allah ne apni Kitab mein farmaya: (فلما جن عليه الليل ........ Ayat: 6:76) "Jab us par Raat chha gayi aur usne Taara dekha" ye Maghrib ja Awwal e Waqt hai aur Shafaq (شفق - twilight) ka ghaib hona iska akheri waqt hai."_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)

                   ♦ _*DARR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (845)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَكَيْفَ أَخَافُ مَا أَشْرَكْتُمْ وَلَا تَخَافُونَ أَنَّكُمْ أَشْرَكْتُمْ بِاللَّهِ مَا لَمْ يُنَزِّلْ بِهِ عَلَيْكُمْ سُلْطَانًا ۚ فَأَيُّ الْفَرِيقَيْنِ أَحَقُّ بِالْأَمْنِ ۖ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ*

_"Mein tumhare thairai hue Sharikon se kaise darun jabke tum Allah ke saath unhen Sharik karte ho nahi darte jinke liye Usne koi Sanad nazil nahi ki. Ham dono fareeqon mein se Amn o Itminaan ka zyada Haqdar kaun hai? Agar ilm rakhte ho jawab do."_
(Surah An'am: 81)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaat se Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke Khuda ke Wujood par Fitri Dalail ka tazkara ho raha hai.
Aksar jo But Parast hain woh Khauf ka Deen rakhte hain, Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke zamane se aaj tak aisa hi hota chala aaya hai. Insaan jis cheez se darta hai uski pooja karna shuru kar deta hai. Aaj bhi agar kisi ke zehen bhi kuchh shak ya wahem ho jaye to woh uska taa'be ho jaata hai. Agar aaj tak jo mein karta aaya hun koi kahe ke ye chhod do woh yehi sochega ke kahin koi kuneth ya badshugni to nahi ho jayegi. Is par ghaur nahi karega ke jo mein kar raha hun woh ghalat hai. Aaj bhi ham aksar dekhte hain ke agar koi Message post karta hai ke itne logon ko bhejo warna itna nuqsan ho sakta hai, aur log is dar ki wajah se Message ko forward karte hain, isse pata chal jaata hai ke uska Imaan kitna kachcha hai.
Khair, Hazrat Ibrahim (as) yehi Daleel pesh kar rahen hain: Mein kyon darun? Ye But mera kiya bigad sakte hain. Inke pas khuda hone ka koi legal certificate hai? Hame to sirf Haqeeqi Khuda Allah se darna chahiye. Jab saari Daleel pesh kar chuke to sawal kar rahe hain ke batao Sahi Haqdar kaun hai? Yani Haq Fitratan bilkul wazeh hai. Sirf Wahm o Guman Insaan ko gumrahi ki taraf le jaata hai.

Bare Ilaha hame Shaitani Waswason se mehfooz rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Ek Shakhs Imam Sadiq (as) ke paas hazir hua aur Khwab ki ta'beer poochhi:
_"Meine Khwab mein dekha ke Suraj mere sar par chamak raha hai jabke mere jism par uski koi chamak nahi hai."_
Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Tujhe izzat o shohrat milegi aur mukammal Deen naseeb hoga. Aur agar Suraj tere wujood par chamakta to to is mein doob jaata...Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne jab Suraj ko chamakte hue dekha to kaha tha ke ye mera Rab nahi hai...."_
Raavi ne sawal kya:
_"Log kahte hain jo Suraj ko dekhe to woh Khalifa ya Badshah banta hai?"_
Imam (as):
_"Tujhe khilafat naseeb na hogi aur na hi teri Aba' o Ajdad mein koi Badshah tha. Deen aur Khudai Noor se badh kar bhala aur Ne'mat kya ho sakti hai jisse tum Jannat jaane ki ummid rakh sakte ho."_
(Roza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

                     ♦ _*IMAAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (846)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَلَمْ يَلْبِسُوا إِيمَانَهُمْ بِظُلْمٍ أُولَٰئِكَ لَهُمُ الْأَمْنُ وَهُمْ مُهْتَدُونَ*

_"Woh log jo Imaan laye aur unhone apne Imaan ko Zulm se alooda nahi kiya unhi ke liye Amn hai aur wohi Hidayat yaafta hai."_
(Surah An'am: 82)

📚📖 🚩
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein ye zikr kiya gaya hai ke sirf Imaan lana kaafi nahi.
🕌
Hazrat Ali (as) ne apne taveel Khutbe mein is Ayat ke zel mein farmaya ke "sirf Imaani dawa hi kaafi nahi hai balke Hidayat Yaafta hona bhi zaroori hai.
Lafz Imaan *ايمان* sadiq aane ki wajah se Nijaat naseeb nahi hoti. Agar aisa hota to Yahood o Nasaara aur Tauheed ka iqraar karne wale tamam afraad bashamul Iblees ke sab ke sab Nijaat pa jaate. (Ayat: 6:82)
Nijaat ka daromadar Imaan par hai lekin zabaani Imaan kaafi nahi hai. Nijaat ke liye aise Imaan ki zaroorat hai jo Dil ki gahraiyon mein maujood ho. Isi liye kuchh logon ki mazammat mein Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: (5:41) _'Woh jinhone zabaan se kaha ham Imaan laye lekin unke Dil Imaan nahi laye.'_ "
(Noorus Saqlain)
🍂
Logon ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) se farmaya: "Ham mein se kaun aisa hai jis ne apne Nafs par zulm na kiya ho?"
Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Is se wo cheez murad nahi jo tum samajh rahe ho. Kya tumne Abde Saleh (H. Luqman (as)) ka qaul nahi padha jo unhone apne farzand ko nasihat karte hue kaha tha. "Aye Farzand! khuda ke saath Shirk Na karna, Shirk Zulm e Azeem hai."_
Hazrat Ali (as) ne farmaya ke ye Ayat Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ka qaul hai.
(Majmaul Bayan)
🍃
Imam Sadiq (as) se manqool hai ke "Zulm" se Shirk murad hai.
(Noorus Saqlain)
☘
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Khutba e Ghadeer mein ye Ayat padhi aur farmaya ye Ali (as) ke doston ke liye hai.
(Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)
🍂
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Nabi e Akram (saww) ne jis Wilayat ka Ailan kiya tha us mein zulm na karen aur Falan Falan ki Wilayat ke saath use makhloot na karen."_
(Usoole Kaafi)
🕌
Khulasa ye ke Imaan ke saath Vilayat bhi zaroori hai. Shaitan Khuda ki Tauheed ka iqraar karta tha, na Shirk karta tha, lekin jab Allah ne apne Muntakhab shuda Khalifa ke saamne Sajdah ka hukm diya to usne jirah ki ke Sajdah to sirf Allah ko hi ho sakta hai. Isse pata yahi chalta hai ke uska Imaan mukammal nahi tha. Kyonki Tauheed thi, Vilayat nahi thi. Isliye woh itni Ibaadat karne ke bawajood Jahannam ka haqdar ho gaya.

Bare Ilaha hamare Imaan ko Vilayat ke saath sabit qadam rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍁
﻿Rasule Khuda (saww):
_*"Ali (as) ki mohabbat Imaan hai aur Ali (as) ka bugz kufr hai."*_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p123)
🍃
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Ali ibne Abi Taalib (as) ki taraf dekhna Ibadat hai. Unka zikr Ibadat hai. Kisi bhi shakhs ka Imaan us waqt tak qubool na hoga jab tak wo Ali (as) se mohabbat na rakhe aur unke dushmanon se nafrat na kare."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p129)
🌿
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo shakhs mujh par Imaan rakhe aur Ali (as) se mohabbat kare aur unki Wilayat ka bhi qaayil ho, uspar Jahannum haraam hai. Khuda la'nat kare uspar jo Ali (as) ka munkir aur unka dushman hai…"_
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v2, p365)
🎋
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Ahlebait (as) ki mohabbat mein marne wala mukammal Imaan ke saath wafaat payega aur uski Maut Shaheed ki maut hogi."_
(Tafseer e Ibne Arabi, Safeenatus Shuhda Fee Maqaatilal Husain (as), p50)

          ♦ _*HUJJAT E KHUDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (847)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَتِلْكَ حُجَّتُنَا آتَيْنَاهَا إِبْرَاهِيمَ عَلَىٰ قَوْمِهِ ۚ نَرْفَعُ دَرَجَاتٍ مَنْ نَشَاءُ ۗ إِنَّ رَبَّكَ حَكِيمٌ عَلِيمٌ*

_"Ye Hamari wo Daleel thi jo Hamne Ibrahim (as) ko unke qaum ke muqabile mein ata ki thi. Ham jise chahte hain buland martabe ata karte hain. Beshak tera Rab Sahibe Hikmat aur Sahibe Ilm hai."_
(Surah An'am: 83)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaat mein Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne Khuda ke Wujood o Wahdaniyat ke kaafi Dalail pesh kiye. Ye Allah ke Taa'leem kardah the.
Hujjat means Proof, Daleel. Daleel yani indicator.
Agar ham yahan se Kaafi door par dhuan (smoke) uthta dekhen to hamen is baat ka yaqeen ho jayega ke dhuen ki jagan Aag hai. Dhuen se hame Aag ka pata chala jabke hamne apni Aankhon se Aag ko nahi dekha.
Ya ham Raat ke Andhere mein tez speed se Gadi bagha rahe hon aur saamne aapko Blue Red light ghoomti hui dikhai de to aap slow ho jayenge, aapko pata chal jayega ke aage police ki gadi hai.
Ya aap Bulb jalte hue dekhte hai to bata dete hain ke wire mein Current/Bijli hai, jabke current aapne apni Aankh se dekha nahi.
Pas Dhuan, Red Blue light, Jalta hua Bulb hamare liye Hujjat (Daleel, indicator) hain unseen, Ghaib ke liye. Jitna pukhta yaqeen Hujjat par hoga utna Ghayeb par hoga. Pas Hujjat ko dekh kar Ghayeb Shay par Yaqeen ho jaata hai. Kisi ne Shaitan ko dekha nahi lekin Gumrahi ko dekh kar log uske wujood par Yaqeen rakhte hain.
Daleel e Fitrat yahi hai ke Makhlooq ko dekh kar Khaliq par Yaqeen aata hai.
Lekin jisko Allah ne hamare liye Hujjat qarar diya ho usse behtar kiya Daleel hogi.
Allah ne Hamari Hidayat ke liye Anbiya, Ausiya wa Aimma (as) ko hamare liye Hujjat qarar diya isliye ham unko Hujjatullah kahte hain. Rivayaat ke mutabiq agar is
Duniya mein Hujjat e Khuda na hoti to ye kab ki halaak ho jaati, isliye aaj bhi Imam Mahdi (as) daur e Hazir mein hamare liye Hujjat hain.
🌿
*قال الامام المهدى (عج):*
*إن الارض لا تخلو من حجة، إما ظاهرا و إما مغمورا.*

_"Beshak Zameen kabhi bhi hujjat e Khuda se khali nahi rahegi, chahe woh Hujjat e Zahir ho ya Pardah e Ghaib mein."_
(Kamaluddin, Vol 2, P-511, H-42, Al Kharaej wal Jaraeh, Vol 3, P-110, H-26, Biharul Anwaar, Vol 53, P-191, H-19)
☘
Imam Kazim (as):
_"Kul (tamaam) admiyon par Allah ki 2 Hujjatein hain, ek Hujjat e Zaahiri aur ek Hujjat e Baatini. Hujjat e Zaahiri to Rasul aur Ambiya aur Aimma e Masumeen (as) hain aur Hujjat e Baatini (inner) khud unki (admiyon ki) Aql hai."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p74)

Bare Ilaha Teri Hujjat ko jald az jald zahir farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)! Tum aur tumhare farzandon mein se Imam mere baad khalq (creatures) par Hujjat e Khuda hain. Aur bandon mein Raah e Khuda ki nishaani (Ayat) hain. Jis shakhs ne unme se kisi ek ka inkaar kiya aur jisne unme se kisi ek ki na-farmaani ki to usne meri na-farmaani ki. Aur jisne unme se kisi par zulm kiya, usne mujh par jafaa ki. Aur jisne tumhare saath mohabbat aur neki ka bartao kiya to usne mere saath mohabbat o neki ka bartaav kiya. Aur jisne tumhari ita'at ki, usne meri ita'at ki. Aur jisne tumse dosti ki usne mujh se dosti ki aur jisne tumse dushmani ki usne mujh se dushmani ki, kyun ki tum mujh se aur mere sulb se paida huwe ho aur main tumse hun."_
(Isbaat e Imamat - Allamah Majlisi, p62)

        ♦ _*SILSILA-E-HIDAYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (848)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَوَهَبْنَا لَهُ إِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ ۚ كُلًّا هَدَيْنَا ۚ وَنُوحًا هَدَيْنَا مِنْ قَبْلُ ۖ وَمِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِهِ دَاوُودَ وَسُلَيْمَانَ وَأَيُّوبَ وَيُوسُفَ وَمُوسَىٰ وَهَارُونَ ۚ وَكَذَٰلِكَ نَجْزِي الْمُحْسِنِينَ * وَزَكَرِيَّا وَيَحْيَىٰ وَعِيسَىٰ وَإِلْيَاسَ ۖ كُلٌّ مِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ * وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ وَالْيَسَعَ وَيُونُسَ وَلُوطًا ۚ وَكُلًّا فَضَّلْنَا عَلَى الْعَالَمِينَ * وَمِنْ آبَائِهِمْ وَذُرِّيَّاتِهِمْ وَإِخْوَانِهِمْ ۖ وَاجْتَبَيْنَاهُمْ وَهَدَيْنَاهُمْ إِلَىٰ صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ*
_"Aur Hamne use Ishaq (as) wa Yaqoob (as) jaisi Aulad ata ki, Hamne sabko Hidayat di aur Nooh (as) ko isse qabl Hidayat ki thi aur uski Aulad mein se Dawood (as), Sulaiman (as) Ayyub (as), Yusuf (as), Musa (as) aur Haroon (as) ko Hidayat di aur Nekokaron ko ham isi ka badla dete hain."_
_"Aur (usi ki Aulad mein se) Zakariya (as), Yahya (as), Esa (as) aur Ilyas (as) ko Hidayat di, woh sab log Nek logon mein se the."_
_"Aur Ismael (as), Al Yasa' (as) aur Lut (as) ko Hidayat di, un mein se har ek ko Hamne tamam Jahano par Fazilat di."_
_"Aur unke Aba' aur unki Nasl aur unke bhaiyon mein se Hamne unhe chuna aur unhen Siraate Mustaqeem ki Hidayat ki."_
(Surah An'am: 84 - 87)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
(Wasayat ke ittesal o tasalsul ke mutalliq)
"Wasayat (Wasi) ka silsila Hazrat Adam (as) se jaari hua aur ye silsila wahan se chalta hua Ibrahim (as) wa Yaqoob (as) tak pahuncha.
*وَوَصَّىٰ بِهَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بَنِيهِ وَيَعْقُوبُ .....*(Baqarah: 132)
"Ibrahim (as) ne iski Wasiyat apni Aulad ko ki thi aur Yaqoob (as) ne bhi apni Aulad ko apna Wasi banaya tha." Allah Ta'ala ne isi Hidayat ke tasalsul (continuity) ko yun bayan farmaya: (Ayat 6:84-87) yani Hamne Ibrahim (as) ki zahmat ka silsila unki nasl mein Nubuwwat de kar ata kiya. _"Aur Hamne isse pahle Nooh (as) ko Hidayat ki thi."_ yani Hamne unhe ye Hukm diya tha ke woh silsila e Wasayat apni Nasl mein jaari karen. Chunanche Silsila e Wasayat chalta hua Ibrahim (as) tak aaya aur Hazrat Ibrahim (as) aur Hazrat Hud (as) ke darmiyan 10 Anbiya ka faisla tha. Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: (An'am: 84-87).
Allah Ta'ala ne hamesha Taa'leemat e Anbiya (as) ki hifazat ke liye unke afraad e khaana ko muqarrar kiya hai. Isi tarah se Allah ne apne Habib (saww) ko tasalli dete hue farmaya ke Aap (saww) kisi ke inkaar ki parwa na karen. Agar Aap (saww) ki Ummat Aapki Taa'leemat ka inkaar karti hai to karti rahe, Hamne Aap (saww) ke Ahle Bait (as) ko Aapki Taa'leemat ka nigehbaan muqarrar kar diya hai. Woh Aap (saww) ki Taa'leemat ka kabhi inkaar nahi karenge aur Mein us Imaan ko zaye nahi hone dunga, jiski Aap (saww) ne Tableegh ki hai aur tere baad Meine tere Ahle Bait (as) ko logon ke liye Hidayat ka Parcham aur Aapka Jaanasheen banaya hai aur Meine unhe apne apne us Ilm ka Ahl e Istinbaat banaya hai jis mein na to koi Kizb hai na koi Gunah aur na koi Bohtaan hai aur na koi Takabbur o Riyakaari shamil hai."
(Kamaluddin wa Tamamun Ne'ma, Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
📖
Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim Qummi mein hai ke Hazrat Musa (as) aur Hazrat Dawood (as) ke darmiyan 5 sadiyon (centuries) ka fasla tha.
🇸🇦
Is Ayat se ye baat wazeh ho jaati hai ke jitne bhi Hadi, Wasi, Rehbar wa Anbiya is Duniya mein aye unko Allah ne chuna. Aur sare Anbiya wa Ausiya ek Nasl o Khandan mein se the.
🇵🇰
Jo log kahte hain ke Islam mein Janbhoori nizam hai, log apni Khalifa ko chun sakte, Rahbari ek hi Khandan mein nahi rah sakti, ye Ayat in baton ka kaat karti hai.

Bare Ilaha hame Paak Naslon ke saath qaem o dayem rakh.
(To be continued...........)

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌿
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Beshak, Ulama Ambiya (as) ke waaris hain kyun ki Ambiya (as) Dirham o Dinaar ko apna waaris nahi banaate balke unke aqwaal o guftaar hi unki Miraas hain. Lihaza, jo shakhs un mein se kuchh haasil kar lega to goya usko bahut bada hissa mil gaya. Lihaza, ye dhyaan rakho ke tum use kis se haasil kar rahe ho kyun ki hum Ahle bait (as) ki har Nasl mein kuchh na kuchh aise Aadil Ulama zaroor paaye jaate hain jo Gulu' (exaggeration) karne waalon ki tehrifaat (distortions), Ahl e Batil ke ilzamat (accusations) aur Jahilon ki tawilaat (interpretations) se Islam ko mehfooz rakhte hain."_ (Usool e Kafi, v1, p32, h1, Adaab e Islami, v2, p45)

       ♦ _*NASLE AHLE BAIT (as)*_ ♦

Start your Day by reading Quran: (849) (Continued.......)

(Surah An'am: 84 - 87)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ahle Bait (as) bhi Anbiya (as) ki Nasl se hain. Jaisa ke pahle hame zikr kiya Allah ke Rahbaron ki Nasl Paak o Pakeeza hai. Kisi ke Waledain Kafir nahi the, balke sab Muwahhid the.
🌿
Kya Hasan (as) aur Imam Husain (as) farzande Rasool (saww) hain?

Imam Baqir (as) se Abu Jarood ne apna kisi shakhs se debate ka tazkara kiya:
Raavi: Woh log Janabe Hasnain (as) ko farzande Rasool manne ko tayyar nahi the.
Meine ye Ayat (6:84-87) pesh ki. Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Esa (as) ko Maa ki wajah se Nasl e Ibrahim qarar diya hai, jabke Janabe Maryam (as) aur Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke darmiyan sadiyon ka fasla hai aur Hazrat Fatema Zehra (sa) aur Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke darmiyan koi fasla nahi hai. Jab Maryam (as) ka beta Ibrahim (as) ka farzand kahla sakta hai to Janabe Fatema Zehra
(sa) ke bete Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke farzand kyon nahi kahla sakte?"
Unhone kaha ke Nawase ko beta to kah sakte hain lekin Sulbi beta nahi.
Raavi ne phir Ayah e Mubahela (3:61) pesh ki. Rasoole Khuda (saww) Mubahela mein beton ki jagah Hasan o Husain (as) ko le kar gaye."
Is par unhone kaha lekin Sulbi Beta nahi kah sakte.
Imam (as) ne ek aur Ayat pesh ki jisko sirf Kafir hi inkaar kar sakta hai.
Imam (as) ne farmaya: Ayat: 
*...وَحَلَائِلُ أَبْنَائِكُمُ الَّذِينَ مِنْ أَصْلَابِكُمْ...*
_"Tum par tumhare Sulbi Beton ki Biwiyan Haraam hain."_
(Surah Nisa': 23)
"Abu Jarood! Hamare mukhalefin se poochho ke kya Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke liye Hasnain (as) ki Biwiyon se Nikah karna Halal hai? Agar jawab mein 'haan' kahen to unhone jhoot bola aur Fisq o Fujoor ka muzahera kiya aur agar woh jawab mein 'nahi' kahen to Hurmat ki wajah yehi hogi ke Hasnain (as) Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke Sulbi bete the. Isi liye to unki Biwiyan Rasoole Khuda (saww) par Haraam ki gayi thi."
(Usoole Kaafi, Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

Khalifa Haroon Rashid ne bhi Imam Musa Kazim (as) se yehi sawal kiya tha aur yehi jawab diya.
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza)

Bare Ilaha sare Sadaat e Karam ki hifazat farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as)
se ek shakhs ne puchha ke, _"Janab Musa (as) jaadugaro'n ke muqable mein ghabra gaye the, jabke Janabe Ibrahim (as) to Aag se bhi na ghabraye?"_
Imam (as) ne jawaab diya: _"Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke Sulb mein Muhammad (saww) aur Aal e Muhammad (as) ke Anwaar the"._
(Tafseer e Anwaar e Najaf, v15, p14)

        ♦ _*IQTEDA (FOLLOWING)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (850)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*ذَٰلِكَ هُدَى اللَّهِ يَهْدِي بِهِ مَنْ يَشَاءُ مِنْ عِبَادِهِ ۚ وَلَوْ أَشْرَكُوا لَحَبِطَ عَنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ * أُولَٰئِكَ الَّذِينَ آتَيْنَاهُمُ الْكِتَابَ وَالْحُكْمَ وَالنُّبُوَّةَ ۚ فَإِنْ يَكْفُرْ بِهَا هَٰؤُلَاءِ فَقَدْ وَكَّلْنَا بِهَا قَوْمًا لَيْسُوا بِهَا بِكَافِرِينَ * أُولَٰئِكَ الَّذِينَ هَدَى اللَّهُ ۖ فَبِهُدَاهُمُ اقْتَدِهْ ۗ قُلْ لَا أَسْأَلُكُمْ عَلَيْهِ أَجْرًا ۖ إِنْ هُوَ إِلَّا ذِكْرَىٰ لِلْعَالَمِينَ*

_"Ye Allah ki Hidayat hai woh apne bandon mein se jis ki chahta hai Rahnumai karta hai aur agar unhone Shirk kiya hota to unke tamam Aamaal zaye ho jaate."_
_"Ye woh log hain jinhe Hamne Kitab, Hikmat aur Nubuwwat ata ki thi aur agar ye log iska inkaar karte to Hamne uske liye ek Qaum muqarrar kar di hai jo uske Munkir nahi hain."_
_"Ye Woh Log hain jinhe Khuda ne Hidayat di thi. Tum unki Hidayat ki pairavi karo. Kah den ke mein is Tableegh e Risalat par tumse koi Ujrat talab nahi karta, ye to tamam Jahano ke liye Nasihat hai."_
(Surah An'am: 88 - 90)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Aqalmand Mo'meneen ke liye iqtada (following) se badh kar koi achcha raasta nahi hai kyonki wo Sahih aur Wazeh Raasta hai. Allah ne poori kaynat mein Apne Mehboob Bande Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww) se farmaya: Ayat 6:90). Aur agar iqteda se koi aur Raasta behtar hota to Allah apne Auliya aur Anbiya ko us par chalne ki dawat deta."_
(Misbahus Shari'ah, Noorus Saqlain)
☘
Rasoole Akram (saww):
_"Sab se Haseen tareen Hidayat Anbiya ki Hidayat hai."_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim Qummi)
🌿
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Mein us Jamaat ka fard hun jinke mutalliq Allah ne farmaya hai: Ayat 6:90), jo poochhna hai poochho."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)
🍃
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Logo! Apne Paighambar ki Hidayat ki itteba' karo, woh sab se Afzal Hidayat hai."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
🍂
Bare Ilaha hame behtareen Hidayat hasil karne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍪
Imam Sadiq(as):
_"Ek qaum ko Khuda ne wasee' Rizq ata kiya jiski wajah se unhone sarkashi (Rebellious) ki Raah apna li aur unhone Roti ki beqadri shuru kar di. Safed Mede ki Rotiyon ke tukde karke apni Raahon mein daalne lage. Kuchh dino ke baad Allah ne Khushksaali (Drought) shuru ki to unhone kaha hamare Godamon mein kai saal ka ghalla maujood hai. Allah ne unke Ghalle mein Ghun (germs) paida kar diya jiski wajah se unka Ghalla naakara ho gaya. Akhir kar ye haalat ho gayi ke Roti ke phenke hue tukde uthate the aur use dho kar khaate the. Ek baar Abul Abbas (Abbasi Khalifa) ke Dastarkhwan par jaane ka ittefaq hua to mein wahan bhi Roti ki beqadri mulaheza ki. Aise logo ke liya farmaya: (Ayat Nahl:112)"_
(Mahasin e Barqi, Noorus Saqlain)

         ♦ _*SIFAAT E KHUDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (851)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا قَدَرُوا اللَّهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ إِذْ قَالُوا مَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَىٰ بَشَرٍ مِنْ شَيْءٍ ۗ قُلْ مَنْ أَنْزَلَ الْكِتَابَ الَّذِي جَاءَ بِهِ مُوسَىٰ نُورًا وَهُدًى لِلنَّاسِ ۖ تَجْعَلُونَهُ قَرَاطِيسَ تُبْدُونَهَا وَتُخْفُونَ كَثِيرًا ۖ وَعُلِّمْتُمْ مَا لَمْ تَعْلَمُوا أَنْتُمْ وَلَا آبَاؤُكُمْ ۖ قُلِ اللَّهُ ۖ ثُمَّ ذَرْهُمْ فِي خَوْضِهِمْ يَلْعَبُونَ*

_"Aur in logon ne Khuda ke mutalliq Sahih andaza nahi lagaya jab unhone kaha ke Allah ne kisi Insaan par kuchh nazil hi nahi kiya. Aap (saww) kah den ke wo Kitab Kisne Nazil ki thi jise Musa (as) laye the jo ke logon ke liye sarasar Roshni aur Hidayat thi jise tum para para kar ke rakhte ho. Jiska kuchh hissa zahir karte ho aur bahut kuchh chhupate ho jiske zariye se tumko wo Ilm diya gaya jo na tumhe hasil tha aur tumhare abaa' o ajdad ko hasil tha. Aap (saww) kah den ke Allah ne hi use Nazil kiya tha. Phir Aap (saww) unhe Daleel Baziyon mein khelne ke liye chhod do."_
(Surah An'am: 91)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah ko Sahih maana mein koi nahi samajh sakta. Jo bhi ham Allah ki Ma'arefat rakhte hain woh Usi ne hame taleem di hai. Jo bhi Uski Sifat ham bayan karte hain, uske baad ham Subhanallah *سبحان الله* kahte hai, iska matlab ye hai jo bhi Sifat hamne bayan ki Allah usse kahi zyada Munazzah منزه hai. Ye Woh in Sifaat se bhi Paak hai. Uski Sifaat hamare Wahm o Khayal mein nahi aa sakte.
☘
Hazrat Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ki Sifaat bayan nahi ki ja sakti kyonki Allah Ta'ala ne khud farmaya: ("Un logon ne Khuda ki Shaan ka Sahih andaza nahi lagaya.") Isi liye uski jo bhi Sifaat bayan ki jayegi Khuda ki Shaan usse kahin buland o bala hogi."_
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🌿
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Kaynat ka koi bhi fard Khuda ki Shaan ka ta'yyun nahi kar sakta."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Aye mere Rab! Aye mere Rab! Aye mere Rab! Main Tujh se Tere Haq ka waasta aur Teri Paakeezgi ka aur Tere bahut Shandar Sifaat aur Naamon ka waasta dekar sawaal karta hun ke mere raat aur din ke waqton ko Apni yaad se bharpoor kar de, aur Apni khidmat mein lage rehne ki dhun lagaa de..
(Dua e Kumail)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Subhanallah' *سبحان الله* ki Tafseer ye hai ke Allah ko har naqs o aib se Paak samjhe."_
(To accept that Allah is free from all defects)
(Sharh Dua e Kumail)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                  ♦ _*QUR'AN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (852)

_"Ye wo Kitab hai jise Hamne Nazil kiya hai, Barkat wali hai, ye un Kitabon ki tasdeeq karti hai jo isse pahle aayi thi taake Aap uske zariye se bastiyon ke Markaz (Mecca) aur iske atraaf mein rahne walon mutanabbe karo. Woh log jo Akhirat par Imaan rakhte hain woh is Kitab par bhi Imaan rakhte hain aur woh apni Namazon ki pabandi karte hain."_
_"Ye wo Kitab hai jise Hamne Nazil kiya hai, Barkat wali hai, ye un Kitabon ki tasdeeq karti hai jo isse pahle aayi thi taake Aap uske zariye se bastiyon ke Markaz (Mecca) aur iske atraaf mein rahne walon mutanabbe karo. Woh log jo Akhirat par Imaan rakhte hain woh is Kitab par bhi Imaan rakhte hain aur woh apni Namazon ki pabandi karte hain."_
(Surah An'am: 92)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein Mushrekin ka eitraz ka zikr hua tha ke Allah ne ham par kuchh nazil nahi kya. Allah Ta'ala ne jawab diya ke itni Aasmani Kitaben nazil hui Kisne ki?
Is Ayat mein hai ke Allah Ta'ala ne Qur'an, Ba Barkat wali Kitab ko nazil kiya. Qur'an khud Rasoole Khuda (saww) ka Mo'jeza hai.
📖
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Quran, Allah ke baad, har shay se afzal hai. Jisne Quran ki izzat ki goya usne Allah ki izzat ki aur jisne Quran ki izzat na ki goya usne Allah ki tauheen ki."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v9, p27)
📖
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Quran ke ajayeb ko shumaar nahi kiya ja sakta aur uske garaib ka ahaata nahi kiya ja sakta. Qur'an Hidayat ka chirag aur Hikmat ka Minar hai."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p557)
🤲🏻
_"Aye Sahib e Karam! Aye Mere Parwardigaar! Tu meri kamzori ko jaanta hai ke Duniya ki zara zara aazmaish aur uski maamuli takleefein aur jo na-pasand cheezein Ahl e Duniya par guzarti rehti hain (unhe main bardaasht nahi kar sakta), bawajood iske ke wo aazmaish aur wo takleefein qaaimi nahi hoti, uski muddat thodi aur uski baqaa chand-roza hoti hai. To bhala phir mujh se Akherat ki balaa aur usme musibato'n ke wurood ki bardaasht kyun-kar ho sakegi? Halaa'nki wahaa'n ki muddat lambi hogi..."_
(Dua-e-Kumail)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

🙇 🤲🏻
*Janabe Fatema Zahra (sa):*
_*"Khuda wand-e-aalam ne NAMAZ ko tumhare liye takabbur se doori karar diya hai."*_
(Ayan-us-Shia, V-1, Pg-316)

                 ♦ _*BOHTAAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (853)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَنْ أَظْلَمُ مِمَّنِ افْتَرَىٰ عَلَى اللَّهِ كَذِبًا أَوْ قَالَ أُوحِيَ إِلَيَّ وَلَمْ يُوحَ إِلَيْهِ شَيْءٌ وَمَنْ قَالَ سَأُنْزِلُ مِثْلَ مَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ ۗ وَلَوْ تَرَىٰ إِذِ الظَّالِمُونَ فِي غَمَرَاتِ الْمَوْتِ وَالْمَلَائِكَةُ بَاسِطُو أَيْدِيهِمْ أَخْرِجُوا أَنْفُسَكُمُ ۖ الْيَوْمَ تُجْزَوْنَ عَذَابَ الْهُونِ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَقُولُونَ عَلَى اللَّهِ غَيْرَ الْحَقِّ وَكُنْتُمْ عَنْ آيَاتِهِ تَسْتَكْبِرُونَ*

_"Aur isse badh kar bhala Zalim aur kaun hoga jo Allah par Jhoota Bohtan ghade ya ye kahe ke mujh par Waḥy hui hai jabke us par kisi cheez ki Waḥy na ki gayi ho, ya jo Allah ki nazil kardah Waḥy ke mutalliq kahe ke mein bhi aisi cheez nazil karke dikha dunga._
_Kaash! Tum Zalimon ki us haalat ko dekh sako jab woh Sakarat e Maut mein dubkiyan kha rahe hote hain aur Malaika apne haath badha kar kah rahe hote hain ke Aaj apni jaan nikal lo. Aaj tumhe Zillat ka Azaab diya jayega kyonki tum Khuda par Na-Haq baten banaya karte the aur tum iski Ayaat ke saamne Takabbur karte the."_
(Surah An'am: 93)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
"Ye Ayat Ibne Abi Sarah ke mutalliq nazil hui hai jisko Khalifa e Salis ne apne daur e Hukoomat mein Misr (Egypt) ka Governor muqarrar kiya tha. Fateh Makkah ke Din Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne uska khoon rayga qarar diya tha aur woh shakhs kuchh Din tak Waḥy likhta tha. Jab Allah *أَنَّ اللَّهَ عَزِيزٌ حَكِيمٌ* nazil karta to woh *أَنَّ اللَّهَ عَلِيمٌ حَكِيمٌ* likh deta tha. Rasoole Khuda (saww) usse farmate the ke Allah waqai *عَلِيمٌ حَكِيمٌ* hai lekin Ayat mein *عَزِيزٌ حَكِيمٌ* ke alfaaz nazil hue hain.
Ye badbakht Munafeqeen se kahta tha ke jaisa mein chahta hun apni marzi se Qur'an mein tabdeeli kar deta hun. Muhammad Mustafa (saww) meri tabdeeli par koi etraz nahi karte. Is jaisa Qur'an to mein khud bhi utar sakta hun. Chunanche Allah Ta'ala ne is ke mutalliq ye Ayat nazil farmayi."
"Abdullah bin Sa'ad bin Abi Sarah Usman ka razai bhai tha. Usne Islam qubool kiya aur Medina aa gaya. Woh khush navees tha. Jab Waḥy nazil hoti to Rasoole Khuda (saww) usse kahte ke likh lo. To likhte waqt pher badal kar deta. Rasool (saww) naraz hote. Kuchh din baad woh murtad ho kar Mecca chala gaya aur Quraish se kaha Muhammad ko to kuchh pata hi nahi chalta ke woh kiya kah rahe hain. Us jaisi Waḥy to mein khud hi bana leta hun. Us jaisa Qur'an to mein khud bhi utar sakta hun. Allah ne is shakhs ke mutalliq ye Ayat nazil farmayi."
"Jab fatah Mecca hui to Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne iske qatl ka hukm jaari kiya tha. Usman iska haath pakad kar Rasool (saww) ke paas laya aur Ma'afi ki darkhwast ki. 3 bar israr kiya to Ma'af kar diya gaya."
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
👹
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Is Ayat mein woh shakhs bhi shamil hai jisne Imamat ka jhoota dawa kiya ho."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
👺
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ye Ayat (ka Akhiri part) Dushmenane Ale Muhammad (as) ke mutalliq nazil hui aur is Ayat mein unke bure anjaam ki khabar di gayi hai."_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim Qummi)

Bare Ilaha hame Dushmanano ke shar mehfooz rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo kisi Momin ya Momena par Bohtaan (tohmat / slander / allegation) lagaye ya uski nisbat wo baat kahe jo usme nahi hai, to Khuda usko Aag ki pusht par jagah dega."_
(Jaame ul Akhbaar, p262)

          ♦ _*HAALAT-E-BE'SAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (854)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَقَدْ جِئْتُمُونَا فُرَادَىٰ كَمَا خَلَقْنَاكُمْ أَوَّلَ مَرَّةٍ وَتَرَكْتُمْ مَا خَوَّلْنَاكُمْ وَرَاءَ ظُهُورِكُمْ ۖ وَمَا نَرَىٰ مَعَكُمْ شُفَعَاءَكُمُ الَّذِينَ زَعَمْتُمْ أَنَّهُمْ فِيكُمْ شُرَكَاءُ ۚ لَقَدْ تَقَطَّعَ بَيْنَكُمْ وَضَلَّ عَنْكُمْ مَا كُنْتُمْ تَزْعُمُونَ*

_"Tum Hamare saamne tan o tanha hazir hoge jaisa ke Hamne tumhe pahli martaba akela paida kiya tha aur Hamne tumhe Duniya mein jo kuchh ataa' kiya tha woh peechhe chhod aaye ho aur Hame tumhare saath tumhare woh Shifarish karne wale dikhai nahi dete jin ke mutalliq tum samajhte ho ke tumhare kaam banane mein unka bhi kuchh hissa hai. Tumhare aapas ke sab raabte toot gaye hain aur tumse woh sab gum ho chuke hain jin ke mutalliq tum sherakat ka guman kiya karte the."_
(Surah An'am: 94)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein jin logon ke liye Azaab ka zikr kiya gaya tha, is Ayat mein bhi wohi zikr jaari hai.
Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya:
_"Is Ayat mein jin Shifarish karne walon ki gumshudgi ki khabar di gayi hai usse logon ke Jhoote Imam murad hain."_
_"( "Tumhare aapas mein Raabte toot chuke hain aur woh sab gum ho gaye jinki sherakat ka tum guman kiya karte the.") Is Ayat ke misdaaq mein Moaviya, Bani Umayya ke bhai band aur unke Aimma bhi shamil hain."_
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚰
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Qayamat ke Din tum barahna (nude) pesh kiye jaoge."_
Is par Aisha ne kaha:
_"Hay hamari pepardagi! Kya us Din Mard Aurat ek doosri ki sharamgahon ko dekhenge?"_
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Us Din har Shakhs ko apni fikr padi hogi kisi ko doosre ki taraf nigah karne ki zaroorat hi nahi hogi."_
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)
👰🏼
Imam Sadiq (as):
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Jab meri Chachi Amma Fatema binte Asad ne ye Ayat suni to unhone cheekh kar kaha tha ke Ya Rasoolallah (saww)! Khuda se kahen ke woh mujhe barhengi se mehfooz rakhe. Phir usne mujh se Munkir Nakir ke mutalliq poochha to meine unki sakht giri ka tazkara kiya. Meri Chachi Amma ne mujh se kaha: Ya Rasoolallah! Allah se Dua mangen ke woh mujhe Munkir o Nakir na dikhai aur meri Qabr ko wasee' kare aur mujhe mere kafan mein mehshoor farmaye. Meine Allah Ta'ala se ye Duayen mangi aur Usne tamam Duayen qubool ki."_
(Al Kharaej wal Jaraeh)

Bare Ilaha hame Qayamat ke Din usi Karbala ke mas kardah Kafan mein hi uthana jo Maut ke waqt diya jaata hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚰
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Apne murdon ko achha Kafan pahnai. Tumhe usi Kafan mein uthna hai."_
_"Ye unke liye zeenat hai."_
(Al Kaafi, Man La Yahzarul Faqih)
⚰
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Log apne apne Kafan mein uthaye jayenge. Jo Khuda unke farsoodah ajsaam (rotten body) ko az sire nau zindagi dega Wohi unke liye Kafan ko bhi naya bana dega. (Jisko Kafan na mila ho) Khuda jis tarah se chahega uski satarposhi (attire) karega."_
(Ehtejaaj Tabarsi)

      ♦ _*DAANA AUR GUTHLI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (855)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ اللَّهَ فَالِقُ الْحَبِّ وَالنَّوَىٰ ۖ يُخْرِجُ الْحَيَّ مِنَ الْمَيِّتِ وَمُخْرِجُ الْمَيِّتِ مِنَ الْحَيِّ ۚ ذَٰلِكُمُ اللَّهُ ۖ فَأَنَّىٰ تُؤْفَكُونَ*

_"Beshak Daane aur Guthli ko shigaafta Karnewala (Splitter) Allah hi hai. Woh Zinda ko Murdah se nikaalta hai aur Murdeh ko Zinda se Nikaalne wala hai. Ye sab kaam Karnewala Allah hai tum kidhar bahke chale jaa rahe ho?"_
(Surah An'am: 95)

📚📖 🌱
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Surah mein Allah ke Tauheed o Sifaat ka zikr jaari. Allah har Ayat mein Apne Aap ko pahchanwa raha hai.
🌾
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Is Ayat mein " *حب* se Momin ki Teenat ( *طينت*) Murad hai jis par Allah ne Apni Muhabbat ko dala hai aur " *نوى*" Kafiron ki Teenat hai. Aur lafz *نوى* " *نا* se mushtaq hai jis ke maani hain door hone ke hain. Kafiron ki Teenat har cheez se door hai. Isi liye use "Nova" kaha gaya hai."_
_"Allah ne mazeed farmaya ("Allah Murde se zinda ko nikalta hai.........") Zinda se murad Momin hai jiski Teenat Kafir ki Teenat se baramad hoti hai aur Murda se murad Kafir hai jiski Teenat Momin ki Teenat se baramad hoti hai."_
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🎋
Is Ayat ka maqsad ye hai ke apni Mehboob Makhlooq ka bhi Khaliq hai aur jo log Haq se door hain unka bhi Khaliq Allah hai. Ek Rivayat ye bhi hai ke iska mafhoom hai ke Woh Aimma ke Uloom ko shigaafta karta hai. Murda ko zinda se baramad karne ka matlab ye hai Allah Kafir se Momin ko paida karta hai aur Momin ko Kafir se paida karta hai.
(Tafseer Ali Ibn Ibrahim Qummi)

Bare Ilaha Tu Apne qeemti Dano ki hifazat farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍅
Imam Husain (as):
_"Rasule Khuda (saww) jab kabhi Anaar (Pomegranate) khaate the to aap kisi ko usme shareek nahi karte the aur farmaate the, "Har anaar mein ek Jannat ka daana zaroor hota hai"._
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p105)

            ♦ _*RAAT O DIN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (856)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَالِقُ الْإِصْبَاحِ وَجَعَلَ اللَّيْلَ سَكَنًا وَالشَّمْسَ وَالْقَمَرَ حُسْبَانًا ۚ ذَٰلِكَ تَقْدِيرُ الْعَزِيزِ الْعَلِيمِ*

_"Parda e Shab ko chaak kar ke Wohi Subah nikaalta hai. Usne Raat ko sukoon ka waqt banaya aur Usne Suraj aur Chand ke Tuloo' wa Ghuroob ka Hisaab muqarrar kiya hai. Ye Ghaalib aur Sahib e Ilm ke thairai hue andaze hain."_
(Surah An'am: 96)

----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Khuda ke Asmaa wa Sifaat ka zikr jaari hai.
🌌
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Agar Allah Din aur Raat mein se kisi ko taweel arse tak qayem kar deta to phir Rizq Rozi ka husool mushkil ho jaata. Isliye Kaynat ke Mudabbir aur Khaliq ne Din ko Roshan aur Raat ko sukoon ka zariya banaya hai."_
(Kitab Ahliljah, Noorus Saqlain)
🌌
Imam Sadiq (as) apne ghulamo ko Raat ke waqt Jaanwar zabah karne se rokte the aur farmate the ke jab tak Fajr tuloo' na ho us waqt Janwar zabah na karo kyonki Allah ne Raat ko har cheez ke liye bayes e sukoon banaya hai.
(Tehzeebul Ahkam)
💕
Imam Baqir wa Imam Reza (as):
_"Sunnat hai ke Shaadi Raat ke waqt ki jaye kyonki Allah ne Raat ko Sukoon ka zariya banaya hai aur Biwiyan bhi Sukoon ka zariya hai."_
(Al Kaafi)
🚌
Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Raat ke pahle hisse mein safar na karo. Allah ne use zariye sukoon banaya hai. Us waqt qayam karo aur apni pusht ko aram pahunchao."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
🤲🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo shakhs chaahe ke musibat ke waqt uski Dua qubool ho, uspar laazim hai ke sukoon ke waqt bahut zyada Dua kare."_
(Kaifar e Gunahaane Kabira , p139)

Bare Ilaha hame hamari zindagi mein sukoon ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

         *4th Jamadi us Sani 1439*

         ♦ _*HIDAYAT KE SITARE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (857)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَهُوَ الَّذِي جَعَلَ لَكُمُ النُّجُومَ لِتَهْتَدُوا بِهَا فِي ظُلُمَاتِ الْبَرِّ وَالْبَحْرِ ۗ قَدْ فَصَّلْنَا الْآيَاتِ لِقَوْمٍ يَعْلَمُونَ*

_"Aur Wohi hai jisne tumhare liye Sitare banaye taake unke zariye tum sahra (Desert) aur Samandar ki tareekyon mein raasta maloom kar sako. Hamne Sahebane Ilm ke liye apni Nishaniyan khol kar bayan kar di hain."_
(Surah An'am: 97)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Sitare logon ko raahon aur simton ki rahnumai faraham karte hain aur Sitaron ko dekh kar log Raat ke waqt Sahih Raaste ka ta'yyun karte hain aur Samandari Jahaz bhi Sitaron ki rahnumai mein apni manzil ki taraf gamzan rahte hain. Agar Sitare na hote to logon ko Raat ke waqt Raasta talaash karne mein dushwari hoti.
Tafseer e Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi ki ek Rivayaat ka ma hasl ye hai ke jis tarah se Sitare Tareekyon mein Raah dikhate hain usi tarah se Ale Muhammad (as) bhi gumrahiyon aur bida'at ki Tareekyon mein Rahnumai karte hain.

Beshak Allah ne sitaron ko zariye Hidayat qarar diya. Jaise Qur'an logon ke liye Hidayat hai. Aql bhi insaano mein Hidayat ka zariya hai lekin ye Hidayat ke zaraye Samit hain (Silent Guide). Allah ne iske saath saath Qur'an e Natiq (Speaking Qur'an) bhi insaano ke liye bheje. Kaise ye Insaan kah sakta hai mere liye sirf Qur'an e Samit Kaafi hai. Book ke saath ek teacher zaroori hai, Car ke liye Driver zaroori hai etc.... Allah ne logon ki Hidayat ke liye 1,24000 Paighambar (Hadi) bheje. Hamari Akheri Nabi (saww) ke baad ye Silsila Aimmah ki surat mein aaj tak jaari hai. Yehi hamari Hidayat ke Sitare hain. Sitare Allah ne banaye hai, kisi insaan ke banaye hue Artificial Star ki koi khusoosiyat nahi, hamare liye woh koi maane nahi rakhta. Ab ek masnooi hadis pesh ki jaati hai Ashaab Sitaron ki maanind hain. Kiya sab Ashaab Masoom the? Kiya sab Ashaab Muttaqi ya Momin the? Hamne tarikh mein kuchh Ashaab ko Munafiq paya, Kuchh Ashaab ko ek doosre se Jang karte paya, Kuchh Ashaab ko Rasool (saww) ne apne dar se naraaz hokar bhagaya. Ye kaise hamare Hadi ho sakte hai?
Hadi woh hai jo Masoom hota hai, jisko Allah muntakhab kare. Kiya Rasool (saww) Ahle Bait (as) ko Sitare nahi bataya? Beshak 14 Sitare hi hamare liye Sahih Raahe Hidayat hain.
Dua e Nudba mein ham yehi to farmate hain:
*...يابن الأنجم الزاهره، يابن السبل الواضحة...*
_"..Aye Chamakte hue Roshan Sitare ke bete, Aye wazeh Raah...."_

Bare Ilaha tere 14 Sitaron ke  saye mein hamari zindagi ko kamyab bana.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Meri beti Fatima (sa) Awwalin se le kar Aakherin khawaatin e Jahan (duniya ki aurato'n) ki Sardar hain. Wo mere badan ka tukda, meri Aankho'n ki Roshni, Mewa e dil aur meri Rooh hai jo mere pehlu ke darmiyan mein hai. Wo insaani shakl mein Hoor hain. Jis waqt Mehraab e Ibadat mein apne Parwardigar ki bargaah mein khadi hoti hain to unka Noor aasmaan ke Farishton ke liye chamakta hai, jis tarah ahl e zameen ke liye aasmaan mein Sitaare chamakte hain."_
(Maarefat e Zahra (sa), p67)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

***********************************
         *5th Jamadi us Sani 1439*
  *22nd February 2018, Thursday,*

                  ♦ _*KHILQAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (858)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَهُوَ الَّذِي أَنْشَأَكُمْ مِنْ نَفْسٍ وَاحِدَةٍ فَمُسْتَقَرٌّ وَمُسْتَوْدَعٌ ۗ قَدْ فَصَّلْنَا الْآيَاتِ لِقَوْمٍ يَفْقَهُونَ*

_"Aur Wohi to hai jisne tumhe ek Jaan se paida kiya. Phir har ek ke liye ek jaye qarar hai aur ek uske sonpe jaane ki jagah hai. Hamne samajh boojh rakhne walon ke liye apni Ayaat khol kar bayan kar di hain."_
(Surah An'am: 98)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah ne is Ayat mein Khilqat ka zikr kiya hai. Guzishta Ayaton ke zel mein ye zikr aa chuka hai.
Allah ne Nafs e Wahid (Ek Jaan) se paida kiya. Iske mukhtalif maana nikale jaa sakte hain. Ek ye ke ham ek Adam ki Aulad hain.
Doosre ye ke Sexual process mein Female Ovum ek jagah mustaqir rahta hai (fix) aur Male Sperm Mustaude' hota hai jo kuchh der ke liye hota hai Ovum mein merge ho kar ek nayi Jaan banta hai. Is tarah ek Nutfe se Insaan ki paidaish hoti hai.
(Tafseer e Namoona)
Isko hadis mein yun farmaya hai:
💫
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Har Shakhs ke liye Rahm e Madar (Womb of Mother) *مستقر* yani Jaye Qarar hai (place of dwelling) aur Sulbha e Pidar (Loins of Father) waqti taur par sonpe jaane ka maqam hai."_
Phir Aap ne farmaya:
_"Imaan bhi do tarah ka hota hai. Ek "Mustaqir" Imaan hota hai jo qaem rahta hai aur jise koi Toofan mutazalzal (hila) nahi kar sakta aur ek Imaan waqti taur par hota hai jo baad mein qaem nahi rahta. Is Imaan ko "Imaan e Mustaude'  *ايمان مستودع* " kaha jata hai."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Roze Ghadeer do Rakat Namaz e Shukrana ada karo. Phir iske baad ye Dua padho: (Aur is Dua mein ye Alfaaz bhi hain):_
_"Khudaya! Ne'mat e Imaan ko hamare Dilon mein "Mustaqir" banana aur ise "Mustawdeh" na banana."_
(Tehzeebul Ahkam)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👥
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)! Main aur aap dono ek teenat (Mitti) se khalq kiye gaye hain. Aur jo mitti us Mitti se bach gayi usse hamare Shiyon ko khalq kiya gaya hai aur jab Qayamat ka Din hoga to logon ko unki Maa ke naam se pukara jayega siwae Aap ke Shiyon ke. Pus unko unke baap ke naam se pukara jaayega, kyun ki unki wiladat paak hai."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p208)

        ♦ _*ALLAH KI KHILQAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (859)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَهُوَ الَّذِي أَنْزَلَ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مَاءً فَأَخْرَجْنَا بِهِ نَبَاتَ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ فَأَخْرَجْنَا مِنْهُ خَضِرًا نُخْرِجُ مِنْهُ حَبًّا مُتَرَاكِبًا وَمِنَ النَّخْلِ مِنْ طَلْعِهَا قِنْوَانٌ دَانِيَةٌ وَجَنَّاتٍ مِنْ أَعْنَابٍ وَالزَّيْتُونَ وَالرُّمَّانَ مُشْتَبِهًا وَغَيْرَ مُتَشَابِهٍ ۗ انْظُرُوا إِلَىٰ ثَمَرِهِ إِذَا أَثْمَرَ وَيَنْعِهِ ۚ إِنَّ فِي ذَٰلِكُمْ لَآيَاتٍ لِقَوْمٍ يُؤْمِنُونَ*

_"Aur Wohi hai jisne Aasman se Paani barsaya. Phir Hamne iske zariye se tamam Nabatat (plants) ugaye. Phir isse hare bhare khet aur darakht (trees) paida kiye. Inse Ham tah bah tah chadhe hue Dane nikalte hain aur Khajoor ke shagufon se Phalon ke guchhe ke guchhe paida kiye jo bojh ki wajah se jhuke hue hain. Aur Angoor, Zaitoon aur Anaar ke Baugh lagai jinke phal ek doosre se milte julte hain aur phir un mein se har ek ki khusoosiyat juda juda bhi hain. Jab ye darakht phalte hain to un mein phal aane aur unke pakne ki kaifiyat ko ghaur se dekho. Imaan rakhne walon ke liye in mein Nishaniyan hain."_
(Surah An'am: 99)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Ali Reza (as):
_"Jaan lo! Khuda tumhe bhalai ki ta'leem de Allah Ta'ala Qadeem *قديم* hai aur *قدم* Uski Sifat hai jo Ahle Aql ko ye Rahnumai faraham karti hai ke isse qabl koi cheez nahi thi aur Uske daem (Everlasting) hone mein koi cheez Uske saath nahi hai aur Uski Baqa' mein koi shay Uske saath nahi hai aur jo log ye guman karte hain ke Khuda se qabl ya Uske saath koi cheez thi, unka qaul batil hai aur agar koi cheez Uske saath Baqa' mein sharik hoti to Woh uska Khaliq na hota kyonki pahle se maujood cheez ko khalq karna be maani hai. Agar isse qabl koi aur cheez hoti to wo Awwal hoti, ye na hota, aur Awwal cheez sani (second) cheez ki Khaliq hoti."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🍁
Imam Reza (as):
(Also Imam Sadiq (as))
_"Bando ke Afa'al Makhlooq hain lekin unki Khilqat ki noiyyat Taqdeeri hai Takveeni hai hai. Allah ne har cheez ko khalq kiya. Ham Jabr o Tafveez ka Aqeeda nahi rakhte."_
_"Bando ki Takhleeq se 2000 Saal qabl bando ke Aamaal Allah ke Ilm mein Muqaddar the."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Kitabul Khisaal)

Note: Ek firqa Insaan ke Aamaal mein Jabr (compulsion) ka nazariya rakhta hai jabke doosre Tafweez ka Aqeeda rakhta tha yani free will, poori azadi ka qael tha. Ahle Bait (as) ka Aqeeda "Amr bainal Amrain" ka Aqeeda hai yani Jabr aur Tafveez ke beech ka raasta. Iski detail Adl ke topic mein ho chuki hai.
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha jaise Tu ne is Duniya mein Apni Ne'maton se nawaza hai Akherat mein isse behtar ata karna.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌧
Imam Ali (as)
_"Beshak! Sahibaan e Aql ko Adab (good manners / achche akhlaaq) (sikhne) ki aisi hi zarurat hai jaise pyaasi kheti ko baarish ki ehtiyaaj (zarurat) hoti hai."_
(Gorar ul Hakam, v1, p69)

                     ♦ _*JINN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (860)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَجَعَلُوا لِلَّهِ شُرَكَاءَ الْجِنَّ وَخَلَقَهُمْ ۖ وَخَرَقُوا لَهُ بَنِينَ وَبَنَاتٍ بِغَيْرِ عِلْمٍ ۚ سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَىٰ عَمَّا يَصِفُونَ * بَدِيعُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ ۖ أَنَّىٰ يَكُونُ لَهُ وَلَدٌ وَلَمْ تَكُنْ لَهُ صَاحِبَةٌ ۖ وَخَلَقَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ ۖ وَهُوَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ * ذَٰلِكُمُ اللَّهُ رَبُّكُمْ ۖ لَا إِلَٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ ۖ خَالِقُ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ فَاعْبُدُوهُ ۚ وَهُوَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَكِيلٌ*

_"(Iske bawajood) logon ne Jinnat ko Khuda ka sharik thaira liya halanki Khuda ne unhe paida kiya hai aur unhone apni jihalat se Khuda ke liye Bete aur Betiyan bana dalin halanki Woh in Ausaaf se Paak o Pakeezah hai jo ye bayan kar rahe hain."_
_"Woh Aasmaano aur Zameen ka mujid (Originator) hai. Uske haan Beta kaise hoga jabke Uske haan to koi Biwi hi nahi hai aur Usi ne tamam cheezon ko paida kiya aur Woh tamam cheezon ka Jannewala hai."_
_"Wohi Allah to tumhara Rab hai. Uske alawa koi Ma'bood nahi hai. Woh har Shay ka Khaliq hai. Tum sab Usi ki Ibaadat karo aur Woh har cheez ka Kafeel hai."_
(Surah An'am: 100 - 102)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Mushrekin ke Batil Aqaed ka tazkara hai.
Arab mein Jinn ki pooja hoti thi. Ek qabeela jiska naam Banu Teeh jiska yehi Aqeeda tha. (Kitab Al Asnaam)
Rome, Unaan aur India mein bhi yahi Aqeeda paya jaata hai. (Tafseer Al Munar) India mein Jinn ko Rakshash kaha jata hai jo ke aaj bhi Hindu iski pooja karte hain.
Qur'an mein Sura Saffat: 159 mein ye bhi zikr hai ke woh Allah aur Jinn mein rishtedari ke qael hain. Quraish ka pahle ye Aqeeda tha ke Khuda ki Jinn se shaadi hui aur Farishte us Shaadi ka natija hain. (Majmaul Bayan)
Qur'an ne Surah Zukhruf: 19 mein zikr hai ke woh Farishton ko Betiyan tasawwur karte hai. Christians Hazrat Esa (as) aur Yahoodi Hazrat Ozair (as) ko ko Khuda ka Beta tasawwur karte hain.
Jabke haqeeqat ye hai ke Allah ko koi family ki zaroorat nahi. Agar aisa hota to Woh majboor hota. Aur Allah Majboor nahi.
📚
Ashairah Jabr ke qael hain isliye unka nazarya hai ke jaisa ke har cheez ka Khaliq Khuda hai to hamare Afa'al (actions) ka bhi Khaliq Wohi hai.
Jabke Ahle Bait (as) ki Taa'leemat mein jaisa ke hamne pahle bataya "Amr bainul Amrain hai"
Agar Afa'al ka Khaliq Khuda hai to ye Jabr hua. Agar Afa'al mein Jabr hai to phir Jaza aur Saza be Maana (meaningless) hua. Nabiyon wa Hadiyon ko bhejna bhi bekar maana jayega. Jabke Ayatul Kursi mein hai ke Deen mein koi Jabr nahi.
Pas sahi Aqeeda ye hai ke ham hamare Afa'al mein poora ikhtiyar rakhte hain, chahe Khair karen ya bad.

Bare Ilaha hame aise behooda Aqeedon se aur Jinnon ke shar se mehfooz rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sajjad (as)
_"Haddiyo’n ko saaf na karo ke isme Jinno’n ka bhi hissa hai aur agar saaf kar daaloge to wo is se zyada qeemati cheezein tumhare ghar se le jayenge."_
(Tehzeeb e Aal e Muhammad (as), p79)

          ♦ _*DEEDAR-E-KHUDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (861)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَا تُدْرِكُهُ الْأَبْصَارُ وَهُوَ يُدْرِكُ الْأَبْصَارَ ۖ وَهُوَ اللَّطِيفُ الْخَبِيرُ*

_*"Nigahen Usko nahin paa sakti aur Woh Nigahon ko paa leta hai. Woh nihayat bareek Been aur Ba Khabar hai."*_
(Surah An'am: 103)

📚📖 👁
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Ali Reza (as):
_"Absaar *ابصار*" se murad ye Ankhen nahi. Dil ke Auhaam Aankho ki Baseeraton se kahin zyada hote hain. Ayat ka maqsad ye hai ke Auhaam *اوهام* Use nahi paa sakte jabke Woh Auhaam ko paa sakta hai. Dilon ke Auhaam Aankho Basaraton se kahin daqeeq hote hain. Tum apne wahem mein Sindh, Hind aur doosre shahron ka tasawwur kar sakte ho jo tumne nahi dekhe. Jabke Dilon ke Auhaam Khuda ko nahin paa sakte to Ankhon ki Basaraten Use kaise paa sakti hain."_
Imam Sadiq (as) se bhi is tarah ki Rivayat hai.
👀
Imam Sadiq (as) se Ismael bin Fazl ne sawal kiya: "Kya Qayamat ke Din Allah ka Deedar naseeb hoga?"
Imam (as) be farmaya:
_"Khuda dikhai dene se kahin buland o bartar hai. Ibne Fazl! Yaad rakho *Aankhen usi cheez ko dekh sakti hain jiska koi rang aur jiski koi kaifiyat ho. Allah Rangon aur Kaifiyaat ka Khaliq hai."*_
_"Allah ki Zaat ke mutalliq ghaur o fikr na karo isse tumhari sargardani wa hairaani mein hi izaafa hoga kyonki Aankhen Use paane se qasir (helpless) hain aur  Use miqdar ke saath Mausoof nahi kiya jaa sakta."_
(Tauheed e Sudooq, Usoole Kaafi, Amaali e Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)
👁
Jabke aam Musalmanon ka ye Aqeeda hai:
👀
Adi bin Hatim se rivayat hai:
_"Tum mein se koi nahi hoga siwae iske uska Rab usse baate karega aur Uske aur unke darmiyan na koi tashreeh karne wala ya koi pardah hael nahi hoga."_
(Means Allah unse direct ru baru hoga)
(Shahih Bukhari, Vol 9, Book 93, Hadith 535 )
👀
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Yaqeenan tum tumhare Rab ko aise dekhoge jaise tum Chaand ko dekhte ho. Usko dekhne mein tumhe koi dushwari nahi hogi."_
(Sahih Bukhari, Vol 1, Book 10, Hadith 529)
👀
_"Qayamat ke Din Uska Deedar hoga."_
(Sunni Tafseer Al Munar, Vol 7, P-653)
👀
Imam Ali Reza (as) se poochha gaya ke Khuda Deedar mein ikhtelaf hai? Haqeeqat kya hai?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Jo Khuda ki Wasf (Attributes) aisi Sifat se kare ke Khuda ne is Sifat se Apni Wasf bayan na ki ho to us ne Khuda par bohtan tarasha. (Ayat 6:103) Isse Dil ki Aankhen murad hain aur Khuda Auhaam (Imaginations) ki sarhad se Buland o Bala hai, Auhaam Uski Mahiyyat *ماهيت* ke idraak se qasir/aajiz hain."_
(Majmaul Bayan)

Qur'an ye Ayat pesh ki jaati hai jaise:
_"Us Din kuchh chehre Pur tarawat aur Pur Raunaq honge aur apne Parwardigar ko dekh rahe honge."_ (Qayamat: 23,24)

Is Ayat ke bare mein Imam Sadiq (as) ke sawal kiya to unhone farmaya:
_"Ye baat kitni buri hai ke insaan 70-80 saal umr guzare, Khuda ke Mulk mein zindagi basar kare aur Uski Ne'mat khaata rahe lekin Usko Sahih tarah se ba pahchanne. Paighambar (saww) ne hargiz Khuda ko is Aankh se nahi dekha. Mushaheda do qism ka hota hai ek Dil ki Aankh se dekhna aur doosre zahiri Aankh se dekhna. Jo shakhs Dil ki Aankh se Mushahede ki baat kahta hai wo to Sahih hai aur jo shakhs zahiri Aankh se Khuda ke Mushahede ki baat karta hai woh jhoot bolta hai aur Khuda aur Uski Ayaat ka Kaafir o Munkir hai. Kyonki Paighambar (saww) ne farmaya ke jo shakhs Khuda ko Makhlooq ke mushabeh (Similar) samjhe woh Kafir hai."_
(Ma'anil Akhbar, Al Mizaan Vol 8, P-268)

Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Musa (as) se bhi jab deedar ka sawal kiya to jawab aya:
*قَالَ لَنْ تَرَانِي* (A'raf 143)
_"Kabhi bhi nahi dekh sakte."_
(Mazeed same topic par tazkara Baqarah: 46 ke zel mein kiya gaya hai.)

Bare Ilaha hame zameen par maujood Tere Ayatullah e Muazzam (atfs) ka jald az jald deedar ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

       ♦ _*LATEEF & KHABEER*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (862)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَدْ جَاءَكُمْ بَصَائِرُ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ ۖ فَمَنْ أَبْصَرَ فَلِنَفْسِهِ ۖ وَمَنْ عَمِيَ فَعَلَيْهَا ۚ وَمَا أَنَا عَلَيْكُمْ بِحَفِيظٍ * وَكَذَٰلِكَ نُصَرِّفُ الْآيَاتِ وَلِيَقُولُوا دَرَسْتَ وَلِنُبَيِّنَهُ لِقَوْمٍ يَعْلَمُونَ*

_"Tumhare Rab ki taraf se tumhare paas Baseerat ki Roshniyan aa chuki hain ab jo binaayi se kaam le to uska apna bhala hoga aur jo andhepan ka saboot de to woh apna hi nuqsan karega aur main tum par koi Paasban (Guardian) laga hua nahi hun."_
_"Is tarah Ham Apni Ayaat ko mukhtalif tareeqon se bayan karte hain aur woh isliye karte hain ke woh log kahen ke tum kisi se padh aye ho aur jo log Ilm rakhte hain un par Ham Haqeeqat ko Roshan kar den."_
(Surah An'am: 104 - 105)

📚📖 👁 (Cont'd.......)
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaat mein Allah ki kuchh Sifaat ka zikr hua. Allah Lateef aur Khabeer hai. Tumhara Muhafiz Rasool (saww) nahi balke Allah hai.
👀
*Lateef:*
Imam Musa Kazim (as):
_"Jab ham Khuda ko "Lateef *لطيف*" kahte hain to mafhoom ye hota hai ke Woh Bareek Been (Subtle) hai. Woh un cheezon ko bhi dekhta hai jinhen hassae chishm (Eye Sight) se mahsoos nahi kiya jaa sakta. Woh intihai bareek Jadi Bootiyon ko hi nahi dekhta balke un mein wadi'at kardah asaraat o khwaas ko bhi dekhta hai. Woh Machhar aur usse zyada bareek Makhlooq ko dekhta hai aur Woh ye bhi dekhta hai ke woh apni zindagi ke taqazon ki kis tarah se takmeel karte hain. Woh Samandaron mein Rihaish Pazeer Jaraseemon (Ocean Germs) ki zindagi ke dauraniyon ko bhi dekh raha hai aur Woh ye dekhta hai ke Woh Jaandar apna Rizq kahan se hasil karte hain aur Aulad ko kaise palte hain aur apne jinsi taqazon (Sexual Needs) ki takmeel kaise karte hain. Al gharz Jise doosri Aankhen na dekh saken Khuda kisi aalaat ke baghair unhe dekhta hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
👀
Imam Mohd Taqi (as):
_".... Jab ham in cheezon par ghaur karte hain to ham kahte hain ke Allah "Lateef" hai magar Woh Kaifiyat ke baghair hai. Kaifiyat to Makhlooq ke liye makhsoos hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
👀
Imam Ali Reza (as):
_"Lafz " *لطيف*" ka kisi qillat aur daqeeq (Deep) cheez ki wajah se Khuda par itlaaq nahi kiya jata. Khuda ke "Lateef" hone ka ye maqsad hai ke Uske liye koi "Hadd-Limit" muqarrar nahi ki ja sakti aur kisi Wasf (Attributes) ke saath Usko mehdood (Limit) nahi kiya ja sakta."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🗞
*Khabeer:*
Imam Ali Reza (as):
_"Lafz "Khabeer *خبير*" ka itlaaq Khaliq par hota hai aur Makhlooq par bhi hota hai lekin dono ke Ma'ani mein farq hota hai. Khuda us Ma'ani mein "Khabeer" hai ke Kainat ka har zarrah Uske saamne maujood hai aur Use zarre zarre ki Khabar hai. Aur Makhlooq ko Khabeer kahne ki wajah ye hai ke Makhlooq ke paas thodi si khabar hoti hai aur woh bhi tajarbe ki buniyad par hasil hoti hai jabke Khuda ko Tajarbe ki zaroorat nahi hai."_
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
📝
Makka ke Quraish Nabi e Akram (saww) par ye ilzaam aaed kiya karte the ke 'Aap hamen jo baten sunate hain unhein Aap Ulama e Yahood se seekhte hain.'
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi)
🤲🏻
_"Parwardigaar! Mujhe aur meri Aulaad ko (bhi) Namaz ka paband bana de aur mere Paalne-waale! Meri Dua qubool farma."_
(Ibrahim, Ayat 40)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ _*ITTABA HUKM-E-ILAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (863)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*اتَّبِعْ مَا أُوحِيَ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ رَبِّكَ ۖ لَا إِلَٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ ۖ وَأَعْرِضْ عَنِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ * وَلَوْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ مَا أَشْرَكُوا ۗ وَمَا جَعَلْنَاكَ عَلَيْهِمْ حَفِيظًا ۖ وَمَا أَنْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ بِوَكِيلٍ*

_"Aap us Waḥy ki pairavi karen jo Aap ke Rab ki taraf se Aap par nazil hui hai. Uske siwa koi Ma'bood nahi hai aur Mushrekin se rukh mod len."_
_"Agar Allah chahta to Woh jabran unko Shirk se rok sakta tha. Hamne Aapko un par Pasban (Guardian) muqarrar nahi kiya hai aur na tum un par Nigehban ho."_
(Surah An'am: 106 - 107)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Tafseer e Ahle Bait (as) mein waarid hai ke Allah chahta to sab ko Jabre Mashiyat se Momin o Masoom bhi bana sakta tha aur koi bhi Uski nafarmani na kar sakta. Aur agar Khuda aisa karta to Use na Jannat banane ki zaroorat hoti aur na Dozakh banane ki ehtiyaj hoti lekin Allah ne kisi se Jabri Ita'at nahi karai. Khuda ne unhe quwwat o taqat aur Aql ata farmayi. Iske baad Usne kuchh Umoor (Orders) baja laane ka Hukm diya aur kuchh Umoor se mana' kiya aur unka Imtihan liya aur un par Hujjat tamam ki taake log Sawab o Etaab ke Haqdar ban saken.
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha hame Tere Imtihan mein kamyabi ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Riwayat:
_*Banda Na Bilkul Majboor Hai Na Mukhtar:*_

Fazal bin Sahal ne Imam Reza (as) se Mamun ke Darbar mein sawal kiya: _"Ye farmaiye ke kya Bande majboor hain?"_ 
Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Khuda Aadil hai. Ye mumkin nahi ke Wo logon se jabran Gunah karaye aur phir us par unko saza de"._
Fazal ne kaha:
_"Achcha, to phir bilkul azad hain?"_
Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Nahi. Uski (Allah ki) hikmat se ye baeed hai ke Wo Apne Bande ko bilkul azad Naqaa e be-mehaar (camel without strings / belagaam Oo'nt) ki tarah chhor de"._
(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v5, p177)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

        *11th Jamadi us Sani 1439*

                   ♦ _*GAALI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (864)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تَسُبُّوا الَّذِينَ يَدْعُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ فَيَسُبُّوا اللَّهَ عَدْوًا بِغَيْرِ عِلْمٍ ۗ كَذَٰلِكَ زَيَّنَّا لِكُلِّ أُمَّةٍ عَمَلَهُمْ ثُمَّ إِلَىٰ رَبِّهِمْ مَرْجِعُهُمْ فَيُنَبِّئُهُمْ بِمَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ*

_"Aur tum unhe (Buton) galiyan na do jinhe ye log Allah ke siwa pukarte hain. Kahin aisa na ho ke ye jihalat o ziyadti karte hue Allah ko galiyan dene lag jayen aur is tarah se Hamne har giroh ke amal ko khushnuma bana diya. Phir inhe apne Parwardigar ki taraf hi laut kar aana hai, us waqt Woh inhe bata dega ke woh kya karte rahe hain."_
(Surah An'am: 108)

----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚📖 🤫
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Taurat mein Allah ne Hazrat Musa (as) se farmaya:_
_"Musa! Mere Raaz apne Dil mein poshida rakho aur Mere Dushmano se bhi khatiro madarat ka sulook rawa rakho aur mere Makhfi Raaz (Hidden Secrets) zahir karke Mujhe Galiyan mat dilwao warna Mere Dushman ke saath tum bhi Mujh par Gali galoch mein sharik qarar paoge."_
(Usoole Kaafi)
🤫
Raavi ne Imam Sadiq (as) se is Ayat ke bare mein sawal kiya. Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Kabhi tumne dekha hai ke koi Khuda ko Galiyan bak raha ho?"_
Raavi ne kaha nahi.
Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Jo Allah ke Vali ko Gali de to usne Khuda ko gali di."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)
🤫
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Khabardar! Dushmanane Khuda ko sunwa kar galiyan na dena warna woh jahalat o nadani ki wajah se Khuda ko Galiyan dene lag jayege."_
(Usoole Kaafi, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)
🚩
Imam Ali Reza (as):
_"Hamare Mukhalefin ne hamare Fazael ke mutalliq Ahadees ghadi hain aur isse unke teen maqasid wabasta hain. Inki tarash kardah kuchh Rivayaat "Ghulu- *غلو*" par mushtamil hain. Kuchh Rivayaat "Taqseer- *تقصير*" par mushtamil hain aur kuchh Rivayaat unhone aisi tarashi hain jin mein hamare Dushman ke naam le kar Uyoob bayan kiye hain."_
_"Jab log Ghaliyana Rivayaat sunenge to woh hamare Shiyon ko Kafir kahenge aur log ye kahenge ke Shia Ahle Bait (as) ko Rab maante hain aur jab log Taqseer par mabni Rivayaat sunenge to woh hamare liye Taqseer par mabni Aqeeda rakhenge. Aur jab log ye sunenge ke Ahle Bait (as) ne naam le kar apne Dushmano ke Uyoob bayan kiye hain to log bhi naam le kar hamko galiyan denge. Jabke Allah Ta'ala ne ye Ayat nazil farmayi (6:108)"_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Noorus Saqlain)
📌
Tabarrah ke maani Gali dena nahi hai. Tabarrah yani Dushman se Nafrat wa bezaari ka izhaar karna. Sirf ye Zahir karna ke aap Dushman e Islam se khush nahi hain. Iska matlab Gali dena nahi hai. Gali ki Islam kisi tarah se ijazat nahi deta. Balke ghair ke saamne mun ba mun naam le kar bura bhala kahne ki sakht mumaniyat hai kyonki isse fasaad ho sakta hai, jabke Islam Amn ka Mazhab hai.
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hamare dil mein Tere Dushman se itni nafrat bhar de jitni mein Tujh se Muhabbat karta hun.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

                 ♦ _*MO'JEZA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (865)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَأَقْسَمُوا بِاللَّهِ جَهْدَ أَيْمَانِهِمْ لَئِنْ جَاءَتْهُمْ آيَةٌ لَيُؤْمِنُنَّ بِهَا ۚ قُلْ إِنَّمَا الْآيَاتُ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ ۖ وَمَا يُشْعِرُكُمْ أَنَّهَا إِذَا جَاءَتْ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ*

_"Aur un logon ne Allah ki Qasamen kha kar kaha hai ke agar Khuda ki taraf se hamare paas koi Nishani (Ayat) aayi to ham us par zaroor Imaan layenge. Aap kah den ke Nishaniyan to Allah ke paas hai. Aur tumhe kaise maloom ho jab Nishaniyan aa bhi jayen to bhi yeh Imaan nahi layenge."_
(Surah An'am: 109)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat ki shaane Nuzool mein hai ke Kuffar e Quraish ke ek giroh ne Rasoole Akram (saww) se Mo'jezat aur Khuda ki Nishaniyon ki jhalak dikhane ka taqaza kiya to Rasoole Akram (saww) ne Allah se Dua ki to jawab ke taur par ye Ayat nazil hui.
(Tafseer e Namoona)

Mo'jeza dekhane ke bhi maqasid hain. Iska istemal sirf entertainment ke liye nahi hota. Chamatkar karke apni badhai ka izhar ya fakhro o mubahat maqsad nahi. Yahan maqsad sirf Allah ki Nishani bata kar Khuda ki Qudrat ka izhar karna hai.
Jab Anbiya ko pata hota hai ke in logon ko Mo'jeza dekhane par bhi koi farq nahi padne wala to woh is par amal nahi karte the.

Bare Ilaha hame Teri Akheri Nishani ke Didar ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Aye Ali (as)! Tum aur tumhare farzandon mein se Imam mere baad khalq par *Hujjat e Khuda* hain. Aur bandon mein *Raah e Khuda ki Nishaani hain. (Ayatullah)* Jis shakhs ne in mein se kisi ek ka inkar kiya aur jisne in mein se kisi ek ki nafarmani ki to usne meri nafarmani ki. Aur jisne in mein se kisi par zulm kiya, usne mujh par jafaa ki. Aur jisne tumhare saath muhabbat aur Neki ka bartav kiya to usne mere saath muhabbat o neki ka bartav kiya. Aur jisne tumhari ita'at ki, usne meri ita'at ki. Aur jisne tumse dosti ki usne mujh se dosti ki aur jisne tumse dushmani ki usne mujh se dushmani ki, kyunki tum mujh se aur mere Sulb se paida huwe ho aur main tumse hun."_
(Isbaat e Imamat - Allamah Majlisi, p62)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ _*HAT DHARMI KA ETAAB*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (866)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَنُقَلِّبُ أَفْئِدَتَهُمْ وَأَبْصَارَهُمْ كَمَا لَمْ يُؤْمِنُوا بِهِ أَوَّلَ مَرَّةٍ وَنَذَرُهُمْ فِي طُغْيَانِهِمْ يَعْمَهُونَ*

_"Hamne unke Dilon aur Nigahon ko pher rahe hain jis tarah se ye pahli martaba is Kitab par Imaan nahi laye. Ham unko unki sarkashi (transgressions) mein bhatakne ke liye chhod dete hain."_
(Surah An'am: 110)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein jin logon ka zikr hua unhi ke bare mein Allah Ta'ala is Ayat mein tazkara kar raha hai. Yeh woh log hain jo apni hat dharmi par date rahte hain.
⚔
Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Log sab se pahle Jihad se inheraf karenge. Logo! Apne haathon se Jihad karo. Agar haathon se mumkin na ho to zaban se Jihad karo. Agar zaban se mumkin na ho to phir apne Dil se hi Jihad karo. Jis shakhs ka Dil Neki ko Neki aur Burai ko Burai na samjhe to uske Dil ko ulat diya jata hai. Uske upar wala hissa niche aur niche wala hissa upar kar diya jata hai. Phir woh kabhi kisi achhi baat ko qubool nahi karta. Jaisa ke Ayat mein hai: (6:110)"_
(Imam Mohd Baqir (as) se bhi aisi rivayat hai.)
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

Tafaseer e Ahle Bait (as) mein marqoom hai ke iska mafhoom ye hai ke Allah logon ko Imaan laane par majboor nahi karega balke unke haal par chhod deta hai.
(Majmaul Bayan)

Bare Ilaha hame hamesha Apne Layeq Bando mein shumar karna.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sajjad (as)
_"Jab hamara Qaim (atfs) qayam karega to Allah Shiyo'n ke jismaani uyoob ko bartaraf kar dega (Allah will remove the physical defects of Shias), unke dilo'n ko Koh e Aahan (iron mountain / lohe ke pahaad) ki maanind (mazboot) kar dega aur ek Shia ki quwwat 40 afraad jitni kar dega aur ye log zameen ke hukkaam (rulers) aur uske buzurgaan honge."_
(Khisaal, p335)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

               ♦ _*HATDHARMI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (867)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَوْ أَنَّنَا نَزَّلْنَا إِلَيْهِمُ الْمَلَائِكَةَ وَكَلَّمَهُمُ الْمَوْتَىٰ وَحَشَرْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ قُبُلًا مَا كَانُوا لِيُؤْمِنُوا إِلَّا أَنْ يَشَاءَ اللَّهُ وَلَٰكِنَّ أَكْثَرَهُمْ يَجْهَلُونَ*

_"Aur agar Ham unki taraf Farishton ko nazil karte aur Murde unse kalam karte aur Ham har cheez unki Ankhon ke saamne jama kar dete tab bhi ye Imaan na laate. Albatta Mashiyat e Ilahi isse mustashna (exception) hai. Lekin unki aksariyat Jihalat mein mubtila hai."_
(Surah An'am: 111)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat ka zikr guzishta Ayaton se marboot hai. In Ayaton mein Kafiron aur Mushrekin ki hatdharmiyan ko zahir kiya gaya hai. Jaisa ke unhone bahut se taqaze kiye jaise Allah ko dekhna, koi Mo'jeza dekhana waghaira. Balke woh Qasmen bhi khaate the ke woh Imaan le ayenge lekin Khuda ne is ayat bata diya ke agar unke saamne Farishta bhi aa jaye, ya unse ek Murda bhi bolne lage tab bhi ye Imaan nahi layenge.
Iski wajah unki Jihalat hai. Jaisa ke pahle bhi explain kar chuke hain, agar Allah chahta to apni Qudrat se sab ko Momin bana deta lekin ye Uski Adalat ke khilaf hota. Isko aisa samjha ja sakta ke ek Teacher apne Student se exam le aur wohi usko copy karne de, to exam meaningless ho jayega, ye Student ke saath ghair insaafi hogi, kyonki woh jahil ka jahil hi rahega.

Bare Ilaha hamare Ilm mein izaafa farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📖🖊
Riwayat
Ek roz Paigambar e Akram (saww) Masjid mein dakhil huwe to dekha ke kuchh log ek shakhs ko ghere huwe baithe hain. Aap (saww) ne sawaal kiya:
_"Ye kaun hai?"_ 
As'haab ne arz ki,
_"Ye 'Allamah' hai"._
Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Kis cheez ka Aalim hai?"_ 

As'haab ne jawaab diya:
_"Arabon ke Ansaab (lineage / vansh), waqiyat aur daur e Jahiliyyat ke Asha'ar ka ilm hai"._
To Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Ye to ek aisa Ilm hai ke agar koi isse jaahil ho to uska koi nuqsan na hoga aur jo jaanta hai usko usse koi fayda hone wala nahi hai. Ilm sirf 3 tarah ka hota hai:_
_*Aqaed, Akhlaqiyat aur Ilm e Ahkaam e Shariyat.*_
_Inke alawa baaqi sab izaafi cheezein hain"._
(Adaab e Islami, v2, p44)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

               ♦ _*SHAYATEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (868)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَكَذَٰلِكَ جَعَلْنَا لِكُلِّ نَبِيٍّ عَدُوًّا شَيَاطِينَ الْإِنْسِ وَالْجِنِّ يُوحِي بَعْضُهُمْ إِلَىٰ بَعْضٍ زُخْرُفَ الْقَوْلِ غُرُورًا ۚ وَلَوْ شَاءَ رَبُّكَ مَا فَعَلُوهُ ۖ فَذَرْهُمْ وَمَا يَفْتَرُونَ*

_"Aur is tarah se Hamne har Nabi ke Dushman bahut se Shaitan paida kiye the, kuchh Insaan aur kuchh Jinn, jin mein se baaz baazon ko chikni Chapri baton ka waswasa dalte rahte the taake unko dhoke mein daal den aur agar tumhara Rab chahta to woh aisa na kar sakte. Aap unhe aur unke iftrapardaziyon ko chhod den."_
(Surah An'am: 112)

📚📖 👺
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ne jitne bhi Nabi bheje un sab ki Ummat mein do Shaitan aise rakhe jo unhe aziyyat dete the aur unke baad unki Ummat ko gumrah karte the. Nooh (as) ke Dushman Faqantayqoos ( *فقنطيقوس*) aur Hazam ( *حزام*) the. Ibrahim (as) ke Dushman Kalthal ( *كلثل*) aur Razam ( *رزام*) the aur Musa (as) ke Dushman Samari ( *سامرى*) aur Mura'qeeba ( *مرعقيبا*) the aur Esa (as) ke Dushman Polas ( *پولس*) aur Maritoon ( *مريتون*) the aur Muhammad Mustafa (saww) ke Dushman Jastar ( *جستر*) aur Zareeq ( *زريق*) the."_
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)
👹
Imam Sadiq (as):
“Jinhe Ahle Haq ke Sifat ka hamil Khuda ne banaya ho to Ins o Jinn se talluq rakhne wale Shayateen hain."_
(Usool e Kaafi)
😈
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Khutba e Ghadeer mein ye farmaya:
_"Agah raho! Ali (as) ke Dushman Ahle Shiqaq hain aur woh tajawuz karne wale hain aur Shayateen ke woh bhai band hain jo ek doosre ki taraf Dunyavi zeenat ki pur fareb baton ka ilqa kiya karte hain."_
(Ehtejaaj Tabarsi)
💩
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Shayateen ek doosre se mulaqat karte hain to woh ek doosre ko gumrah karne ke taur tareeqe ilqa karte hain aur woh ek doosre se gumrah karne ki taleem hasil karte hain."_
(Majmaul Bayan)

🤲🏻
*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*
*قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ النَّاسِ * مَلِكِ النَّاسِ * إِلَٰهِ النَّاسِ * مِنْ شَرِّ الْوَسْوَاسِ الْخَنَّاسِ * الَّذِي يُوَسْوِسُ فِي صُدُورِ النَّاسِ * مِنَ الْجِنَّةِ وَالنَّاسِ*(Surah Nas 1 - 6)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👤👥
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Logon ki 3 qismen hain:_
_(1) Jo Arshe Ilahi ke saye mein hogi. Jis Din Uske saye ke alawa koi saya nahi hoga._
_(2) Jinhe Hisaab o Azaab ke marahil tay karne padenge._
_(3) Jin ke chehre Insaano jaise hain aur unke Dil Shayateen jaise hain."_
(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

        ♦ _*JABR O MASHIYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (869)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلِتَصْغَىٰ إِلَيْهِ أَفْئِدَةُ الَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِالْآخِرَةِ وَلِيَرْضَوْهُ وَلِيَقْتَرِفُوا مَا هُمْ مُقْتَرِفُونَ*

_"(Aur Hamne Jabr e Mashiyat se isliye kaam nahi liya) taak jo log Akherat par Imaan nahi rakhte unke Dil uski taraf mael (incline) hon aur woh is par khush ho jayen aur aisi buraiyan sar anjam den jinhe woh sar anjam dena chahte hain."_
(Surah An'am: 113)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat guzishta Ayat ke topic ka continuation hai. Guzishta Ayat mein ye zikr tha ke 'agar tumhara Rab chahta to woh aisa (Gunah) na kar sakte.' Is bare mein ham pahle bhi explain kar chuke hain, mazeed hadis mulaheza farmayen.

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Aamal 3 tarah ke hain:_
_(1) Faraez_ ( *فرائض*)
_(2) Fazael_ ( *فضائل*)
_(3) Ma'asi_ ( *معاصى*)
_Aur jahan tak Ma'asi ka talluq hai to iska talluq Amr e Khuda se Nahi hai albatta Khuda ki Qaza o Qadar aur Mashiyat o Ilm se iska wasta hai, Allah us par Saza dega."_
(Kitabul Khisaal)
📌
'Ma'asi ka talluq Allah ki Qaza (Faisle) se hai,' ke jumle ka mafhoom ye hai iska talluq Allah ki Nahy *نهى*(Prohibition) se hai kyonki Allah ne isse rukne ka hukm diya hai aur 'Ma'asi ka talluq Qadar e Khuda wandi se hai,' ke is jumle ka maqsad ye hai ke Allah Uske Mubligh, Andaze aur Miqdar ko Jaanta hai. Aur 'Ma'asi (Gunehgar) ka talluq Khuda ki Mashiyat se hai,' ke is Jumle ka maqsad ye hai ke Khuda nahi chahta ke kisi Gunah karne wale ko Jabran Gunah se rok de albatta khuda ne Qaul o Nahy aur Waeed (Warnings) se burai karne walon ko mana kiya hai lekin Apni Qudrat e Kamila se kisi ko burai se nahi roka.
(Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
*..فأسئلك بالقدرة التى قدرتها و بالقضية التي حتمتها و حكمتها و غلبت من عليه أجريتها.....*
_"Khudaya! Mere Sardar! Mein Teri Muqaddar kardah Qudrat aur Teri Hatmi Hikmat o Qazawat aur har Mahfil e Nifaz par Ghalib aanewali Azmat ka hawala de kar Tujh se sawal karta hun ke mujhe isi Raat mein aur isi waqt Ma'af kar de....."_
(Dua-e-Kumail)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤲🏻
Hadees e Qudsi
Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: _""Mere Bando'n! 6 cheezein tumhari taraf se hain aur 6 meri taraf se hain:_
_(1) Tauba karna tumhara kaam hai aur Ma'af farmana Mera kaam hai,_
_(2) Ita'at tumhari hogi, Jannat hamari taraf se hogi,_
_(3) Shukr tumhari taraf se hoga, Rizq hamari taraf  se hoga,_
_(4) Reza tumhari jaanib se hogi, Qaza Meri jaanib se hogi,_
_(5) Sabr tumhari taraf se hoga, aazmaish Meri taraf se hogi,_
_(6) Dua tumhari taraf se hogi aur qubuliyyat Meri taraf se hogi._
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p368)

                 ♦ _*JUDGE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (870)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَفَغَيْرَ اللَّهِ أَبْتَغِي حَكَمًا وَهُوَ الَّذِي أَنْزَلَ إِلَيْكُمُ الْكِتَابَ مُفَصَّلًا ۚ وَالَّذِينَ آتَيْنَاهُمُ الْكِتَابَ يَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّهُ مُنَزَّلٌ مِنْ رَبِّكَ بِالْحَقِّ ۖ فَلَا تَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْمُمْتَرِينَ*

_"Kiya mein Allah ke alawa koi aur Hukm talash karun halanki Woh to Wohi hai jis ne tumhari taraf mufassal Kitab nazil ki hai. Jin logon. Ko Hamne Kitab di hai woh jaante hain ke yeh Kitab tumhare Rab ki taraf se Haq ke saath nazil ki gayi hai lehaza tum shak karne walon mein se hargiz na banna."_
(Surah An'am: 114)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
"Hakam *حكم*" means Arbitration, yani jab koi dispute hota hai to ham kisi Neutral shakhs jo Haq goyi aur Adl se kaam leta ho, Insaafwar ho, use faisle ke liye muntakhab kiya jata hai. Lekin Dunyavi Judge ko aksar dekha gaya hai ke woh bhi bik jaate hain aur ghair munsifana faisla kar dete hain. Aisa hi ek waqea hame Amr Aas ki harkat ka nazar aya jisne Moaviya ke haq mein faisla kiya. Abhi haliya daur mein Bohra ke do Leader jo apni aapko Dayi ke dawedar the, apne Deeni leaders ke faisle ke liye Dunyavi Court mein chale gaye, yani Boriyon ke Mazhabi leader ko court muntakhab karegi.
Ye sab isliye tab hota hai jab Allah ke alawa ham ghair ko apna Judge maante hain. Sare jhagde ki jad ye hai ke Insaan ka Allah par eteqaad kamzor ho gaya hai.
Jabke Allah Qur'an mein farmata hai:
*وَمَا كَانَ لِمُؤْمِنٍ وَلَا مُؤْمِنَةٍ إِذَا قَضَى اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَمْرًا أَنْ يَكُونَ لَهُمُ الْخِيَرَةُ مِنْ أَمْرِهِمْ ۗ وَمَنْ يَعْصِ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ فَقَدْ ضَلَّ ضَلَالًا مُبِينًا*
(Surah Ahzab: 36)
_"Kisi Momin Mard aur Aurat ko ye haq nahi ke jab Allah aur Uska Rasool kisi maamle ka faisla kar de to phir use apne is maamle mein khud faisla karne ka ikhtiyar hasil rahe aur jo koi Allah aur Uske Rasool ki nafarmani kare to woh sarihan gumrahi mein padegi"_

To jab Ghadeer mein Allah aur Uske Rasool (saww) ne Ali (as) ki Vilayat ka faisla suna diya to phir Saqeefa mein phir se chunao hua ye bata kar ke Rasool (saww) kisi ko bana kar hi nahi gaye.
Janabe Fatema Zehra (sa) ne bhi Haq ka taqaza kiya aur Allah aur Uske Rasool (saww) ko gawah banaya lekin ye gawahi qubool nahi ki gayi.
Pas Allah ko to sab maanne ko tayyar ho gaye jo ke ek Fitri taqaza hai lekin Uske faisle qubool nahi.
🤲🏻
_"Mere Ma'bood! Agar Tu Ma'af kar de to kaun Tujh se zyada Ma'af karne wala hai? Agar Tu Azaab de to kaun Faisla karne mein zyada Aadil hai?"_
(Imam Sajjad (as): Dua e Abu Hamza Shimali)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Allah farmata hai, "Pus jaan lo ke Allah koi amal qubool na karega jab tak qaum Adl (insaaf / justice) ke qaail na hongi"._
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p110)
