         ♦ _*KALMA-E-ILAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (871)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَتَمَّتْ كَلِمَتُ رَبِّكَ صِدْقًا وَعَدْلًا ۚ لَا مُبَدِّلَ لِكَلِمَاتِهِ ۚ وَهُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ*

_"Aur Tumhare Rab ki baat Sidq o Adl (with Truth & Just) ke lehaz se Kamil (Perfect) hai aur Uske Kalemat ko koi tabdeel nahi kar sakta aur Woh Sunnewala aur Jannewala hai."_
(Surah An'am: 115)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
"Word *كلمة* ke literature mein kai meaning hain. Is mein se ek meaning hai "Waa'da" (Promise), doosre maani hain Qur'an wa Ahkam, Deen. Urdu mein bhi wada ke meaning mein istemal hota jaise ke ham kisi ko "Zaban" dete hain.
Is Ayat se zahir hai ke Allah ne Qur'an wa Ahkam o Shariyat ki takmeel ki. Lekin Allah ne Ghadeer ke mauqe par ye Surah Maeda ki Ayat nazil ki ke Aaj Deen Kamil ho gaya. Isliye ke Aaj Vilayat-e-Ali (as) ka Ailan ho gaya. Yani Aaj Allah ne Apni Hidayat ko pura kiya, Wada pura kiya, Wada nibhaya. Is Din Nabuwwat tamam hui aur Imamat ka aagaaz hua. Isliye Imam ko Ma'ood موعود  kahte hain. Ab Uske Kalme mein koi tabdeeli nahi ayegi kiyonki hamare Akhiri Nabi par Nubuwwat khatm hui. Imam bhi Kalma e Ilahi hain aur Allah ka Kalma Qayamat tak baqi rahega.
🍃
Ziyarat e Waresa mein Imam (as) ko "Kalma e Taqwa" se zikr kiya gaya hai:
*أَشْهَدُ أَنَّكَ اَلْإِمَامُ اَلْبَرُّ اَلتَّقِيُّ اَلرَّضِيّ اَلزَّكِيُّ اَلْهَادِي اَلْمَهْدِيُّ وَ أَشْهَدُ أَنَّ اَلْأَئِمَّةَ مِنْ وُلْدِكَ كَلِمَةُ اَلتَّقْوَى وَ أَعْلاَمُ اَلْهُدَى وَ اَلْعُرْوَةُ اَلْوُثْقَى وَ اَلْحُجَّةُ عَلَى أَهْلِ اَلدُّنْيَا*
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha Mahdi e Ma'ood (atfs) ka jald az jald Zahoor farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
_*Aimma (as) ki Paidaish:*_
Aimma (as) ki paidaish ki tafseeli Rivayaat maujood hain jin mein unke Nutfe aur Rahme Madar mein is ke isteqrar ka bayan kiya gaya hai. Rivayat ke akhir mein ye jumle mazkoor hain:
_"...Jab Nutfa 4 maah tak Shikam e Madar mein qayam karta hai aur is mein Rooh dakhil ki jaati hai to Allah ek Farishte ko bhejta hai jiska naam "Haywan- *حيوان*" hai woh Imam ke dayen bazoo par ye Ayat tehreer karta hai: (6:115)"_
(Usool e Kafi)
🌿
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala jab kisi Imam ko paida karna chahta hai to Woh ek Farishte ko hukm deta hai ke woh Arsh ke neeche se Paani le kar Imam ke Walid ko pilata hai, usse Imam paida hota hai. Woh 40 Din Raat tak Maa ke Shikam mein qayam pazeer rahta hai. Is dauran woh koi awaz nahi sunta. Iske baad woh kalam sunne lag jata hai. Jab Imam paida hota hai to woh Farishta nazil hota hai aur uske dono Aankho ke darmiyan ye Ayat tehreer karta hai: (6:115). Aur jab pahle wala Imam Duniya se rukhsat hota hai to naye Imam ke liye Minarah e Noor qayem kiya jaata hai jisse woh Makhlooqat ke Aamaal dekhta hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ _*AKSARIYAT (MAJORITY)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (872)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنْ تُطِعْ أَكْثَرَ مَنْ فِي الْأَرْضِ يُضِلُّوكَ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ ۚ إِنْ يَتَّبِعُونَ إِلَّا الظَّنَّ وَإِنْ هُمْ إِلَّا يَخْرُصُونَ * إِنَّ رَبَّكَ هُوَ أَعْلَمُ مَنْ يَضِلُّ عَنْ سَبِيلِهِ ۖ وَهُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِالْمُهْتَدِين*

_"Agar Aapne Ahle Arz (inhabitants) ki aksariyat ki ita'at apna li to woh tumhe Allah ke Raaste se bhatka denge. Ye log sirf guman (Assumption) ki pairavi kar rahe hain aur ye sirf qayas aarayiyon (guess) se kaam le rahe hain."_
_"Yaqeenan Aap (saww) ka Rab zyada behtar jaanta hai ke Uski Raah se bhatka hua kaun hai aur Woh Hidayat yafta logon ko bhi jaanta hai."_
(Surah An'am: 116 - 117)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Duniya ka dastoor ye hai ke woh darya ki ravani ke saath bahti hai. Log andhi Taqleed karte hue kisi ke bhi peeche daudte rahte. Lekin aqliyyat hi kuchh apni Aql ka istemal karti hai. Kamyabi ki raah Quality mein hai na ke Quantity mein. Jange Badr mein Nav Muslim 313 the jabke doosri taraf 1000 Kuffar. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Taif ka safar karke sirf ghulam ko Musalman banaya aur Aap ne farmaya ke mera safar kamyab raha. Karbala mein 72 afraad ne lakhon ke Yazidi Lashkar ke saamne Jang jeet li. Aaj kahne ko to sab Musalman hain lekin Momin wa Muttaqi kuchh hi log hain.
Allah ne jabke har insaan ko samajhne ke liye Aql o Kitab di hai lekin sirf ye uski liye kafi nahi hai, nahi to aksariyat mein itne ikhtelafat na hote. Isliye iske saath Allah ki taraf se Rahbar ki zaroorat hai. Isliye Allah ne 124000 Paighambar insaan ki hidayat ke mab'oos kiye aur inke baad Aimma ka silsila aaj tak jaari hai. Yaad rakhen jis Lashkar ka sipehsalar na ho woh muntashir ho jaata hai. Isliye ye kahna ke hame hidayat ke liye Kitab kafi hai Aql ke manafi hai. Musalmano mein ye hadis mashoor hai ke Rasool ne farmaya ke meri Ummat khata par jama nahi ho sakti. Ye bhi Aql ke daire ke bahar hai. Aise kaise mumkin hai ke ek group mil kar ijtemayi taur par gunah nahi kar sakta. Duniya mein aise bahut cases ham dekhte rahte hain. Ummat ka Rahbar wohi ho sakta hai jo har gunah se paak ho.
Allah ne is aayat mein aksariyat ke formula ki mazammat ki hai. Democracy mein aksariyat ek Zalim hukmaran ko chun leti hai aur phir uske mazalim ko khud hi bhugatti hai. Ye sab isliye, kyonki logon ne Islami Taalimat ko chhod apne rules bana kar apni zindagi ki ravish bana rakhi hai.
🤲🏻
_"Bare Ilaha! Mushtaqeen ke darmiyan Tere Qurb mushtaq shumar hun aur Mukhlesin ki tarah Teri Qurbat ikhtiyar karun. Sahebane Yaqeen ki tarah Tera Khauf paida karun aur Mominon ke saath Tere Jawar mein hazri dun."_
(Dua-e-Kumail)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🧔🏻
Imam Taqi (as)
_"Agar Ulema apni nasihat ko chhupa le'n, yaani sargardaa'n (bhattakte / aawara) aur gumraah insaan ki hidayat na karein ya (ma'anvi / spiritually) murda insaan ko dekh kar usay zinda na karein to unhone apne saath khayaanat ki."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p207)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          ♦ _*HALAAL FOOD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (873)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَكُلُوا مِمَّا ذُكِرَ اسْمُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ بِآيَاتِهِ مُؤْمِنِينَ * وَمَا لَكُمْ أَلَّا تَأْكُلُوا مِمَّا ذُكِرَ اسْمُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ وَقَدْ فَصَّلَ لَكُمْ مَا حَرَّمَ عَلَيْكُمْ إِلَّا مَا اضْطُرِرْتُمْ إِلَيْهِ ۗ وَإِنَّ كَثِيرًا لَيُضِلُّونَ بِأَهْوَائِهِمْ بِغَيْرِ عِلْمٍ ۗ إِنَّ رَبَّكَ هُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِالْمُعْتَدِينَ*

_"Jis Janwar par Allah ka naam liya gaya ho uska gosht khao agar tum Uski Ayaat par Imaan rakhte ho."_
_"Akhir kiya wajah hai ke tum woh cheez na khao jis par Allah ka Naam liya gaya ho? Jabke halate izterar (majboori) ke siwa jin cheezon ka khaana Haraam hai unki tafseel Woh tumhe bata chuka hai. Logon ki aksariyat apni khwahishat ke tahet Ilm ke baghair gumrah karne mein masroof hai aur yaqeenan Tera Rab had se tajawuz karne walon ko achhi tarah se janta hai."_
(Surah An'am: 118 - 119)

📚📖 🐮🐄🐐
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Sura Ale Imran: 93, Sura Maeda ki shuru ki Ayaton mein is topic par tafseel se zikr ho chuka hai. Readers hamari website par in Ayaat ki Tafseer padh sakte hain. Mazeed is topic par Sura Naml: 115 mein bhi zikr hai.
Guzishta Ayaat mein Tauheed e Ilahi ka zikr hue, Tauheed sirf zabani nahi ya Dil mein Aqeeda ki baat nahi balki hamari practical Zindagi mein bhi ye zaroori hai jise Tauheed e Afa'al kahte hain. Un mein ek ye ke jo khao woh bhi Allah ka Naam le kar khao. Allah ka Naam le kar zibah kiya hua Janwar hi hamare liye Halaal hai. Zibah ke Islami tareeqe ke khud scientific benefits (fawaid) hain jo ke mukhtalif kitabon mein darj hain, un mein se ek ye ke woh bimariyon se paak ho jaata hai.
Allah ka Naam na lena khud shirk ka izhar hai isliye Khuda sawal kar raha hai ke akhir Allah ka Naam lene mein kya mushkil hai?
Jaisa ke pahle bhi zikr ho chuka hai ke sirf Islam mein hi nahi balke guzishta Nabiyon ke Mazahib mein bhi yehi hukm tha. Yahoodiyon mein bhi Halaal Food ko Kosher Food kahte hain aur woh yehi khaate hain.
Read on Kosher Food:
http://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kosher_foods
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Jaez aur Halaal Ghaza Khaane ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🐮🐄🐐
Imam Baqir (as) se poochha ke agar koi Majoosi Allah ka Naam le kar Zebah kare to kya iska khaana Halaal?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Tum woh gosht kha sakte ho."_
Phir poochha gaya ke ek Musalman ne zebah kiya lekin usne Allah ka Naam nahi liya to kya zabeehe ka Gosht khaana Halaal hai?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Nahi kha sakte kyonki Allah Ta'ala farmata hai (6:118)"_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                  ♦ _*GUNAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (874)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَ ذَرُوا ظَاهِرَ الْإِثْمِ وَبَاطِنَهُ ۚ إِنَّ الَّذِينَ يَكْسِبُونَ الْإِثْمَ سَيُجْزَوْنَ بِمَا كَانُوا يَقْتَرِفُونَ*

_"Aur tum khule aur chhupe hue dono tarah ke Gunah ko chhod do. Jo log Gunah karne mein lage hue hain unhe anqareeb unki kamai ka badla diya jayega."_
(Surah An'am: 120)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Tafseer e Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi mein hai ke Zaheri Gunah se murad Khuda ki khullam khulla nafarmani hai aur Bateni Gunah se Shirk aur Dil ka shak murad hai.
🍂
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Jo bhi Momin Khuda ka zikr karta hai to Allah uska bhi Achhai se zikr karta hai. Tum Ita'at e Khuda ke liye poori jadd o jahed baja lao. Khuda ki taraf se koi Bhalai tab milti hai jab Insaan Uski ita'at kare aur Uski Haraam kardah cheezon se parhez kare. Kiyonki Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: (6:120)"_
(Roza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Khudaya!  Un Gunahon ko bakhs de jo Namoos ko batta laga dete hain, Nuzool e Azaab ka baes hote hain, Ne'maton ko change kar dete hain, jo Duaon ko rok dete hain, umeedon ko qata kar dete hain, jo nuzoole bala ka sabab hote hain, to mere khataon ko bakhs de.
(Dua-e-Kumail)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as)
se ek shakhs ne arz ki, _"Fulan shakhs Gunahan e Kabira ka murtakib hai aur tumhara Shia hai."_
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Agar wo shakhs Gunahan e Kabira karne ke bawajood hamari mohabbat ka dum bharta hai to wo hamara Mohib (chahne-wala) hai, Shia nahi. Aur tera usko Shia kehna jhoot hai. Aur agar wo shakhs na hamara Mohib ho aur na hamare Dushmanon se bezaar ho aur Gunahan e Kabira bhi karta ho, to tera usko Shia kehna dohra (double) jhoot hai."_
(Tafseer e Anwaar e Najaf, v12, p44)
🍃
Riwayat
Ek shakhs ne apni biwi se kaha ke jaa kar Janabe Fatima (sa) se daryaaft karo mere mutalliq ke kya main aap ke Shiyon mein se hun? Chunanche, us Aurat ke sawal ka Janabe Fatima (sa) ne jawab diya,
_"Use kaho ke agar wo hamare awamir o nawahi (commandments / Ahkam) ka paband hai to hamara Shia hai, warna nahi."_
Jab Aurat ne wapas aa kar bataya to ye shakhs sakht pareshan huwa ke,
_"Hay, hay! Gunahon se kaun bach sakta hai. Pus, main to phir Dozakhi huwa."_
Chunaanche, us Aurat ne dobara jaa kar Janabe Fatima (sa) se apne shauhar ke izterab (bechaini) ka tazkera kiya to Janabe Fatima (sa) ne farmaya,
_"Baat ye hai ke hamare Shia Jannat ke buland manazil par faaiz honge. Aur unke alawa jo hamare Mohib (chahnewale), hamare doston ke dost aur hamare dushmanon ke dushman hain, jo hum ko dil o jaan se tasleem karte hain wo agar Wajibat aur muharramat mein agar hamari mukhalifat karein to yaqeenan hamare Shia nahi hain lekin gunahon ki saza bhugatne ke baad Jannat mein zarur jayenge; wo Duniya mein masaib o aalaam ki takleefein sahenge; kuchh arsa Mehshar mein sakhti dekhenge; aur sakht Gunahgar ek waqt tak Dozakh ke upar waale tabqe mein Azaab bhi chakhenge aur uske baad hamari mohabbat ki ba-daulat unko Jannat naseeb hongi."_
(Tafseer e Anwaar e Najaf, v12, p45)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦ _*HALAAL FOOD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (875)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تَأْكُلُوا مِمَّا لَمْ يُذْكَرِ اسْمُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ وَإِنَّهُ لَفِسْقٌ ۗ وَإِنَّ الشَّيَاطِينَ لَيُوحُونَ إِلَىٰ أَوْلِيَائِهِمْ لِيُجَادِلُوكُمْ ۖ وَإِنْ أَطَعْتُمُوهُمْ إِنَّكُمْ لَمُشْرِكُونَ*

_"Aur jis Janwar par zibah ke waqt Allah ka naam na kiya gaya ho, iska Gosht mat khao aur aisa karna Fisq hai. Yaqeenan Shayateen apne doston ki taraf shukook o shubhat ilqa karte hain taake woh tum se jhagda karen aur tumne unki ita'at ki to Yaqeenan tum Mushrek qarar paoge."_
(Surah An'am: 121)

📚📖 🐃🐂🐄🐑🐐🦌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat 118, 119 ka same Topic continue hai.
🐐
Kisi ne Imam Sadiq (as) se poochha ke ham kabhi apne Christians friends ki dawat par chale jaate hain aur woh hamare liye Murghi ya Bakri waghaira zabah karte hain aur hame khilate hain. Imam (as) ne unke in khaano ko mana kiya kiyonki woh zabah ke waqt ek khaas baat kahte hain. Jab un Christians doston se poochha ke kiya kahte hain to bataya ke woh kahte hain " *باسم المسيح*" means Allah ka naam nahi lete.
(Al Kaafi)
🐐
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Agar koi Yahoodi zabah kare to uska mat khao, agar uska Gosht beche aur tumhe iski qeemat dena chahe to is raqam ko apne Maal mein shamil na karo kyonki aisa karna Gunah hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🐐
Imam Musa Kazim (as):
_"Yahoodi Nasaara ke zabeeha ke qareeb na jao."_
(Tehzeebul Ahkam)
🐐
Imam Sadiq (as)
se puchha gaya ke ek shakhs ne ek jaanwar zibah kiya aur Khuda ka naam nahi liya.
Aap (as) ne farmaya,
_"Agar wo bhool gaya tha to beech mein jab Khuda ka naam yaad aaye Khuda ka naam le le aur ye bhi kahe 'Bismillahi 'Alaa Awwalihi Wa Aakhirihi.''_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p73)
🐐
Ahle Kitab ke Zabeeha ke mutalliq hamare Ulama mein ikhtelaf hai kuchh ke haan jaez hai to kuch ke haan jaez nahi. Ye isliye ke kuchh Ahadis milti hai jis mein kaha gaya hai ke kabhi kabhar kha sakte hain. Pas aap jiski Taqleed karte hain us par amal karen.
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Halaal Ghaza Khaane ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🐐
Imam Reza (as)
_"Nabi e Akram (saww) par Durood / Salwaat bhejna har maqaam par zaruri hai; chhi'nk ke waqt aur jaanwar ko zibah karne ke waqt bhi Durood Shareef padhna chahiye."_
Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p39
🐐
Imam Sadiq (as)
se ye bhi sawaal huwa ke ek shakhs ne zibah ke waqt 'Subhanallah', ya 'Allahu Akbar', ya 'La Ilaha Illallah', ya 'Al Hamdu Lillah' keh le to kaafi hai?
Imam (as) ne farmaya,
_"Haa'n. Kyun ki un sab mein Allah ka naam maujood hai, koi harj nahi."_
Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p74
🐐
Imam Reza (as):
_"Tamam qism ki mitti haraam hai jaise murdaar, khoon aur wo zibah-shuda halaal jaanwar jispar Allah ka naam na liya gaya ho haraam hain, siwaaye H. Imam Husain (as) ki qabr ki mitti ke. Usko khana jaayez hai kyun ki usme har bimari ke liye shifa maujood hai."_
(Amaali – Shaikh Toosi, v2, p424)

 ♦ _*MURDEH KO ZINDAGI DENA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (876)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَوَمَنْ كَانَ مَيْتًا فَأَحْيَيْنَاهُ وَجَعَلْنَا لَهُ نُورًا يَمْشِي بِهِ فِي النَّاسِ كَمَنْ مَثَلُهُ فِي الظُّلُمَاتِ لَيْسَ بِخَارِجٍ مِنْهَا ۚ كَذَٰلِكَ زُيِّنَ لِلْكَافِرِينَ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ*

_"Kya woh shakhs jo pahle Murda tha phir Hamne use Zindagi bakhshi aur uski roshni ata ki jiske ujale mein woh logon ke darmiyan chalta hai, woh us shakhs ki manind ho sakta hai jo tareekyon mein ho aur unse bahar na aa sakta ho? Is tarah se Kafiron ke liye unke Aamaal khushnuma bana diye gaye hain."_
(Surah An'am: 122)

📚📖 ⚰
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Baqir (as) is Ayat ke zel mein farmate hain:
_"Jab koi haqeeqat se nawaqif ho to woh Murdah hai aur Allah farmata hai ke Hamne use Zindagi di, yani Hamne use Daulat e Islam ata ki. Phir Allah ne kaha ke "Hamne usko Roshni ata ki jiske ujale mein woh logon ke darmiyan chalta hai" maqsad ye hai ke Hamne use Sachcha Imam o Rahbar ata kiya. Phir Khuda ne farmaya: "Kya woh us shakhs ke manind ho sakta hai jo tareekyon mein ho aur unse bahar na aa sakta ho" isse woh shakhs murad hai jise Sachcha Imam na mila ho."_
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚰
Imam Sadiq (as) ne ek Dua tilqeen ki jis mein ye alfaaz hain:
_"(Ayat Ale Imran: 27). Zinda se Murad Momin hai jiski Teenat ko Allah ne Kafir ki Teenat se juda karta hai aur Murdah se Kafir murad hain jiski Teenat ko Allah Momin ki Teenat se alaidah karta hai. Isliye Allah farmata hai: Ayat (6:122) Woh is lehaz se Murdah tha ke uski Teenat Kafir ki Teenat se makhloot thi aur use Zindagi is tarah se ata hui ke Allah ne apne Hukm se uski Teenat ko alaidah kar diya. Allah Ta'ala Ahle Imaan ko Tareekyon se nikal kar Noor mein le aata hai aur Taghoot e Kafiron ko Roshni se nikal kar tareekyon mein le jaate hain. Isi Haqeeqat ko Allah ne yun bayan kiya hai taake woh use khauf dilaye jo zinda ho aur Kafiron par hamari baat sach sabit ho."_
(Noorus Saqlain, Tafseer Ayyashi, Kitabul Manaqib, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hamare Murdah Dilon ko zindagi ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📝
Imam Baqir (as)
_*"Is baat mein koi shak nahi ke hamaari Ahadees murda dilo'n ko zinda karti hai."*_
(Nawaadirul Ahadees, v1, p41)
🌿
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_*"Mere Bando'n mein Ilm ka tazkera murda dilo'n ko zinda kar deta hai."*_
(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p350)
🌱
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"4 cheezein Dil ko Murda kar deti hain:_
_(1) Gunah par gunah karna,_
_(2) Auraton se zyada hum-kalaam hona (Auraton se zyada baaten karna),_
_(3) Ahmaq (bewaqoof) ke saath mubahesa (debate / argument) karna aur uska anjaam kabhi bhi achcha nahi hota, aur_
_(4) Murdon ka hum-nasheen hona."_
Sahaba ne daryaaft kiya,
_"Ya Rasulallah (saww)!_ Murda kaun hai?"
Aap (saww) ne farmaya: _"Fuzool-kharch daulatmand."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p243)
🧔🏻
Imam Taqi (as):
_*"Agar Ulema apni nasihat ko chhupa len, yaani sargardaan (bhattakte / aawara) aur gumrah insaan ki hidayat na karein ya (ma'anvi / spiritually) murda insaan ko dekh kar use zinda na karein to unhone apne saath khayanat ki."*_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p207)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ _*MOHALLE KE GUNDE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (877)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَكَذَٰلِكَ جَعَلْنَا فِي كُلِّ قَرْيَةٍ أَكَابِرَ مُجْرِمِيهَا لِيَمْكُرُوا فِيهَا ۖ وَمَا يَمْكُرُونَ إِلَّا بِأَنْفُسِهِمْ وَمَا يَشْعُرُونَ*

_"Aur is tarah Hamne har Qarye (City) mein bade bade Mujrimon ko laga diya hai ke woh wahan apne Makr o Fareb ka jaal phailayen jabke woh to apne aap se hi Fareb kar rahe hain, unhe kuchh sha'oor nahi hai."_
(Surah An'am: 123)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke guzishta Ayat mein zikr hua tha ke kuchh log tareekyon mein hi rahte hai aur woh isse bahar aa hi nahi paate. Is tarah ke log Raat ki tareekyon mein clubs ya kuchh aur 2 no. ke kaamon mein mast rahte hain. Woh inhi kaamon mein achhai aur khushi mehsoos karte hain. Phir is Ayat mein Allah farma raha hai ke Hamne aise log har shaher mein rakhen hain. Aur ye Bhai log Raat ki tareekyon mein Makr o Fareb ke jaal bunte rahte hain, balke apni hi banaye jaal mein phanste rahte hain.
Sawal ye paida hota hai kya Allah ye sab karwa raha hai jaisa ke is Ayat mein hai?
Pahle bhi bata chuke hain Allah ne hame apni zaban mein samjhaya hai. Allah jab Rasool ko dat ta hai ya nasihat karta hai yani  poori Ummat ko dat raha hai.
Poori Khilqat wa Aamaal ka Actual Source Allah hai. Agar Allah hame ikhtiyar nahi deta to ham gunah nahi kar sakte the. Exam ki misal ham pahle bhi de chuke hain. Teacher Student ka test le raha hai. Kuchh ghalat Question bhi poochhta hai, iska matlab ye nahi ke teacher jahil hai.
Allah ne is Ayat mein akhir bata diya ke jo kuchh woh kar rahe hain woh apne aap se kar rahe hain. Jiska natija woh khud to bhugatte hi hain balke saath mein doosron ko bhi le doobte hain.
🤲🏻
*ومن ارادنى بسوءفأرده و من كادنى فكده.*  
_"Ya Allah! Aur jo shakhs mere saath kisi tarah ki badee karne ka irada kare to Tu waisa hi iraada uske haq mein karna, aur jo mere saath fareb kare to Tu uske fareb ki sazaa de."_
(Dua e Kumail)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🧔🏻
_*Ahmiyyat e Marjiyyat*_
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Agar Imam Aakhir uz Zaman (atfs) ki Ghaibat ke baad Ulama Imamat ko sabit karne wale aur Shiyon ko Shayateen ke makr o fareb se bachane wale na hote, to tamam Shia murtad ho jate, magar unke haathon mein us giroh ki mehar is tarah hai jaise mallah (naavik) kashti ke langar ko sambhaale rehta hai. Is liye unka martaba Khuda ke nazdeek sab se behtar hai."_
(Roohul Hayaat, p243)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ _*RAHBAR-E-ILAHI AZ JAANIB-E-ILAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (878)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا جَاءَتْهُمْ آيَةٌ قَالُوا لَنْ نُؤْمِنَ حَتَّىٰ نُؤْتَىٰ مِثْلَ مَا أُوتِيَ رُسُلُ اللَّهِ ۘ اللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ حَيْثُ يَجْعَلُ رِسَالَتَهُ ۗ سَيُصِيبُ الَّذِينَ أَجْرَمُوا صَغَارٌ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ وَعَذَابٌ شَدِيدٌ بِمَا كَانُوا يَمْكُرُونَ*

_"Jab unke saamne koi Ayat aati hai to kahte hain ham hargiz Imaan nahi layenge jab tak hame woh cheez na di jaye jo Allah ke Rasoolon ko di gayi hai. Allah behtar jaanta hai ke Woh RISAALAT ka mansab kahan rakhe. Woh waqt qareeb hai jab ye Mujrim apni saazishon ki wajah se Allah ke haan zillat aur sakht Azaab se dochar honge."_
(Surah An'am: 125)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Kuffar o Mushrekin ke Sardaron ne jab Waḥy e Ilahi ko suna aur Anbiya ke Mo'jezaat dekhe to unhone kaha jab tak is jaisi Waḥy o Tanzeel khud ham par nazil na ho jaye us waqt tak ham Imaan nahi layenge.
Allah Ta'ala ne unke jawab mein ye Ayat pesh ki. (6:124)
(Noorus Saqlain)
📚
Kuffar o Mushrekin ke Sardaron ka ye taqaza karne ka asl maqsad is Paak o Pakeeza Mansab ko apne haath mein lena tha. Allah ne saaf saaf jawab diya kisko kaunsa Mansab dena hai ye Uske ke haath mein hai, is mein hamara tumhara koi dakhl nahi hai. Mansab e Risalat Deen e Ilahi ki hidayat ke liye hai. Isliye Rahbar chahe Nabi ya Imam ho khaati (mistake karne wala), Gunehgar nahi ho sakta, Ilm mein Afzal, ba Hukm e Khuda Mo'jeza dekhane wala hona chahiye. Warna Nabi wa Imam ke bajai log uski hidayat karne lag jayenge. Ye khud ek Fitri wa Aqli taqaza hai. Allah behtar Jaanta hai kisko Apne Deen ka Rahbar banana hai. Lekin jo log is mansab ke mutamanni the aur unhone baad e Shahadat e Rasool apni murad poori bhi ki, unka hashr kiya hoga ye Allah ne is ayat ke akhiri hisse mein bata diya.
(Sab is baat ka iqrar karte hain ke Rasool (saww) ne Ahle Bait (as) ko sab se afzal bataya, ye bhi maante hai baad mein logon ne apna kisi ko Rahbar khud se chun liya, kiya ye sab is Ayat se ikhtelaf nahi rakhta?)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Tere Haqeeqi Rahbar ke naqse qadam par chalne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Husain (as)
se jab Walid ne baiyat ka sawaal kiya to Imam (as) ne kaha:
_"Aye Governor! Hum Nabuwwat ke Ahlebait aur Risaalat ki kaan hain. Hamare ghar Farishton ka nuzool hota hai. Allah Ta'ala ne Kaainaat ki ibteda hum se ki thi aur Wo Kaainaat ka khatima hum par karega. Aur Yazeed (Mal'oon) ek faasiq aur sharaabi mard hai, wo nafs e mohtaram ka qaatil hai, wo khullam khulla gunah karta hai. Aur mujh jaisa oos jaise ki baiyat nahi kar sakta."_
(Maqtal e Mukarram, p31; Lahoof - Sayed Ibne Taoos, p15)
🕌
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Shab e Meraaj Jibreel e Amin ne Azaan aur Iqamat kahi. Rasule Khuda (saww) ne farmaya,
_"Jibreel aage aao aur Imamat karo."_
Jibreel (as) ne arz kiya:
_*"Jab se Allah ne humein Sajda e Adam ka hukm diya hai tab se hum Bani Adam (Adam (as) ki aulaad) ke Imam nahi bante."*_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p112)

♦ _*ISLAM KE LIYE KUSHADA DIL KI ZAROORAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (879)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَمَنْ يُرِدِ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَهْدِيَهُ يَشْرَحْ صَدْرَهُ لِلْإِسْلَامِ ۖ وَمَنْ يُرِدْ أَنْ يُضِلَّهُ يَجْعَلْ صَدْرَهُ ضَيِّقًا حَرَجًا كَأَنَّمَا يَصَّعَّدُ فِي السَّمَاءِ ۚ كَذَٰلِكَ يَجْعَلُ اللَّهُ الرِّجْسَ عَلَى الَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ*
[Surat Al-An'am 125]

_"Khuda ko jiski Hidayat matloob hoti hai to uske seene ko Islam ke liye kushada kar deta hai aur jiski gumrahi matloob hoti hai to uske seene ko tang kar deta hai aur use aisa bheench deta (constraint) hai ke use apna dam ghutta hua mehsoos hota hai jaisa ke woh bulandi ki taraf parwaz (fly) kar raha ho. Is tarah se Allah Imaan na laane walon par Napaaki dal deta hai."_
(Surah An'am: 125)

📚📖 💗💝
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ne be tauseeq shakhs ke seene ko "Zeeq wa Haraj - *ضيق و حرج*" qarar diya hai. "Zeeq" aise tang ko kaha jata hai jis mein koi na koi surakh ho jisse dekha ja sakta ho aur baat suni ja sakti ho. Lekin "Haraj" aise band darwaze ko kaha jaata hai jis mein koi surakh maujood na ho aur jahan rah kar insaan na kuchh dekh sake aur na kuchh sun sake."_
(Kitabul Khisaal)
🌟
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jab Khuda kisi bande se bhalai ka iraada karta hai to uske Dil mein Noor ka ek Nuqta qaem kar deta hai jiski wajah se uske Kaan aur Dil roshan ho jaate hain aur jab kisi bande ki burai ka iraada karta hai to uske Dil mein ek Siyah Nuqta qaem kar deta hai jiski wajah se uske Kaan aur Dil tareeki mein doob jaata hai." (Phir ye Ayat 6:125 padhi)_
(Usoole Kaafi)
💫
Hazrat Imam Reza (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala jis shakhs ke Dunyavi Imaan ki wajah se apni Jannat aur Dar e Karamat ki Rahnumai ka irada karta hai to Tasleem, Etemaad aur Sawab ke wade par taskeen ke liye uske Seene ko Kushada kar deta hai aur maqam e Itminaan par faez ho jata  hai aur jiske Dunyavi Kufr o Nafarmani ki wajah se Khuda use apni Jannat aur Dar e Karamat ko faramosh karane ke iraada karta hai to uske Seene ko tang aur ghuta hua bana deta hai aur naubat yahan tak jaa pahunchti hai ke woh apne Kufr mein bhi shak karne lag jata hai aur apne Eteqaade Qalb se bhi muztarib ho jata hai aur yun ghutan mehsoos karta hai jaisa ke Aasmaan ki taraf chadh raha ho. (Jahan ghadi ghadi Oxygen kam ho rahi ho aur saans lene mein dushwari pesh aa rahi ho) is tarah se be Imaan logon par Napaaki dal deta hai."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Noorus Saqlain)

Bare Ilaha har waqt Teri Inayat o Karam ke umidwar hai taake ham Tere Ibaadat Guzar bande ban saken.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🧔🏻
Imam Sadiq (as)
_*"Ulema e Soo (wicked scholars) ke liye aatish e Jahannum ke sholay buri tarah uski khabar lenge."*_
(Al Kaafi, v1, p100)
🧔🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ulama e Deen mein kuchh aise bhi honge jo Fatwa dene par tayyar ho jayenge aur is baat ke muddaee bhi ho jayenge (is baat ka daawa bhi karenge) ke jo kuchh puchhna ho hum se puchho, halaanki shayad ek harf bhi theek na bata sakte honge. Allah Ta'ala aise logon ko dost nahi rakhta."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p114)

      ♦ _*TAUFEEQ & KHIZLAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (880)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَهَٰذَا صِرَاطُ رَبِّكَ مُسْتَقِيمًا ۗ قَدْ فَصَّلْنَا الْآيَاتِ لِقَوْمٍ يَذَّكَّرُونَ * لَهُمْ دَارُ السَّلَامِ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ ۖ وَهُوَ وَلِيُّهُمْ بِمَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ*

_"Aur ye tumhare Rab ka Seedha Raasta hai aur Hamne Naseehat qubool karne walon ke liye Ayaat ki wazahat kar di hai. Unke Rab ke haan unke "Salamati ka Ghar (Darus Salam)" hai aur unke Nek Aamaal ki wajah se woh unki sarparast hai."_
(Surah An'am: 126 - 127)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat no. 125 ka mazmoon jaari hai. Ayat mein jo mafhoom zikr hua woh Taufeeq aur Khizlaan hai.
🌾
Taufeeq *توفيق* ka Root hai *وفق* means 'muttafiq, 'mufahemat' (Agree, reconcile), Kamyabi waghaira. Taufeeq yani kuchh Naseeb hona. Ye ek tarah ka Grant hai. Misal ke taur par ek shakhs agar chhat par Bulb lagana chahta ho to usko is kaam ke liye ek seedhi (ladder) ki zaroorat hogi. Ye shakhs ye kaam karna chahta hai lekin agar seedhi na ho to woh is kaam mein fail ho sakta hai. Lekin agar koi iske nek iraada dekh kar seedhi de de to woh shakhs kamyab ho jaata hai. Ye seedhi is shakhs ke liye Taufeeq hai. Is tarah Allah Ta'ala jab kisi Momin ke Nek iraade ko dekhta hai usko Taufeeq deta hai taake woh is mein kamyabi hasil kare.
Iska opposite lafz "Khizlaan' - *خذلان*" yani ye grant khench lena. Jab Allah dekhta Mera pyara banda Rizq ki dua maang raha hai lekin agar Usne dua qubool kar li to woh Use bhool jayega aur Seedhe Raaste se bhatak jayega, pas Allah uski Dua qubool na karke uske saath khizlan karta hai, ya koi shakhs itna bhatak jaata hai ke use Seedhe Raste par aana mushkil hai to Allah us par Ghazab ke taur par bhi Khizlaan karta hai.
Taufeeq lafz aam log apni zaban mein aksar istemal karte. Taufeeq aur Khizlaan ke alfaaz hamari aksar Duaon mein ayen hain. Un mein ek Dua-e-Hamza Sumaali hai jisko Imam Zainul Abedin (as) ne ata ki hai.
🤲🏻
*اوْ لَعَلَّكَ فَقَدْتَنِي مِنْ مَجَالِسِ ٱلْعُلَمَاءِ فَخَذَلْتَنِي*
_*"Ya Majlise Ulama se alag dekh kar (Tu ne mujhe) tark kar diya hai."*_
_"Mujhe Hajj Baitullah ke liye is saal aur har saal Taufeeq de."_
(Dua-e-Abu Hamza Sumali)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Imam Taqi (as)
_"4 baatein insaan ko amal par ubhaarti hai: Sehet, Maaldaari, Ilm, Taufeeq."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p205)
🕌
Allah (swt):
_"Mere kuchh Bande aise bhi hote hain jo Mujh se kisi Neki ke karne (ki taufeeq) ka sawaal karte hain taaki Main unse Mohabbat o Pyaar karun. Magar Main unhe us Neki se baaz rakhta hun taaki us amal ki wajah se unme Ujb o Guroor (ahankaar aur takabbur) paida na ho jaye jo ulta unse Meri nafrat ka baais ban jaaye."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v1, p92)
🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Jis shakhs ko Parwardigaar ne mere Ahlebait (as) ki maarefat aur mohabbat ki taufeeq de di goya uske liye tamaam khair jamaa kar diya."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ _*ZALIM KA SAATHI BHI ZALIM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (881)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَيَوْمَ يَحْشُرُهُمْ جَمِيعًا يَا مَعْشَرَ الْجِنِّ قَدِ اسْتَكْثَرْتُمْ مِنَ الْإِنْسِ ۖ وَقَالَ أَوْلِيَاؤُهُمْ مِنَ الْإِنْسِ رَبَّنَا اسْتَمْتَعَ بَعْضُنَا بِبَعْضٍ وَبَلَغْنَا أَجَلَنَا الَّذِي أَجَّلْتَ لَنَا ۚ قَالَ النَّارُ مَثْوَاكُمْ خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا إِلَّا مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ ۗ إِنَّ رَبَّكَ حَكِيمٌ عَلِيمٌ * وَكَذَٰلِكَ نُوَلِّي بَعْضَ الظَّالِمِينَ بَعْضًا بِمَا كَانُوا يَكْسِبُونَ*

_"Aur jis Din Allah un sab ko mehshoor karega (aur Woh Jinnat se kahega) Ay giroh e Jinnat! Tumne no' e Insaani par khoob haath saaf kiya hai aur Insaano mein se jo unke dost the woh kahenge ham mein se har ek ne doosre se istefada (benefit) kiya hai aur ham is waqt par pahunche hain jo Tu ne hamare liye muqarrar kiya tha. Allah kahega: Dozakh tumhara thikana hai jahan tumhe hamesha rahna hai. Albatta jinke mutalliq Khuda chahe woh isse mustashna (exception) hain. Beshak Tera Parwardigar Sahib e Hikmat aur Sahib e Ilm hai."_
_"Is tarah Ham baaz Zalimon ko baaz Zalimon ka saathi banayenge, us kamai ki wajah se jo woh kiya karte the."_
(Surah An'am: 128 - 129)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein saaf taur par kaha gaya hai ke jo Jinnon se madad lete hain aur ghalat kaam karvate hain, ye Jinn Shayateen hain, to inko bhi unke saath mehshoor kiya jayega, jo unka haal hoga inka bhi wohi haal hoga.
Shariyat ke tareeqa ke alawa jo bhi Amal kiye jaate hain, yani Riyazat ke zariye Jinnon ko apne qabze mein lena phir unse kaam karwana, to Qayamat mein in logon ka bhi wohi haal hoga jo un Shaitani Jinnon ka hoga. Ye sab Haraam kam hain. Islam mein Zuhd o Pakeezgi hai, Riyazat ki mazammat ki gayi hai. Bahut si Duayen ta'aleem di gayi hain, ek shakhs khud unko padh sakta hai, agar koi shariyat ke mutabiq Taweezat hain woh khud likh sakta hai basharte ke uske Aamaal Pak o Pakeeza hon. In kaamon ke liye kisi Gandedar Maulvi ya Baba ke pas jaana sahi raaste se bhatakna hai.
👥
Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi mein marqoom hai ke jo bhi kisi qaum se Dosti rakhe woh un mein se qarar pata hai agarche unki jins alaihda kiyon na ho. (Ayat: 6:129)
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala hamesha Zalim se Zalim ke zariye se hi inteqam leta hai jaisa ka farman e Ilahi hai: (6:129)"_
(Usoole Kaafi)
👥
Imam e Masoom (as):
_"Qayamat ke Din har shakhs apne Auliya ke saath hoga."_
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi)
🤲🏻
_Aye Ma'bood! Beshak Tu ne Apni Kitaab mein ye Hukm naazil kiya hai jo hum par zulm kare use Ma'af kar de. Zaroor hum ne apne nafson par zulm kiya, Tu humein Ma'af farma._
(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumali)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👹
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jo koi najumi / jyotishi (astrologer) ki peyshangoi (bhavishyavaani / prediction) par yaqeen karta hai to usne Quran ka inkaar kiya."_
(Greater Sins II, Sorcery - 31st Greater Sin)
💩
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Wo jo kisi Jadugar, Ojha, Kaazib ke paas jaata hai aur uske kahe ko sach qaraar deta hai, wo Allah ki sab kitabon ki nazar mein Kafir ho gaya."_
(Greater Sins 2, Sorcery)

        ♦ _*JINN O INS KE NABI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (882)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا مَعْشَرَ الْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ أَلَمْ يَأْتِكُمْ رُسُلٌ مِنْكُمْ يَقُصُّونَ عَلَيْكُمْ آيَاتِي وَيُنْذِرُونَكُمْ لِقَاءَ يَوْمِكُمْ هَٰذَا ۚ قَالُوا شَهِدْنَا عَلَىٰ أَنْفُسِنَا ۖ وَغَرَّتْهُمُ الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا وَشَهِدُوا عَلَىٰ أَنْفُسِهِمْ أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا كَافِرِينَ*

_"Aye giroh e Jinn o Ins! Kya tumhare pas khud tum mein se aise Rasool nahi aye the jo tumhare saamne meri Ayaat sunaate aur tumhe us Din ke anjaam se darate? Woh kahenge ke ham apne khilaf khud gawahi dete hain. Unhe Dunyavi zindagi ne dhoke mein dala hua hai woh apne khilaf gawahi denge ke woh Kafir the."_
(Surah An'am: 130)

📚📖 🍁
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ameerul Mo'meneen Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Duniya mein apni Makhlooq ko abaad kiya aur apne Rasoolon ko Jinn o Ins ki taraf bheja taake woh unke saamne Duniya ko be naqab karen aur uski muziraton se unhe darayen, dhamkayen aur uski (bewafai ki) misaalein bayan karen aur uski aur uski sehet o bimari ke taghayyurat (changes) se ek dam unhe poori poori ibrat dilane ka samaan kar den aur iske ma'yoob aur Halaal o Haraam ke (zaraye iktesaab, source) aur farmanbardaron aur nafarmano ke liye jo bahisht o Dozakh aur izzat o Zillat ke jo samaan Allah ne muhayya kiye hain woh unhen dikhlayen."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
🍁
Shaami (Syrian) ne Hazrat Ali (as) se sawal kiya ke kya Allah Ta'ala ne Jinnat mein se bhi kisi ko Nabi bana kar bheja tha?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Ji haan, Allah Ta'ala ne un mein se ek Nabi unki taraf se mab'oos kiya tha jiska naam Yusuf tha. Us ne unhe Khuda ki dawat di thi lekin Qaum e Jinnat ne use qatl kar diya tha."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Noorus Saqlain)
🍁
*Imam Muhammad Baqir (as):*
_*"Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww) ko Jinn o Ins ki taraf mab'oos kiya tha."*_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Tere ita'at guzar bandon mein shamil kar.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍁
Imam e Shafaee (Ahle Sunnat ke Imam)
ne Imam Ali (as) ki shaan mein Ashaar kahe:
_“Ali (as) ki mohabbat Jahannum se bachne ke liye dhhaal hai, Ali (as) Jannat aur Jahannum ke taqseem karne wale hain, Hazrat Mustafa (saww) ke bar-haq Wasi aur Jinn o Ins ke Imam hain.”_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p125)

        ♦ _*ALLAH ZALIM NAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (883)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*ذَٰلِكَ أَنْ لَمْ يَكُنْ رَبُّكَ مُهْلِكَ الْقُرَىٰ بِظُلْمٍ وَأَهْلُهَا غَافِلُونَ * وَلِكُلٍّ دَرَجَاتٌ مِمَّا عَمِلُوا ۚ وَمَا رَبُّكَ بِغَافِلٍ عَمَّا يَعْمَلُونَ*

_"Baat ye hai ke tumhara Rab Zulm se Bastiyon ko tabah karne wala nahi tha jabke unke bashinde (inhabitants) Haqeeqat se ghafil hon. Har shakhs ka darja uske amal ke lehaz hai aur jo kuchh woh kar rahe hain Allah usse Be Khabar nahi hai."_
(Surah An'am: 131 - 132)

📚📖 ⚖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Allah ki Adalat ka zikr ho raha hai. Allah Aadil hai, Woh kisi par Zulm nahi karta. Aql o fitrat ka taqaza hai *عقاب بلا بيان* Zulm hai. Adl ka taqaza ye hai ke Test lene ke pahle padhaya aur sikhaya jaye. School mein ek saal Student ko Teacher padhata hai tab uska Exam leta hai. Usi tarah Allah ne apne bandon ki taa'leem o Hidayat ke liye 1,24,000 Paighambar/Anbiya bheje aur baad mein Aimma ka silsila jaari raha. Itne Hadi bhej kar Allah ne Apni Hujjat tamam ki. Uske baad hi Allah ne Apne bande ko Mukallaf banaya aur Sawab wa Eqaab muayyan kiya aur Jannat o Jahannum banayi.
Allah ka Azaab agar kisi bande par nazil hota hai to woh Allah ka Zulm nahi. Banda apne Aamaal ki wajah se khud bhugat raha hota hai, woh Allah ko dosh nahi de sakta. Qudrati afaat Toofan, Zalzala aur Selaab ya insaani jangon mein halakat bhi insaani aamal ka natija hai. Lekin aisa hota hai Zalim ke saath kabhi kabhi begunah bhi halaak ho jaate hain, Allah unko iska Ajr dega. Lekin asbaab khud insaan hi Farahan karta hai. Ahadis mulaheza farmayen.

Fazal bin Sahal ne Imam Reza (as) se Mamun ke Darbar mein sawal kiya, "Ye farmaiye ke kya Bande majboor hain?"
Imam (as) ne farmaya: _"Khuda Aadil hai. Ye mumkin nahi ke Wo logon se jabran Gunah karaaye aur phir uspar unko saza de."_
Fazal ne kaha,
"Achcha, to phir bilkul Azad hain?" 
Imam (as) ne farmaya, _"Nahi. Uski (Allah ki) hikmat se ye baeed hai ke Wo Apne Bande ko bilkul azaad naqaa e be-mehaar (camel without strings / belagaam oont) ki tarah chhod de."_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v5, p177)
🤲🏻
_"Mere Ma'bood! Agar Tu Ma'af kar de to kaun Tujh se zyada Ma'af karne wala hai? Agar Tu Azaab de to kaun Faisla karne mein zyada Aadil hai? Rahem farma...."_
(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumali)
🤲🏻
_"Aye Khuda! Agar Tu chaahe to Apne Fazal se humko Ma'af kar sakta hai aur agar Tu humko Azaab karna chaahe to Tere Adl ke sabab se hoga."_
(Sahifa e Kaamila, Dua No.10)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✋
Imam Ali (as)
_"Aye giroh e Musalman! Zina se bacho kyunki isme 6 (bad / buri) khusoosiyat hain jinme se 3 Duniya mein aur 3 Akherat mein hain._
_3 Duniyavi khususiyaat ye hain:_
_(1) Husn ka khaatma karta hai,_
_(2) Pareshaani aur tang-dasti laata hai,_
_(3) Umr ko kam karta hai._ _

Jab ke Akherat ki 3 khususiyaat ye hain:_
_(1) Khuda ki naraazgi,_
_(2) Hisaab ki badi,_
_(3) Hamesha ke liye Aatish e Jahannum mein rehna."_
(Kaifar e Gunahaane Kabira , p47)

       ♦ _*ALLAH BE NIYAZ HAI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (884)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَرَبُّكَ الْغَنِيُّ ذُو الرَّحْمَةِ ۚ إِنْ يَشَأْ يُذْهِبْكُمْ وَيَسْتَخْلِفْ مِنْ بَعْدِكُمْ مَا يَشَاءُ كَمَا أَنْشَأَكُمْ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّةِ قَوْمٍ آخَرِينَ * إِنَّ مَا تُوعَدُونَ لَآتٍ ۖ وَمَا أَنْتُمْ بِمُعْجِزِينَ*

_"Aur Tera Rab Be Niyaz (Needless) aur Sahibe Rahmat hai. Agar Woh chahe to tumhe Zameen se kar de aur tumhari jagah jin logon ko chahe le aaye jis tarah se Us ne tumko kuchh aur logon kiNasl se uthaya hai. Tum se jis cheez ka wada kiya jaa raha hai woh# yaqeenan aane wali hai aur tum Khuda ko aajiz nahin kar sakte."_
(Surah An'am: 133 - 134)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat is baat ka zikr hai ke Khuda hamara Mohtaj nahi, Woh Be Niyaz hai. Ham sab ko Us taraf palatna hai. Uski Zameen se ham kahi bhag nahi sakte.

🤲🏻
Imam Sajjad (as):
_Mere Sardaar! Main wohi bachcha hun jise Tu ne paala. Main wohi kora hoo'n jise Tu ne Ilm diya. Main wohi gumraah hun jise Tu ne raah dikhayi. Main wo pust hun jise Tu ne buland kiya. Main wohi khauf-zada hun jise Tu ne amn diya. Main wo bhooka hun jise Tu ne seyr kiya. Aur wo pyaasa hun jise Tu ne seyraab kiya. Main wo uryaan hun jise Tu ne libaas diya. Main wo mohtaj hun jise Tu ne ghani banaya. Main wo kamzor hun, jise Tu ne quwwat bakshi. Main wo pust hun jise Tu ne izzat ataa farmayi. Main wo beemar hun jise Tu ne sehet di. Main wo sawaali hun jise Tu ne bahut kuchh ataa kiya. Main wo gunahgaar hun jise Tu ne dhaa'np liya. Main wo khata-kaar hoo'n jise Tu ne muaaf kiya. Main wo kam-tar hun jise Tu ne badha diya hai. Main wo kamzor kiya hua hun jiski Tu ne madad ki aur main wo nikaala hua hun jise Tu ne panaah di."_
(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumali)
🤲🏻
_"Khudaya Teri Saltanat Azeem hai, Teri Manzelat Buland, Teri Tadbeer Makhfi, Tera Amr Zahir, Tera Qahr Ghalib, aur Teri Qudrat Nafiz hai aur Teri Hukumat se faraar namumkin hai._
(Dua-e-Kumail)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤲🏻
Imam Ali (as)
_"Jab Khaaliq se daro to Usi ki taraf faraar karo aur jab makhlooq se daro to us se faraar karo."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p340)

                 ♦ _*AAMAAL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (885)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ يَا قَوْمِ اعْمَلُوا عَلَىٰ مَكَانَتِكُمْ إِنِّي عَامِلٌ ۖ فَسَوْفَ تَعْلَمُونَ مَنْ تَكُونُ لَهُ عَاقِبَةُ الدَّارِ ۗ إِنَّهُ لَا يُفْلِحُ الظَّالِمُونَ*

_"Aap (saww) kah den ke tum apni jagah Amal karte raho, mein apni jagah amal kar raha hun. Tumhe anqareeb maloom ho jayega ke Anjam kar kis tarah behtar hota hai. Is mein shak nahi ke Zalim Falah (Success) nahi pate."_
(Surah An'am: 135)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Akhir mein Allah is baat ki takeed kar raha hai ke Nek Amal karo. Nek Amal mein hi Kamyabi hai. Yahan Kufr ke bajay Zulm lafz istemal hua hai, means Zulm ka dayra wasee hai. Jabke Kufr bhi Zulm hai, lekin Muslim bhi Nek Amal na karke apne upar zulm kar raha hota hai. Kafir bhale hi zulm o jaur se Duniya mein Kamyabi hasil kar le lekin daymi zindagi ke liye uske pas kuchh nahi rahta. Zalim kabhi kamyab nahi ho sakta.
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Nek Amaal karne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌 🧔🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Ulema ke 2 qismein hain; kuchh wo hain jo apne Ilm par Amal karte hain, ye najaat yaafta hain. Lekin kuchh aise hain jo apne Ilm par amal nahi karte, aise afraad halaak ho jayenge aur ahl e Jahannum aise be-amal Aalim ki bad-boo se sakht aziyyat mein rahenge aur Ahl e Jahannum ke darmiyaan sab se zyada nidamat aur hasrat usko hogi jisne kisi ko Khuda ki taraf daawat di hogi aur aur wo uski baat maan kar ita'at e Khuda kar ke Jannat mein daakhil ho jayega magar ye be-amal Aalim apni be-amali aur khwaish e nafs ki pairavi aur lambi lambi aarzuo'n ki bina par Jahannum mein daal diya jayega, kyun ki khwaishaat e nafs ki pairavi insaan ko raah e haq se rok deti hai aur lambi lambi aarzuein Akherat ka khayaal tak insaan ke zehen se nikaal deti hain."_
(Usool e Kaafi, v1, Adaab e Islami, v2, p61)
👺
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Mujhe 3 afraad ke alaawa Ummat ke tamaam afraad ki najaat ki ummeed hai jo hamare haq ki maarefat rakhte ho'n._
_(1) Zaalim badshah,_
_(2) khwaishaat ka gulaam,_
_3) Jo khule aam bad-kaariyaa'n karta hai."_
(Khisaal, p76)
👺
Imam Reza (as):
_"Zaalim hukkam (badshah) ke kaamo'm mein daakhil hona, unki madad karna, unki haajato'n ke liye koshish karna Kufr ke barabar hai. Unki taraf jaan bujh kar nazar rakhna gunahaan e kabira mein daakhil hai jis par aadmi mustahaq e Jahannum hota hai."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p185)

♦ _*MUSHREKIN KI KANDA BANT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (886)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَجَعَلُوا لِلَّهِ مِمَّا ذَرَأَ مِنَ الْحَرْثِ وَالْأَنْعَامِ نَصِيبًا فَقَالُوا هَٰذَا لِلَّهِ بِزَعْمِهِمْ وَهَٰذَا لِشُرَكَائِنَا ۖ فَمَا كَانَ لِشُرَكَائِهِمْ فَلَا يَصِلُ إِلَى اللَّهِ ۖ وَمَا كَانَ لِلَّهِ فَهُوَ يَصِلُ إِلَىٰ شُرَكَائِهِمْ ۗ سَاءَ مَا يَحْكُمُونَ*

_"Un logon ne Allah ki paida ki hui Kheti aur Maveshiyon (cattles) mein Uske liye ek hissa muqarrar kiya hai aur woh kahte hain ke ye Allah ke liye hai apne guman ke mutabiq. Aur ye hamare thairai hue Sharikon ke liye hai. Jo hissa unke thairai hue Sharikon ke liye hai woh to Allah tak nahi pahunchta aur jo hissa Allah ke liye muqarrar hai wo unke thairai hue Sharikon tak ja pahuncha hai. Ye log kaise bure Faisle karte hain."_
(Surah An'am: 136)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Majmaul Bayan mein marqoom hai ke is Ayat ki wazahat ke mutalliq Mufasserin se bahut se aqwaal marvi hain jin mein se doosra aqwaal ye hai ke Mushrekin ka ye wateera tha ke agar Buton ke Maal ke saath Khuda ka Maal makhloot (mix) ho jata to woh  Buton ki Mannat bila kisi kam o kast ke ke ada karte the lekin Khuda ka muqarrar kardah hissa unhe ada nahi karte the aur kahte the ke Khuda to badi Izzat o Shaan wala hai Use bhala is haqeer se hisse ki zaroorat hi kya hai.
Kheti ka jo hissa Khuda ke liye muqarrar hota tha agar uska Paani toot kar Buton ke muqarrar kardah hisse mein chala jata to woh use jaane dete the lekin agar Buton ke liye muqarrar kardah Khet ka Paani toot kar Khuda ke liye muqarrar hisse ki taraf chala jata to woh use fauran band kar dete the aur kahte the ke Allah sab se Bada Daulatmand hai. Use kya zaroorat hai ke Woh Buton Ghareebon  ke hisse ka Paani apne Khet mein le jaye.
Aimma Ahle Bait (as) se iski yehi Tafseer marvi hai.
(Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha ham par karm farma aur hamari Kheti ko abaad rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌾🌾
Imam Askari (as):
_"Tum ko kam hone wali umren mili hain aur chand gine chune din miley hain. Maut kisi bhi waqt achanak aa sakti hai. Jo khair ki zara'at (kheti) karega, wo khushi o nafaa kaatega. Aur jo sharr aur burai ki kaasht (kheti) karega, wo nidamat (sharmindagi) kaatega. Har shakhs ko wohi cheez milegi jiski wo kaasht (kheti) karega."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p243)
🌾🌾
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo Musalman koi cheez kaasht (kheti) karta hai ya darakht lagaata hai aur oos se parinde ya insaan khaayein, to kheti karne waale ki taraf se Sadqa shumaar hota hai."_
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v1, p68)
🎲
Imam Ali Naqi (as):
_*"Nard (paasa / dice), Shatranj aur 14 patto'n ka khel sab ek hi cheez hain aur jis bhi cheez par shart lagayi jaye wo Jua hai."*_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p413)
💐
Imam Naqi (as):
_*"Insaan ki izzat o shakhsiyat duniya mein amwaal (wealth / maal) se hai aur Akherat mein aamaal se hai."*_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p227)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ _*MUSHREKIN KI QURBANI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (887)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَكَذَٰلِكَ زَيَّنَ لِكَثِيرٍ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ قَتْلَ أَوْلَادِهِمْ شُرَكَاؤُهُمْ لِيُرْدُوهُمْ وَلِيَلْبِسُوا عَلَيْهِمْ دِينَهُمْ ۖ وَلَوْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ مَا فَعَلُوهُ ۖ فَذَرْهُمْ وَمَا يَفْتَرُونَ*

_"Aur is tarah bahut se Mushrekin ke liye unke Sharikon ne unki Aulad ke qatl ko khushnuma bana diya hai taake woh unhe halaak karen aur un par unke Deen ko mushtaba kar den aur agar Allah Jabr e Mashiyat se kaam leta to woh aisa na karte. Aap unhe chhod den taake apni aftra parwaziyon (inventions-Bidaat) mein masroof rahen."_
(Surah An'am: 137)

📚📖 🕍
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat ke mazmoon se is Ayat ka mafhoom munsalik hai. Guzishta Ayat mein Mushrekin ki ek khusoosiyat unka Kanda Bant bataya tha. Is Ayat mein is baat ka zikr hai ke woh apne Buton ke itne fidai the ke unke liye apne Auladon ko bhi qurban kar dete the. Woh Mannat mante the aur usko Buton ke saamne usko poora karte the. Unke Mandir ke Pujari unhe uksate the. Jabke do lakdiyon ko thaile dal kar Lottery nikalte the. Jaise saara chadhawa ye Pujaari rakh lete the. Yehi Mushrekin ko apne qabze mein rakhte the. Woh sab unki andhi Taqleed karte the.
Aaj bhi is tarah ke waqeat runuma hote rahte hai. Arab ka Jahiliyyat ka rivaj khud India aur Pakistan mein bhi amal mein aate hai. Chahe woh Mandir ho ya koi Baba ki Dargah ho.
Allah is baat par Qadir hai ke Woh ye sab ghalat rivaaj ko rok de, lekin ye Jabr hai, aur Allah Jabr nahi karta. Allah ne bande ko Ikhtiyar de rakha hai chahe woh sahi Amal kare ya bhatka rahe.
Isliye Allah ne unko chhod diya taake woh isi Bidaton mein masroof rahen. Jo bekar ke kaamon mein masroof rahega woh hamesha ghaate mein rahega, kabhi usko Kamyabi naseeb nahi hogi.

Riwayat
Fazal bin Sahal ne Imam Reza (as) se Mamun ke darbaar mein sawaal kiya, _"Ye farmaiye ke kya Bande majboor hain?"_
Imam (as) ne farmaya, _"Khuda Aadil hai. Ye mumkin nahi ke Wo logo'n se jabran gunah karaaye aur phir uspar unko saza de."_
Fazal ne kaha,
_"Achcha, to phir bilkul azaad hain?"_
Imam (as) ne farmaya,
_"Nahi. Uski (Allah ki) hikmat se ye baeed hai ke Wo Apne Bande ko bilkul azaad naqaa e be-mehaar (camel without strings / belagaam oo'ntt) ki tarah chhod de."_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v5, p177)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hamare Dilon ko Tu Apni taraf mod de taake Teri Ibaadat mein badh chadh kar hissa len.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🛤
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Har Bid'at gumrahi hai aur har gumrahi ka raasta Jahannum ki taraf jaata hai."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v3, p362)

Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Yaqeenan jab fitna shuru hoga to logon ko jadd se ukhaad phenkega, sirf wohi shakhs najaat paayega jo apne Ilm par amal karta hai."
(Hadiyat u_sh Shia, p35)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 *8th Rajab 1439*
       *27th March 2018, Tuesday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
      ♦ _*MUSHREKIN KA IFTERA'*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (888)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالُوا هَٰذِهِ أَنْعَامٌ وَحَرْثٌ حِجْرٌ لَا يَطْعَمُهَا إِلَّا مَنْ نَشَاءُ بِزَعْمِهِمْ وَأَنْعَامٌ حُرِّمَتْ ظُهُورُهَا وَأَنْعَامٌ لَا يَذْكُرُونَ اسْمَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهَا افْتِرَاءً عَلَيْهِ ۚ سَيَجْزِيهِمْ بِمَا كَانُوا يَفْتَرُونَ*
*وَقَالُوا مَا فِي بُطُونِ هَٰذِهِ الْأَنْعَامِ خَالِصَةٌ لِذُكُورِنَا وَمُحَرَّمٌ عَلَىٰ أَزْوَاجِنَا ۖ وَإِنْ يَكُنْ مَيْتَةً فَهُمْ فِيهِ شُرَكَاءُ ۚ سَيَجْزِيهِمْ وَصْفَهُمْ ۚ إِنَّهُ حَكِيمٌ عَلِيمٌ*

_"Aur unhone kaha hai ke ye Khet aur Janwar mehfooz hain. Unhe sirf wohi khaa sakte hain jinhe ham khilana chahen halanki ye unki khud sakhta pabandi hai. Phir kuchh janwar aise hain jinki pusht sawari mamnoo qarar de di gayi hai aur kuchh Janwar aise hain jin par Allah ka Naam nahi lete. Ye sab Khuda par iftera' parwaziyon ka badla dega."_
_"Aur unhone kaha hai jo kuchh un Janwaron ke Pet mein hai hamare Mardon ke liye Halaal hai aur hamari Aurton par Haraam hai. Agarche Janwar mar gaya ho to phir sab us mein hissedar hain. Ye baten jo unhone tarashi hain Khuda unka unhe badla dega. Beshak Woh Sahebe Hikmat aur Sahebe Ilm hai."_
(Surah An'am: 138 - 139)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein un pabandiyon ka zikr hai jo khud Mushrekin ne doosron par khud sakhta laga rakhin thi. Kuchh is mein se Sura Maeda: 103 mein zikr ho chuka hai. "Hijr  *حجر*" Pabandi ke maani mein istemal hota hai. Isi se bana hai *حجارة* yani patthar jo raaste mein rokne ke liye rakh dete hain. Hajr e Aswad ka mafhoom bhi yehi hai jis ke zariye Masjidul Haraam ko alag kiya gaya hai. Aql ko bhi kabhi kabhi Hijr kaha jaata hai kyonki ye buraiyon se rokti hai.
Is mein aise Janwar bhi the jin par Bismillah ke bajae Buton ka naam liya jaata tha. Kuchh Janwar aise the jin par sawari Haraam thi. Aur woh in sab Pabandiyon ki nisbat Khuda se dete the jo ke man ghadat thi.
(Al Munar, Tafseer Majmaul Bayan)
Unke sab ye Ahkam behuda the aur Aql se pare the. Jaise ke unka ek qanoon ye tha ke Janwar ke pet mein se jo bachcha (Fetus) agar zinda nikle to unka aur murda nikle to sabka. Aur ye proved fact hai ke inka khaana nihayat hi muzir nuqsandeh hai kyonki aise Gosht aksar kharab hote hain.
Is tarah se Allah ne hamko ye bataya ke dekho kausa raasta behtar hai Islam ka ya Mushrekin ka.
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Mushrekin ke shar se door rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🐐
Muhammad bin Fuzail kehte hain ke maine Imam Sadiq (as) se Qurbani ke gosht ke masraf ke baare mein daryaaft kiya to Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Imam Zainul Abideen (as) aur Imam Baqir (as) is gosht ka tihaai (one third) hissa padosiyon ko aur ek tihaai Mohtaajon aur Miskeenon ko aur ek tihaai apne Ahl o Ayaal (family) par taqseem farmate the."_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v4, p79)
🐐
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Wo jaanwar jo saaf langda nazar aata ho ya wo jo saaf kaana ho uski ek aa'nkh zaaya ho gayi ho, ya jo bilkul laagar (patla) dubla ho, ya jo khaarshi ho baal jhadd gaye ho'n, ya jis ke kaan jadd se katey huwe ho'n, ya jis ke kaan phatey huwe ho'n, uski qurbaani na ki jaaye."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v2, p291)
🚩
Imam Sajjad (as)
_"Tum hum se wo mohabbat rakho jo Islami qanoon ke hudood (within boundaries of Islamic laws) mein ho. Tumhari humse mohabbat aisi honi chahiye ke wo hamare liye aib ka baayis (sabab) na ho aur hamari na-khushi ka baes bhi na ho."_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v6, p86)

           ♦ _*QATL-E-AULAAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (889)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَدْ خَسِرَ الَّذِينَ قَتَلُوا أَوْلَادَهُمْ سَفَهًا بِغَيْرِ عِلْمٍ وَحَرَّمُوا مَا رَزَقَهُمُ اللَّهُ افْتِرَاءً عَلَى اللَّهِ ۚ قَدْ ضَلُّوا وَمَا كَانُوا مُهْتَدِينَ*

_"Yaqeenan un logon ne Khasare ka sauda kiya jinhone jihalat o nadani ki wajah se apni Aulad ko qatl kiya hai aur Khuda par iftrapardazi karte hue Khuda ke diye hue Rizq ko Haraam kiya hai. Ye log bhatak gaye hain aur woh Hidayat paane walon mein se na the."_
(Surah An'am: 140)

📚📖 🧟‍♂
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaton mein Mushrekin iftrapardaziyon ka zikr hua. Allah ne unke rasm o rivaj ki mazammat ki. Un mein se ek ye ke woh apni Aulad ka qurbani ke Naam par qatl karte the. Is mein aksar ladkiya hoti thi. Qatl ki doosri wajah woh ghuraba the jo darte the ke ham apni Aulad ko kaise paale posenge. Aur aaj bhi aisa hota hai Abortion ke zariye. Insaan bhool jaata hai ke Allah Raziq hai. Woh samjhta hai ke jo mein kama raha hun woh meri mehnat hai. Rizq sirf Khaane peena ka naam nahi balke har wo Ne'mat jo Allah ne di woh uske liye Rizq hai. Aulad bhi Rizq hai, aur Rizq e Halaal hai. Allah is baat ka zikr kar raha hai ke tum kyon Allah ke Rizq ko thukra rahe ho. Sura Bani Israel: 31 mein bhi is baat ka zikr hai. Ibne Abbas kahte hain ke Jo shakhs Zamana Jahiliyyat ki Qaumon ki pasmandgi (backwardness) ke meezan (scale) ko janna chahe woh ye Ayat (6:140) padh le.
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame ek aisi besharm harkaat karne se mehfooz rakhna.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👨‍👩‍👧‍👧
Imam Ali (as)
_"Aulaad ki maut dilo'n ko jalaa deti hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p46)
👨‍👨‍👦‍👦
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Jo shakhs apni Aulaad ke liye bad-Dua karta hai, usay Allah faqeeri aur tang-dasti ke hawaale kar deta hai."_
Rizq (Haji Naji)
🧟‍♂
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Nek Aulaad Jannat ke khushbu-daar phoolo'n mein se ek khushbu-daar phool hai."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v15, p103)

     ♦ _*ZARA'AT (AGRICULTURE)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (890)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَهُوَ الَّذِي أَنْشَأَ جَنَّاتٍ مَعْرُوشَاتٍ وَغَيْرَ مَعْرُوشَاتٍ وَالنَّخْلَ وَالزَّرْعَ مُخْتَلِفًا أُكُلُهُ وَالزَّيْتُونَ وَالرُّمَّانَ مُتَشَابِهًا وَغَيْرَ مُتَشَابِهٍ ۚ كُلُوا مِنْ ثَمَرِهِ إِذَا أَثْمَرَ وَآتُوا حَقَّهُ يَوْمَ حَصَادِهِ ۖ وَلَا تُسْرِفُوا ۚ إِنَّهُ لَا يُحِبُّ الْمُسْرِفِينَ*

_"Aur Wohi to hai jisne Takhto par chadhaye hue Baghat aur Takhto par na chadhaye hue Baghaat paida kiye hain. Khajoor aur Zara'at (Kheti) paida ki hai jin ke zaiyqe mukhtalif hain. Zaitoon (Olive) aur Anaar paida kiye hain un mein se baaz ek doosre se milte julte hain aur baaz mukhtalif hain. Jab wo Phal pak jayen to khao aur jab katne ka Din aaye to unka haq ada karo aur israaf na karna. Is mein shak nahi ke Allah israaf karne walon (extravagant) ko pasand nahi karta."_
(Surah An'am: 141)

📚📖 🌴🌾
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ek Yahoodi ne Hazrat Ali (as) se sawal kiya:
_"Rooye Zameen par sab se pahle kaunsa darakht paida hua tha?"_
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Tumhara khayal ye hai ke sab se pahle Zaitoon ka darakht paida hua lekin tumhara ye khayal jhoot par mabni hai. Sab se pahle Allah ne "Ajwa - *عجوه*" Khajoor ko paida kiya tha. Hazrat Adam (as) ise Jannat se le kar Zameen par aaye the aur phir Duniya mein Khajoor ki jitni qismen payi jaati hain woh sab ki sab "Ajwa" se hi paida hui hain."_
(Kamaluddin wa Tamamun Ne'ma)
🌴
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jab Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Adam (as) ko paida kiya to kuchh Mitti bach gayi thi. Us bachi hui Mitti se Khuda ne Khajoor paida ki. Us mein insaano ki sifaat payi jaati hain. Jis tarah se insaan ka Sar kat jaye to woh mar jaata hai usi tarah se jab Khajoor ka Sar kaat diya jaye to wo bhi mar jaati hai. Insaano ki tarah Khajoor ko bhi Zarpashi (agriculture) ki ehtiyaj hoti hai."_
(Ilalush Sharay, Noorus Saqlain)
🌾🌾
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Fasal ke waqt do qism ke Huqooq ki adaygi zaroori hai. Ek Haq wo hai jo tumse liya jaata hai aur ek Haq wo hai jise tumne khud logon tak pahunchana hai. Wo Haq jo tumse liya jaata hai wo Fasal ka Daswan (¹/10) ya Beeswa (¹/20) hissa hai aur doosra Haq jo tumne khud dena hai wo ye ke Fasal ki katai ke Din kuchh ghalla ya phal ka hissa le kar ghuraba wa Masakeen mein taqseem karo."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🌾🌴
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Is Ayat ka maqsad ye hai ke jab tum apni Fasal kaato to apne Qareebi Azeezon ko bhi is mein kuchh hissa do."_
_"Khajoor ka Phal ya koi bhi Fasal Raat ke waqt na kaati jaye."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha Tere ata karda hamare Baghaat o Zara'at hari bari wa phali phooli rahen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍎🍊
*Imam Muhammad Taqi (as):*
_"4 baatein insaan ko amal par ubhaarti hai: Sehet, Maaldaari, Ilm, Taufeeq."_
Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p205
🥗🥙🌮
*Imam Muhammad Taqi (as):*
_"Jis Ne'mat ka shukriya adaa na kiya jaaye wo us gunah ke misl hai jo baksha na jaaye."_
(Aqwaal 14 Masumeen (as), p207)

                  ♦ _*ISRAAF*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (891)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

وَهُوَ الَّذِي أَنْشَأَ جَنَّاتٍ مَعْرُوشَاتٍ وَغَيْرَ مَعْرُوشَاتٍ وَالنَّخْلَ وَالزَّرْعَ مُخْتَلِفًا أُكُلُهُ وَالزَّيْتُونَ وَالرُّمَّانَ مُتَشَابِهًا وَغَيْرَ مُتَشَابِهٍ ۚ *كُلُوا مِنْ ثَمَرِهِ إِذَا أَثْمَرَ وَآتُوا حَقَّهُ يَوْمَ حَصَادِهِ ۖ وَلَا تُسْرِفُوا ۚ إِنَّهُ لَا يُحِبُّ الْمُسْرِفِينَ*

_"Aur Wohi to hai jisne Takhto par chadhaye hue Baghat aur Takhto par na chadhaye hue Baghaat paida kiye hain. Khajoor aur Zara'at (Kheti) paida ki hai jin ke zaiyqe mukhtalif hain. Zaitoon (Olive) aur Anaar paida kiye hain un mein se baaz ek doosre se milte julte hain aur baaz mukhtalif hain. *Jab wo Phal pak jayen to khao aur jab katne ka Din aaye to unka haq ada karo aur israaf na karna. Is mein shak nahi ke Allah israaf karne walon (extravagant) ko pasand nahi karta."*_
(Surah An'am: 141)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein jahan Katai wa Buwai ka zikr hai, jabke ye Fasal, Phal sab Allah ki Ne'maten hai, wahi Israaf na karne ki takeed ki gayi hai.
🌾🌴
Imam Musa Kazim (as) is Ayat mein "Musrefeen" ka mafhoom is taraf farmate hain:
_"Mere Walid farmate the ke Katai aur Buwai (Harvesting & Sowing) ke Din do hathon se bhar kar ghalla taqseem karna bhi Israaf (extravagance) mein shamil hai. Aur jab mere walid apne kisi Ghulam ko dono hatheliyon se ghalla taqseem karte hue dekhte to Aap cheekh kar usse kahte the ke ek haath se khairat do. Aur agar Fasal Khoshon ki shakal mein hoti to Sael ko ek mutthi bhar kar khoshe diya karte the."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Musrefeen mein shamil na karna.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💰
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ko jahan Fuzool Kharchi Na-Pasand hai wahan Kanjoosi bhi Na-Pasand hai. Insaan ko Fuzool Kharchi aur Kanjoosi dono se parhez karna chahiye aur darmiyani raasta (moderate) ikhtiyar karna chahiye. Aisa na ho ke saari daulat luta de phir Khuda se Rizq ka sawal kare aur Khuda uski Dua qubool na kare."_
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Qurbul Asnaad,  Noorus Saqlain)
🎊🎉
Imam Sadiq (as) se poochha Israaf ke hudood ki ibteda kaha se shuru hoti hai?
Aap ne farmaya:
_"Bila zaroorat libaas badalna, khwah ma khwah Paani udelna aur Khajooren kha kar idhar udhar guthliyon ko phekna Israaf mein shamil hain."_
(Al Kaafi)
🎊🎉
Imam Askari (as):
_"Sakhaawat ki ek hadd muqarrar hai, agar us se badhh jaye to Israaf hoga. Door-andeshi (far-sight) ki ek hadd muqarrar hai, agar us se badh jaye to buzdili hogi. Iqtesad aur miyana-rawi (moderation) ki ek hadd hoti hai, agar usse badh jaye to bukhl (Kanjoosi) hoga aur shuja'at (bahaduri) ki bhi ek hadd muqarrar hai, agar us se badh jaaye to tahawwur (bewaqoofi) hoga."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p222)
🎊🎉
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Israaf karne wale ki 3 Nishaniyan hain:_
_(1) Woh Aisi cheez ki kharidari karega jiski zaroorat na hogi._
_(2) Woh aisa libaas pahnega jo uski isteta'at se bahar hoga._
_(3) Woh aisi ghaza khayega jo uski hasiyat se buland hogi."_
_"Ta'am mein koi Israaf nahi hai."_
(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                *12th Rajab 1439*
       *31st March 2018, Saturday,*

♦ _*BADE AUR CHHOTE JANWAR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (892)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمِنَ الْأَنْعَامِ حَمُولَةً وَفَرْشًا ۚ كُلُوا مِمَّا رَزَقَكُمُ اللَّهُ وَلَا تَتَّبِعُوا خُطُوَاتِ الشَّيْطَانِ ۚ إِنَّهُ لَكُمْ عَدُوٌّ مُبِينٌ*

_"Aur Chaupaon (Cattles) mein se kuchh bojh uthane wale hain aur kuchh Zameen par ghisat kar chalne wale hain. Khuda ne jo tum ko Rizq diya hai us mein se khao aur Shaitan ke Nishan e Qadam par na chalo. Beshak woh tumhara khula hua Dushman hai."_
(Surah An'am: 142)

📚📖 🐃🐑
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein Allah Apni Ne'maton mein se Zara'at wa Baghaat wa phalon ka zikr kiya jisko ham apne Khaane mein istemal karte hain.
Is Ayat mein aur agli Ayaat mein Janwaron ka zikr hai jinko ham istemal karte hain chahe Khaane mein ya Dhone (carry) mein, ye sab Allah ki Den hain.
Is Ayat mein 2 tarah ke Janwaron ka zikr hai: Bade aur chhote Janwar. Qur'an mein hamne dekh mukhtalif tarjuma paya gaya hai.
Haml *حمل* yani sawari wale Janwar. Doosra lafz istemal hua hai: *فرش* Farsh, iske maani wohi hain jo ham jaante hain, zameen, carpet ya qaleen. Ye yahan inki khusoosiyat batayi hai. Noorus Saqlain mein tarjuma hai ghisat kar chalne wale Janwar, jabke doosri jagah tarjuma hai: Chhote Qad ke Janwar, woh Janwar jo Khaane aur bichhane ke kaam mein aate hain. Isliye isse murad Reptiles nahi hain. Reptiles ko ham khaa nahi sakte. Bhed (Sheep) jise Khaa bhi sakte hain aur uske Oon (Wool) se carpet bhi bana lete hain waghaira. Isliye Allah farmata hai jo Halaal wa Jaez hai uske diye Rizq se khao. Haraam wa Halaal Janwaron ke bare mein Sura Baqarah: 168 mein tauzeeh ki gayi hai. Allah ne isi liye kaha ke Shaitan ke Naqshe qadam par na chalen, kyonki Islami Shariyat ki pabandi na karna, Khaane Peene mein Ehtiyat na baratna Shaitan ki pairavi karna hai.
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Halaal Ghaza Khaane ki taufeeq ata farma
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ka ek Farishta rozana manaadi deta hai ke 'Allah ke Bando! Uski na-farmaani se baaz aa jao. Agar be-zubaan chaupaaye (jaanwar) na hote, sheer-khwaar (dudh peene waale) masoom bachche na hote aur Ruku karne waale budhhe na hote to tum par Azaab ka meenah (baarish) barsa diya jaata, jiske zariye se tumhe pees diya jaata."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p198)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹
*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*
*(Shahadat Janabe Zainab (as) wa Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) ba Rivate digar)*

       *3rd April 2018, Tuesday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
     ♦ _*8 CHAUPAON KE JODE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (893)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*ثَمَانِيَةَ أَزْوَاجٍ ۖ مِنَ الضَّأْنِ اثْنَيْنِ وَمِنَ الْمَعْزِ اثْنَيْنِ ۗ قُلْ آلذَّكَرَيْنِ حَرَّمَ أَمِ الْأُنْثَيَيْنِ أَمَّا اشْتَمَلَتْ عَلَيْهِ أَرْحَامُ الْأُنْثَيَيْنِ ۖ نَبِّئُونِي بِعِلْمٍ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ*

_"Ye 8 Jode (pairs) hain. Bhed (Sheep) ki qism se do aur Bakri ki qism se do. Aap poochhen ke Allah ne unke nar (male) Haraam kiye hain ya maada (female)? Ya wo bachche jo Bhedon aur Bakriyon ke pet mein hon? Theek theek Ilm ke saath khabar do agar tum sachche ho."_
(Surah An'am: 143)

📚📖 🐑🐏🐐🐄🐪🐫
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat no. 142 mein kuchh Chaupaon ki taraf ishara kiya tha taake ham Halaal tariqe se un mein se khaa sakte hain. Unke naam is Ayat mein darj hain:
📝
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Qurbani ke liye Bhed Bakri ki paltu (pet) qism ko qurban karna chahiye. Jangli aur Pahadi qism ko qurbani mein zabah nahi karna chahiye. Aur Oont ki jins mein se aam Arabi Oont qurbani mein zabah karna chahiye. "Bakhati - *بخاتى*" (do kohan wala Oont) zabah nahi karna chahiye. Aur Gay (Cow) ki jins mein se gharelu Gay ko Qurbani mein zabah karna chahiye. Sahrai Gay (Neel Gay) ki Qurbani nahi karni chahiye."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🐑🐏🐐🐄🐪🐫
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Hazrat Nooh (as) ne apni Kashti mein Halaal Janwaron ke 8 Jode sawar kiye the. Do Bhed ki jins ki qismen thin aur do Bakri ki qismen thi, do Oont ki qismen thin aur do Gaye ki qismen thin. Bhed ki ek paltu hai jise log apne gharon mein palte hain aur ek qism pahadon mein rahti hai jiska shikar logon ke liye Halaal qarar diya gaya. Isi tarah se Bakri ki jins mein se ek paltu janwar hai jise log gharon mein palte hain aur iski doosri qism Hiran (Deer) hain jo ke sahraon mein paye jate hain. Oont ki ek qism aam Oonton par mushtamil hai aur doosri qism "Bakhati" Oonton par mushtamil hai. Gaye ki ek jins (nomenclature) gharon mein payee jaati hai aur doosri jins sahraon mein rahti hai (yani Neel Gaye). Iske alawa tamam Paak Sahrai aur gharelu Parinde bhi Hazrat Nooh (as) ki Kashti mein sawar the."_
(Roza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Halaal Rizq Khaane ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

🙇🐎🐺🐕
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Jaanwar Jannat mein daakhil na honge siwaaye 3 ke: Balam e Ba'oor ka gadha, H. Yusuf (as) ka bhediya aur As'haab e Kahaf ka kutta."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p94)
🔪
Imam Ali (as)
_*"Halaal ki talaash har Musalman mard aur aurat par waajib."*_
Meezan ul Hikmah, v4, p236
🥣🍪
Rasule Khuda (saww)
_"Jab ta'am (Khaane) mein 4 cheezein jama ho jaayein to usme Barkat hoti hai: Jab ta'am Halaal se tayyar kiya jaaye, uske khaane waale zyada ho'n, ibteda mein Bismillah padhhi jaaye, aakhir mein bhi Alhamdulillah kaha jaaye."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p253)

(Meezan ul Hikmah)

        ♦ _*OONT AUR GAI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (894)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمِنَ الْإِبِلِ اثْنَيْنِ وَمِنَ الْبَقَرِ اثْنَيْنِ ۗ قُلْ آلذَّكَرَيْنِ حَرَّمَ أَمِ الْأُنْثَيَيْنِ أَمَّا اشْتَمَلَتْ عَلَيْهِ أَرْحَامُ الْأُنْثَيَيْنِ ۖ أَمْ كُنْتُمْ شُهَدَاءَ إِذْ وَصَّاكُمُ اللَّهُ بِهَٰذَا ۚ فَمَنْ أَظْلَمُ مِمَّنِ افْتَرَىٰ عَلَى اللَّهِ كَذِبًا لِيُضِلَّ النَّاسَ بِغَيْرِ عِلْمٍ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَهْدِي الْقَوْمَ الظَّالِمِينَ*

_"Aur Oont ki qism mein se do aur Gay mein se do. Unse kahiye ke Khuda ne Naron (Male) ko Haraam kiya hai ya Maada (Female) ko ya unko jo Maada ke shikam (Womb) mein hain? Kya tum log us waqt hazir the jab Khuda unko Haraam karne ki wasiyat kar raha tha? Phir usse bada Zalim kaun hai jo Khuda par jhoota ilzaam lagaye taake logo ko baghair jaane boojhe gumrah kare. Yaqeenan Allah Zalim Qaum ko Hidayat nahi deta."_
(Surah An'am: 144)

📚📖 🐪🐫 🐄🐄
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaton mein kuchh Mushrekin ki harkaat ka zikr kiya gaya tha kaise unhone apni taraf apne fayde ke mutabiq apni shariyat bana rakhi thi, kuchh cheezen Halaal aur kuchh Haraam kar di gayin thi. Ye sab woh Khuda ko mansoob karte the. Yani Bhagwan ka adesh hai aur palan na karne par Bhagwan naraz ho jayega, Murtiya sharap uglengi. Sab behooda Aqaid rakhte the. Is Ayat mein Allah unhi ki baat ko dohraya hai aur sawal kar raha hai ke jab Allah Haraam Halaal kar raha tha jab kya ye majood the? Hargiz nahi. To kaise khud qanoon bana rahe hain aur mansoob Allah ko kar rahe hain, ye to Allah par Tohmat hai. Allah par Tohmat kitna bada Zulm hai. Allah aise Zalim ki Hidayat nahi karega.

Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim Qummi mein hai ke Oont ki do qisme yani do Kohan wale aur aam Oont murad hain, unhe Khuda ne Halaal kiya hai.

🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Halaal Ghaza khaane ki taufeeq ata farma
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😏
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Kisi ke pichhe aisi baat kehna jo (usme maujud ho aur) usay buri lage wo Gaabat hai. Aisi baat kehna jo usme maujood na ho to ye bohtaan hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v7)
😍
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jhoot na sanjeedgi (seriousness) mein behtar hai aur na ha'nsi mazaaq mein."_
(Adaab e Islami, v1, p329)
🌵
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"3 logo'n ne Rasulallah (saww) par Jhoot baandha (jhooti Ahadees mansoob ki / ascribed false traditions to the Holy Prophet (saww)), 1) Abu Huraira, 2) Anas Bin  Maalik aur 3) Ek Aurat."_
(Khisaal, p105)

        ♦ _*HARAAM JANWAR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (895)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ لَا أَجِدُ فِي مَا أُوحِيَ إِلَيَّ مُحَرَّمًا عَلَىٰ طَاعِمٍ يَطْعَمُهُ إِلَّا أَنْ يَكُونَ مَيْتَةً أَوْ دَمًا مَسْفُوحًا أَوْ لَحْمَ خِنْزِيرٍ فَإِنَّهُ رِجْسٌ أَوْ فِسْقًا أُهِلَّ لِغَيْرِ اللَّهِ بِهِ ۚ فَمَنِ اضْطُرَّ غَيْرَ بَاغٍ وَلَا عَادٍ فَإِنَّ رَبَّكَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ*

_"Aap kah dijiye ke mein apni taraf aane wali Waḥy mein kisi bhi Khaane wale ke liye koi Haraam nahi pata magar ye ke Murdar ho ya bahaya hua Khoon ya Suar ka Gosht ho ke ye sab Rijs aur Gandgi hai ya woh nafarmani ho jise ghair e Khuda ke naam par zabah kiya gaya ho. Iske baad bhi koi majboori ho jaye aur na sarkash ho, na hadd se tajawuz karne wala, to Parwardigar bada Meherban hai."_
(Surah An'am: 145)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein jo sawal kiya gaya tha, Allah uska jawab is Ayat mein de raha hai.
🐬🐋🦈🐖
Imam Baqir (as) se " *جریث* Jet Fish" ke bare sawal kiya to Aap (as) ne ye Ayat padhi (6:145) aur farmaya:
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Qur'an mein Janwaron mein se sirf Suar (Pork) ko Haraam qarar diya hai. Samandar ke wo tamam Janwar jin par chandi jaisa chhilka (scale) na ho to unka khana Makrooh hai, Haraam nahi."_
Jerry Fish ( *جری*) aur Marmahi *مارماہی* aur "Zameer *زمیر* aur un Machhliyon ke mutalliq poochha jin par chhilka na ho ke aaya wo Haraam hain?
Aap (as) ne ye Ayat padhi aur farmaya:
_"Haraam wohi hai jise Allah aur Uske Rasool (saww) ne Haraam qarar diya hai. Albatta log kucch cheezon se parhez karte hain, ham bhi un se parhez karte hain."_
(Tehzeebul Ahkam, Noorus Saqlain)
🐎🎠
Imam Baqir (as) se Shikari Parindon aur wahshi Janwaron Khar pusht watat ke Gadhe, Ghode aur Khachchar ke mutalliq poochha to Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Haraam wohi hai jise Allah ne Apni Kitab mein Haraam qarar diya hai. Rasoole Akram (saww) ne Gadhe (Donkey) Gosht ki is liye mumaniyat (prohibition) ki thi ke kahin unki nasl hi khatm na ho jaye magar Gadhe Haraam nahi hain. Phir ye Ayat padhi: (6:145)."_
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Halaal Ghiza Khaane ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Zameen par Imam ka hona zaroori hai jo Halaal o Haraam aur un tamaam umoor (affairs) ka Aalim ho jinke log mohtaaj hai."_
(Kamaluddin, v1, p248)

Imam Ali (as):
_"Agar Allah ne Haraam se Na roka hota phir bhi Aqalmand ke liye us se parhez karna laazim tha."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, Vol 3)

♦ _*YAHOODIYON KE LIYE HARAAM JANWAR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (896)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَعَلَى الَّذِينَ هَادُوا حَرَّمْنَا كُلَّ ذِي ظُفُرٍ ۖ وَمِنَ الْبَقَرِ وَالْغَنَمِ حَرَّمْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ شُحُومَهُمَا إِلَّا مَا حَمَلَتْ ظُهُورُهُمَا أَوِ الْحَوَايَا أَوْ مَا اخْتَلَطَ بِعَظْمٍ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ جَزَيْنَاهُمْ بِبَغْيِهِمْ ۖ وَإِنَّا لَصَادِقُونَ*

_"Aur Yahoodiyon par Hamne har Nakhoon wale Janwar ko Haraam kar diya aur Gaye aur Bhed ki charbi ko Haraam kar diya magar charbi peeth par ho ya Aanton par ho ya jo Haddiyon se lagi hui ho. Ye Hamne unki baghawat aur sarkashi ki saza di hai aur Ham bilkul Sachche hain. Phir agar ye Aapko jhutlayen to kah den ke tumhara Parwardigar badi wasee Rehmat wala hai lekin iska Azaab mujremeen se taala bhi nahi jaa sakta."_
(Surah An'am: 146)

📚📖 🐄 🐑🐏
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat ahm tazkara ye hai ke Allah ne Yahoodiyon par ye Janwar unki sarkashi aur zulm ki wajah se Azaab ke taur par Haraam kiye.
'Zufr- *ظفر* means 'Nakhoon-Nails' lekin yahan isse murad Sumdar Janwar hain, woh jinka sum phata na ho.
🦅🦇🐇🐰😼
Imam Reza (as):
_"Har panje rakhne wala darinda aur parindon ko panjon se daboch lene wala har Parinda Haraam hai."_
_"Khargosh ka khaana isliye Haraam qarar diya gaya ke wo Billi (Cat) ki manind hai. Billi aur doosre Darindon ki tarah se uske bhi panje hain."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Noorus Saqlain)
📚
Qur'an ne jo is Ayat mein zikr kiya hai wo sab Torah mein bhi maujood hai, misal ke taur par peshe khidmat hai:
_4 "‘There are some that only chew the cud or only have a divided hoof, but you must not eat them. The camel, though it chews the cud, does not have a divided hoof; it is ceremonially unclean for you."_
_26 “‘Every animal that does not have a divided hoof or that does not chew the cud is unclean for you; whoever touches the carcass of any of them will be unclean."_
_27 "Of all the animals that walk on all fours, those that walk on their paws are unclean for you; whoever touches their carcasses will be unclean till evening."_
_28 "Anyone who picks up their carcasses must wash their clothes, and they will be unclean till evening. These animals are unclean for you."_
(Book of Leviticus, Chap. 11, Verse:4, 26-28)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Yahoodiyon ke shar se door rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕍 🕎
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"7 aadmiyo'n ka azaab sab se zyada shadeed hoga: Qaabil, Namrood, Baani e Yahoodiyat (Founder of Jewism), Baani e Nasraniyat (Founder of Christianity), Firoun aur 2 aadmi is Ummat ke."_
(Khisaal, Chapter7)
🌌
Ameerul Mo'meneen Hazrat Ali (as):
*آنا قابض ارواح و بأس الله الذي لا يرده عن القوم المجرمين.*
_"Mein Rooh ko Qabz karne wala hun aur Mein Khuda ka wo Azaab hun jise Mujrim qaum se hataya nahi jaa sakta."_
(Kitab Ma'anil Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

♦ _*JABR: MUSHREKIN KA AQEEDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (897)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَإِنْ كَذَّبُوكَ فَقُلْ رَبُّكُمْ ذُو رَحْمَةٍ وَاسِعَةٍ وَلَا يُرَدُّ بَأْسُهُ عَنِ الْقَوْمِ الْمُجْرِمِينَ * سَيَقُولُ الَّذِينَ أَشْرَكُوا لَوْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ مَا أَشْرَكْنَا وَلَا آبَاؤُنَا وَلَا حَرَّمْنَا مِنْ شَيْءٍ ۚ كَذَٰلِكَ كَذَّبَ الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ حَتَّىٰ ذَاقُوا بَأْسَنَا ۗ قُلْ هَلْ عِنْدَكُمْ مِنْ عِلْمٍ فَتُخْرِجُوهُ لَنَا ۖ إِنْ تَتَّبِعُونَ إِلَّا الظَّنَّ وَإِنْ أَنْتُمْ إِلَّا تَخْرُصُونَ*

_"Anqareeb ye Mushrekin kahenge: 'Agar Khuda chahta to na ham Mushrik hote na hamare Baap Dada aur na ham kisi cheez ko Haraam qarar dete.' Isi tarah unse pahle walon ne Rasoolon ki takzeeb ki thi yahan tak ke hamare Azaab ka Maza chakh liya. Unse kah dijiye ke tumhare paas koi daleel hai to Hamen batao. Tum sirf khayalat ka itteba' (follow) karte ho aur niri qayas araiyyan karte ho."_
(Surah An'am: 147 - 148)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Al Hamdo lillah 1 Para khatm hua aur doosre Para ka aghaz hota hai.
Is Ayat se ye zahir hota hai ke Mushrekin "Jabr" ka Aqeeda rakhte the. Isi mafhoom ka zikr Ayat Surah Nahi: 35 aur Surah Zukhruf: 20 mein bhi hai.
Jabr o Tafveez ki bahes ham pahle bhi kar chuke hain. Hamari Tafseer mein isi Surah An'am ki Ayat 99-113 ke zel mein bhi Jabr o Tafveez ka hamne tazkara kiya hai, refer kar sakte hain.
Deen mein Jabr yaani jo hamare haath se sarzad ho raha hai wo Allah karwa raha hai. Jabke Allah Ayaatul Kursi mein farmata hai 'Deen mein koi Jabr nahi.' Tafveez yani Insaan apne Amaal mein mukammal Azaad hai. Imam Sadiq (as) ke mutabiq na poora Jabr hai, na poori tarah Azaad hain balke beech ka raasta hai. Khulafa ne Jabr ka raasta apnaya. Yazeed ne jo kuchh zulm Ahle Bait (as) par kiya us par se apna daman saaf jhad kar kahne laga ke ye sab to taqdeer ka khel hai, Allah ne mere muqaddar mein zulm karna likha tha to meine kiya aur Allah ne karwaya. Aaj bhi Ashairah yehi Aqeeda rakhte hain. Qur'an ki is Ayat mein bhi Allah hame bata raha hai ke ye Mushrekin ka Aqeeda tha aur guzishta Nabiyon ki Ummat bhi yehi Aqeeda rakhti thi.
Allah ne is Aqeeda e Jabr ko is Ayat mein jhutlaya hai. Aur ye sab guman o qayas hai, koi thos daleel nahi.
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame aise khurafati se Aqeedon se bachai rakhna.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"…Jo shakhs Ameerul Mo'meneen (as) ki Ziyarat karega, jabke wo Aap ke Haq ki Ma'arefat rakhta ho aur *agar wo Jabr ka qaail na ho* aur mutakabbir bhi na ho to aise shakhs ko Allah Ta'ala ek laakh shaheed ke barabar Sawab ata farmayega aur uske guzishta aur aainda ke tamam Gunah Ma'af kar dega. Qayamat ke din usko oon logon mein mehshoor karega jo Azaab e Khuda se amaan mein honge aur uspar hisaab o kitaab ko aasaan kar dega aur Malaaika uska isteqbaal karenge. Jab wo Zaair Shia waapas jaane lagega to Farishte uske ghar tak chhodne aayenge. Agar wo mareez ho jaayega to uski ayaadat karenge aur agar wo mar jayega to qabr tak uske saath jayenge aur uske liye Astagfar karenge…"_
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v2, p171)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
