       ♦ _*HUJJATUL BAALIGHA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (898)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ فَلِلَّهِ الْحُجَّةُ الْبَالِغَةُ ۖ فَلَوْ شَاءَ لَهَدَاكُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ*

_"Kah dijiye ke Allah ke paas manzil tak pahunchane wali Daleelen hain. Woh chahta to Jabran tum sab ko Hidayat de deta."_
(Surah An'am: 149)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as) ne is Ayat ke zel mein farmaya:
_"Allah Ta'ala Qayamat ke Din bande se kahega: 'Mera Banda! Kya tu Aalim tha? Agar Banda 'Haan' mein jawab dega to Khuda kahega: 'Phir tu ne apne Ilm par amal kyon nahi kiya?' Agar kisi ne nafi (No) mein jawab diya aur kaha Khudaya mein Jahil tha to Allah usse farmayega tu ne us ka Ilm hasil kyon na kiya taake amal kar sakta. Aur is daleel se Allah Aalim o Jahil sab ko khamosh kar dega."_
(Aamali e Tusi)
🌟
Imam Moosa Kazim (as) ne Hisham bin Al Hakam se farmaya:
_"Hisham! Allah ki taraf se logon par do tarah ki Hujjaten hain: (1) Zahiri Hujjat (2) Baatini Hujjat. Zahiri Hujjat Anbiya wa Rusul aur Aimma (as) hain aur Baatini Hujjat Aql hai."_
_"Imam ke Baghair logon par Allah ki Hujjat tamam nahi hoti."_
(Usool e Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🌟
Ayyam e Hajj mein Imam Sadiq (as) ki unke walid ne Janab e Ilyaas (as) se mulaqat karai.
Janabe Ilyaas (as) ne sawal kiya:
'Munkarin e Imamat kahte hain ke Qur'an Allah ki taraf se Hujjat hai (Aur iski maujoodgi mein kisi Imam ki zaroorat nahi)?'
Imam Baqir (as) ne jawab diya:
_"Qur'an Majeed ki zahiri zaban nahi hai aur ye bol kar na to Neki ka hukm de sakta hai aur na hi kisi burai se mana' kar sakta hai. Qur'an ke Ahkam ke bayan ke liye Allah ne kuchh afraad muqarrar kiye hain jo ke Qur'an ke Zer e Farman e Amro Nahy karte hain aur wohi shakhsiyat Khuda ki taraf se Imam hote hain. Isi liye Qur'an ki maujoodgi mein Imam ki zaroorat baqi rahti hai."_
_"Baaz auqaat aise Masael bhi pesh aa jaate hain jin ka hal na to Qur'an Majeed mein kahin dikhayi dete hai aur na hi unka hal Hadees mein maujood hota hai aur ye baat Khuda ke Adl ke khilaf hai ke woh koi aisa Masla paida kare jiska Jawab na ho. Isi liye Allah ne kuchh shakhsiyat ko Qur'an o Sunnat ka khusoosi Ilm de kar rawana kiya taake jab kahin koi mushkil aa jaye to woh uska hal pesh kar saken aur aisi shakhsiyat ko Aimma (Imams) kaha jaata hai."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha Tere Hujjatul Baaligha ka Zahoor mein tajeel ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🚩
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
_"Main hi Mahdi hoo'n, main hi Qaim uz Zamaan hoo'n, main hi zameen ko is tarah adl o insaaf se bhar doonga jis tarah wo zulm o jaur se bhar chuki hogi. Zameen Hujjat e Khuda se khaali nahi rehti."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p255)

                ♦ _*GAWAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (899)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ هَلُمَّ شُهَدَاءَكُمُ الَّذِينَ يَشْهَدُونَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ حَرَّمَ هَٰذَا ۖ فَإِنْ شَهِدُوا فَلَا تَشْهَدْ مَعَهُمْ ۚ وَلَا تَتَّبِعْ أَهْوَاءَ الَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا وَالَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِالْآخِرَةِ وَهُمْ بِرَبِّهِمْ يَعْدِلُونَ*

_"Kah dijiye ke zara apne gawahon ko to lao. Jo gawahi dete hain ke Khuda ne is cheez ko Haraam qarar diya hai. Iske baad woh gawahi bhi de den to Aap (saww) unke saath gawahi na dijiyega aur un logon ke khwaheshat ka itteba' na kijiyega jinhone Hamari Ayaton ko jhutlaya hai aur woh Akherat par Imaan nahi rakhte hain aur apne Parwardigar ka hamsar (equate) qarar dete hain."_
(Surah An'am: 150)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke Guzishta Ayaton mein bayan hua tha ke Mushrekin ne apne hisab se kuchh cheezon ko Halaal aur kuchh cheezon Haraam kar rakha tha aur is baat ko Allah ki taraf mansoob karte the. Is Ayat mein Allah ne unke gawahon ka taqaza kiya hai agar woh sachche hain lekin unki gawahi bhi qubool nahi hogi kyonki unke gawah bhi jhoote honge.
Allah wa Rasool (saww) ne jo Halaal Haraam bataya wo ta Qayamat Halaal o Haraam rahega. Lekin tarikh mein hamne dekha ke Rasoole Akram (saww) ke jaane ke baad Halaal ko Haraam aur Haraam ko Halaal kiya gaya. Misal ke taur par Mut'ah Jaez tha jisko baad mein najaez bana diya, Taraweeh ka koi hukm nahi tha jo baad mein raej hui. Qur'an ne takeed ki hai Deen mein koi Jabr nahi, baad mein Ashairah ka Jabriya Aqeeda raej ho gaya. Waghaira... Yani jo Mushrekin kar rahe the wohi Muslemin kar rahe hain. Isliye Qur'an Qayamat tak ke liye Hidayat hai aur Kitab ko baghair Teacher ke nahi samjha ja sakta. Ahle Bait (as) se badh kar hamare liye koi Teacher nahi ho sakta.

🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame in Bidatiyon se door rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Har Bid'at gumraahi hai aur har gumraahi ka raasta Jahannum ki taraf jaata hai."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v3, p362)
🌟
Imam Ali (as)
_"Fitnon aur Bid'aton ki Alaamatein (nishani) na bano balke Ahl e Jamaat ne jo kuchh tai kiya hai usi ke paaband raho."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Giroh, Jamaat p107)

      ♦ _*ALLAH KI WASIYYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (900)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ تَعَالَوْا أَتْلُ مَا حَرَّمَ رَبُّكُمْ عَلَيْكُمْ ۖ أَلَّا تُشْرِكُوا بِهِ شَيْئًا ۖ وَبِالْوَالِدَيْنِ إِحْسَانًا ۖ وَلَا تَقْتُلُوا أَوْلَادَكُمْ مِنْ إِمْلَاقٍ ۖ نَحْنُ نَرْزُقُكُمْ وَإِيَّاهُمْ ۖ وَلَا تَقْرَبُوا الْفَوَاحِشَ مَا ظَهَرَ مِنْهَا وَمَا بَطَنَ ۖ وَلَا تَقْتُلُوا النَّفْسَ الَّتِي حَرَّمَ اللَّهُ إِلَّا بِالْحَقِّ ۚ ذَٰلِكُمْ وَصَّاكُمْ بِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَعْقِلُونَ*

_"Aap kah den ke aao jo cheezen tumhare Rab ne tum par Haraam ki hain mein tumhe wo padh kar sunaun ye ke kisi cheez ko Khuda Sharik na banao aur Maa Baap ke saath Nek sulook karo aur Muflisi ke khauf se apni Aulad ko qatl na karo. Ham tumhe bhi Rizq dete hain aur unhe bhi Rizq dete hain aur Badkariyon ke qareeb na phatko khwah wo zahiri ho ya poshida aur jiske qatl ko Khuda Haraam kiya hai Haq ke alawa use qatl na karo. Ye wo baaten hain jinka Khuda ne tumhe hukm diya hai taake tum samajh sako."_
(Surah An'am: 151)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ayat No 151 - 153 mein Khuda ke 10 farman hain:
(1) Shirk se parhez.
(2) Waledain (Parents) ke saath Nek Sulook.
(3) Tangdasti ki wajah se Aulad ko qatl na karna.
(4) Fuhush wa Badkar Amal se parhez chahe zaheran ya chhup kar.
(5) Begunahon ka qatl na karna.
(6) Yateen ke Maal par nigah na rakhna.
(7) Nap-tol barabar rakhna. (Kanta na marna)
(8) Faisla wa Gawahi mein Adalat ka khayal rakhna.
(9) Allah ke Ahd (Promise) ko nahi todna.
(10) Allah ka bataya hua Raasta Seedha hai. Baqi sab Raaste tedhe hain.
📚
(1) Jis mein sab se Awwal Ahmiyat ka Nuqta Tauheed e Islam hai. Yani Khuda ke saath kisi ko sharik qarar na dena.
(2) Teeno Ayat mein *ذالك وصاكم به* comon hai yani Allah wasiyat kar raha hai: Pahle Samajhdar logo ko jo Aql rakhte hain, doosri Ayat mein ke log in baaton ko yaad rakhen, teesri Ayat mein taake Taqwa ikhtiyar karen.
(Baqi 2 Ayaten ainda pesh karenge.)
📚
Ye baaten guzishta Adyan (Religions) mein bhi batayi ja chuki hain lekin logon ne inhe faramosh kar diya.
Inshaallah ainda ham alaidah ek ek topic par zikr karenge Jaise Waledain, Qatl e Aulaad waghaira.

🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Tere bataye hue Ahkam par karne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo shakhs logo'n ke liye (logo'n ko impress karne ke liye) amal e khair karega to uska Sawaab logo'n par hi hoga. Har Riyaa (amal mein dikhawa, show-off) Shirk hai."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v9, p393)
Yani agar Imam ki Niyaz ka maqsad mein agar show off hai to ye Shirk hoga. Niyaz khalis Qurbatan ilallah ki Niyat se honi chahiye.
🔰✋🏻🤚🏻
Imam Ali (as):
_"Subhanallah' *سبحان الله* yaani Allah Azz wa Jall ki Buzurgi ki taazim karna aur Usko un tamaam baaton se Paak aur Munazza (Distinct) qaraar dena ke jo har Shirk karne wala Uske silsile mein kahta hai. PUS, JAB KOI BANDA SUBHANALLAH KAHTA HAI TO TAMAAM FARISHTE USKE LIYE RAHMAT TALAB KARTE HAIN."_
(Maani Al Akhbaar, Part 1, P-50)

♦ _*WALEDAIN SE NEKI KARNA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (901)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

قُلْ تَعَالَوْا أَتْلُ مَا حَرَّمَ رَبُّكُمْ عَلَيْكُمْ ۖ *أَلَّا تُشْرِكُوا بِهِ شَيْئًا ۖ وَبِالْوَالِدَيْنِ إِحْسَانًا ۖ* وَلَا تَقْتُلُوا أَوْلَادَكُمْ مِنْ إِمْلَاقٍ ۖ نَحْنُ نَرْزُقُكُمْ وَإِيَّاهُمْ ۖ وَلَا تَقْرَبُوا الْفَوَاحِشَ مَا ظَهَرَ مِنْهَا وَمَا بَطَنَ ۖ وَلَا تَقْتُلُوا النَّفْسَ الَّتِي حَرَّمَ اللَّهُ إِلَّا بِالْحَقِّ ۚ ذَٰلِكُمْ وَصَّاكُمْ بِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَعْقِلُونَ)

_"Aap kah den ke aao jo cheezen tumhare Rab ne tum par Haraam ki hain mein tumhe wo padh kar sunaun ye ke *kisi cheez ko Khuda Sharik na banao aur Maa Baap ke saath Nek sulook karo* aur Muflisi ke khauf se apni Aulad ko qatl na karo. Ham tumhe bhi Rizq dete hain aur unhe bhi Rizq dete hain aur Badkariyon ke qareeb na phatko khwah wo zahiri ho ya poshida aur jiske qatl ko Khuda Haraam kiya hai Haq ke alawa use qatl na karo. Ye wo baaten hain jinka Khuda ne tumhe hukm diya hai taake tum samajh sako."_
(Surah An'am: 151)

📚📖 🤷‍♂🙅🏻‍♂
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Islam mein Waledain (Parents) ki zyada ahmiyat di gayi hai. Qur'an main mutaddid jagahon par Waledain ke saath Neki se pesh aane ki takeed ki gayi hai. Jaise (17:23) (46:15) (31:14) etc. Qur'an ne unko Murabbi *مربى* yani palne wala bataya hai. Unke hukm ki taameel bete par Wajib qarar di hai siwai Shirk ke. Ek aur Ayat peshe khidmat hai: 📜
_"Tumhare Rab ne Faisla kar diya hai: Tum log kisi ki Ibadat na karo, magar sirf uske Waledain ke saath Nek Sulook karo, agar tumhare pas un dono mein se koi ek, ya dono, boodhe ho gaye hon to unhe 'uff' tak na kaho, na unhe jhidak kar jawab do, balke ehtram ke saath baat karo. Aur Narmi aur Rahem ke saath unke saamne jhuk kar raho, aur Dua kiya karo: 'Parwardigar! Un par rahem farma jis tarah unhone Rehmat o shafaqqat ke saath mujhe bachpan mein paala tha."_
(Surah Bani Israel: 23-24)
🍁
Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim Qummi mein marqoom hai ke jahan jis mein Waledain ke Nek Sulook ka hukm diya gaya hai wahan Roohani Waledain yani Rasoole Khuda (saww) aur Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen (as) ke saath bhi Nek Sulook ka hukm diya gaya hai.
🤲🏻
_"Parwardigar! Un par rahem farma jis tarah unhone Rehmat o shafaqqat ke saath mujhe bachpan mein paala tha."_ 
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌹
Imam Ali (as):
_*"Jo shakhs apne Waledain ke saath Neki karta hai, uske saath uska beta Neki karega."*_
(Gorar ul Hakam, v1, p3)
😡
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"3 gunah aise hain jinki saza Duniya mein mil jaati hai aur wo ye hain:_
_(1) *Waledain ki na-farmani ki wajah se Aaq (disown) hona,*_
_(2) Logo'n par zulm o sitam karna aur
_(3) Ehsaan ka inkaar aur Kufr karna._
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p45)
😊
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aalim ki taraf nazar karna Ibadat hai, Aadil Imam ki taraf dekhna Ibadat hai, *Waledain ki taraf rafa'at o Mohabbat se dekhna Ibadat hai* aur us bhai ko dekhna bhi Ibadat hai jis se Khuda ke liye Mohabbat karta hai."_
(Adaab e Islami, v2, p220)
😠
Imam Sadiq (as):
_*"Jo apne Waledain ko Ghusse se dekhta hai to woh Allah ko is qadar Ghussa dilaata hai ke Allah uski koi Ibadat qubool nahi karta, agar unhone uske saath na-insaafi ki ho tab bhi."*_
(Islamic Morals, Man's Duty With Regard To his Parents)

        ♦ _*QATL-E-AULAAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (902)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

قُلْ تَعَالَوْا أَتْلُ مَا حَرَّمَ رَبُّكُمْ عَلَيْكُمْ ۖ أَلَّا تُشْرِكُوا بِهِ شَيْئًا ۖ وَبِالْوَالِدَيْنِ إِحْسَانًا ۖ *وَلَا تَقْتُلُوا أَوْلَادَكُمْ مِنْ إِمْلَاقٍ ۖ نَحْنُ نَرْزُقُكُمْ* وَإِيَّاهُمْ ۖ وَلَا تَقْرَبُوا الْفَوَاحِشَ مَا ظَهَرَ مِنْهَا وَمَا بَطَنَ ۖ وَلَا تَقْتُلُوا النَّفْسَ الَّتِي حَرَّمَ اللَّهُ إِلَّا بِالْحَقِّ ۚ ذَٰلِكُمْ وَصَّاكُمْ بِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَعْقِلُونَ.

_"Aap kah den ke aao jo cheezen tumhare Rab ne tum par Haraam ki hain mein tumhe wo padh kar sunaun ye ke kisi cheez ko Khuda Sharik na banao aur Maa Baap ke saath Nek sulook karo aur *Muflisi ke khauf se apni Aulad ko qatl na karo. Ham tumhe bhi Rizq dete hain aur unhe bhi Rizq dete hain* aur Badkariyon ke qareeb na phatko khwah wo zahiri ho ya poshida aur jiske qatl ko Khuda Haraam kiya hai Haq ke alawa use qatl na karo. Ye wo baaten hain jinka Khuda ne tumhe hukm diya hai taake tum samajh sako."_
(Surah An'am: 130)

📚📖 👨‍👨‍👦‍👦💉
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta topic mein Huqooq e Waledain bayan kiye.  Iske saath saath Huqooq e Aulad bhi hain. Un mein se ek sangeen Gunah qatl e Aulad hai. Zaman e Jahiliyyat mein Arab aksar apni Ladkiyon ko paida hote hi qatl kar dete the aur Ladkon ko bhi. Islam ne is riwaaj ko khatm kiya aur iski kaafi mazammat ki hai.
Qur'an ki ye Ayat isi taraf Ishara kar rahi hai. Ek aur Ayat is tarah hai:
_"Aur Khabardaar! Apni Aulaad ko faaqe ke darr se Qatl na karna, ke Hum unhe bhi Rizq dete hain aur tumhe bhi Rizq dete hain."_
(Surah Bani Israel: 31)
Qatl ki asl wajah Rizq hai jo ke Baap par Wajib hai. Baap is dar ki wajah se ke mein apni Aulad kar kharch nahi utha sakta isliye paida hote hi qatl kar dete the. Lekin Advance style mein ye system aaj bhi jaari hai, yani Abortion ( *إسقاط حمل*).
Insaan ye bhool jaata hai ke Rozi ata karne wala Khuda hai. Insaan sirf us Rozi ko talash karta hai. Aur har Insaan jo is Duniya mein aata hai woh apni Rozi le kar aata hai. Har Insaan ki Rozi likhi hui hai, usko utni milni hai jab tak woh zinda hai. Jaise hi uski Rozi khatm hoti hai, iske saath hi zindagi tamam hoti hai. Pas Aulad ka Rizq uske Waledain ke zimme likh diya jaata hai, uski zimmedari hai ke use talaash kar ke hasil kare. Insaan jab koshish karta hai to Allah ki taufeeq shamil e haal ho jaati hai. Rozi kam wa zyada hone ki bahut si illaten (Factors) hain, kisi aur Ayat ke zel mein bayan karenge.
Pas yahi wajah hai ke Aulad ko Ne'mat kaha gaya hai. Hasil e Kalam ye ke Family Planning jaisi koi cheez Islam mein nahi hai. Insaan ka Khaaliq Allah hai, Waledain sirf zariya hain. Agar Waledain Ghareeb hain to ho sakta hai Allah Aulad ke tufail mein unhe Ameer kar de.
Lekin agar ham kuchh ghareeb families ko dekhte hain aur unki Aulade bhi zyada hoti hain aur woh apne bachchon ko sambhal bhi nahi paa rahe hote hain uska Khuda ke Rizq se talluq nahi. Uski wajah awwal to Jahiliyyat hai, kahili aur la sha'oori hai. Allah ne Insaan ko Aulad ke paida hone se rokne ka Ikhtiyar paida hone se pahle diya hai. Allah ne Aulad ko paida karne par zor nahi diya hai balke paida hone ke baad aisa koi action se manaa kiya jo ke ek tarah ka qatl hai. Insaan ki muflisi khud uske liye Imtehan hai jo use pass karna hai, agar woh ghabra gaya, to uski na Kamyabi hogi. Jiske natije mein woh Gunah ka murtakib ho jayega.
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Rizq mein izafa farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👨‍👨‍👦‍👦
Imam Sadiq (as)
se sawaal huwa ke kin hastiyo'n ka kharch uthhana Wajib hai?
Imam (as) ne farmaya:

_"Maa, Baap, Aulaad aur teri Biwi."_
(Khisaal, p132)
👨‍👨‍👦‍👦
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo shakhs apni Aulaad ke liye bad-Dua karta hai, use Allah faqeeri aur tang-dasti ke hawaale kar deta hai."_
(Book 'Rizq' by Haji Naji)

      ♦ _*FAHSHA (INDECENCY)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (903)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

قُلْ تَعَالَوْا أَتْلُ مَا حَرَّمَ رَبُّكُمْ عَلَيْكُمْ ۖ أَلَّا تُشْرِكُوا بِهِ شَيْئًا ۖ وَبِالْوَالِدَيْنِ إِحْسَانًا ۖ وَلَا تَقْتُلُوا أَوْلَادَكُمْ مِنْ إِمْلَاقٍ ۖ نَحْنُ نَرْزُقُكُمْ وَإِيَّاهُمْ ۖ *وَلَا تَقْرَبُوا الْفَوَاحِشَ مَا ظَهَرَ مِنْهَا وَمَا بَطَنَ ۖ* وَلَا تَقْتُلُوا النَّفْسَ الَّتِي حَرَّمَ اللَّهُ إِلَّا بِالْحَقِّ ۚ ذَٰلِكُمْ وَصَّاكُمْ بِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَعْقِلُونَ.

_"Aap kah den ke aao jo cheezen tumhare Rab ne tum par Haraam ki hain mein tumhe wo padh kar sunaun ye ke kisi cheez ko Khuda Sharik na banao aur Maa Baap ke saath Nek sulook karo aur Muflisi ke khauf se apni Aulad ko qatl na karo. Ham tumhe bhi Rizq dete hain aur unhe bhi Rizq dete hain aur *Badkariyon ke qareeb na phatko khwah wo zahiri ho ya poshida* aur jiske qatl ko Khuda Haraam kiya hai Haq ke alawa use qatl na karo. Ye wo baaten hain jinka Khuda ne tumhe hukm diya hai taake tum samajh sako."_
(Surah An'am: 151)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ek hi Ayat mukhtalif unwan ka zikr jaari hai.
Fuhsha mein sabhi gandi baaten shamil jinko Allah ne Haram qarar diya hai.
👰🏼
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Zahiri Burai Zina hai aur Baatini Burai ghair Aurton se Muhabbat (Love Affair) badhana hai."_
(Majmaul Bayan)
🧕🏼
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Allah Ghayoor hai aur Woh Ghairat mand Insaanon se Muhabbat rakhta hai aur Allah ne apni Shane Ghairat ki wajah se Zahiri aur Baatini Buraiyon ko Haraam kiya hai."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame aise mahaul se door rakh jahan Badkar log rahte hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🎋
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Gandagi par ugne-wali sabzi se shaadi karne se bacho."_
Sawaal kiya gaya,
_"Ya Rasulallah (saww), gandagi ki sabzi kya hoti hai?"_
Farmaya,
_"Wo khubsoorat aurat jo bure mahaul mein paida huwi ho."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v4, p498)
👹
Imam Ali (as):
_*"Shaitan ke paas gussa aur Aurat se mazboot koi aur rassi nahi hai."*_
(Gorar ul Hakam, p408, Adaab e Islami, v2, p122)
🤵🏻👰🏼
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_*"Aurat aur mard ko Tanhaai mein kabhi nahi baithna chahiye, wahan teesra Shaitan hota hai."*_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p32)
❣
Imam Ali (as):
_"Wo Dil Nasihat se fayda uthhane wala nahi hai *jo Shehwaton (desires) mein uljha hua hai.*"_
Gorar ul Hakam v1, p740
🙄
Imam Ali (as):
_"Tajjub hai us shakhs par jo Azaab ka darr to rakhta hai lekin (jin badkaariyo'n ki wajah se Azaab hoga unse) wo rukta nahi aur Sawab ki Ummeed to rakhta hai lekin (gunahon se) na to rukta hai aur na (Sawab ke liye) amal karta hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p337)
😜
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"3 qism ke bande aise hain ke jin par Khuda Qayamat ke din nazr e Rehmat nahi dalega aur na hi unka tazkiya karega aur unke liye dardnaak azaab hoga:_
_(1) Dayyus aur be-gairat aadmi,_
_(2) *Fahash-goyi karne wala aur Gaali galoch karne wala* aur_
_(3) Aur jo shakhs bawajood tawangari (maldari) ke logon se sawaal kare (maange)."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v6, p260)

         ♦ _*QATL - MURDER*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (904)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

قُلْ تَعَالَوْا أَتْلُ مَا حَرَّمَ رَبُّكُمْ عَلَيْكُمْ ۖ أَلَّا تُشْرِكُوا بِهِ شَيْئًا ۖ وَبِالْوَالِدَيْنِ إِحْسَانًا ۖ وَلَا تَقْتُلُوا أَوْلَادَكُمْ مِنْ إِمْلَاقٍ ۖ نَحْنُ نَرْزُقُكُمْ وَإِيَّاهُمْ ۖ وَلَا تَقْرَبُوا الْفَوَاحِشَ مَا ظَهَرَ مِنْهَا وَمَا بَطَنَ ۖ *وَلَا تَقْتُلُوا النَّفْسَ الَّتِي حَرَّمَ اللَّهُ إِلَّا بِالْحَقِّ ۚ ذَٰلِكُمْ وَصَّاكُمْ بِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَعْقِلُونَ*

_"Aap kah den ke aao jo cheezen tumhare Rab ne tum par Haraam ki hain mein tumhe wo padh kar sunaun ye ke kisi cheez ko Khuda Sharik na banao aur Maa Baap ke saath Nek sulook karo aur Muflisi ke khauf se apni Aulad ko qatl na karo. Ham tumhe bhi Rizq dete hain aur unhe bhi Rizq dete hain aur Badkariyon ke qareeb na phatko khwah wo zahiri ho ya poshida aur *jiske qatl ko Khuda ne Haraam kiya hai Haq ke alawa use qatl na karo. Ye wo baaten hain jinka Khuda ne tumhe hukm diya hai taake tum samajh sako."*_
(Surah An'am: 151)

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
📚📖  👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Pas is Ayat ke akhir mein kisi na Haq ke Qatl ko Haraam qarar diya hai. Isse Mutalliq Ahadis mulaheza farmayen:
⚔🔪
Rasule Khuda (saww)
se puchha gaya ke, _*"Qayamat ke din kis shakhs ko sabse zyada azaab diya jayega?"*_
Aap ne farmaya,
_"Us shakhs ko jisne *kisi Nabi ko qatl kiya hoga* ya kisi aise shakhs ko qatl kiya jo nekiyo'n ka hukm deta ho aur buraaiyo'n se manaa karta ho."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p9)
⛓⚔🔗
Imam Sadiq (as):
_*"Jo shakhs khud amadan (jaan bujh kar) apne ko qatl kar le (suicide kar le) to wo Jahannum mein hamesha hamesha ke liye jayega."*_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v3, p362)
💰
Imam Ali (as):
_*"Apne maal ki hifazat ke liye qatl ho jaane wala Shaheed hai."*_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p605)
⚔🔪
Imam Ali (as):
_"3 qism ke logo'n par Behisht haraam hai: Chugal-khor, *Qaatil* aur Sharaabi."_
Iqaabul Aamaal, p475
📝
Imam Baqir (as)
_"Jo kisi ka *Qatl karta* hai to Allah marnewale ke saare gunah qaatil ke naam likh deta hai aur marnewale ko paak kar deta hai."_
(Sawaabul Aamaal o Iqaabul Aaamal)
🍛🔪
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"…Jo shakhs hamare kisi dushman ko pet bhar kar khana khilaaye to goya usne hamare kisi dost ko *qatl* kiya hai."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v16, p328)
⚔🔪
Imam Ali (as):
_"Teen cheezein halaak kar dene waali hai:_
_(1) Takabbur (Pride) - Jisne Iblees (Shaitan) ko apne martabe se gira diya,_
_(2) Laalach (Greed) - Jisne Adam ko Jannat se nikalwa diya, aur_
_(3) Hasad (Jealousy) - Jisne Adam ke bete ko *apne bhai ke qatl par aamaada kiya.*_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame qatl o ghaarat se door rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*EVENT OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🏴
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ek martaba Jibreel (as) Rasoole Khuda (saww) par naazil huwe aur kaha, _"Khallaq e Aalam aap ko Salaam kehta hai aur farmata hai ke Maine uspar Aatish e Dozakh ko haraam qaraar diya hai jiski sulb (loins) se tum paida huwe aur jiske shikam (Pet) mein tum rahe (Yaani J. Abdullah aur J. Aamina par) aur *Aatish e Dozakh ko haraam kiya hai uspar jisne tumhari kifaalat aur muhafizat ki hai (Yaani Abu Talib (as) par).*"_
(Hayaat ul Quloob, v2, p67)

               ♦ _*YATEEM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (905)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تَقْرَبُوا مَالَ الْيَتِيمِ إِلَّا بِالَّتِي هِيَ أَحْسَنُ حَتَّىٰ يَبْلُغَ أَشُدَّهُ ۖ* وَأَوْفُوا الْكَيْلَ وَالْمِيزَانَ بِالْقِسْطِ ۖ لَا نُكَلِّفُ نَفْسًا إِلَّا وُسْعَهَا ۖ وَإِذَا قُلْتُمْ فَاعْدِلُوا وَلَوْ كَانَ ذَا قُرْبَىٰ ۖ وَبِعَهْدِ اللَّهِ أَوْفُوا ۚ ذَٰلِكُمْ وَصَّاكُمْ بِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَذَكَّرُونَ.

_*"Aur Yateem ke Maal ke qareeb bhi na jao lekin is tareeqe par jo ke uske haq mein behtar ho. Yahan tak ke woh apni jawani ki hadd tak pahunch jaye* aur Naap Tol ko insaaf se poora karo. Hamne kisi bhi shakhs ko uski taqat se badh kar takleef (shariyat) nahi dete aur jab baat karo Adl ke taqazon ke mutabiq karo agarche woh tumhara qareebi rishtedar hi kyon na ho aur Khuda ke Ahd o Paiman ko poora karo. Ye wo baaten hain jinka Khuda ne tumhe hukm diya hai taake tum Nasihat hasil karo."_
(Surah An'am: 152)

📚📖 😞
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is tarah ki Ayaat guzishta ayaton bhi aa chuki hain jiske zel mein ham tazkara kar chuke hain. Kuchh Ahadis mulaheza farmayen.
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Yateemon ke saath achhe sulook karne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😞🖐🏻
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jo Momin ya Momina *pyaar se kisi Yateem ke Sar par haath phere* to Allah Ta'ala har-har baal ke badle jis par uska haath phira hai, ek-ek Neki uske naama e aamaal mein likhega."_
(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p275)
💰
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Quran e Majeed mein us shakhs ke liye ke *jo Yateem ka maal na-haq khaaye,* 2 azaab muqarrar farmaye hain. Ek to azaab e Jahannum jo Akherat mein hoga aur doosra Azaab e Duniya. Ye (azaab e duniya) wo hai ke log uske baad uske Yateemon ke saath wohi maamla karenge jo usne auron ke Yateemon ke saath kiya hoga."_
(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p275)
🏡
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jannat mein ek ghar hai jiska naam 'Daar ul Farah' (Khushi ka ghar) hai. Usme sirf wohi shakhs jayega *jo Mo'meneen ke Yateem bachcho'n ko khush karta hoga.*"_
Meezan ul Hikmah, v4, p739
😭
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_" *Jab Yateem rota hai* to Arsh e Ilahi laraz jaata hai. Us waqt Parwardigar e Aalam farmata hai ke "Mere is Bande ko jiske Maa-Baap ko Maine utha liya hai, kisne rulaya hai? Main Apni Izzat o Jalaal ki qasam khaata hun ke jo isko tasalli de kar chup karega, uspar Bahisht wajib karunga"._
(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p275)
🙂
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)! Jibreel 7 wajah se insaan banna chahte the, wo ye hai:_
_(1) Namaz e Jamaat,_
_(2) Aalimon ki sohbat,_
_(3) Do logon mein sulah karwana,_
_(4) *Yateemon ki izzat karna,*_ 
_(5) Beemaron ko milne jaana,_
_(6) Janaze mein sharik hona,_
_(7) Zaireen ko paani pilana."_
(A Bundle Of Flowers. P38)
🚩
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Tum log hum Ahle Bait (as) ke Haq ki usi tarah hifazat karo jis tarah *Abd e Saaleh (J. Khizr (as)) ne 2 Yateem bachchon ke haq ki hifazat ki thi* sirf is bena par ke un dono Yateemon ka Baap Mard e Saleh tha (aur hum to Aulaad e Rasul (saww) bhi hain."_
(Bihar ul Anwar, v8, p33)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ _*NAAP-TOL MEIN ADALAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (906)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

وَلَا تَقْرَبُوا مَالَ الْيَتِيمِ إِلَّا بِالَّتِي هِيَ أَحْسَنُ حَتَّىٰ يَبْلُغَ أَشُدَّهُ ۖ *وَأَوْفُوا الْكَيْلَ وَالْمِيزَانَ بِالْقِسْطِ ۖ لَا نُكَلِّفُ نَفْسًا إِلَّا وُسْعَهَا ۖ وَإِذَا قُلْتُمْ فَاعْدِلُوا وَلَوْ كَانَ ذَا قُرْبَىٰ* ۖ وَبِعَهْدِ اللَّهِ أَوْفُوا ۚ ذَٰلِكُمْ وَصَّاكُمْ بِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَذَكَّرُونَ.

_"Aur Yateem ke Maal ke qareeb bhi na jao lekin is tareeqe par jo ke uske haq mein behtar ho. Yahan tak ke woh apni jawani ki hadd tak pahunch jaye aur *Naap-Tol ko insaaf se poora karo. Hamne kisi bhi shakhs ko uski taqat se badh kar takleef (shariyat) nahi dete aur jab baat karo Adl ke taqazon ke mutabiq karo agarche woh tumhara qareebi rishtedar hi kyon na ho* aur Khuda ke Ahd o Paiman ko poora karo. Ye wo baaten hain jinka Khuda ne tumhe hukm diya hai taake tum Nasihat hasil karo."_
(Surah An'am: 152)

📚📖 ⚖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Allah ne Dukandaron se ye takeed ki hai len den naap-tol mein Adalat se kaam len.
Qur'an doori jagah par bhi aisi Ayat ayi hai.
⚖
_"Aur jab Naap-Tol kar dena ho to Paimaane ko poora bhar diya karo aur bilkul theek Tarazu se tola karo. Yehi tarika behtar hai aur anjaam bhi uska achha hai."_
(Surah Bani Israel: 35)
⚖
Imam Ali (as)
ek martaba ek Kaneez ki taraf se hokar guzre jo ek Qasai se gosht kharid rahi thi aur kehti jaa rahi thi ke mujhe aur do (Wazn se thoda zyada). Aap ne Qasai se farmaya,
_*"Use de do, isme badi barkat hai."*_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v3, p125)
⚖
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Kharidar mol-tol aur qeemat ghatane ke liye baat kare (bargain kare), .. Is liye ke kharid-farokht (kharidne-bechne) mein dhoka khana na qaabil e taarif hai aur na isme koi Sawaab hai."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v3, p126)
⚖
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Ek ghadi ka Adl (insaaf) behtar hai 60 baras ki Ibadat se."_
(Jaame ul Akhbaar, p212)
🤲🏻
_"Aye Khuda! Agar Tu chaahe to Apne Fazal se humko Ma'af kar sakta hai aur agar Tu humko Azaab karna chaahe to Tere Adl ke sabab se hoga."_
(Sahifa e Kamila -Imam Sajjad (as), Dua No.10)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇😭
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Duniya mein har cheez ka Wazn aur Paimaana hai siwaaye Aansuon ke, kyunki aansu ka ek qatra aatish (Jahannum) ke samandar ko bujha sakta hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p667)

*SHIA CHANNEL CELEBRATES WILADAT OF JANAB E ZAINAB (sa)*
🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹
          *WILADAT MUBARAK*
🍁🍁🍁🍁🍁🍁🍁🍁🍁🍁
                       *بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*.      
                       *إِنَّا فَتَحْنَا لَكَ فَتْحًا مُبِينًا*
_"Hamne Haqeeqatan tumko Khuli Fatah ata' ki."_
(Surat Fath: 1)

Jab Janabe Zainab (sa) ki Wiladat hui tab ye Ayat nazil hui.
🍂🍃🍂🍃🍂🍃🍂🍃🍂🍃

    ♦ _*SIRAATE-E-MUSTAQEEM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (907)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَأَنَّ هَٰذَا صِرَاطِي مُسْتَقِيمًا فَاتَّبِعُوهُ ۖ وَلَا تَتَّبِعُوا السُّبُلَ فَتَفَرَّقَ بِكُمْ عَنْ سَبِيلِهِ ۚ ذَٰلِكُمْ وَصَّاكُمْ بِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَتَّقُونَ*

_"Aur beshak Yehi Mera Seedha Raasta (Sirat e Mustaqeem) hai, tum isi ki pairavi karo aur ise chhod kar mukhtalif raaston par na chalu, woh tumhe Khuda ke Raaste se hata denge. Ye wo Baaten hain jinka Khuda ne tumhe Hukm diya hai taake tum Muttaqi o Parhezgar ban sako."_
(Surah An'am: 153)

📚📖 🛤
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah ne ab tak jo Ahkam bayan kiye yehi Allah ka Seedha Raasta Hai.

_*Part of Khutba e Ghadeer:*_
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Allah ne kuchh Ahkam baja laane ke Ahkam nazil kiye aur kuchh cheezon se bachne ka Hukm diya. Khuda ke Amr par Amal karo aur Uski ita'at karo, Hidayat paa loge. Aur jin cheezon se Usne mana kiya hai unse baaz aa jao Raahe Raast paa loge. Aur Khuda ka Raasta chhod kar doosre raahon par mat chalo warna Khuda ke Raaste se bhatak jaoge. Mein Khuda ki taraf se muqarrar kiya hua Sirat e Mustaqeem hun aur tumhe meri itteba' (obedience) ka Hukm diya gaya hai. Mere baad Ali (as) Sirat e Mustaqeem hai. Uske baad unke Sulb ke Imam Haq ki hidayat dene wale aur Uske mutabiq Adl karne wale hain."_
(Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)
🛣
Buraid Ajali ka bayan hai hai ke Imam Mohd Baqir (as) ne is Ayat ke zel mein farmaya:
_"("Mera Seedha Raasta") se Hazrat Ali (as) aur Ausiya ki Vilayat murad hai aur ("tum uski pairavi karo") se ye murad hai ke tum Ali (as) ki pairavi karo. ("Aur doosre Raahon ki pairavi na karo warna.....") se murad ye hai ke Hazrat Ali (as) ke siyasi raqeebon ki Vilayat ikhtiyar na karo warna tum Ali (as) ke Raaste se bhatak jaoge."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
"Jab ye Ayat nazil hui to Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Hazrat Ali (as) ke liye dua maang kar kaha:
_"Khudaya! Ali (as) ke Raaste ko Sirat e Mustaqeem banana."_
(Rozatul Waizain Shaikh Mufeed, Noorus Saqlain)

*اهْدِنَا الصِّرَاطَ الْمُسْتَقِيمَ*.  (Surah Fatihah: 6)
Bare Ilaha hame Seedhe Raaste par chalne ki Hidayat kar.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🛤
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Khuda ki Qasam! Ali (as) hi Sirat e Mustaqeem aur Meezan hain."_
(Basaerud Darajat Abu Hamza Sumali se rivayat)
🛣
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Wo Seedha Raasta ham hi hain jisne is Raaste ko chhoda woh Gumrah hua."_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

        ♦ _*HAZRAT MUSA (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (908)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*ثُمَّ آتَيْنَا مُوسَى الْكِتَابَ تَمَامًا عَلَى الَّذِي أَحْسَنَ وَتَفْصِيلًا لِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَهُدًى وَرَحْمَةً لَعَلَّهُمْ بِلِقَاءِ رَبِّهِمْ يُؤْمِنُونَ*

_"Phir Hamne Musa (as) ko Kitab ata ki jo bhalai ki ravish apnane wale Insaan par Ne'mat ki takmeel aur har zaroori cheez ki tafseel aur sarasar Hidayat o Rahmat thi aur uske nuzool ka maqsad ye tha ke shayad log apne Rab ki mulaqat par Imaan layen."_
(Surah An'am: 154)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta kuchh Ayaat mein Allah ne abhi 10 Nasihaten bayan ki thi. Hazrat Musa (as) ko bhi Allah ne 10 Commandments nazil kiye the. Allah ne Mukammal Asmani Kitab nazil ki. Allah ke Kalam wa Ahkam mein koi nuqs nahi hota lekin log use tabdeel kar dete hain. Isliye phir agla Nabi nayi updated shariyat lata hai. Iska matlab ye nahi pichhli shariyat mein kuchh kamiyan rah gayi thi. Allah ne Shariyat makhlooq ki capacity ke mutabiq nazil ki. Ghadeer mein ye Shariyat mukammal hui jab Ayat Akmalto...nazil hui.
🤲🏻
 _"Aye Allah! Mein Tujh se iltija karta hun ke mujhe zyada se zyada hissa de, har us Bhalai se jo Teri taraf se nazil ho, har us Ehsaan se jo Tu Apne Fazl se kare, har us Neki se jise Tu phalai, har us Rizq se jis mein Tu wus'at de, har us Gunah se jise Tu Ma'af kar de aur har us ghalti se jise Tu chhupa le."_
(Hazrat Ali (as), Dua-e-Kumail)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌🏞
*Hikayat (True Incident):*
Ek roz H. Musa (as) ek viraan pahadi ki taraf se guzre. Dekha ke ek Aabid pahadi ke poshida daman (cave) mein masroof e Ibadat hai. H. Musa (as) ka shauq e mulaqaat badha, qareeb gaye, usko Salaam kiya. Aabid ne badi be-rukhi se (disinterestedly) puchha,
_"Kaun ho?"_  
H. Musa (as) ne kaha,
_"Main Musa hun."_
Aabid ne kaha,
_"Kya aap hi Khuda ke Nabi hain?"_ 
H. Musa (as) ne farmaya,
_"Haa'n". 
Aabid ne kaha,
_"To phir Khuda se mera kaam kara dijiye."_
H. Musa (as) ne kaha,
_"Batlao, kya kaam hai?"_ Aabid ne kaha,
_"Kaam sirf itna hai ke main 100 saal se yahan par masroof e Ibadat hun aur siwaye Ibadat ke doosra koi kaam anjaam nahi deta. Aap zara Khuda se ye to maloom kijiye ke meri is Ibadat ke sile mein mujhe kya inaam milega?"_
H. Musa (as) ne farmaya, _"Ye to main abhi maloom kiye leta hun."_
Aur usi waqt pahad par chadh gaye aur ba-awaaz e buland kaha,
_"Paalne wale! Tera Banda apni Ibadat ka sila daryaft karta hai. Batla, us se kya keh dun."_
Awaaz aayi,
_"Aye Musa! Keh do, kal batlaenge."_
H. Musa (as) ne Aabid se aa-kar kaha ke,
_"Khuda e Ta'ala ne irshad farmaya hai ke kal batlayenge."_
Aabid ne kaha,
_"Behtar hai. Kal bhi door nahi hai."_
Aabid ka ye dastoor (routine) tha ke Subah Sadiq se qabl ek neher (canal) par jaya karta tha jo wahan se qareeb thi. Wahan jaa kar nahata aur kuchh Paani apne hum-raah doosre roz ke liye bhi le aata tha. Chunaanche, hasb e dastoor doosre roz jab wo neher ki taraf chala to raasta bhool gaya aur neher par jaane ki bajaaye kisi aur taraf nikal gaya. Kaafi door jaane ke bawajood neher par na pahunch saka. Dhoop ki shiddat se nidhaal aur be-haal ho gaya. Pyaas ne haalat tabah kar di. Thak kar ek chattan par baith gaya aur Maut ka intezaar karne laga ke saamne se ek shakhs aata huwa nazar aaya. Jaan mein jaan aayi. Ishaare se usko bulaya aur badi aajizi se kehne laga ke,
_"Thoda se Paani pila do."_ Usne kaha,
_"Is viraane mein Paani kahaa'n hai? Aur mere paas jo kuchh hai wo meri apni zaroorat ke liye hai."_
Woh Aabid rone laga. Tab us musafir ne kaha,
_"Achcha, ek glass paani de sakta hun. Batlao kya qeemat adaa karoge?"_
Aabid ne kaha,
_"Mere paas kuchh nahi hai. 100 saal se Ibadat e Khuda mein mashgool hun."_
Usne kaha,
_"Agar is Ibadat ka Sawab mujhe se do to main tumhe ek glass Paani deta hun."_
Aabid ne socha agar zindagi rahi to Ibadat ki jaa sakti hai. Kehne laga,
_"Main apni Ibadat dene ke liye tayyar hun."_
Usne ek glass Paani Aabid ko de diya. Aabid ne Paani pi liya aur phir apni Ibadat-gaah mein palat aaya. Subah ko H. Musa (as) ko Waḥy hui ke,
_*"Us Aabid ki 100 saal ki Ibadat sirf ek glass paani ke ewaz kharidi jaa chuki hai.* Us se keh do ke 100 saal jo paani ke glass tu ne piye hain unki qeemat adaa kar de."_
Chunaanche, H. Musa (as) Aabid ki qayaam-gaah par jaa pahunche, Salaam kiya aur farmaya,
_"Allah ne bheja hai."_
Aabid ne kaha,
_"Ya Nabiallah! 100 saal ki Ibadat to main farokht (sell) kar chuka."_
H. Musa (as) ne kaha,
_"Haan, mujhe maloom hai magar Allah ne ye irshad farmaya hai ke jab 100 saal ki Ibadat ki qeemat ek glass paani hai to 100 saal mein jo paani tu ne piya hai uski qeemat adaa kar de."_
Aabid ne jab ye suna to bada pashemaan huwa aur chilllaya aur H. Musa (as) se kaha,
_"Ya Nabiallah! Allah Ta'ala se mere gunah o qusoor maaf karne ki sifaarish kijiye. Main naadim (sharminda) hun aur Allah Ta'ala bada Gafoor o Raheem hai."_
H. Musa (as) ko Waḥy hui,
_*"Us Aabid se kah do ke us waqt ki girya o zaari aur nidamat aur pashemani teri  saal ki Ibadat se zyada 100 qeemti hai jiske ewaz Hum ne Tujhe 1000 (ek hazaar) saal ki Ibadat ka Sawab ataa kiya."*_
(Roohul Hayat, P-259)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

               ♦ _*QUR'AN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (909)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَهَٰذَا كِتَابٌ أَنْزَلْنَاهُ مُبَارَكٌ فَاتَّبِعُوهُ وَاتَّقُوا لَعَلَّكُمْ تُرْحَمُونَ * أَنْ تَقُولُوا إِنَّمَا أُنْزِلَ الْكِتَابُ عَلَىٰ طَائِفَتَيْنِ مِنْ قَبْلِنَا وَإِنْ كُنَّا عَنْ دِرَاسَتِهِمْ لَغَافِلِينَ*

_"Aur Kitab ko Hamne Nazil kiya hai. Ye ba Barkat Kitab hai tum iski pairavi karo aur Taqva ki ravish apnao taake tum par rahem kiya jaye."_
_"Qur'an ke nuzool ka maqsad ye bhi hai ke tum ye na kah sako ke ham se pahle do girohon par Kitab nazil ki gayi thi aur hamko kuchh khabar na thi ke woh kiya padhte padhate the."_
(Surah An'am: 155 - 156)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah ne Qur'an is liye nazil kiya taake ye excuse (uzr) baqi na rahe ke Allah ne do Nabi (H. Musa (as) aur H. Esa (as)) ko Aasmani Kitabi nazil ki aur Arabon ko nahi. Arab ye bahana banate ke hame to Allah ne kiya Ahkam bheje is baat ka Ilm nahi. Isliye Allah ne Qur'an ko nazil kiya jo pichhli Aasmani Kitabon ki tasdeeq karta hai.
📖
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Quran, Allah ke baad, har shay se afzal hai. Jisne Quran ki izzat ki goya usne Allah ki izzat ki aur jisne Quran ki izzat na ki goya usne Allah ki tauheen ki."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v9, p27)
📖
Imam Sadiq (as)
_"Quran ke 4 hisse hain:_
_Ek hissa hamari taarif mein aata hai,_
_ek hissa hamare dushmano'n ki mazammat mein hai aur_
_ek hissa Sunan o imsaal (Traditions and Anecdotes) aur ek hissa faraaiz o ahkaam par mushtamil hai._
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p332)
📖
Imam Ali (as):
_"Quran 3 hisso'n mein utra: Ek tihaai (one third) hamari madah (taarif) aur hamare dushmano'n ki mazammat mein naazil huwi aur ek tihaai Sunan o Imsaal (Traditions and Anecdotes) par mushtamil hai aur ek tihaai ka talluq faraaiz o ahkaam se hai."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p331)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Qur'an ke bataye hue Ahkam par amal karne ki taufeeq ata farmaQ
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌾
Imam Ali (as):
_"Aib-daar log apne aibon ke liye uzr (excuse / bahaana) talaash karne ki khaatir dusro'n ke aibo'n ki tash'heer karenge (phailayenge)."_
(Kirdaar Saazi, p31)
🍃
Imam Husain (as):
_"Jis feyl (amal) par uzr-khwaahi karna (excuse / bahaane bataana) pade, wo kaam hi na karo is liye ke Momin na bura kaam karta hai na bahaane-baazi karta hai aur munafiq roz bura kaam karta hai aur uzr-khwaahi karta hai."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p101)
🍂
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Main apni Ummat mein 3 cheezo'n se darta hoo'n:
_(1) Aalim ki galati se,_
_(2) Munafiq se jo apne_ galat muddua (daawe) ka saboot Quran se pesh kare,_
_(3) Duniya se jo tumhari gardan maar de aur uska ilzaam (bhi) tumhare upar lagaaye."_
(Khisaal, p94)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ _*AYAAT E ILAHI SE MUNH MODNA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (910)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَوْ تَقُولُوا لَوْ أَنَّا أُنْزِلَ عَلَيْنَا الْكِتَابُ لَكُنَّا أَهْدَىٰ مِنْهُمْ ۚ فَقَدْ جَاءَكُمْ بَيِّنَةٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ وَهُدًى وَرَحْمَةٌ ۚ فَمَنْ أَظْلَمُ مِمَّنْ كَذَّبَ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَصَدَفَ عَنْهَا ۗ سَنَجْزِي الَّذِينَ يَصْدِفُونَ عَنْ آيَاتِنَا سُوءَ الْعَذَابِ بِمَا كَانُوا يَصْدِفُونَ*

_"Ab tum ye bhi nahi kah sakte ke agar ham par Kitab utari jaati to ham un se zyada raast roo saabit hote (rightly guided). Tumhare paas tumhare Rab ki taraf se ek Roshan Daleel, Hidayat aur Rahmat aa gayi hai. Ab isse bada Zalim bhala aur kaun hoga jo Allah ki Ayaat ko jhutlaye aur unse munh mode aur jo log hamari Ayaat se munh modte hain unhe rugardani ki padash (reward) mein Ham badtareen Azaab denge."_
(Surah An'am: 157)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah ne Jahil Arabon ke ek aur excuse ka jawab diya.

Hayan Al Siraj Imam Sadiq (as) ke paas aya. Woh Mohd Bin Hanfiya ki Imamat ka Aqeeda rakhta tha aur maanta tha unki wafat nahi hui aur woh zinda hain, Khuda ki taraf se Rizq hasil karte hain, means Ghaibat hain.
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) ne farmaya:
_"Mere walid ne khabar di thi ke unhone Mohd bin Hanfiya ki marz e Maut mein ayadat ki thi aur unhone marne ke baad unki Aankhen band ki thi aur unhe lahed mein utara tha aur unki wafat ke baad unki Bewagan ne naye Nikah kiye the aur unki miras taqseem hui thi."_
Hayan: "Unki misal Esa bin Maryam (as) jaisi hai unka maamla logon par mushtaba (doubt) ho gaya hai."
Imam (as): _"Mushtaba doston doston par hua ya dushmanon par?"_
Yahya: "Dushmanano par!"
Imam (as): _"To kya Imam Mohd Baqir (as) apne chacha Mohd bin Hanfiya ke Dushman the.?"_
Yahya: "Nahi."
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Hayan! Tum Allah ki Ayat (Ayatullah) se munh mod chuke ho aur jo log bhi Uski Ayat se munh modenge Allah unhe badtareen Azaab dega."_
(Isse pata chala ke Imam haqeeqi Ayatullah e Uzma hain.)
(Kamaluddin wa Tamamun Ne'ma, Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Khuda ki Ayaat ki pairavi karne ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)! Tum aur tumhare farzandon mein se Imam mere baad khalq par Hujjat e Khuda hain. Aur bandon mein raah e Khuda ki Nishaani (Ayat) hain. Jis shakhs ne un mein se kisi ek ka inkaar kiya aur jisne un mein se kisi ek ki na-farmaani ki to usne meri na-farmaani ki. Aur jisne un mein se kisi par zulm kiya, usne mujh par jafaa ki. Aur jisne tumhare saath muhabbat aur Neki ka bartao kiya to usne mere saath Muhabbat o Neki ka bartao kiya. Aur jisne tumhari ita'at ki, usne meri ita'at ki. Aur jisne tumse dosti ki usne mujh se dosti ki aur jisne tumse dushmani ki usne mujh se dushmani ki, kyunki tum mujh se aur mere sulb se paida hue ho aur main tumse hun."_
(Isbaat e Imamat - Allama Majlisi, p62)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          ♦ _*AYAAT E ILAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (911)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هَلْ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَّا أَنْ تَأْتِيَهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ رَبُّكَ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ ۗ يَوْمَ يَأْتِي بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ لَا يَنْفَعُ نَفْسًا إِيمَانُهَا لَمْ تَكُنْ آمَنَتْ مِنْ قَبْلُ أَوْ كَسَبَتْ فِي إِيمَانِهَا خَيْرًا ۗ قُلِ انْتَظِرُوا إِنَّا مُنْتَظِرُونَ*

_"Kya ye log ab is baat ke Muntazir hain ke unke paas Farishte aa jayen ya tumhara Rab unke paas aa jaye ya tumhare Rab ki kuchh Nishaniyan aa jayen? Jis Din tumhare Rab ki baaz Makhsoos Nishaniyan namudar hongi to phir kisi aise shakhs ko Imaan kuchh fayda na dega jo pahle Imaan na laya ho ya apne Imaan mein koi bhalai hasil na ki ho. Aap kah den ke tum INTEZAR karo, Ham bhi INTEZAR karte hain."_
(Surah An'am: 158)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah ne Kuffar o Mushrekin  ke saamne saari Daleelen pesh kar den phir bhi unki hat dharmi baqi rahi. To ab kis baat ka intezar hai ke unki Hidayat ke liye Malaika ayen ya Khud Allah unke saamne khada ho ya Allah ni Nishaniyan. Allah ka bando ke paas aana Uski shaan ke khilaf hai, uske liye Usko jismani libas zebe tan karna hoga, ye ek majboori hai aur majboori nuqs hai aur Allah har nuqs se Paak hai. Farishte Insaanon ke liye namoona e amal nahi ban sakte, is baat ka pahle zikr ho chuka hai. Isliye Allah ne apne bandon ke liye baaz Apni Nishaniyan rakhi. Insaan ka farz banta hai ke pahle Uski Nishaniyon par Imaan rakhe. Allah ke jitne Hadi o Rahbar guzre ye bhi sab Allah ki Nishaniyan the (Ayatullah). Kuffar o Mushrekin ke baad Munafeqeen ki ta'daad badhi aur unhone ne in Ayat e Ilahi se inkaar kiya. Yahan tak ke Akhiri waqt aa jayega aur us waqt unka Imaan lana koi fayda nahi dega.

Rivayat mein hai:
_"Jab Suraj Maghrib se tulu' hoga to us Din tamam log Imaan layenge lekin us Din ka Imaan faydemand nahi hoga."_
(Kitab Al Khisaal, Al Kaafi, Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Akhiri Zamane mein apne Imaan par sabit qadam rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Baqir (as) & Imam Sadiq (as):
_" 'Baaz Nishaniyon' se murad Suraj ka Maghrib se tulu'hona, Dabbatul Arz ka khurooj aur Dajjal ka zahir hona hai aur us waqt agar koi shakhs Imaan layega to uska Imaan use kuchh fayda na dega. Jo Momin Khuda ki nafarmaniyon mein dooba hoga aur usne Imaan ke bawajood bhi koi Neki na ki hogi to uska Imaan uske liye faydemand sabit nahi hoga."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ _*ZAHOOR KI NISHANIYAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (912)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هَلْ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَّا أَنْ تَأْتِيَهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ رَبُّكَ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ ۗ يَوْمَ يَأْتِي بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ لَا يَنْفَعُ نَفْسًا إِيمَانُهَا لَمْ تَكُنْ آمَنَتْ مِنْ قَبْلُ أَوْ كَسَبَتْ فِي إِيمَانِهَا خَيْرًا ۗ قُلِ انْتَظِرُوا إِنَّا مُنْتَظِرُونَ.*

_"Kya ye log ab is baat ke Muntazir hain ke unke paas Farishte aa jayen ya tumhara Rab unke paas aa jaye ya tumhare Rab ki kuchh Nishaniyan aa jayen? Jis Din tumhare Rab ki baaz Makhsoos Nishaniyan namudar hongi to phir kisi aise shakhs ko Imaan kuchh fayda na dega jo pahle Imaan na laya ho ya apne Imaan mein koi bhalai hasil na ki ho. Aap kah den ke tum INTEZAR karo, Ham bhi INTEZAR karte hain."_
(Surah An'am: 158)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein kuchh Khas Nishaniyon ka zikr kiya gaya hai. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne bhi kuchh Nishaniyon ki peshengoyi ki. Lekin kuchh Qayamat ki Nishaniyan hain to kuchh Imam Mahdi (atfs) ki Zahoor ki Nishaniyan hai. Qayamat se pahle Imam (as) ka Zahoor hoga, is ayat mein ye Nishaniyan Imam (as) ke Zuhoor ke pahle waqe hone wali Nishaniyan hain, jo ke rivayaton se sabit hai.
👉🏻
Imam Baqir (as) & Imam Sadiq (as):
_" 'Baaz Nishaniyon' se murad Suraj ka Maghrib se tulu'hona, Dabbatul Arz ka khurooj aur Dajjal ka zahir hona hai aur us waqt agar koi shakhs Imaan layega to uska Imaan use kuchh fayda na dega. Jo Momin Khuda ki nafarmaniyon mein dooba hoga aur usne Imaan ke bawajood bhi koi Neki na ki hogi to uska Imaan uske liye faydemand sabit nahi hoga."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)
🚩
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_*"Ayat بعض أيات se murad Imam Mahdi (atfs) ka Zahoor aur Aimma (as) ki Raja'at murad hai. Jis Din Imam Mahdi (as) Talwar le kar khurooj karenge to us waqt ka Imaan logon ko fayda nahi dega."*_
(Kamaluddin wa Tamamun Ne'ma, Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha Tere Hujjat (atfs) ko jald az jald zahir farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
_"Main jis waqt bhi khurooj karun, kisi Taghoot ki baiyat meri gardan mein na hogi (yaani na main Taqayya karunga aur na main kisi ke muqable mein khamosh hoonga, balke unse jung karunga)."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p257)
*قال رسول الله (ص):*
*من خلع يداً من طاعة لقي الله يوم القيامة ولا حجة له ومن مات وليس في عنقه بيعة مات ميتة جاهلية*

        ♦ _*ALAMAAT E ZAHOOR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (913)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هَلْ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَّا أَنْ تَأْتِيَهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ رَبُّكَ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ ۗ يَوْمَ يَأْتِي بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ لَا يَنْفَعُ نَفْسًا إِيمَانُهَا لَمْ تَكُنْ آمَنَتْ مِنْ قَبْلُ أَوْ كَسَبَتْ فِي إِيمَانِهَا خَيْرًا ۗ قُلِ انْتَظِرُوا إِنَّا مُنْتَظِرُونَ*

_"Kya ye log ab is baat ke Muntazir hain ke unke paas Farishte aa jayen ya tumhara Rab unke paas aa jaye ya tumhare Rab ki kuchh Nishaniyan aa jayen? Jis Din tumhare Rab ki baaz Makhsoos Nishaniyan namudar hongi to phir kisi aise shakhs ko Imaan kuchh fayda na dega jo pahle Imaan na laya ho ya apne Imaan mein koi bhalai hasil na ki ho. Aap kah den ke tum INTEZAR karo, Ham bhi INTEZAR karte hain."_
(Surah An'am: 158)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Allah ka wada hai ke agar Duniya ke khatme ke liye ek Din bhi baqi rah jaata hai to Allah Apni Makhsoos Nishani Imam Mahdi (atfs) ko zahir karega.

*فقد ثبت في المهدي عدة أحاديث صحيحة منها ما رواه أحمد والترمذي وأبو داود أن النبي صلى الله عليه وسلم قال:*
*"لا تذهب -أو لا تنقضي- الدنيا حتى يملك العرب رجل من أهل بيتي، يواطئ اسمه اسمي، واسم أبيه اسم أبي"*
(Tirmizi, Abu Dawood)

Kuchh Nishaniyan jo Imam (as) ke Zahoor ke pahle Zahir hongi woh ye hain:
(1) Zulm o Jaur apne Shabab par pahunchega.
(2) Dajjal ka Khurooj.
(3) Sufyani ka Khurooj.
(4) Aasmani Awaaz.
(5) Hazrat Esa (as) ka Zahoor jo Imam Mahdi (as) ke peechhe Namaz padhenge.
6. Singers ka ehteram hoga.
7. Jang e zyada hogi.
8. Juwa bazi aam hogi.
9. Log apne Ghar mein mehfooz nahi rahenge.
10. Zameenen Registaan ho jayengi.
11. Zalzale, Volcano aur doosri Qudrati Afaton ki kasrat hogi.
12. Nek Aamaal kam honge.
13. Jhoote Rehbar aksariyat ko gumrah karenge.
14. Masjiden Khoobsurat hongi lekin Roohe Masjid ghayeb hogi.
15. Accidental Death (Hadsati Amwat) zyada hongi.
16. Amir Khuda parwar aur Aqeedatmand gunehgar ho jayenge.
17. Jhooti gawahi qubool ki jayegi jabke sachchi gawahi  nahi.
18. Qur'an ko ek daqyanoosi Kitab maana jayega.
19. Kare Gunah par koi tanqeed nahi hogi.
20. Log Deen mein apni ray ko shamil karenge.
21. Sood (Interest) jaez maana jayega.
22. Nek logon ka Khuda par Imaan mayooskun hoga.
23. Insaan Nafsani Khwaheshat ka taa'be hoga.
24. Zulm par fakhr kiya jayega.
25. Nek log Badkar log ki bad zabani ke dar se khamosh rahenge.
26. Gheebat mamool ban jayegi.
27. Maldar shakhs ki ba nisbat Nek shakhs ka zyada ehtram hoga.
28. Aulad apne Waledain par Laanat karegi aur jald Maut ke liye Dua karegi.
29. Mahe Ramzan mein do Gahen (Eclipses) honge.
30. Qiraat e Qur'an bojh maana jayega.
31. Homosexuality aam hogi.
32. 3 bar East aur West mein Zameen khiskegi. (Landslides)
(Ref: Al Ghaiba Toosi, Ghaibat e Nomani, Al Khisaal,  Biharul Anwar, Vol: 52,53, Al Kaafi, Kamaluddin wa Tamamun Ne'ma, Kitabun Nujum, Al Irshaad, Kashful Ghummah.)

For more Detail Read:
https://www.al-islam.org/life-imam-al-mahdi-baqir-shareef-al-qurashi/signs-reappearance-imam-time-0#f_d6e3bed7_1
🤲🏻
Allahumma Ajjil le Valiyyekal Faraj.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
_"Main hi Mahdi hun, main hi Qaim uz Zamaan hun, main hi Zameen ko is tarah Adl o Insaaf se bhar doonga jis tarah wo zulm o jaur se bhar chuki hogi. Zameen Hujjat e Khuda se khaali nahi rehti."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p255)

        ♦ _*ALAMAAT E ZAHOOR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (914)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هَلْ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَّا أَنْ تَأْتِيَهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ رَبُّكَ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ ۗ يَوْمَ يَأْتِي بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ لَا يَنْفَعُ نَفْسًا إِيمَانُهَا لَمْ تَكُنْ آمَنَتْ مِنْ قَبْلُ أَوْ كَسَبَتْ فِي إِيمَانِهَا خَيْرًا ۗ قُلِ انْتَظِرُوا إِنَّا مُنْتَظِرُونَ*

_"Kya ye log ab is baat ke Muntazir hain ke unke paas Farishte aa jayen ya tumhara Rab unke paas aa jaye ya tumhare Rab ki kuchh Nishaniyan aa jayen? Jis Din tumhare Rab ki baaz Makhsoos Nishaniyan namudar hongi to phir kisi aise shakhs ko Imaan kuchh fayda na dega jo pahle Imaan na laya ho ya apne Imaan mein koi bhalai hasil na ki ho. Aap kah den ke tum INTEZAR karo, Ham bhi INTEZAR karte hain."_
(Surah An'am: 158)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):
_"Dajjal Zahir hoga aur woh qatl kiya jayega. Phir Dabbatul Arz ka Maqam e Saffa se zahoor hoga uske paas Sulaiman (as) ki Anguthi aur Musa (as) ka asa hoga. Woh Momin ke munh par Anguthi rakhega to us waqt uske chehre par ye ibaarat raqam ho jayegi: *هذا مؤمن حقا* (ye Momin sachcha hai). Aur har Kafir ke munh par Anguthi rakhega to uske chehre par ye ibaarat aa jayegi: *هذا كافر حقا* (ye pakka Kafir hai). Jab har shakhs ka Imaan o Kufr Zahir ho jayega to Momin Kafir se kahega: Aye Kafir! Tere liye halakat ho, aur Kafir Momin se kahega: Momin tere liye Khushkhabri ho. Kaash mein bhi teri tarah se Momin hota aur aaj ke Din Kamyabi hasil karta. Phir Suraj Maghrib se tulu' hoga, us waqt Tauba ka darwaza band ho jayega. Us waqt na to tauba qubool hogi aur na kisi ka amal buland hoga aur jo pahle se Imaan na laya hoga ya jisne Imaan mein bhalai hasil na ki hogi to use us waqt ka Imaan koi fayda na dega."_

Phir Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Iske baad ke halaat mujh se mat poochho kyonki mere Habib Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne mujh se Ahd liya tha ke mein un waqeat ko apni Itrat ke alawa kisi aur ke saamne bayan nahi karun."_
(Kamaluddin wa Tamamun Ne'ma, Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Teri Akheri Hujjat (atfs) ke awan o ansaar mein shamil kar.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 _*Qaul e Imam e Haazir (1):*_

Imam Mahdi (atfs):
*الحق معنا فلن يوحشنا من قعد عنا، و نحن صنائع ربنا، و الحق بعد صنائعنا.*
_"Haq, ham Ahle Bait (as) ke saath hai, kuchh logon ka ham se juda hona hamare liye wahshat ka sabab nahi hai, kyonki ham Parwardigar ke tarbiyat yaftah hain, aur doosri Makhlooq hamari tarbiyat yaftah hain."_
(Al Ghaiba-Tusi, P-285, H-245, Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Vol 2, P-278, Biharul Anwar, Vol 53, P-178, H-9)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (915)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هَلْ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَّا أَنْ تَأْتِيَهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ رَبُّكَ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ ۗ يَوْمَ يَأْتِي بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ لَا يَنْفَعُ نَفْسًا إِيمَانُهَا لَمْ تَكُنْ آمَنَتْ مِنْ قَبْلُ أَوْ كَسَبَتْ فِي إِيمَانِهَا خَيْرًا ۗ قُلِ انْتَظِرُوا إِنَّا مُنْتَظِرُونَ*

_"Kya ye log ab is baat ke Muntazir hain ke unke paas Farishte aa jayen ya tumhara Rab unke paas aa jaye ya tumhare Rab ki kuchh Nishaniyan aa jayen? Jis Din tumhare Rab ki baaz Makhsoos Nishaniyan namudar hongi to phir kisi aise shakhs ko Imaan kuchh fayda na dega jo pahle Imaan na laya ho ya apne Imaan mein koi bhalai hasil na ki ho. Aap kah den ke tum INTEZAR karo, Ham bhi INTEZAR karte hain."_
(Surah An'am: 158)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Zameen par hamesha Hujjat e Khuda ka wujood raha hai jo Halaal o Haram batata hai aur logon ko Allah ke Raaste ki Dawat deta hai aur Qayamat se 40 Din pahle Hujjat Zameen se munqata (cut-off) ho jayegi. Jab Hujjat ka wujood na rahega to us waqt Tauba ka darwaza band ho jayega aur Hujjat ke uth jaane se qabl jisne Imaan qubool na kiya hoga to uska Imaan use koi fayda nahi dega. Hujjat ke baad jo log baqi rahenge woh badtareen log honge aur unhi par Qayamat qaem hogi."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Us Makhsoos Din us shakhs ko Imaan laane se koi fayda hasil na hoga jo Meesaq (Covenant) mein Imaan na laya hoga aur jisne Anbiya, Ausiya aur bil khusoos Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) ki Vilayat ka iqrar na kiya hoga."_
(Usoole Kaafi)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hamare Imaan ko is zamana e Ghaibat mein sabit qadam rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🙇 _*Qaul e Imam e Haazir (2):*_

Imam Mahdi (atfs):
*إنى لأمان لأهل الأرض كما أن النجوم أمان لأهل السماء.*
_"Beshak mein Ahle Zameen ke liye Amn o Salamti hun, jaisa ke Sitaare Aasmaan walon ke liye Amaan ka baaes hain."_
(Al Ghaiba-Tusi, P-292, H-247, Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Vol 2, P-284, Biharul Anwar, Vol 53, P-181, H-10, Kamaluddin, Vol 2, P-485, H-10)

♦ _*INTEQAM-E-IMAM-E-ASR (atfs)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (916)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ أَغَيْرَ اللَّهِ أَبْغِي رَبًّا وَهُوَ رَبُّ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ ۚ وَلَا تَكْسِبُ كُلُّ نَفْسٍ إِلَّا عَلَيْهَا ۚ وَلَا تَزِرُ وَازِرَةٌ وِزْرَ أُخْرَىٰ ۚ ثُمَّ إِلَىٰ رَبِّكُمْ مَرْجِعُكُمْ فَيُنَبِّئُكُمْ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ فِيهِ تَخْتَلِفُونَ*

_"Aap kah den ke kya mein Allah ke siwa koi aur Rab talash karun jabke Wohi tamam cheezon ka Rab hai aur har shakhs apne Aamaal ka khud zimmedar hai. Koi bojh uthane wala doosre ka bojh nahi uthata. Phir tum sab ko apne Rab ke huzoor palatna hai, us waqt Woh tumhe tumhare ikhtelafat ki haqeeqat se agah kar dega."_
(Surah An'am: 164)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Abu Harvi ne Imam Reza (as) se Imam Sadiq (as) ki us hadis ke bare mein sawal kiya ke "Jab Qaem e Ale Muhammad (atfs) khurooj karenge to Qatelane Imam Husain (as) ki Aulad ko unke Aba' ke Afa'al ki wajah se qatl karenge?"
Imam Reza (as) ne farmaya:
_"Ji haan sahih hai."_
Raavi ne sawal kiya ke is Ayat (6:164) ke mutabiq koi kisi doosre ka bojh nahi uthayega?
Imam Reza (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ka farman bilkul Barhaq hai. Asl baat ye hai ke Qatelane Imam Husain (as) ki Aulad ko is liye qatl kiya jayega ke woh apne Aba' ke is fe'l (action/ par raazi honge aur is par fakhr karte honge aur kisi ke fe'l par raazi hone wala uske fa'el (doer) ke ki manind hota hai. Agar ek shakhs East mein qatl ho aur West mein rahne wala koi shakhs uske qatl par raazi ho to woh bhi Khuda ki nazar mein Qatil ka sharik qarar pata hai. Hazrat Qaem (as) (Imam Mahdi atfs) unhe unki Razamandi ki wajah se qatl karenge."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Noorus Saqlain)

*لَعَنَ اللهُ اُمَّۃً قَتَلَتْكَ وَ لَعَنَ اللهُ اُمَّۃً ظَلَمَتْكَ وَلَعَنَ اللهُ اُمَّۃً سَمِعَتْ بِذَالِكَ فَرَضِیَتْ بِہِ۔*
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame Aimma e Athaar (as) ke Raaste par chalne ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 _*Qaul e Imam e Haazir (3):*_

Imam Mahdi (atfs):
*إجعلوا قصدكم إلينا بالمودة على السنة الواضحة، فقد نصحت لكم، والله شاهد على و عليكم.*
_"Ham (Ahle Bait Ismat o Taharat) se Muhabbat o Dosti ka maqsad Ahkam e Ilahi ka nifaaz aur Sunnat amal ki buniyad qarar do, beshak hamne zaroori shafarishon aur lazim Mau'ezon ko anjam diya hai, Khuda Wande Aalam ham aur tum sab par gawah hai."_
(Al Ghaibah- Tusi, P-286, H-245, Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Vol 2, P-279, Biharul Anwar, Vol 53, P-179, H-9)
🚩
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Mazahib, tumko door na kar den, Khuda ki Qasam! Hamara Shia woh hai jo Khuda Wande Aalam ki ita'at kare."_
(Kaafi, Vol 2, P-73, H-1, Wasailus Shia, Vol 15, P-233, H-20360)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

        ♦ _*INTEZAR-E-FARAJ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (917)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

هَلْ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَّا أَنْ تَأْتِيَهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ رَبُّكَ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ ۗ يَوْمَ يَأْتِي بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ لَا يَنْفَعُ نَفْسًا إِيمَانُهَا لَمْ تَكُنْ آمَنَتْ مِنْ قَبْلُ أَوْ كَسَبَتْ فِي إِيمَانِهَا خَيْرًا ۗ *قُلِ انْتَظِرُوا إِنَّا مُنْتَظِرُونَ*

_"Kya ye log ab is baat ke Muntazir hain ke unke paas Farishte aa jayen ya tumhara Rab unke paas aa jaye ya tumhare Rab ki kuchh Nishaniyan aa jayen? Jis Din tumhare Rab ki baaz Makhsoos Nishaniyan namudar hongi to phir kisi aise shakhs ko Imaan kuchh fayda na dega jo pahle Imaan na laya ho ya apne Imaan mein koi bhalai hasil na ki ho. *Aap kah den ke tum INTEZAR karo, Ham bhi INTEZAR karte hain."*_
(Surah An'am: 158)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ayat ka ye hissa Qur'an mein kai jagah par milta hai.  Is mein Intezar ka zikr hai. Allah us waqt ka zikr ke jab Tauba ka darwaza band ho jayega jab Imam ka Zahoor ho jayega, kar ke farma raha hai ke tum bhi Intezar karo, Ham bhi Intezar kar rahe hain.
Har Insaan ki Fitrat hai ke woh apne Mehboob ka Intezar karta hai, ghair ka nahi. Agar kisi Insaan ko pata ho ke uske ghar uska Khaas Dost Muhib jo kafi arse se juda ho, aane wala ho to uske liye usse jitna achhe se achha ho sakta hai tayyari karega. Uske aane se pahle sari tayyariyan mukammal karta hai taak uske aane wale mehman ko koi cheez nagawar na lage.
Aga hamara Imam hamare liye aisa hai aur pata hai ke aane wala hai to phir hamari tayyari bhi us level ki honi chahiye.
💐
Imam Zainul Abedin (as):
*اِنَّ اَھْلَ زَمَانِ غَیْبَتِہِ الْقَٔائِلِیْنَ بِاِمَامَتِہِ وَالْمُنْتَظِرِیْنَ لِظُھُوْرِہِ اَفْضَلُ مِنْ اَھْلِ کُلِّ زَمَانٍ لِاَنَّ اللّٰہَ تَبَارَکَ وَتَعَالیٰ اَعْطَاھُمْ مِنَ الْعُقُوْلِ وَ الْاَفْھَامِ وَالْمَعْرِفَۃِ مَا صَارَتْ بِہِ الْغَیْبَۃُ عِنْدَھُمْ بِمَنْزِلَۃِ الْمُشَاھِدَۃِ وَ جَعَلَھُمْ فِیْ ذٰلِکَ الزَّمَانِ بِمَنْزِلَۃِ الْمُجَاھِدِیْنَ بَیْنَ یَدَیْ رَسُوْلِ اللّٰہِ بِالسَّیْفِ اُوْلٰئِکَ الْمُخْلِصُوْنَ حَقًا وَشِیْعَتُنَا صِدْقًا وَالدُّعَاۃُ اِلیٰ دِیْنِ اللّٰہِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ سِرًّا وَّجَھْرًا.*

_"Beshak zamana e Ghaibat ke log jo Imam Mahdi (atfs) ki Imamat ke qael hain aur unke Zuhoor ke Muntazir hain woh sare zamane se afzal hain kyonki Allah Ta'ala ne unko itni Aql o Ifhaan aur Ma'arefat se nawaza hai ke woh Imam (as) ka unki Ghaibat mein bhi Mushaheda karte hain. Aur Allah ne unko Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke saath Talwar liye Mujahedeen ka darja diya hai. Woh Mukhlis aur Sachche Shia hain. Ye woh hain jo Allah ke Deen ki taraf zaheran aur makhfi taur par dawat dete hai."_
(Kamaluddin, P-302)
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hamare Tere Hujjat ki Intezar ki ghadiyon ko kam kar de.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 _*Qaul e Imam e Haazir (4):*_
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
*فليعمل كل امرء منكم بما يقرب به من محبتنا، و يتجنب ما يدنيه من كراهتنا و سخطنا.*
_"Lehaza tum mein se har shakhs ko aise kaam karna chahiye jo hamari Muhabbat aur dosti mein izaafa ka sabab banen, aur jo cheezen hamen napasand hain, aur jo cheezen hamari narazgi o karahat ka sabab banti hain un se parhez kare."_
(Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Vol 2, P-323,324, Biharul Anwar, Vol 53, P-176, H-7)

(Mazeed tafseel ke liye is Topic par Kitaben refer karen.)

        ♦ _*INTEZAR-E-FARAJ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (918)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

هَلْ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَّا أَنْ تَأْتِيَهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ رَبُّكَ أَوْ يَأْتِيَ بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ ۗ يَوْمَ يَأْتِي بَعْضُ آيَاتِ رَبِّكَ لَا يَنْفَعُ نَفْسًا إِيمَانُهَا لَمْ تَكُنْ آمَنَتْ مِنْ قَبْلُ أَوْ كَسَبَتْ فِي إِيمَانِهَا خَيْرًا ۗ *قُلِ انْتَظِرُوا إِنَّا مُنْتَظِرُونَ.*

_"Kya ye log ab is baat ke Muntazir hain ke unke paas Farishte aa jayen ya tumhara Rab unke paas aa jaye ya tumhare Rab ki kuchh Nishaniyan aa jayen? Jis Din tumhare Rab ki baaz Makhsoos Nishaniyan namudar hongi to phir kisi aise shakhs ko Imaan kuchh fayda na dega jo pahle Imaan na laya ho ya apne Imaan mein koi bhalai hasil na ki ho. *Aap kah den ke tum INTEZAR karo, Ham bhi INTEZAR karte hain."*_
(Surah An'am: 158)

📚📖 🌟
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Qur'an mein doosri Ayaat ye hain:
*وَارْتَقِبُوا إِنِّي مَعَكُمْ رَقِيبٌ*(Surah Hud:93)

*فَانْتَظِرُوا إِنِّي مَعَكُمْ مِنَ الْمُنْتَظِرِينَ* (Surah Araaf:71)
🌟🌟
Imam Mahdi (atfs) ke Zahoor ka Intezar se mutalliq kuchh hadisen:
🌟🌟
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
*طُوْبٰی لِشِیْعَۃِ قَٔائِمِنَا الْمُنْتَظِرِیْنَ لِظُھُوْرِہِ فِیْ غَیْبَتِہِ وَالْمُطِیْعِیْنَ لَہٗ فِیْ ظُھُوْرِہٖ اُوْلٰئِکَ اَوْلِیَآءُ اللّٰہِ الَّذِیْنَ لَا خَوْفٌ عَلَیْھِمْ وَلَا ھُمْ یَحْزَنُوْنَ.*
_"Hamare Qaem ke Shia Mubarak ho, jo Ghaibat mein unke Zuhoor ke Muntazir hain aur Zahoor ke baad unke mutee' o farmabardar honge. Woh Allah ke Auliya hain, unke ke liye na koi dar na koi gham hai."_
(Kamaluddin, Chap 33, H-54)
🌟🌟
Imam Sadiq (as):
*مَنْ سَرَّہُ اَنْ یَّکُوْنَ مِنْ اَصْحَابِ الْقَٔائِمِ فَیَنْتَظِرْ وَلْیَعْمَلْ. بِالْوَرَعِ وَ مَحَاسِنِ الْاَخْلَاقِ وَھُوَ مُنْتَظِرٌ.*
_"Jo hamare Qaem ke Ashaab mein rahna chahta hai, use chahiye ke (Zahoor ka) Intezar kare, Wara' ورع Burdbari aur Husne Akhlaq se pesh aaye. Wohi Sachcha Muntazir hai."_
(Ghaibat e Nomani, P-200, Muntakhabul Asar, P-497)
🌟🌟
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo log Qaem ki Hukumat ka Intezar karte karte inteqal kar gaye woh unki tarah hain jo Qaem ke saath the. Nahi, balke unki tarah jo Ghode sawar the aur unke saath Talwar chala rahe the."_
Phir kuchh der khamoshi ke baad farmaya:
_"Khuda ki Qasam! woh unki tarah hain jinhone Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke saamne Shahadat payi."_
(Muntakhabul Asar, P-498)
🤲🏻
*اَللّٰھُمَّ اِنَّا نَرْغَبُ اِلَیْکَ فِیْ دَوْلَۃٍ کَرِیْمَۃٍ تُعِزُّ بِھَا الْاِسْلَامَ وَاَھْلَہُ وَتُذِلُّ بِھَا النِّفَاقَ وَاَھْلَہُ.*
_"Bare Ilaha, ham Tujhse sawal karte hain us ba Azmat Hukoomat ka jisse Islam aur Ahle Islam ko izzat mile aur Nifaaq aur Ahle Nifaaq ko zillat naseeb ho."_
(Dua-e-Iftetah)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌟
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Yaqeenan! Jab hamare Qaem ka zahoor hoga, zameen Allah ke Noor se jagmagah uthegi aur use Suraj ki Roshni ki koi zaroorat nahi hogi."_
(Biharul Anwar, Vol 52, P-337)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦ _*FIRQAWARIYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (919)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ فَرَّقُوا دِينَهُمْ وَكَانُوا شِيَعًا لَسْتَ مِنْهُمْ فِي شَيْءٍ ۚ إِنَّمَا أَمْرُهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ ثُمَّ يُنَبِّئُهُمْ بِمَا كَانُوا يَفْعَلُونَ*

_"Beshak woh log jinhone apne Deen ko tukde tukde kar diya aur giroh dar giroh ban gaye. Yaqeenan unse Aapka koi talluq nahi hai. Unka maamla Allah ke supurd hai, Wohi unko unke Aamaal ki khabar dega."_
(Surah An'am: 159)

📚📖 💔
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ab ham hamare silsile ko aage badhate hain. Ham Ayat no. 158 par ruk gaye the aur yeh ejaaz dekhiye ke ye Ayat jo Imam Mahdi (as) ke mutalliq thi unke Wiladat ke mauqe par mauqoof hui.
💔
Aaj ki Ayat Islam mein Firqawariyat se talluq rakhti hai. Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim Qummi ke mutabiq isse woh log murad hain jinhone Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ko chhod diya aur girohon mein taqseem ho gaye.
Imam Baqir (as):
*فارقوا أمير المؤمنين عليه السلام و صاروا أحزابا.*
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Hamare mukhalefin ne apne Deen ke tukde kar diye."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
💔
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Mere baad ye Ummat mukhtalif giroh mein bat jayegi."_
(Tafseer e Namoona)
💔
Islam mein sab se pahle 2 main group bane: Shia wa Sunni jo ke aaj tak ye do major group hain. Iske alawa khud Sunni aur Shia mein chhote chhote firqe bante chale gaye.
Ayat mein jo Shia *شيعا* lafz aya hai uska Shia firqe se talluq nahi. Yahan is lafz ke maani hai groups (giroh). Ye saare tafarraqe eteqadi ikhtelafat ki buniyad par hain. Asl Ikhtelaf Khilafat par hua. Jab Khilafat e Haqqa par kisi ne qabza kiya to Musalman do giroh mein bat gaya. Bareeki se dekha jaye to Islam do tukdon mein bata ek Political Islam to doosra Spritual Islam. Spirituality Ahle Bait (as) mein rahi to Khilafat siyasat o iqtedar mein tabdeel ho gayi. Uske baad Islam nazaryati ikhtalefat mein bat gaya. Masoomeen (as) wa Sahaba ki rivayaton ka fabrication shuru ho gaya. Ek aam admi ke liye mushkil ho gaya ye samajhna ke sahi Islam kaunsa hai.
Qur'an mein koi tabdeeli nahi hui kyonki Allah ne uski hifazat ki zamanat li hai.
Allah ne Apne Rasool (saww) ko bata diya ke aap fikr na karen, inko to Mein dekh lunga.

Ye topic kaafi wasee hai jo is mukhtasar jagah tafseel ki gunjaish nahi hai. Qare'een Kitaben refer kare. Neeche diye gaye graph Image mein bataya gaya hai jis mein Islam ke main firqe darj hain.
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha tamam Mo'meneen ko ittehad ki taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💞
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
*و لو أن أشياعنا على اجتماع من القلوب فى الوفاء بالعهد عليهم......*
_*"Agar hamare Shia (Khuda unko ita'at ki taufeeq de) apne Ahd o Paiman ko poora karne ki koshish mein HAMDIL hon to phir hamari mulaqat ki barkat mein takheer nahi hoti, aur hamare deedar ki sa'adat jald hi naseeb ho jaati, aisa Deedar jo haqeeqi Ma'arefat aur hamari nisbat sadaqat par mabni ho aur hamare makhfi rahne ki wajah ham tak pahunchne wale Aamaal ke alawa koi aur cheez nahi hai jabke hame unse aise Aamal ki ummeed nahi hai."*_
(Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Vol 2, P-315, Biharul Anwar, Vol 53, P-177, H-8.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ _*NEKI AUR BADI KA AJR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (920)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَنْ جَاءَ بِالْحَسَنَةِ فَلَهُ عَشْرُ أَمْثَالِهَا ۖ وَمَنْ جَاءَ بِالسَّيِّئَةِ فَلَا يُجْزَىٰ إِلَّا مِثْلَهَا وَهُمْ لَا يُظْلَمُونَ*

_"Jo koi Allah ke haan ek Neki layega to uske liye Das guna Ajr hai aur jo Badi le kar ayega use utna hi badla diya jayega jitna usne qusoor kiya hoga aur un par Zulm na kiya jayega."_
(Surah An'am: 160)

----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat ke zel mein kuchh Rivayaat mulaheza farmayen:
🎁
Imam Baqir (as) se Raavi ne sawal kiya Fazail, Ahkam o Hudood mein Momin aur Muslim ke darmiyan koi farq hai?
Imam (as): _"Nahi, lekin Momin ko Muslim ke banisbat Sawab zyada hai."_
Raavi: Lekin dono Namaz, Roza, Hajj aur Zakat mein barabar hain?
Imam (as):
_"Baat yahin tak mehdood nahi hai. Allah ne farmaya: "Khuda uske Ajr ko Das gunah badha dega." Jitna jiska Imaan mazboot hota hai utna hi Ajr mein izafa hota hai. Allah Ta'ala ek Momin ko Das se laa kar 70 guna tak Ajr ataa' kar deta hai."_
(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🎁
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_*"Ek Neki ke evaz Khuda 10 Nekiyan deta hai", lekin Neki ke liye Vilayat e Ali (as) zaroori hai. Jo shakhs Aqeeda e Vilayat rakh kar Neki kare to use har Neki ke evaz kam az kam Das Nekiyon ka Ajr milta hai. Agar Aqeeda e Vilayat ke baghair koi shakhs Neki karta hai to us Neki ki wajah se Duniyavi takleef khatm kar di jaati hai lekin Akherat mein uska koi hissa nahi hota."*_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)
🎁
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jab Allah ne Iblees ko bahut taqat ataa' ki to us waqt Hazrat Adam (as) ne kaha: "Parwardigar! Tu ne Iblees ko meri Nasl par musallat kar diya hai aur Tu ne use meri Aulad mein khoon ki tarah dakhil hone ki khuli chhoot de di hai, ab mera aur meri Aulad ka kiya banega?"_
_"Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: Tu aur Teri Aulad burai karegi to ek burai ke evaz ek burai likhi jayegi aur agar tum Neki karoge to ek Neki ke evaz 10 Nekiyan likhi jayengi."_
_"H. Adam (as): Parwardigar! Is mein aur izafa farma."_
_Allah ne farmaya: "Teri Aulad ke liye akheri saanso tak Tauba ka darwaza khula rahega."_
_"H. Adam (as): Parwardigar! Is mein aur izafa farma."_
_"Allah ne farmaya: "Mein Bakhsh dunga aur koi parwa na karunga."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🎁
Imam Zainul Abedin (as):
_"Us shakhs ke liye halakat hai jiska "Ikai" (One Unit) uski "Dahai" (Tens) par ghalib aa jaye."_
Logon ne iska matlab poochha.
Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya burai ke badle ek burai likhi jaati hai jabke ek Neki ke evaz Khuda 10 Nekiyan deta hai. Lehaza burai Ikai hai aur Neki Dahai hai. Woh shakhs bad naseeb hai jiski Ikaiyan (Units) unki Dahaiyon ko khaa jayen yani woh shakhs jo Din mein 10 buraiyan kare lekin ek Neki kare ke Mizan (Balance) Aamal barabar ho jaye."_
(Ma'anil Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
_"Aye Parwardigar! Tu mujhe pukarta hai to main Tujhse munh modta hun. Tu mujh se mohabbat karta hai, main Tujh se khafgi karta hun. Tu mere saath ulfat karta hai, main berukhi karta hun, jaisa ke mera Tujh par koi ehsaan raha ho. To bhi mera ye amal Tujhe mujh par Rehmat farmane aur mujh par apni ataa' o bakshish ke saath fazl o ehsaan karne se baaz nahi rakhta. Pus, Apne is nadaan bande par Rahem farma aur ispar Apne fazl o ehsaan se sakhawat farma. Beshak, Tu bada dene waala Sakhi hai."_
(Dua e E Iftitah)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

     ♦ _*NEKI AUR BADI KA AJR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (921)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَنْ جَاءَ بِالْحَسَنَةِ فَلَهُ عَشْرُ أَمْثَالِهَا ۖ وَمَنْ جَاءَ بِالسَّيِّئَةِ فَلَا يُجْزَىٰ إِلَّا مِثْلَهَا وَهُمْ لَا يُظْلَمُونَ*

_"Jo koi Allah ke haan ek Neki layega to uske liye Das guna Ajr hai aur jo Badi le kar ayega use utna hi badla diya jayega jitna usne qusoor kiya hoga aur un par Zulm na kiya jayega."_
(Surah An'am: 160)

----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
_*Sunnati Roza:*_
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Agar tum mein se kisi ne Sunnati Roza rakha hua ho aur woh is haalat mein apne kisi Momin bhai ka Mehman ho aur Mezbaan usse khaane ki farmayish kare to use Momin ko khush karne ke liye Roza tod dena chahiye. Allah Ta'ala us 10 Sunnati Rozon ka Sawab ataa' karega. Jaisa ke farmane Ilahi hai (6:160)."_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🎁
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Har mahine mein 3 Sunnati Roze rakhne chahiye. Pahle ashre mein Jumerat ke Din Roza rakhna chahiye aur Mahine ke doosre ashre mein Budh ke Din Roza rakhna chahiye aur teesre ashre mein Jumerat ka Din Roza rakhna chahiye."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🎁
Imam Ali (as):
_"Har mahine 3 Roze rakhne se Seene ke waswase khatm ho jaate hain aur har mahine ke 3 Roze "Saumud Dahr - *صوم الدهر* hamesha ka Roza shumar hota hai. Kyonki Allah farmata hai: (6:160)"_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🕌 _*Namaz:*_
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jo shakhs Namaz-e-Juma ki adayegi ke liye Imam se pahle Masjid mein jaye aur khamoshi se Khutba sune to ainda Juma tak uska ye amal unke gunahon ka Kaffara shumar kiya jayega. Iske alawa use mazeed 3 Dino ki ria'ayat bhi di jayegi kyonki farmane Khuda wandi hai (6:160)."_
(Amali Toosi)
🕌
Imam Zainul Abideen (as) ne apne walid se arz kiya:
_"Bhala Iski kya wajah hai ke jab Shabe Me'raj Allah Ta'ala ne hamare Naana Rasoole Khuda (saws) aur unki Ummat par 50 Namaze farz ki thi to unhone khuda se us waqt tak takhfeef (reduce) ki darkhwast na ki jab tak Moosa (as) ne unhe takhfeef ka mashwara nahi diya tha?"_
Imam Ali (as) ne farmaya:
_"Rasule Khuda (saws) ne Khuda darkhwast ki jab Musa (as) Shafa'at kuninda bane aur Hazrat Musa (as) ne shafa'at ki aur Rasoole Khuda (saws) ko khuda ki janib se 50 Namazon ki bajae sirf 5 baqi rah gayi aur ye 5 Namazen 50 Namazon ke Barabar hain Kyonke Allah Ta'ala ka farman hai.(6:160)"_
(Kitab At Tawheed, Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
_"Aye Ma'bood! Uske (Apne Wali e Amr (atfs) ke) zariye se hamare sinon ko shifa de aur hamare dilon se bughz keena mita de. Jis Haq mein hamara ikhtelaf hai, Apne hukm se uske zariye humein hidayat ataa' farma. Beshak, Tu jise chaahe seedhe raaste ki taraf le jaata hai. Uske zariye Apne aur hamare dushman par humein galba ataa farma. Aye sachche Khuda, aisa hi ho!"_
(Dua e Iftitah)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ _*MILLAT-E-IBRAHIM (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (922)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ إِنَّنِي هَدَانِي رَبِّي إِلَىٰ صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ دِينًا قِيَمًا مِلَّةَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حَنِيفًا ۚ وَمَا كَانَ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ*

_"Aap kah den ke mere Rab ne mujhe Seedhe Raaste ki Hidayat kar di hai. Bilkul Seedhe Deen ki jis mein koi kaji nahi hai. Woh Ibrahim ka tareeqa hai jise yaksoo ho kar (Upright) usne ikhtiyar kiya tha aur woh Mushrekin mein se nahi tha."_
(Surah An'am: 161)

📚📖 🕋
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein kis Deen ka zikr kiya gaya Rivayaat mulaheza farmayen:
🚩
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_*"Ibrahim (as) ka Deen mera Deen hai aur mera Deen uska Deen hai aur uski Sunnat meri Sunnat hai aur meri Sunnat Ibrahim (as) ki Sunnat hai aur meri Fazilat Ibrahim (as) ki Fazilat hai jabke mein usse Afzal hun.*"_
(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)
🚩
Imam Hasan Mujtaba (as):
_*"Millat e Ibrahim (as) par sirf ham aur hamare Shia hi qaem hain baqi log isse bezaar hain."*_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🚩
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Hazrat Ali (as) se farmaya:
_"Jis ne apne Deen ke tahaffuz ke liye mujhe Muhabbat ki aur tere Raaste par chala to woh un logon mein shumar kiya jayega jinhe Seerate Mustaqeem ki rahnumai naseeb hui hai."_
(Amali Toosi, Noorus Saqlain)
🕌
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Hanfiyat mein tamam cheezen maujood hain yahan tak us mein moochhon ka katrawana aur Nakhoon katwana aur Khatna tak shamil hai."_
_"Hamare aur hamare Shiyon ke alawa is Ummat mein se koi bhi Deen e Ibrahim par nahi hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🕌
Hazrat Ali (as):
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Allah ne apne Khaleel ko haqeeqat ke saath mab'oos farmaya aur use moochhe aur Nakhoon ke katne aur baghal (Armpit) saaf karne aur aur zere Naaf (Navel) Baal saaf karne aur Khatna (Circumcision) ka Hukm diya "_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🤲🏻
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
_"Bare Ilaha Mo'meneen ke Aamaal qubool farmaye, unhe Neki ki mazeed taufeeq ataa kare."_
(Falsafa e ghaibat e Mahdi (atfs) , p215)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sajjad (as)
ki khidmat mein ek shakhs ne arz ki ke main Aap ke khaalis (sincere) Shiyon mein se hun to aap ne farmaya:
_"Aye Banda e Khuda! Kya tu Ibrahim Khaleel (as) ke darje par faaiz hai? Allah ne to apne Khaleel ko Shia kaha hai:_
*وَإِنَّ مِنْ شِيعَتِهِ لَإِبْرَاهِيمَ * إِذْ جَاءَ رَبَّهُ بِقَلْبٍ سَلِيمٍ*
( _"Aur yaqeenan unhi ke Shiyon mein se Ibrahim (as) zarur the, jab wo apne Parwardigar ki taraf aisa dil liye huwe badhe jo har aib se paak tha."_ )
(Surah Saaffaat, Ayat 83, 84).
_Agar tera dil Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke dil ki tarah hai to tu beshak hamara Shia hai warna tu Faalij (paralysis) ya Juzaam (leprosy) ka mustaheq (deserving / layeq) hai taaki tere is jhoot ka kaffara ho."_
(Tafseer e Anwaar e Najaf, v12, p45)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 ♦ _*NAMAAZ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (923)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ إِنَّ صَلَاتِي وَنُسُكِي وَمَحْيَايَ وَمَمَاتِي لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ * لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ ۖ وَبِذَٰلِكَ أُمِرْتُ وَأَنَا أَوَّلُ الْمُسْلِمِينَ*

_"Aap kah den ke yaqeenan *meri Namaz* aur meri qurbani, mera jeena aur mera marna sab kuchh Allah Rabbul Alemeen ke liye hai Jiska koi shareek nahi hai. Mujhe iska Hukm diya gaya hai aur sab se pahle Sar Tasleem jhukane wala mein hun (First Muslim)."_
(Surah An'am: 162 - 163)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein jaisa ke tazkara hua ke Deen e Ibrahim aur hamare Deen ek hi Deen hai. Shariyat Muhammadi sab Allah ke liye hai. Namaz aur tamam Ibadaten sab Allah ke liye hai. Yahan tak hamari poori zindagi Allah ke liye hai.
Islam ki buniyad Tauheed hai aur Namaz Tauheed bil Fe'l hai. Jisne Namaz se inkaar ki usne Kufr ikhtiyar kiya. Is mazmoon par pahle bhi kafi Rivayaat pesh kar chuke hain.
Is Mahine Mubarak jis mein Imam e Asr ki Viladat hui unke qaul mulaheza farmayen:
🕌
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
*ما أرغم ألف الشيطان أفضل من الصلاة، فصلها و أرغم أنف الشيطان.*

_"Namaz ki tarah koi bhi cheez Shaitan ki Naak ko zameen par nahi ragadti, lehaza Namaz padho aur Shaitan ki Naak zameen par ragdo."_
(Kamaluddin, Vol 2, P-520, H-49, Biharul Anwar, Vol 53, P-182, H-11)
🕌
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
*ملعون ملعون من أخر الغداة إلى أن تنقضى النجوم.*

_"Mal'oon hai, Mal'oon hai woh shakhs jo Namaz e Subh mein (jan boojh kar) itni takheer (delay) kare jiski wajah se (Aasmaan ke) Sitaare doob jayen."_
(Al Ghaibah Toosi, P-271, Biharul Anwar, Vol 52, P-16)
🕌
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
*الصلوة عمود الدين، إن قبلت قبلت ما سواها و إن ردت ردت ما سواها.*
_"Namaz Deen ka Pillar hai, agar ye qubool to sab Aamaal qubool, ye radd to sab Aamaal radd."_
🤲🏻
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
*أكثروا الدعاء بتعجيل الفرج، فإن ذلك فرجكم.*
_"Mere Zuhoor ke liye kasrat se Dua kiya karo, kyonki is mein khud tumhare liye asaaesh hai."_
(Kamaluddin, Vol 2, P-485, H-4, Biharul Anwaar, Vol 53, P-181, H-10)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww):
ki Wasiyyat:
_"Aye Ali, main tumhein hidayat karta hun ke kuchh aadaton ki hifazat karna…_
_Namaz e Shab padhna,_
_Namaz e Shab padhna,_
_Namaz e Shab padhna."_
(40 Hadith)
🕌
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Namaz e Shab padha karo. Ye Hazrat Muhammad (saww) ki Sunnat hai, tumse pehle waale Swaliheen ki Aadat hai aur tumhare jismon se bimariyan door karti hai."_
(Sawaabul Aamaal, p89)
