        ♦ _*HAYAT O MAUT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (920)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ إِنَّ صَلَاتِي وَنُسُكِي وَمَحْيَايَ وَمَمَاتِي لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ * لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ ۖ وَبِذَٰلِكَ أُمِرْتُ وَأَنَا أَوَّلُ الْمُسْلِمِينَ*

_"Aap kah den ke yaqeenan meri Namaz aur *meri qurbani, mera jeena aur mera marna sab kuchh Allah Rabbul Alemeen ke liye hai Jiska koi shareek nahi hai.* Mujhe iska Hukm diya gaya hai aur sab se pahle Sar Tasleem jhukane wala mein hun (First Muslim)."_
(Surah An'am: 162 - 163)

📚📖 🌱🍃
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Maut o Hayat sab Allah ke mein hai. Ye Takveenat e Ilahiyah mein se hai. Yani ye hamare liye muqaddar kar di gayi hai.
Ab chunke ye Allah ki ataa' karda hai to ye bhi Allah ke liye honi chahiye. Isi liye kahte hain. (Qur'an mein bhi hai):
*الَّذِينَ إِذَا أَصَابَتْهُمْ مُصِيبَةٌ قَالُوا إِنَّا لِلَّهِ وَإِنَّا إِلَيْهِ رَاجِعُونَ*
(Baqarah: 156)
Iska matlab ye hai ke ham Allah ke saamne tasleem (surrendered) hain. Ab jo Allah ka Hukm hoga uski ta'meel honi chahiye. Ye raasta hame nahi maloom, Muhammad wa Ale Mohammad hamko is Jeevan Shaili ki taa'leem dete hain.
😏
Imam Sadiq (as)
se ek shakhs ne kaha, _"Main zindagi se ukta gaya (kantal gaya) hun, main Allah se Maut ki tamanna karta hoon."_(Suicide karna)
Imam (as) ne farmaya:

_"Zindagi ki qeemat ye hai ke tum ita'at karo aur na-farmani na karo. Lihaza, agar tum zinda raho aur ita'at karo to ye tumhare liye Maut se behtar hai jisme tum na to ita'at kar sakte ho aur na hi na-farmani kar sakte ho."_
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p28)
🌏
Imam Ali (as):
_"Duniya Momin ka qaid-khana, Maut uska tohfa aur Jannat uski manzil hai. Duniya kaafiro'n ki Jannat hoti hai aur maut use is (Jannat) se judaa karnewali aur Aag uski manzil hoti hai."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Duniya)
🤲🏻
*اللهم اجعل محياي محيا محمد وآل محمد، ومماتي ممات محمد وآل محمد*

_Khudaya! Meri Hayat ko Muhammad wa Aale Muhammad ki Zindagi aur meri Maut ko unke raaste par qarar dena."_
(Ziyarat e Ashura)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
*Imam Mahdi (atfs):*
*أقدار الله عزوجل لا تغالب و إرادته لا ترد و توفيقه لا يسبق.*

_"Jo cheezen Khuda wande Aalam ne muqaddar farma Di hain wo kabhi maghloob (overcome) nahi hoti, aur Uska Iraada kabhi radd nahi hota, aur uski Taufeeq par koi cheez sabqat hasil nahi kar sakti."_
(Kamaluddin, Vol 2, O-511, H-42, Biharul Anwaar, Vol 53, P-191, H-19.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

        ♦ _*AWWAL MUSLIM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (925)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

قُلْ إِنَّ صَلَاتِي وَنُسُكِي وَمَحْيَايَ وَمَمَاتِي لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ * لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ ۖ وَبِذَٰلِكَ أُمِرْتُ *وَأَنَا أَوَّلُ الْمُسْلِمِينَ*

_"Aap kah den ke yaqeenan meri Namaz aur meri qurbani, mera jeena aur mera marna sab kuchh Allah Rabbul Alemeen ke liye hai Jiska koi shareek nahi hai. Mujhe iska Hukm diya gaya hai *aur sab se pahle Sar Tasleem jhukane wala mein hun (First Muslim)."*_
(Surah An'am: 162 - 163)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Paighambar e Islam (saww) ko Awwal Muslim kaha gaya hai, jabke ham pahle sabit kar chuke hain ke sabhi Anbiya Muslim the. Qur'an mein jahan Anbiya ko Muslim qarar diya hai wo Ayaat ye hain:
(Yunus: 72) (Baqarah: 128) (Yusuf: 101).... etc. Iske alawa aur bhi hain.
Iske bahut se wujuhat hain: Ek to ye ke is Islam ki Importance, kyonki rivayat hai:
*الاسلام هو التسليم*
( _"Islam bus sirf Tasleem hai."_)
Pas Paighambar e Islam (saww) Tasleem ke aala darje par the.
Baaz Rivayaat ke mutabiq Paighambar e Islam (saww) ne Aalam e Arwah / Alam e Zar mein Allah ne apni Uloohiyat ka iqrar liya to Aap (saww) ne sab se pahle jawab diya. Jaisa ke Aap (saww) ki hadis hai:
*كنت نبيا و آدم بين الماء و الطين.*
( _"Mein us waqt bhi Nabi tha jab Adam (as) Aab o Gil ke darmiyan karwat le rahe the."_)
Isliye bhale Aap (saww) is Duniya mein Khatamul Anbiya hain lekin unki Noorani Khilqat Hazrat Adam (as) se bhi pahle hui.
*اول ما خلق الله نورى.*
_"Sab se pahle mera Noor Khalq hua."_
🤲🏻
Bare Ilaha hame ba Imaan Muslim ki hasiyat se uthana.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Wilayat e Ali (as) ka itteba (follow / paalan) karna aur unki *Wilayat ko Tasleem karna* tumhare umoor (affairs) ko pareshaan na hone dega, Adl o Insaaf ko tumse qaem rakhega aur aakhir tumko Jannat mein pahuncha dega."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p81)
🕌
Imam Reza (as):
_"Hamare Shia hamare hukm ke saamne *sar Tasleem kham karte hain* aur hamare Ahkam ko baja laate hain, hamare dushman ke mukhalif hain. Pus, jo in sifaat ba-kamaal ka malik nahi hai wo hum mein se nahi hai."_
(Ausaaf ush Shia - Shaikh Sadooq, p22)
🕌
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jab Allah kisi bande ko Ne'mat ata kare aur wo banda *Dil se Tasleem kare* aur pehchan le ke ye ne'mat Allah ki taraf se hai to usne jaise Shukr ka haq ada kar diya."_
(Aimma Allah ki Ne'mat hain.)
(Mishkaat ul Anwaar (Urdu), p63)
🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_*"Khush-Naseeb hai wo shakhs jisne mere Ahle Bait (as) ke Qaim (atfs) ko dekha aur unke Qayam se pehle unki iqteda ki, unhe Imam Tasleem kiya aur unse pehle Aimma e Huda (as) ko Imam maana aur unke Dushmanon se bezaari ki. Wohi mere rafeeq aur meri nazar mein meri Ummat mein sabse zyada moazziz (honorable) hai."*_
(Jamaal e Muntazar, p801)

      ♦ _*MUJRIM KE AAL KO SAZA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (926)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ أَغَيْرَ اللَّهِ أَبْغِي رَبًّا وَهُوَ رَبُّ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ ۚ وَلَا تَكْسِبُ كُلُّ نَفْسٍ إِلَّا عَلَيْهَا ۚ وَلَا تَزِرُ وَازِرَةٌ وِزْرَ أُخْرَىٰ ۚ ثُمَّ إِلَىٰ رَبِّكُمْ مَرْجِعُكُمْ فَيُنَبِّئُكُمْ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ فِيهِ تَخْتَلِفُونَ*

_"Aap kah den ke kya mein Allah ke siwa koi aur Rab talash karun jabke Wohi tamam cheezon ka Rab hai aur har shakhs apne Aamaal ka khud zimmedar hai. Koi bojh uthane wala doosre ka boojh nahi uthata. Phir tum sab ko apne Rab ke Huzoor mein palatna hai aur waqt tumhare ikhtelafat ki haqeeqat se agah kar dega."_
(Surah An'am: 164)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat ke kuchh hisse ka tazkara hamne 29th April, 2018 ko kar chuke hain, refer kar sakte hain.
🕌
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah Gunahgar ke evaz be-Gunah ko nahi pakadta aur Waledain ke Gunahon ke evaz Aulad ka muhaseba nahi karta. Jaisa ke Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya (6:164)"_
(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)
🕌
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Tere bayen haath ka badla tere dayen haath se nahi liya jayega."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Noorus Saqlain)
🕌
Imam Mohd Baqar (as):
Imam Zainul Abedin (as) Bani Ke giroh ka tazkara karte the jinhe Khuda Maskh karke Bandar bana diya tha. Qisse ke tamam hone ke baad hazerin na sawal kiya:
_"Maula! Ye Buraiyan to aaj se hazaron saal qabl Israeliyon ne ki thi magar iski kya wajah hai ke Qur'an mein Allah ne Yahoodiyon ko unke Afa'al ki sarzanish ki jabke Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke waqt jo Yahoodi the unhone is tarah ka koi Jurm nahi kiya tha. Aur ye Ayat bhi hai (6:164)?"_
Imam Zainul Abedin (as) ne farmaya:
_"Qur'an Majeed Arabi zaban mein nazil hua aur iske khitab ka andaza bhi wohi hai jo ke Ahle Arab ke khitab ka hai. Agar Bani Teem ka ek giroh kisi Shahr ko apni loot mar ka nishana banaye to Ahle Arab har Tameemi se ye kahte hain, "hamne Bani Falan ke saath ye sulook kiya," "hamne Falan ke Khandan ko qaed kiya, aur hamne Falah Shahr ko tabah kiya." Is tarah ke jumlon se unka maqsad ye nahi hota ke unhone bazaate khud ye kaam sar anjam diye hain, is tarah ke alfaaz se woh ye zahir karte hain ke ye kaam unki qaum ne kiye the. Lehaza in Ayaat mein La'anat malamat to dar haqiqat unke Aslaaf (purvaj) ko ki gayi ha albatta Lughat e Arab ke tahet khitab unki naslon se kiya gaya hai aur is khitab ki ahm wajah ye thi ke is waqt ke Yahoodi apne buzurgon ke Qabeeh Afa'al (bad Actions) par Raazi the aur unhe durust qarar dete the. Is liye unko is tarah ke alfaaz kahna Sahih the ke tumne ye kiya. *Maqsad ye hai unke Qabeeh Aamaal par Raazi hon."*_

Ziyarat e Ashura mein Ale Marwan wa Alo Ibne Zyad par La'anat ki bhi yehi wajah hai.
🤲🏻
*لَعَنَ اللهُ اُمَّۃً قَتَلَتْكَ وَ لَعَنَ اللهُ اُمَّۃً ظَلَمَتْكَ وَلَعَنَ اللهُ اُمَّۃً سَمِعَتْ بِذَالِكَ فَرَضِیَتْ بِہِ۔*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
*انا خاتم ألاوصياء، و بى يدفع الله عزوجل البلاء عن أهلى و شيعتى.*

_"Mein Khatemul Ausiya hun aur Khuda wande Aalam mere sabab aur waseele se mere Ahl aur mere Shiyon se Balaon ko door karta hai."_
(Kamaluddin, Vol 2, P-441, H-12, Al Ghaiba Toosi, P-246, H-415, Biharul Anwaar, Vol 52, P-30, H-25)

        ♦ _*ALLAH KA KHALIFA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (927)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَهُوَ الَّذِي جَعَلَكُمْ خَلَائِفَ الْأَرْضِ وَرَفَعَ بَعْضَكُمْ فَوْقَ بَعْضٍ دَرَجَاتٍ لِيَبْلُوَكُمْ فِي مَا آتَاكُمْ ۗ إِنَّ رَبَّكَ سَرِيعُ الْعِقَابِ وَإِنَّهُ لَغَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ*

_*"Wohi Allah to hai jisne tumhe Zameen par Janasheen banaya* aur tum mein baaz ko baaz ke muqabile mein zyada darje diye taake Usne jo kuchh tumko diya hai us mein tumhari azmaish kare. Beshak tumhara Rab saza dene mein bahut tez hai aur Woh bahut Darguzar (forgive) karne wala aur Rahem karne wala hai."_
(Surah An'am: 165)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat main  *خلائف* jama hai *خليفة* ki. Yani Janasheen.

Allah ne Hazrat Adam (as) ke liye farma:
*وَإِذْ قَالَ رَبُّكَ لِلْمَلَائِكَةِ إِنِّي جَاعِلٌ فِي الْأَرْضِ خَلِيفَةً ۖ*
(Baqarah: 30)
_"Mein Zameen par Khalifa bana raha hun."_
*يَا دَاوُودُ إِنَّا جَعَلْنَاكَ خَلِيفَةً فِي الْأَرْضِ* (Sad: 26)
_"Ay Dawood! Hamne tumko Zameen par Khalifa banaya."_
In Ayaat se pata chalta hai ke *Khalifa* ko banane ka haq sirf Allah ko hai. Is mein Insaan ka koi dakhal nahi. Insaan ko ye haq nahi ke woh apna Khalifa chune. Chunke Deen Allah ka hai to iska paricharak bhi Allah ka Numainda / partinidhi hona chahiye. Agar ham khud se kisi ko chun lenge to woh apni man mani karega jaisa ke aajkal Neta ke chunne mein hota hai. Insaan jab apni Ma'arefat nahi rakhta to doosre ko kya pahchanega ke kaun sahi Rahbar hai. Isliye Khalifa ke liye "Ismat" *عصمت* shart hai.
Is Ayat ko aksar tafasir mein ye zahir kiya hai ke iske maani ye hain ke Allah ne ham sabko pichhle Aslaaf ka khalifa banaya. Ye Aqlan ghalat hai. Ek company mein agar sab manager ho jayen to kaun kisko follow karega.
Jabke is Ayat ke sahi maani zahir hain.
Allah apni Nabi se khitab kar raha hai ke Allah ne tumhe Zameen par apna Janasheen banaya.
Jab Allah ke Khalifa Nabi hain to Nabi ke Khalifa Imam bhi *منصوص من الله* hain.
Logon ke banaye hue Khalifa ke haalat logon ke saamne hain aur Zahir hain.

Sura An'am ki Akheri Ayat khatm hui. Inshaallah Ramzan ke baad aage silsilah jari rahega.

(Surah Baqarah se An'am tak ki Tafseer hamari Website par refer kar sakte hain.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤲🏻
Imam Mahdi (atfs):
_"Aye Ma'bood! Rehmat farma Apne Wali e Amr (atfs) par ke jo Qaem, Ummeed-gaah, Aadil aur Muntazar hai. Uske gird Apne muqarrab Farishton ka ghera laga de. Aur Roohul Qudus ke zariye uski ta'eed farma. Aye jahanon ke Parwardigar! Use Apni Kitab ki taraf dawat dene wala aur Apne Deen ke liye Qaem qarar de. *Use Zameen mein Apna Khalifa bana, jaise unko Khalifa banaya jo us se pahle ho guzre hain.* Apne pasandida Deen ko uske liye paedaar bana de. Uske khauf ke baad use aman de ke wo Tera Ibadat-guzar hai, kisi ko Tera shareek nahi banata."_
(Dua e Iftitah)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

The End of Surah.
